ɣef waya skecmen-t ɣer lḥebs seg laɛḍil ad iɛeddi deg ccraɛ
tenniḍ ihi yessenger tawacult
llan aṭas n yinehharen ur llin ara d isekranen xedmen ibaxixen gellun-d ula d nutni s ungar n waṭas n twaculin maca ɣas akken ur ten-skecmen ara ɣer lḥebs ur ten-urdin s wanɣa
maca mi ara nwali igemmaḍ ad ten-naf kif-kif-iten  timenɣiwt n yimdanen imeɣban ulac acu xedmen
maca ameddekkel-nneɣ tuɣ-it d asekran
yernu yeẓra s wacu tgellu tenhart ma yesker umdan
d acu n umgired yellan gar tmasit n usekṛan-agi d tmasit n unehhar ur neḥbis ara sdat n tafat tazaggaɣt dɣa yenɣa albaɛḍ  anehhar-agi ula d netta yeẓra yella umihi ma ur yeḥbis ara sdat n tafat tazeggaɣt neɣ ma yezger i ujerriḍ awraɣ deg yimekwan uḍyiqen
d tidet ayen i d-teqqareḍ
ɣas akken imsulta ad ḍeggren amezwaru deg lḥebs maca wis sin ulac acu ad as-xedmen ad yuɣal s axxam-is
ur ufiɣ ara acu ad as-rreɣ
yerna si nasser ikemmel deg wawal-is 
d inɣiyen n tallit tatiknuluǧit ar tura mazal ur tt-yefri ara usaḍuf yid-sen
anɣi deg usaḍuf icudd ɣer nniya n win i t-ixedmen ma yella s tidet yebna ɣef ccer mačči ɣer yiqurar swyes igellu
s unamek niḍen ma yella baɛmada i t-yexdem
win ara yewwten albaɛḍ s ujenwi yettwaḥseb d aneḍlib acku yenwa ad yuqem ccer ma yella d abaxix n ṭumubil ulac nniya-nni n ccer deg lasel
d acu ara as-nexdem ihi  d wagi i d ugur n teɣdemt ama i unezzarfu neɣ i umastan
tigawin n umdan ddsent kersent yewɛer fell-aneɣ ad tent-nefreq s sshala gar lxir d ccer
teɣli-d tsusmi gar-aneɣ kra n lweqt sakin yesseqsa-yi-d si nasser 
ɣur-k keččini d acu-tt tawuri n umastan 
ad iḥudd ɣef wid yettuḍelmen
kečč d arumansi iban teɣriḍ
nniɣ-as s unecraḥ 
ɣriɣ-as  imeɣban  yegzem tasa-w
s tidet teɣriḍ ungal-agi  tafransisst n tewɛer
ɣriɣ tasuqilt-ines ɣer taɛrabt d ungal i d-yeffɣen deg tmurt n lubnan
ah
lmuhim ilaq ad teẓreḍ belli tawuri n umastan d aḥuddu ɣef yal yiwen yurdan s wanɣi ɣas iqqer-d yis-s mebla ma nefka azal i wayen yexdem
anamek n uḥuddu ɣef yineḍliben mačči d aɛǧab i aɣ-yeɛǧeb wayen i yexdem
anamek n uḥuddu d tikci i win yellan deg lḥebs yakk allalen i as-ilaqen akken ad iḥudd ɣef yiman-is acku acḥal d abrid i nufa ttwaḥebsen deg lbaṭel
tura ma iban-d ayen i yexdem d tidet s ttbut ad yawi tarrut ɛlaḥsab asaḍuf
akka i uɣaleɣ d amastan
d zzher i yi-yeldin tiwwura ɣer twuri-agi
nabil nemḍel-it ass-a umbaɛd taẓallit n lɛesr
aṭas i nɛeṭṭel deg ssbiṭar
sserwan-aɣ tazzla deffir n lekwaɣeḍ
urag sya wayeḍ syihin
yernu yal tikkelt nessutur deg yiɛessasen d tullas n tmarit neɣ n ssikritarya ad aɣ-ɛiwnen akken ad naf aɣella n umeẓlu iwakken ad aɣ-yezmel neɣ ad-aɣ-yestenyi arraten-nni i aɣ-ssutren
tcetkayen irkelli ɣef lxedma i ten-staqfen
s nnefxa i ttaṭṭafen amru ad bdun sakin acetki ɣellin-d kan ɣef uqerruy-iw deg uxeddim ttqelliben fell-i deg ssaḥ ulac d aḍu kan  lfayda d nitni i tt-yewwin tiwuɣa d nekkni i tent-ibubben ad luzinat n yisaffagen yettafgen gar tɣileḍ sefraken yimtiwgen
dayen ula d imasayen imeẓyanen yekcem-iten waṭṭan n temɣer n ccan uɣalen ttwalin imdanen seg yigenni
mi ara tefkeḍ i unawar adabu n uzmal yettuɣal d azrem axeddim-is yuɣal d tuqqsa kan yernu ur tselleḍ ɣef yiles-is ḥala   akud-inu ɣlay yettwaḥseb s ddqiqa tura ad nejmaɛeɣ akked mass anemhal  ɣur-i ccɣel deg tenmehla
 d tagi i d lezzayer
yal yiwen yebna tigduda deg uqerruy-is yesselḥa-yi-tt s leqwanen-ines netta
ur nessaweḍ ara ad nessuffeɣ tafekka armi i inessef wass nerfa mačči d kra qrib ad neṭṭerḍeq
nruḥ srid s axxam anda i t-nessers deg usalun iɣef yemmeɣ leḥzen d yimeṭṭawen kra nufa-ten deɛɛun sidi rebbi s rreḥma ɣef umerḥum ur nɛeṭṭel ara neffeɣ ad nerǧu deg tlemmast n umraḥ n uɣerbaz alemmas
racid benɣusa yessusem kan ur yeẓri ara akk ayen i iḍerrun din ad as-tiniḍ d taɛeqqact n lehyuf i yečča
deg tsebḥit-nni daɣen ur yembawel ara maḍi netta i yuɣen tannumi ireffu mebla ma tella ssebba tameqqrant
yeqqim kan yettraǧu deg-i ur iḥerrek ara nekk seg tama-w ur ḥbiseɣ tazzla gar tgennariyin imeqqranen ttqellibeɣ ɣef yimasayen rekkmeɣ reggmeɣ weḥd-i am uderwic
mi yedden ṭṭhur muqqleɣ ssaɛa-inu sakin muqqleɣ-t netta ur iḥerrek ara irkelli yesbek
nniɣ-as s uɛeggeḍ akken ad iyi-isell 
d lawan ad nruḥ ɣer tmeqbert
yeldi allen-is brarḥent ad as-tiniḍ seg uqeggel i d-yuki yesrugmet kra n wawalen ur negzi ara sakin yeṭṭef ddruǧ akken ad yali s axxam
nekker-d neḍfer-it mebla axemmem
abrid ɣer tmeqbert yeččur s waluḍ d yibellaɛen n waman
s ṭṭul n yiḍ ur yeḥbis ara ugeffur
tagnawt berriket s usigna i iɣummen tamdint
ula d asemmiḍ yessenta accaren-is deg tizi-agi taɛlayant i iqublen illel seg tama n ugafa d yignan n mitiǧa d yidurar n ccriɛa seg tama n wunẓul yexdeɛ yakk wid yeqqimen s yiselsa n unebdu
deg wussan n ugeffur ḥezzneɣ mliḥ acku tettekkes-as i temdint ula ciṭuḥ n ccbaḥa-nni i tesɛa
ini n ssiman yettaɣ yakk iɣurab ur nettwasebɣen ara seg tallit n
sidna nuḥ
aluḍ yettaččar iberdan
tikli n ṭumubilat tettiwɛir mliḥ
yettuɣal yinig ɣas d awezzlan d tarrut ara k-yessuffɣen laɛqel
deg tallit-agi i tselleḍ imdanen reggmen neṭṭqen s yir lehdur
nesseḥbes ṭumubilat ɣef ubrid yessan s ugudrun
uzzleɣ akken ad ten-ɛiwneɣ deg urfud n nneɛc am wakken i xedmeɣ deg ssbiṭar
maca zwaren-iyi kra n yilmeẓyen jehdit mačči d kra kra deg-sen s yiččumar d yiqendyar kksen-aɣ nneɛc seg yifassen-nneɣ sersen-t ɣef tuyat-nsen dɣa serḥen-as s tazzla ɣer tmeqbert ur cliɛen deg waluḍ ur sen-tuqiɛ deg yixejḍan n waman ttalsen s uɛeggeḍ   la ilaha illa llah 
la ilaha illa llah
banen-iyi-d d iberraniyen
muqqleɣ ɣer kra n wudmawen ahat ad ɛeqleɣ yiwen deg-sen
ulac  ur ten-walaɣ ara uqbel  dagi i ten-tuɣ ttraǧun deg-neɣ  tuɣ-iten deg umraḥ n uɣerbaz alemmas maca ur rriɣ ara tidmi-w ɣur-sen 
ssikdeɣ ɣer racid limmer ad iyi-d-yini kra
yezmer lḥal ttilin-as ɣas seg mbaɛid  rraw n watmaten n leɛmum neɣ n lexwal
ufiɣ ulac acu i ibeddlen deg-s teɣli-d fell-as twaɣit dɣa yeggugem
tuɣal-d ɣer wallaɣ-iw tugna n
nabil mi yeẓẓel ɣef lqaɛa ddaw n umesbaḥ s yiselsa-ines n
afɣanistan
hatta tiyita n udfel s aqerruy-iw i yi-yesfaqen
amek i yi-truḥ tidet-agi
ḥemdeɣ yakuc mi yeɣleq racid ɣef yiman-is yakk tiwwura tili atan irekkem seg wurfan ur yettaǧǧa ara wid yenɣan mmi-s am wakken i sen-yessawal ad ḥeḍren i tenṭel-is
ad nɣen lmegget wa ad ttrun deg tenṭel-ines
iban ulac acu ad asen-yeǧǧ ad ten-yergem wa ad ten-yesseɛseq
ireffu ɣef wulac yernu ur ixeddem ara leḥsab i yinalkamen n tigawin-ines
ǧǧiɣ iberraniyen-nni ad kemmlen abrid-nsen s tazzla nekk kemmleɣ abrid-iw s laɛqel kan uggadeɣ ad ccḍeɣ deg waluḍ
d tidet nekk d mmi-s n taddart sɛeddaɣ temẓi-inu irkelli d tazzla gar yiberdan n umadaɣ d tẓegwa ttaliɣ tsubbuɣ maca uɣaleɣ mi ad mmektiɣ imekwan-nni d uqrur-nni amcum iqerreḥ-iyi lḥal mačči d kra
ccfawat-agi ttuɣalent-iyi-d deg tegnatin n leḥzen d ticeqqufin kan mi ara qqimeɣ weḥd-i ttbadaɣ mgal-nsent ttuɣalent ɣur-i mebla anaɛruḍ dɣa ad rreɣ yakk tiwwura akken ur keccment ara ɣur-i
yernu gulleɣ ur ttuɣaleɣ ara s imeḍqan-nni seg wasmi temmut yemma umbaɛd n tmettant n gma i tt-yerẓan seg daxel yekkes-as lbenna n tudert
lliɣ d aqrur ameẓyan yeskerkiren iḍarren-is deg yicifaḍ iqdimen qersen ur k-ttḥamin ɣef usemmiḍ wala ɣef tubezgin neɣ ɣef waluḍ
tura uɣaleɣ d amastan yesɛan deg uxxam-is seddiset n tyugwin n yissebbaḍen ɣlayit sefḍeɣ-tent yal tikkelt mi ara ffɣeɣ
yernu tura ur sseɛyayeɣ ara iḍarren-iw ṭumubil tekkes-iyi ugur n tikli ɣas ulamma i twinest n lmitrat
ɛuhdeɣ iman-iw ad meḍleɣ lḥif aberkan i lebda
yettbin-d seg berra am wakken meḍleɣ-t s tidet maca yugi ad ifareq ccfawat-inu yuɣal yezdeɣ-iyi yesseɛya-yi yettarez-iyi ɣur-s i waṭas n lweqt
win ara i yi-iwalin ttzuxxuɣ s tkustimt-inu tahuskayt s tekrabaḍt-inu d yissebbaḍen-iw yeṭṭiriqen ad t-terkeb tismin acku ad yiɣil deg lǧennet i ttidireɣ
ɛeddi ɣef uɛemmi-k telsiḍ ur yeẓri ɣef wacu tensiḍ  ayen yeffren d uffiren n dir-i ddaw n tlaba-agi d ccfawat qerriḥen ur ten-tekkes ara ula d tamnafet n yigelliden n wagim n yuḍan d yiwen n yiḍ
ussan-agi ineggura zgiɣ deg tmqebrin
ad yester rebbi
ur ḥemmleɣ ara ad beddreɣ ayen n dir
d yir lfal  iḍelli kan neḥḍer i tenṭelt n sin seg seddis n yimsulta yemmuten deg tcerket n yiḍelli
d arraw n ɛin-el-kerma
wiyaḍ wwin-ten ɣer tudrin-nsen akken ad ten-meḍlen
timeqbert teččur s yiselsa tizegzawin d leslaḥ
kra kan seg yimezdaɣ i iḥedren tinṭelt yernu uɣen tannumi zewwiren ɣer tmeqbert mi ara yettwamḍel walbaɛḍ ssnen-t neɣ ur t-ssinen
ɣer tuget n lmumnin d lwaǧeb am wakken tella deg yisɣanen niḍen
uɣalen medden ttmuqulen tigawt n tuddin deg tneṭlin s wallen n tnezzut ɣur-sen d tagnit anda ad jemɛen amur ameqqran n lḥasanat akken ad kecmen ɣer lǧennet
tesderwec-iten lǧennet n yakuc mi uysen seg lǧennet n umdan
ɣef waya nettwali imdanen xedmen seg wul yal tigawt i igellun s lḥasanat
ad slen kan tella tanṭelt n walbaɛḍ ad ǧǧen lecɣal-nsen wa ad azlen ɣer tmeqbert i d-yezgan tura deg tlemmast umbaɛd mi tt-ttuɣ ɣef rrif n ɛin-el-kerma asmi tella d tameẓyant
amdan d uḍɛif sdat n tmettant ladɣa ma mačči d tin n
rebbi am ubaxix n ubrid neɣ timenɣiwt
ttwalin deg yibaxixen-agi d afus n leqder i yekkaten kan yezmer ad ten-inal ula d nitni ɛla ɣila
ɣef waya ttemyizwaren ɣer tneṭlin ad ten-tafeḍ ttmeslayen mebla aneḥbus ssawalen i teḥkayin yessewhamen ɣef yibaxixen yeḍran aṭas aya deg lqern n ddunit am wakken bɣan ad ssizdgen iman-nsen seg lxuf n tmettant i ten-izedɣen ad as-tiniḍ s ibeddi-nsen ɣef yiri n uẓekka bɣan ad siḥnen ul n tmettant akken ad ten-tezgel
maca ass-a wehmeɣ mi ur ten-walaɣ ara deg tenṭelt
yenna-yi-d umastan buɛlam seɛdun iwumi ssawalen yimidawen-is takubanit n buɛlam i yisallen acku ulac asali i as-yettruḥun yesla-d sɣur ukewwac tasebḥit-agi d akken teffeɣ-d yiwet n lfetwa i igedlen aneḥḍur deg tneṭlin n yimsulta yettwanɣan
anwa i d-yessuffɣen lfetwa-agi  ẓran irkelli wid i tt-yessuffɣen maca ulac win i izemren ad ten-yessenzen
tenṭelt ssuffɣen kra n yimsulta taggara n timeẓyanin-nsen bdan tiyita n rrsas ɣer yigenni
d tiririt n ttar i bɣan ad sbeggnen s tigawt-agi neɣ d tuggdi i ran ad snejlin seg wulawen-nsen  udmawen-nsen berrikit seg wurfan allen-nsen ččurent s ddɣel d lbeɣḍ
beggsen i umennuɣ
qrib i d-tuɣal tmeqbert-nni d annar i uselmed n usemres n leslaḥ amer ur yessekcem ara iman-is yiwen n ufesyan i yerran talast i lkarnafal-agi
rriḥa n lbarud tɛeṭṭel deg yinzaren-nneɣ
iban ur yaɛǧib ara lḥal i yimsulta imi d iserdasen i iḍefren imzernanen i sen-irewlen
si aḥmed yella ɣef uqerru n wid yerfan
azekka-nni tameddit mi d-ruḥeɣ ɣur-s s axxam n yimsulta akken ad waliɣ acu i as-yeḍran i yusef ɛeyyaci win i ttḥudduɣ yenna-iyi-d llan kra n yisallen i d-yeqqaren yakk imeḥbas rewlen anagar yiwen ufan-t yettwajreḥ dɣa wwin-t ɣer ssbiṭar
xemmemeɣ ad ruḥeɣ ɣer ssbiṭar maca ẓriɣ amejruḥ deg tegnatin yecban tigi ttɛassan fell-as mliḥ acku yettuɣal d inigi ayiwan ḥala netta i izemren ad as-yinin d acu yeḍran s tidet
ḥala ameddakkel-iw si aḥmed i yi-d-yegran akken ad iyi-yefk isallen i ḥwaǧeɣ
ruḥeɣ ɣur-s armi tɛedda lmeɣreb zriɣ deg lweqt-nni ineɣess fell-as ccɣel i d-yennernan fell-as ass-nni
ur yerǧi ara iseqsiyen-inu
ɛeggu d truẓi banent ɣef wallen-is akked ɣef tergagayt n taɣect-is
 acu ad ak-d-iniɣ a gma ɛebdelqader  ur cukkeɣ ara llan wawalen i zemren ad gelmen tucmit-nni i walaɣ tanezzayt-agi  tiwelfin nuɣ tannumi nettwali-tent kan deg yisura n lxuf
tettḥaz-aɣ kan mi ara tent-nwali acku neẓra d ddikur kan imawlan-is ttuɣalen srid ɣer taḍsa asmi ara kfun asewwer
maca ayen walant wallen-iw tikkelt-a ur yelli ara d ddikur
d tifekkiwin tiɛeryanin kksen fell-asent sser kksen-asent iselsa unsiben d leslaḥ-nsen ukren-ten rraw n leḥram akken ad ten-sxedmen deg tsergalin-nsen neɣ mi ara ẓeḍmen ɣef yimdanen deg yiḍ
tuget deg-sen mezzlen ttwawten s yijenwiyen ad tegzem tasa-k
iqerra-nsen qrib ad qelɛen ɣef tfekwin-nsen
iban tuget deg-sen ur mmuten ara s rrsas dɣa kemmlen fell-asen lewḥuc-nni s yijenwiyen
cwi kan wwḍen yisexsayen uqbel ma ttečč times ayen yellan yakk deg ukamyun sensen times dɣa smenɛen tfekkiwin seg tmerɣiwt
nekk i iḥesben iman-iw d bu-tissas ulac acu ara yessagden ur skidibeɣ ara fell-ak feqɛeɣ mliḥ ḥulfaɣ i lemrar d terẓeg deg yimi-w qrib i rriɣ ayen yellan deg uɛebbuḍ-iw
umbaɛd mraw d semmus n yiseggasen deg twuri-agi n umsaltu urǧin walaɣ lḥaǧa i yessexlaɛen am wayen walant wallen-iw
acu-t ddɣel-agi i zedɣen ulawen-nsen akken ad kemmlen ɣef yimejraḥ s talɣa-agi  inselmen imezwura llan am wakken nessen uqbel mi ara d-snulfun ilugan n ṭṭrad deg tallit tamirant ttqadaren izerfan n yimeḥbas-nsen
d acu-t usaḍuf iɣef leḥḥun wigi  anagar imakaren war tiruggza i ineqqen imejraḥ seg yimsulta neɣ wiyaḍ akken ur sen-ttfiqin ara
maca wigi la aɣ-qqaren bɣan ad sbedden lxilafa tineslemt
d acu-tt lxilafa-agi ara ibedden ɣef tmenɣiwin 
furṣeɣ tallit-nni n tsusmi akken ad t-sseqsiɣ ɣef yisem n umeḥus yettujerḥen
maca ur iyi-d-yerri ara ikemmel kan deg wawal-is am wakken ur yesli ara i tuttra-inu
 deg tazwara newweḍ kan ɣer tqenṭert n  tsefsaft  nxemmem ad neḍfer wid i ten-yewwten
maca tisestanin d tsunḍiwin yemgaraden skerfent-aɣ
ruḥent-d kra n ṭumubilat tiberkanin ta deffir ta rekben-tent yifesyanin ttaken-d tisunḍiwin ta ur tesɛi assaɣ d tayeḍ
qerḥent-aɣ tmeẓẓuɣin-nneɣ seg ssuɣat d zzux-nsen mebla lmaɛna
myekcamen lumur tluɣ tegnit
mxalafent tmuɣliwin ɣef tezmert n ucengu d yiberdan i yuɣ deg trewla-ines
ula d yiwen ur aɣ-iccawer ara
ula d yiwen deg-sen ur d-yessuter rray-iw
usan-d s kra n tenfaliyin am   ad ten-nessuffeɣ seg yiɛebbaḍ n tyemmatin-nsen
ad ten-nessenger am tizit 
zmumgeɣ ciṭuḥ xemmemeɣ s usqecmeɛ  ur nessaweḍ ara ad nessenger ula tizit n tidet i d-yettemɣen ɣef yixxamen mi ara yeɣli yiḍ isufar yellan deg tmurt neɣ wid i d-yusan seg berra ur ssawḍen ara ad ten-kksen
uqbel mi ara nxemmem deg usenger n tizit yessefk fell-aneɣ ad nessizdeg idciren seg yiguduyen ad nekkes amalus yeččan imekwan ideg nettidir u nettrebbi tarwa-nneɣ
yenna-d yiwen n ufesyan bu-laɛsis akkenni ad as-tiniḍ d tameṭṭut s tadist   ẓriɣ tteffren deg yidciren iɣerfanen deg yitemma ifuḥen deg lfirmat yezzin i tudrin d temdinin
ad nqelleb ixujḍan n yiɣerdayen-agi yiwen yiwen
u ma terra-aɣ tmara ad d-nawi abilduzir akken ad ten-nhudd ɣef yiqerra-nsen
d inawen ilmawen ssebba-nsen d urfan
bɣan ad sengren imezdaɣ igellilen tezzmen-ten ɣef yibeddi-nsen ɣer tama n yineslemẓra imnafqen ayɣer ur ten-steqsan ara ɣef ssebba n yibeddi-agi ɣer yidis-nsen  amer slan ciṭuḥ kan i wayen suturen amer uɣen-asen awal tili ur nettaweḍ ara ɣer ṭṭrad-agi war udem
iserdasen n fransa yernu neẓra d acu-tt
fransa sin n yigiman n lɛesker akked lujistik n urakwal
aṭlanti yellan deffir-s ur tessaweḍ ara ad terkeḍ aɣref-agi yettwassnen s nnfaq yernu deg tallit-nni ur iɛedda ara tẓa n yimelyan n yimeɣban ur sɛin acemma ur ɣrin ara
ass-a ata yewweḍ ɣer kraḍet n tmerwin n yimelyan ma yeddukkel deg nnfaq-ines yessexdem yakk tazmert-ines ulac win i izemren ad t-yernu ɣas yekseb iserdasen n
hitler
inessef wass ur msefhamen ara ɣef wamek ad xedmen akken ad ten-ḍefren
yernu ikemmel-as ugeffur i yebdan tiyita
anda ffren yimzernanen-nni  acḥal deg-sen 
d iseqsiyen mebla tiririyin
adcir n  lebrarik  yezga-d deffir n umkan anda ndan tacerket-nsen
d tiwinas n yitemma i d-yezgan ɣef leryaf n wasif
yernu imezdaɣ n udcir-a bedden d yineslemẓra tuget n yimeɣnasen-nsen d wid iɛemren asqamu n tɣiwant kkan-d seg udcir-a
asmi d-yusa buḍyaf ṭṭfen amur ameqqran deg-sen rran-ten deg leḥbus n sseḥra
maca sserḥen-as ledwar-agi ineggura
yessusem kra n lweqt yeqqim yettxemmim
nniɣ 
wwḍen-aɣ kra n yisallen i d-yeqqaren wid iwumi sserḥen fsin am lmelḥ ur neẓri sani ruḥen
kecmen ɣer tigawt tuffirt anamek n waya ddan d trebbuyaɛ timselḥin
d tidet deg ledwar timezwura llan ttasen-d ɣur-neɣ akken ad zemlen ɣef yizmamen n tihawt sakin bdan ttbanen-d yinabayen wa deffir wa
nuzen irgazen-nneɣ ad nadin fell-asen deg yixxamen-nsen tiririyin i aɣ-d-ttakkent tlawin-nsen wezzilet  ulac-it
ma ḥetteten yirgazen-nneɣ ad aɣ-d-rrent s yiwet n tririt s talɣa n terdayt   iruḥ-n ɣur-wen ad yezmel ɣef uzmam n tihawt ur d-yuɣal ara 
neɣ  usan-d yirgazen-nwen deg yiḍ wwin-t
 nqelleb yakk ixxamen nuqem tisergal deg yiberdan nekcem s ixxamen deg yiḍ ulac acu nufa
ur nufi ara iqerra dɣa neččur leḥbus s wid i sen-yettilin ncuk deg-sen
am wid irewlen ass-a
swa swa 
tadyant teḍra deg tnezzayt yeshel fell-awen ad ten-tḍefrem wa ad ten-teṭṭfem
iserdasen tamsulta tamsetla tatersant-agi irkelli ur tenfiɛ i ucemma
ayen i d-teqqareḍ d tidet tatersant-agi ur tenfiɛ ara
tatersant taẓayant ur tettḥerrik ara alamma wwḍent agim n tsunḍiwin
 aɣerrabu ma ṭṭuqten deg-s rreyas ad yeɣreq kečč d lmir nekk d lmir anwa ara inehren iɣyal ihi 
d tagi d tilawt-nneɣ
uggten rreyas uggten ccifan ḥekkmen irkelli yal yiwen deg-sen yettak tisunḍiwin-ines deg taggara ulac win ara yembawlen
tasunḍa tneqq tayeḍ
lemɛawna n yiserdasen armi d tameddit i d-tewweḍ imir-n kan i yebda yekkat ugeffur
d tidet amḍan n yiserdasen meqqer
maca ma ten-tawliḍ amek i leḥḥun amek i ttaṭṭafen timekḥal gar yifassen-nsen ad ten-tɛeqleḍ seg wid yesɛeddayen lɛesker
d učči i ten-ttaken i yimrad n ṭṭrad am wakken i d-qqaren
d asfel i tegduda n lbaṭaṭa d yijiniralen n lbanan d lkiwi
uɣen amkan wa deffir wa s laɛqel kan ad as-tiniḍ d ifekrunen allen-nsen zgan ttmuqulent ɣer deffir ttganin kan aɣelluy n yiṭij ttraǧun kan tasunḍa n tuɣalin ɣer deffir ur cliɛen ara s unadi deg wannar yeččuren s umadaɣ i asen-yezzin
tekcem yiwet n terbaɛt seg temsetla ɣer udcir n yitemma tseqsin imdanen ma yella acu i walan
tiririt tban deg yixxamen-nsen i ten-tuɣ mi teḍra tedyant ulac acu walan
slan i tiyita n rrsas am nitni am wiyaḍ
ma d nekkni at-uxxam neqqim kan deg tnariyin-nneɣ nettgani
ṭṭfen yiserdasen tiqenṭert
sbedden tasergelt akken ad hewwjen wa ad luɛjen iɣermanen ur teɛni temsalt n umennuɣ-a
ula d nekk nniɣ-asen ad sbedden tasergelt deg yimi n tewwurt n temdint sɛeddayen yirgazen-inu lweqt-nsen deg usenqed deg tsendyaq n ṭṭumubilat akked deg lekwaɣeḍ n yinehharen ɣas akken neẓra ulac lfayda deg wayen nxeddem
nessekter seg tsergalin deg yiberdan urkiden akken ad nessebgen i medden tazmert-nneɣ
neqqim kan nettrǧu deg tsunḍiwin ara aɣ-d-yasen seg
susmeɣ yiwet n tasint
seqsaɣ  usawen tikkelt d aẓḍam tikkelt niḍen d tuɣalin ɣer deffir ɛla ḥsab liḥala-nsen tikkelt nnecraḥen tikkelt ɣuccen
mmel-iyi-d isem n umeḥbus yettwajerḥen
ah tesmektaḍ-iyi d amejjay yurda s usemres n uɣray deg ssbiṭar-ines i d-yeglan s tmettant
d yiwet n tmeṭṭut i skecmen yimawlan-is ɣer ssbiṭar mi ugin ad ḥebsen yidammen-is seg tazzla temmut kra n sswayeɛ umbaɛd
faqen yimejjayen iwayen i as-yeḍran seɣlin-as tadist bessif dɣa xebbren tamsulta
tessaweḍ-aɣ tsestant ɣer ssbiṭar n umajjay s tewriqt n yisufar i nufa ɣer teqcict-nni
skecmen-t lḥebs seg laɛḍil ad t-carɛen
nufa ameɣbun-nni yettuḍegger daxel n umadaɣ semmuset n tmerwin n lmitrat ɣef tqenṭert
deg tazwara nɣil yemmut
maca yiwen seg yisexsayen yenna-aɣ-d ul-is mazal yekkat
yettwawet s tersast deg yidmaren wwin-t srid ɣer ssbiṭar akken ad t-dawin
deg tidmi-k ayɣer i t-ufan yebɛed ɣef tkamyunt 
aṭas n turdiwin yellan ahat yettwajreḥ deg uẓḍam bɣan yirebraben ad t-awin yid-sen mi sen-yeɣli deg ubrid ɣilen yemmut dɣa ǧǧan-t din
ur cukkeɣ ara ad yili uẓḍam mebla ma ttwajerḥen yimeḥbas
turda tis snat irebraben bɣan ad t-awin yid-sen s yiɣil mi yugi wwten-t s rrsas akken ur yettili ara d inigi
ilaq ad teḥsuḍ mačči yakk irebraben i ulin ɣer udrar
kra deg-sen sɛeddayen ussan-nsen deg temdint leḥḥun deg leswaq mi ara d-ṭṭrad n yeɣli yiḍ tteffɣen akked yirebraben
d yiremmuɛen ulac tin i iwaɛren neɣ yumsen am ṭṭrad-agi
ɣef waya ur ttaǧǧan ara inigan deffir-nsen
anamek n waya tudert n umejjay-a teṭṭef ɣef yiwen n unẓaḍ
atan imir-a seddaw n lɛessa ad t-nerr ɣer lḥebs mi ara d-yerfed ciṭuḥ iman-is
ayɣer deg lḥebs ulac acu ara t-yaɣen  lḥebs yeččur s yirebraben zemren ad t-nɣen s sshala
d tidet maca d tagi d tilawt ur nesɛi ara abdil i waya
sani i iruḥ yusef ɛeyyaci  seqsaɣ iman-iw ɣef tsebbiwin i t-yerran ad yeddu d yirebraben  amek ad yidir umbaɛd  ad yuɣal d arebrab ṭṭafaren-t deg yidurar  ur t-ssineɣ ara mliḥ maca ttwaliɣ-t d amraḍi yettnaɣ mgal takriḍt seg wansi i d-tusa
nɛeṭṭel deg umeslay nekk d si aḥmed newwi-d isental niḍen maca ur neffiɣ ara ɣef usentel agejdan n umennuɣ i yessazzlen aṭas n yidammen
amennuɣ ugin imasayen n tmurt ad as-semmin ṭṭrad acku ṭṭrad yettili d ucengu aberrani mgal tmurt niḍen d ugdud niḍen
maca ṭṭrad i yettilin gar tarwa n yiwen n ugdud iɣef necna ɣef llsal iseḥḥan n tdukli-ines i t-ijemɛen nettak-as yakk ismawen anagar isem-is aḥeqqani
ad naf amedya ɣef waya deg ṭṭrad n tmunent i tugi fransa tunsibt ad as-tsemmi ṭṭrad n lezzayer armi ɛeddan semmuset n tmerwin n yiseggasen ɣef tnekra-ines acku tella tettwali tamurt-a d ugdud-is d amur ulac win i izemren ad t-yebḍu ɣef fransa
tsemma-as tidyanin n lezzayer am nettat am tmesbaniyin neɣ d imerẓiyen gar yiɣarimen iɣuccen d yiɣallen n laman
ayen yaɛnan tanfalit  ṭṭrad aɣarim  awal-agi kerhen ad as-slen yessagad mačči d kra yettwagdel deg umeslay acku astaɛref s waya igellu-d s uhuddu swayes nnumen yakan anamek n waya tidet iɣef tebna yal tmetti d yal anagraw n leḥkem
ma yekker ṭṭrad gar tarwa n yiwet n twacult d baba-tsen ara ibubben tamasit
ma neqbel s usemmi-agi lmaɛna-s d astaɛref s ubrir ameqqran deg usefrek n lumur n udabdu seg tmunnent
ssneɣ si aḥmed seg wasmi i d-yusa ɣer temdint-a semmus n yiseggasen aya
ula d netta yeɣra deg ugezdu n tmussniwin tizerfanin yernu iḥemmel tugrint d yisuḍaf
yezga yettɛawad i tinawt n
 taɣdemt war tazmert d tuḍɛift tazmert war taɣdemt d tamesbaṭlit 
d amenzay ibedd uxeddim-ines
iḥemmel ugar lkulunil hewwari bumedyen i kerheɣ am qeḍran acku ɣef ssebba-s i yemmut gma milud
maca si
aḥmed xelḍent-as yimmektan
anda-tent tilisa n teɣdemt  anda-tent tilisa n tezmert  anda yella umgired gar tazmert s wudem yelhan d tekriḍt s wudem n dir-i 
nezmer ad neḥseb nnfaq ɣef lbaṭel d taɣdemt  nezmer ad nessemres tazmert neɣ takriḍt akken ad d-nawi isallen ara aɣ-yalen akken ad neṭṭef aneḍlib  d ugur i yettmagar yal ass akked yimakaren d yineḍliben uqbel irebraben d wid i ten-yettɛawanen i tetteṭṭef temsulta i tesqqiri deg yixerdusen-ines iɣef temmeɣ nnwa
acḥal d abrid i nefka iseqsiyen-agi nkeccem deg yiwen n uskasi mebla lqaɛ akken ad naf ahat tiririyin ara aɣ-yesqenɛen
ɣef waya tejmeɛ-iyi yid-s yiwet n tdukkli d yiwet n teflest tejhed mačči d kra terra-iyi ur ttsetḥiɣ ara ad as-sbeggneɣ adduden-inu d wayen i yi-yerḥan mebla akukru am wakken ixeddem ula d netta yid-i
yettas-d ɣur-i s axxam deg yiḍ akken ad nsew kra n teqbucin n lbira wa ad nemmeslay ɣef wuguren d lehmum n tmurt-a ur neffiɣ ara seg yiwen n ṭṭrad i yeṭṭfen ugar n uwines armi tekcem deg wayeḍ yeɣleb-it deg terẓeg d lejruḥ
timḍelt n nabil tewɛer-aɣ mliḥ ɣef demma n ugeffur i yewten mebla cceḥḥa
akal yebzeg irkelli yuɣal yettenṭad d yigelzimen d lbalat d ayen i ten-yerran waɛrit i usexdem
maca nnmara n wat-iččumar yessewhem-iyi mliḥ
iḍarren-nsen ẓẓan deg waluḍ armi d tigecrar kra deg-sen tuɣ-iten ḥafi ttḍeggiren akal daxel n uxjiḍ mebla ma yuli-asen ula yiwen n wawal
ulac win ara iserrḥen i ufus n ugelzim seg yiḍuḍan-is armi s bessif
senndeɣ ɣef yiwet n txerrubt kemmleɣ amuqel deg-sen wehmeɣ
sugneɣ iman-iw deg tlemmast n waluḍ-nni s uselsu d ussebbaḍ-inu i yumsen irkelli
ur yi-yaɛǧib ara maḍi ayen sugneɣ dɣa sefḍeɣ-t seg wallaɣ-iw am wakken lliɣ xeddmeɣ asmi i yi-tuɣ d aselmad
deg taggara mi sersen ccahed ɣef uẓekka zzin-as ɣran taldayt neɣ lfatiḥa ɣef terwiḥt-is sakin uɣalen am wakken i d-usan s tuffra
ur ruḥen ara ad walin baba-s n umerḥum am wakken xedmen tuget seg wid i d-yusan ad wajhen zzin-as-d ɣas akken yekkat ugeffur
mɛanaqen s temɣawla mbaddalen kra n tenfaliyin i susruyen s laɛqel yal yiwen seg yirgazen yuɣal seg wansi
imuqel-iyi-d ihuzz aqerruy-is iban ɛerqent-as ciṭuḥ d-yusa iqerra-nsen kecmen deg tuyat-nsen akken ad ten-smenɛen seg ugeffur
walaɣ akumisar deg tenṭelt ileḥḥu kan s laɛqel deg tlemmast n ubrid yessan s wakal
yewwet wul-iw
iruḥ-d ad iwajeh neɣ tella ssebba niḍen i t-id-yewwin 
ccil n wayen yeḍran iḍelli ur ttuɣ ara amek i nɣan nabil
tafekka ur aɣ-tettunefk ara armi tɛedda ɣef tesleḍt n yimejjayen d tira n uneqqis i temsulta
iqerreb-d
si aḥmed ɣer racid isellem fell-as am wakken xedmen imɛezziyen irkelli yejbed iman-is yeqqim yettraǧu
iban yebɣa ad as-yini kra i netta kan
yella umaynut deg tedyant n umerḥum  sakin yerra-yi-d 
si ɛebdelqader 
bɣiɣ ad meslayeɣ akked si racid
ẓriɣ mačči d lawan maca ayen yellan d amaynut deg tsestant tḥettem fell-i ad as-hedreɣ
iban d tamsalt ur nezmir tagganit maca racid atan deg yir liḥala tewɛer mliḥ
ur yenṭiq s yiwen n wawal seg tnezzayt
ẓriɣ  ẓriɣ ɣef waya ttekleɣ fell-ak ad t-id-tawiḍ yid-k ɣer tnarit-inu deg wussan-a mebla ma terra-aɣ tmara ad nessemres allalen-nneɣ
ur yerǧi ara tiririt
yezzi-iyi-d s uɛrur-is s temɣawla sakin yerkeb ṭumubil i t-yettraǧun ɣer yimi n tewwurt n ubrid-nni yessan s wakal
deg yiseggasen-agi ineggura ladɣa seg wasmi yewwi
racid benɣusa taɣtast-ines texser ṭṭbiɛa-s yuɣal ireffu ɣef wulac
yernu tidet kan ddunit ur ḥninet ara yid-s
ɣlin-d fell-as wuguren d imeqqranen am tbuciḍant n yijdi
ad as-tiniḍ tiwuɣa n ddunit irkelli rǧant ad yawi taɣtast akken ad dduklent mgal-is wa ad sberkent ddunit-is
cfiɣ mliḥ ɣef taggara n uzal-nni aḥmayan
aggur n wunbir qrib ad yekfu ula yiwet n tiqit n ugeffur ur d-teɣli ara
azɣal aqesḥan n unebdu i yesfiliten s ḍerru n kra n twuɣa yessaggaden
ḥebseɣ ṭumubil-inu sdat n tewwurt n umraḥ n uɣerbaz alemmas kraḍet n tyitwin ɣef tẓemmart am lɛada qqimeɣ ttganiɣ melmi ad yeffeɣ
yiwet n ddqiqa snat semmuset ur d-iban ara
yettu ttiɛad-nneɣ  maca yesnum-iyi ma yefka-iyi-d awal yezga yettas-d deg lawan
ulseɣ tiyita ɣef tẓemmart n ṭumubil ssuffɣeɣ ciṭuḥ aqerruy-iw akken ad waliɣ axxam-ines i d-yezgan deg wannag wis sin ideg yuɣ tannumi yettḍili-d ɣur-i wa ad yessuter deg-i ad t-rǧuɣ ciṭuḥ ma yettwaṭṭef s kra n lecɣal
ass-nni teɣli-d fell-aneɣ yiwet n tsusmi d taẓayant
nniɣ-as ahat yeffeɣ ad yaɣ kra n tɣawsiwin wa ad d-yuɣal
senseɣ amseddu ssiɣeɣ yiwen n ugarru tamuɣli-inu tettneggiz seg tawwurt tameẓyant n wuzzal ileḥḥu s ɣer uṭrutwar i tt-iqublen gar-asen yella yiwen n ubrid i yettawin ɣer yiwen n udcir yeččuren s tḥuna
ɣer taggara yeffeɣ-d umeddakkel-iw laɛqel kan yeldi tawwurt iḍegger iman-is ɣef ukersi mebla ma yenṭeq s yiwen n wawal
nniɣ 
ini-d meqqar ssalam  tebda  timɛellemt  tḥekkem deg-k wa ad ak-d-temmal d acu i ilaq ad txedmeḍ 
imuqel-iyi-d s wallen ɛyant mliḥ imir-n kan faqeɣ yella acu yuɣen ameddakkel-iw ad ssusmeɣ axir
iwehha-iyi-d s ufus-is akken ad bduɣ tikli uqbel ad yinig wallaɣ-is anda niḍen
neffeɣ seg temdint neṭṭef abrid n yillel i nettwali ddaw-nneɣ racid yeɣleq ɣef yiman-is yugi ad iyi-yini acu t-yuɣen
grarben yiseqsiyen ɣef yiles-iw maca ṭṭfeɣ-ten kra n lweqt uqbel ad ten-ddzeɣ gar tuɣmas-iw
iban d amennuɣ i yennuɣ d tmeṭṭut-is ur yebɣi ara ad yekcef ɣef wuffiren n umennuɣ-nsen
tuget n yirgazen ɣuccen ɣef tlawin-nsen
tezga tewtemt i ikemnen deg uxxam d acetki ur teẓri ara amek leḥḥun lumur amek ttemcubakkent temsal
mi ara tesɛu aqcic wis kraḍ neɣ wis ukkuẓ ad tekkes asɣum n yikerri amḍuɛ ad tessuffeɣ accaren-is i temsed aṭas-aya s tuffra wa ad tessemɣi acciwen s warraw-is asergel-nni ara tt-iḥuden seg lbaṭel n urgaz d usḥillef-ines s berru
ɣas akken ad ikemmel urgaz deg usḥillef-ines maca urǧin ad as-yebru yettaf-d dima ifukal am tuggdi ɣef dderya-ines
mi ara iyi-awḍen imeṭṭawen-agi ttaraɣ nnehta ferrḥeɣ mačči d kra acku menɛeɣ seg twuɣa-a
tikwal tudert d awḥid tif tudert d yiwen ara k-yesqelqen
ɣef waya ad ten-tafeḍ uḍnen irkelli wa s waṭṭan n ssukker wa s walluy n tussda n yidammen wayeḍ s waṭṭan n lmaɛidda yernu urɛad wwḍen seddiset n tmerwin n yiseggasen
uguren ma ṭṭuqten ttuɣalen d annar ideg ttefruruxen ifirusen ara ihudden tafekka n umdan
tafekka-inu tuɣal am udrar i ifessin ddaw-as yakk ifirusen n ddunit
ɛeddaɣ ciṭuḥ seddiset n tmerwin tafekka-inu urǧin i tt-iqelleb umejjay ur ssineɣ ara anezgum s lfeḍl n temdekkelt-iw taɛzizt ur nessin leḥzen tin i ttafeɣ lebda tama-w ma ḥwaǧeɣ-tt
s lfeḍl-is mazal-iyi jehdeɣ ulac acu yuɣen tazmert-iw  d nettat i yessekcamen anecraḥ ɣer wul-iw
tasebḥit-agi wwiɣ tameṭṭut-iw ɣer umejjay
yesduqes-yi-d umeddakkel-iw uɣaleɣ ɣer tilawt muqleɣ ɣur-s ttraǧuɣ ad ikemmel awal-is
ata yefsi takerrist i yiles-is maca ur ikemmel ara awal-is
yessusem i tikkelt niḍen ikemmel amuqel ɣer yigli azegzaw i ɣ-iqublen
iban d tawaɣit i yuɣen tameṭṭut-is yewɛer-as umeslay fell-as
qudreɣ tasusmi-ines kemmleɣ tanhert ttraǧuɣ kan ad ikemmel imeslayen-is
teẓriḍ d acu i yufa umejjay 
d lxir ncallah
anda yella lxir-agi ay argaz 
ur ttqelliq ara iman-ik ulac aṭṭan ur yurǧi usafar-is 
ulac asafar i waṭṭan am ukunsir
akunsir 
ih akunsir akunsir n yidmaren aṭṭan ur nreḥḥem ara
ahat yeɣleḍ umejjay deg umnined-ines  
teẓriḍ axir-iw aswir n yimejjayen n wass-a asileɣ ulac axeddim ad d-yawi rebbi
ala aṭṭan iban-d mliḥ
tesɛiḍ tura ddurt mi tt-wwiɣ ɣer yiwen n umejjay amazzag seg wid yeɣran deg d yiwen seg tsuta-nneɣ seg wid yerẓan iqerra-nsen akken ad awin anefḍis n umejjay mačči am  lmuhim  yetḥeqqeq mliḥ aṭṭan yudef-itt maca ɣas akken yessuter deg-i ad rnuɣ ad as-xedmeɣ rradyuyat
tasebḥit mi iwala rradyuyat yefka-yi-d yiwet n tebrat yenna-yi-d   ur ttraǧu ara awi-tt mebla laɛḍil ɣer ssbiṭar 
maca tameṭṭut-iw yeffeɣ-itt laɛqel ur teḥbis ara imeṭṭawen ugar n waya ccil n uḥellel-inu tugi ad truḥ yid-i ɣer ssbiṭar
ǧǧiɣ-tt teẓẓel ɣef umeṭreḥ tettru ɣef lbext-is
ayen i yi-yeswehmen deg waya tettwali deg waṭṭan-a d tarrut sɣur yakuc
d acu-ten ddnub-agi i texdem tmeɣbunt akken ad yelthu mass n yigenwan d wakal s tarrut-ines 
yessusem yemmekta-d kra i yesfeḍ wakud aṭas-aya seg wallaɣ-is
d taḥkayt taqdimt seg wasmi nemyussan
d acu i texdem nasira tamḍuɛt akken ad tḥulfu s nndama wa ad twali aṭṭan-ines d tarrut sɣur yakuc 
qqimeɣ ttalaseɣ i useqsi-agi deg wul-iw wehmeɣ rǧiɣ melmi ad ikemmel asegzi-ines
teẓriḍ belli tameṭṭut-iw tebda taẓallit
tettẓalla  ur i yi-d-tenniḍ ara d taneɣrimt i tella tumen s tikta tinesfarayin am keččini  ciṭuḥ yeqmec allen-is am wakken
ih akka i tella neɣ akka i tt-ttwaliɣ zik
maca tbeddel s  n tfesniwin
yernu ẓriɣ anta i tt-ibeddlen ulac tayeḍ anagar tameddakkelt-nni yettlusun ajelbab i tt-yettẓurun dima
d taselmadt txeddem yid-s deg tesnawit
tenna-yi-d tettemsefham yid-s u ttemyudlunt
ur ttɛassaɣ tameṭṭut-iw ur sekcameɣ iman-iw deg wassaɣen-is d temddukkal-ines
maca iban ɣelṭeɣ ǧǧiɣ azrem areqman ad yessames tezdeg n wul-is
tameṭṭut s umata d tuḍɛift zemren ad as-ččen allaɣ-is s sshala yernu ur tettaf ara iman-is alamma tekcem daxel n terbaɛt
sakin lqella n tmussni n tmeṭṭut tettara-tt tettamen s ssḥur d lkaramat n lawliya
asmi meẓẓeyeɣ deg taddart-nneɣ tella yemma tessuter deg-i ad dduɣ yid-s ɣer lemqam n sidi lmexfi
din nettaf tilawin zzint-as i uẓekka deɛɛunt seg wul   sidi dawi mmi 
sidi zzwej-as i yelli 
sidi err-iyi-d argaz-iw u err-d ttar seg tnuḍt-iw tamcumt 
sidi ssuffeɣ-iyi seg twaɣit-a
sliɣ i laɛǧeb
deg uxxam ttaɛraḍeɣ ad as-kkseɣ seg wallaɣ-is tikti-nni i iressan belli lwali-agi yezmer ad yerr ɣef usuter-ines ladɣa ḥellu n baba d uletma
 ccayeb  yella yeṭṭef tasga yenɣa-t lberd ma d uletma tella tettaṭṭef-itt legrina
yemma treffu nezzeh tettameṛ-iyi ad ṭṭfeɣ imi-w dɣa ad tessuter deg sidi lmexfi ad i yi-yessuref acku mazal-iyi d ameẓyan ulac acu i ssneɣ
akka i gant tlawin
tilawin ur neɣri ara ur nessin ara  kečč tettmeslayeḍ ɣef tallit n temharsa
tameṭṭut d tameṭṭut ur tettbeddil ara
ulac amgired gar tin yeɣran d tin urǧin neɣri amen-iyi
ayen i ttwaliɣ deg imeẓyanen
d acu uxxam n teɣdemt yessebgan-iyi-d belli nekkni d agdud yumnen s ssḥur d iḥeckulen armi d iɣes
tameṭṭut kter n urgaz
maca tameṭṭut-iw ur telli ara am tlawin niḍen
nettat 
yessusem racid ɛla ɣila am wakken ur yumin ara s wayen yeqqar ɣef tmeṭṭut-is
nniɣ 
ur ttqelliq ara iman-ik ɣef tẓallit n tmeṭṭut-ik
medden yakk ttẓallan ttẓummun
cfiɣ deg taddart-nneɣ ulac win ur nettẓalla ara neɣ ur nettuẓum ara irgazen d tlawin d umur ameqqran n warrac i yessewhamen deg waya 
wigi d imesnasen imasɣanen ssneɣ-ten ula d nekk yernu serwan-iyi lmerta
baba akken ad nẓal yella yesddukkul-aɣ deffir-s deg sin n lesfuf wiyen i warrac wayeḍ i tullas
yuɣ tannumi yessakay-aɣ-d deg tafrara s taɣect-ines tazurant d uɛeggeḍ-ines yettaččaren amkan akken ad nẓal taẓallit n lefjer d tin n ssbeḥ
terwi ɣef win ur nettaweḍ ara deg lawan
lliɣ d ameqqran deg watmaten-iw yessefk fell-i ad zwireɣ akken ad iyi-ḍefren wiyaḍ
mačči d tanekra zik i yi-sqelqen d tiɣin n luḍu deg tnezzayin n tegrest aman d agris yernu ilaq ad neffeɣ ɣer umraḥ seg lḥamu n tduli ɣer tasmuḍi n berra sakin ɣer ubduz ibeɛden i d-yezgan deg yiwet n teɣmert yettulsen nettnaɣ anwa deg-neɣ ara ikecmen d amezwaru nettneggiz am yigḍaḍ imecṭaḥ mebla afriwen nennekmac ɣef yiman-nneɣ akken ur ɣ-ineqq ara usemmiḍ d ugeffur
deg wuḍan n unebdu nettɣimi nuki akken ad nerǧu lawan n tẓallit n lɛica
nella nesɛedday ass s lekmal-is deg yigran d tebḥirin nettuɣal nemmut seg ɛeggu nessaram kan ad neẓẓel ɣef wusu akken ad neṭṭes maca baba yezga ɣef yiqerra-nneɣ d aɛessas am win n leḥbus itezzi ɣef yiqerra-nneɣ yettɛeggiḍ yettsuɣu
tikkwal nettkellix-as ur nettaɣ ara luḍu ladɣa gar lmeɣreb d lɛica
mi ara yekker ad nbedd deffir-s d imḍuɛen nessader i yiqerra-nneɣ ma yeseqsa-aɣ ɣef luḍu yernu dayen i ixeddem dima nesrugmut kra n wawalen deg wulawen terkeb-aɣ tuggdi nugga-d ad aɣ-ifiq
maca amek ad iẓer ma yerwel-aɣ yiwen n wuriḍ neɣ sin seg yiqerqyar-nneɣ  d amennuɣ i iḍerrun yal ass deg tsusmi  netta s tezmert-is d usḥillef-ines nekkni s tḥerci d wurfan-nneɣ mebla ma yezmer walbaɛḍ ad ibedd deg wudem-is ad as-yeffeɣ abrid neɣ ad yemmeslay yid-s
atmaten-iw deg semmus yid-sen xeddmen ayen xedmeɣ ulac win ara yi-izwiren ma ur zwareɣ ara nekkini s timmad-iw nemsefham mliḥ
tullas msakit ttaɣent awal n ubabat am tqeddacin
mi ara yesneḥneḥ kan yessuffeɣ-d ssaɛa-ines seg lǧib ad kkrent ad qellbent ɣef yijelbaben d lximarat-nsent ad beddent iqerra-nsent deg lqaɛa deffir-neɣ
deg wuḍan n remḍan yezzuɣur-aɣ am wulli ɣer lǧameɛ akken ad neẓẓal taẓallit n tarawiḥ
d baba i yi-yeskerhen asɣan
tuɣal-iyi tẓallit am ukurfi i ilaq ad xedmeɣ yal ass ttraǧuɣ-tt am tarrut taseṭṭaft
d leqraya i yi-yesmenɛen
yefreḥ yis-i baba asmi d-wwiɣ aselkin n ulmud alemmas
cwi kan taddart-nneɣ ur tesɛi ara tasnawit dɣa yessekles-iyi deg ddaxiliya deg temdint n blida
ɣas asaḍuf agensay iẓeyyer maca umreɣ mliḥ acku thennaɣ seg tẓallit semmus n yiberdan deg wass i iḥettem fell-i baba deg uxxam-nneɣ
deg ddaxiliya i ssneɣ d acu iwumi ssawalen lbenna n tɣuri
ur lliɣ ara seg wid iḥemmlen uraren n lkarṭa ɣas ma yella tuget n yinelmaden n tesnawit sɛeddayen acḥal n sswayeɛ deg wurar s uɛeggeḍ ama daxel n yisganen neɣ deg lawan n usgunfu deg tɣemmar n umraḥ neɣ daxel n tneɣriyin tilmawin
ttkeyyifen ttnaɣen ttawin-d awal ɣef wayen n dir-i tikkwal ttuɣalen ɣer yifassen d rrkel akken ad frun lxilaf d lemgarda yellan gar-asen
griɣ tamkerḍit d ugerruj ur nfennu i teffer
ɣliɣ s ugacur ɣef kra n yidlisen n yenna-d deg-sen d akken aflusuf almani ur yenɣi ara yakuc acku aneggaru-a aṭas aya segmi yemmut
tafyirt-a teɣli-d fell-i am tirmegt neɣ rrɛud
d acu-ten yimeslayen-agi  amek ad yemmet win yellan d ameɣlal  d tafyirt-agi i yi-yewwin ɣer teflusuft n  sakin ɣer akked
ɣliɣ imir-n ɣef yidlisen n teflusuft bdiɣ ttxemmimeɣ ɣef tikti-a n tmettant n yakuc d wamek i yexdem umdan akken ad yaɣ amkan-is deg lqaɛa
yakuc swayes numen d tmeɣlelt-ines win i nettaggad tarrut d unazir-ines yuɣal d tikti i yesnulfa umdan yettidiren deg tallit taqburt akken ad yessegzi tuggdi-ines seg tumanin tigamanin
tressa tekti deg wallaɣ-iw thucc tigensas-inu timezwura
lliɣ ḥemmleɣ mliḥ idlisen n teflusuft ɣef waya ɣriɣ iqdimen d idlisen n yimussnawen-ines yimaynuten seg aflaṭun armi d mebla ma ttuɣ
yezzi-d fell-i uqusis ur zemireɣ ad ffɣeɣ seg-s
yernu ur cukkeɣ ara ad d-yas wass ad as-ffɣeɣ
umbaɛd n taggazt n uselmed i teẓriḍ d lbakalurya i d-wwiɣ deg tegnatin tidinkuciṭin skelseɣ iman-iw deg tneɣrit n teflusuft maca tasertit tamcumt teskerker-iyi nekk mazal-iyi d ameẓyan deg yiwet n tallit ḥesbeɣ iman-iw d
lmehdi i tettraǧu talsa win ara ibeddlen amaḍal s usunded neɣ tamesbanit n yinelmaden
d taḥkayt taɣezzfant ahat ad d-yas wass ad k-tt-id-alseɣ s telqi
yessusem umeddakkel-iw yeɣreq deg yiwet n tsusmi ad as-tiniḍ deg tenṭelt i yella
qudreɣ leḥzen-ines ur t-hewwjeɣ ara s yiseqsiyen-inu
deg uzal-nni nruḥ ad nmerreḥ deg tmersit
sḥebseɣ ṭumubil sdat n ugenna n yiɣerruba n useggeḍ anda llan kraḍ neɣ ukkuẓ n yilmeẓyen ttɛummun s zzux d uɛeggeḍ deg waman yumsen sekkren ahruḥu
nniɣ-as i racid ad nsew taqbuct n lbira neɣ snat ɣer umeddakkel-nneɣ lǧilali maca ihuzz aqerruy-is akken ad iyi-yini ala
akka i yettwaxdem
racid iɣelleq ɣef yiman-is ma yeqber wul-is yettsusum
maca ẓriɣ irekkem daxel-is acku walaɣ ifassen-is amek i ttergigin mi ara yebdu ameslay ddaw n tuɣmest
mi d-nuɣal aṭas i mmeslayeɣ nniɣ-as akk ayen sɛiɣ d nnhayat limmer ad ssifsusent fell-as taẓayt n twaɣit i yeɣlin fell-as
sakin mebla ma xemmemeɣ bdiɣ ameslay i tikkelt tamezwarut ɣef lḥif n ledwar tineggura n baba
yal tikkelt mi ara d-mmektiɣ tadyant-agi yettneqbaḍ wul-iw kerrheɣ tudert-iw
atemmu-nni yettulsen ideg yeṭṭef baba tasga
yiwet n tsusmi yessaggaden yemmɣen ɣef wadeg-nni ḥala tusut taqesḥant n baba i tt-igezzmen
asemmiḍ yesergagay lemfasel ccil n lkanun i ireqqen deg-s tirgin ibezgen nessefqad-itent nekk d gma s nnuba ad tent-nsuḍ iwakken ur xessint ara
nesseqrab lkanun-nni ɣer wusu n baba maca abbu-nni i itteffɣen seg-s irennu deg tusut-ines dɣa ad t-nessebɛed fell-as s lxuf
yemma i iɣuccen tettneggiz seg tama ɣer tayeḍ am uzɣuɣ tettawi tettarra deg ufus-is tiqraɛtin ččurent s waṭas n yimemdas tettak-iten i baba akken ad ten-yeskef nettat ur tḥebbes ara ameslay ɣef lfayda-nsen tsellek flan d flan seg lmut baba ur iḥebbes ara acetki  turin-inu rekkment reqqent qerḥent-iyi tagerjumt-iw tergel ferrej ya rebbi dawi neɣ awi
nekk d gma neqqim kan nettmuqul deg ssikis-ines d laɛtab-is mebla ma nessaweḍ ad nexdem kra nreffed kan allen-nneɣ ɣer yigenni nettales  amin a mass n sin n yimaḍalen
ula d nekkni nella nessaram ad iferrej rebbi maca s ḥellu mačči s tmettant
yemma tettru s tsusmi tezzuɣur-iyi deffir-s akken ad nẓur lewliya d sellaḥ d yiderwicen tessutur deg-sen lkaramat tettraǧu kan melmi ad teḍru tamkarra
maca tamkarra n ḥellu ur d-teḍri ara
yusa-d lferj s tmettant i yessekcmen axxam-nneɣ deg leḥzen d lḥif ur ẓriɣ ara amek i sen-nerwel
yeǧǧa-aɣ am yifrax i itezzin ɣef tyemmat i ilan yiwet n tezmert annect ilat maca ur tesɛi ara leslaḥ iwulmen akken ad tqabel lḥif aberkan i ɣ-yeččan
deg tazwara wwḍent-aɣ kra n lemɛawnat d ssadaqat sɣur lǧiran d twacult-nneɣ maca ḥebsent umbaɛd
taddart-nneɣ tettwaɛzel deg tlemmast n udrar akal-is ur yelhi ara i tfellaḥt am wakken ur tesɛi ara aṭas n tliwa
anwa ara yalen wayeḍ  nekk d gma nella nleḥḥu aṭas n yikilumitren ɣef uḍar akken ad naweḍ ɣer telmat ideg llant lfirmat n ukulun iwakken ad nelqeḍ ayen ssagren deffir-nsen seg lxeḍra d lfakya am lbaṭaṭa ṭumaṭic aẓalim d yibawen
deg tallit n tmegra nesɛedday ussan-nneɣ d tikli deffir n tmacinin n tmegra akken ad nejmeɛ tiyedrin i ḍeggrent
amyezwer gar-aneɣ yejhed mliḥ ddaw n yiṭij aqesḥan n unebdu d timerwin n warrac d tlawin ula d irgazen ẓeddmen ɣef yiger mi ara teffeɣ tmacint n tmegra d uɛessas i yeṭṭfen deg ufus-is aɛekkaz sekcamen ifassen-nsen deg tlemmast n tuga yeččuren d isennanen akken ad qellben ɣef tyedret i tezgel tmacint
nella njemmeɛ tiyedrin nettara-tent daxel n tcekkart s lferḥ ameqqran nessugun aɣrum aḥmayen ara teg yemma-tneɣ wa ara t-tessew ɣef uskir neɣ daxel n lkuca
ah ɣef wussan-nni iwaɛren
deg uzal-nni uɣaleɣ ɣer uxxam rẓeɣ ulac acu d-yegran deg-i
bɣiɣ ad sneɣseɣ cedda d ssikis ɣef umeddakkel-iw ufiɣ iman-iw ttalseɣ i ccfawat-nni i yi-iqerḥen yernu yal mi ara tent-id-mmektiɣ sɛeddayeɣ ayen i yi-d-yegran seg wass-nni deg leḥzen acku smektayent-iyi-d s twaɣit niḍen
tawaɣit n uletma i yessaɛya waṭṭan n legrina i tt-yeččan seg daxel uqbel ad taɛyu tfekka-ines tuḍɛift wa ad tessuffeɣ tarwiḥt ɣef wusu anda yemmut baba
temmut nettat mazal-it d tajeǧǧigt urɛad tefsi
deg useggas n tmunent gma yella ixeddem deg lfirma qrib yal ass yettaɣ tajernaḍt ugar n waya yettawi-aɣ-d yal tameddit aḍellaɛ yeččur s lxeḍra d lfakya
ečč ay igellil seg lɣella n tmunent
maca uletma fatiḥa ulac acu testenfeɛ seg tmunent izad fell-as waṭṭan tebda tettusu am baba yemma tettazzal seg lemqam ɣer wayeḍ seg ṭṭaleb ɣer wayeḍ seg uderwic ɣer gma-s ula d yiwen seg yisufar-nsen ur yessexfef seg laɛtab-is
ah ya rebbi ɣef tsebḥit-nni tamelɛunt neǧǧa-tt nekk d yemma weḥd-s ɣas akken teqqim tettḥellil deg-neɣ ad neqqim yid-s
nruḥ ɣer yiwen seg wid iḥefḍen leqran akken ad as-yaru taḥerzet qqaren-d afus-is d tira-ines sɛan lbaraka gellun dima s ḥellu
yezdeɣ deg yiwet n taddart laqent-as snat n tsaɛtin n tikli s temɣawla gar yinijel d umadaɣ
ulac zzher ass-nni ur t-nufi ara neqqim din nettraǧu deg-s akked yimẓuren niḍen
nnan-aɣ-d iruḥ ad yeḥḍer tanṭelt n yiwen n umerḥum wa ad iɣer leqran ɣef rruḥ-is
iɛeṭṭel nekkni daɣen nɛeṭṭel
yemma telha deg umeslay d tlawin niḍen ttemyeḥkunt timucuha d ccfawat tiqerḥanin ttawint-d awal ɣef lewliya ssalḥin d yisufar n yimɣan i teɛreḍ yal yiwet deg-sent
qqimeɣ deg ṭṭerf ṭṭafareɣ lehdur-nsent allen-iw zgant ɣef uzniq ahat ad waliɣ aqendur n ccix akken ad ɣ-ihenni seg tganit-a
allaɣ-iw iruḥ ɣer uletma d ssuɣat-ines yettzenzunen deg yimeẓẓuɣen-iw
ur ẓriɣ ara ayɣer i yuggadeɣ mliḥ ass-nni
ruḥeɣ ɣer yemma snat n tikkal akken ad as-iniɣ ilaq ad nekker ad nruḥ
wwiɣ-as-d ifakul belli ccix ur d-yettuɣal ara uqbel n uɣelluy n yiṭij
deg tikkelt tis snat tɛeggeḍ-d fell-i tenna  qqim deg umkan-ik tessusmeḍ ma ulac
lḥiɣ ciṭuḥ deg tkessart-nni i d-yettawin armi d abrid ameqqran ẓẓleɣ ɣef tuga ttmuquleɣ deg usigna i yettḥerrik waḍu axfifan
acḥal ɣezzif wass-nni  ad t-yenɛel
rebbi daɣen  ayɣer i nruḥ ɣer ṭṭaleb-nni aberkan neǧǧa fatiḥa weḥd-s tettnaɣ d lmut
mi d-nuɣal ǧǧiɣ yemma deffir-iw ɣas akken ur teḥbis aɛeggeḍ akken ad llukkzeɣ tikli
mačči d tikli i leḥḥuɣ d agrireb i ttegriribeɣ gar yiberdan ad tɣileḍ yella win i yi-yeṭṭafaren
seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ ttmuquleɣ ɣer deffir
ad waliɣ kan lḥayek-ines ad rnuɣ tazzla gar umadaɣ ttneggizeɣ ɣef yiẓra d yidabdaren n wakal
mi ara yedreg uzɣuɣ n yemma ur ttɣamayeɣ ara deg umakan-iw ad tt-rǧuɣ ad uɣaleɣ ɣer deffir ad aliɣ wa ad subbeɣ mi ara tt-waliɣ ad ɛeggḍeɣ ula d nekk akken ad tɣiwel tikli dɣa ad kemmleɣ tikli-inu s tazzla ad baɛdeɣ fell-as ayen iwumi zemreɣ akken ur selleɣ ara i ssuɣat d uɛeggeḍ-ines
yewwet wul-iw mi d-ldiɣ tawwurt n utemmu ur sliɣ i ssut n unazeɛ wala n yimeṭṭawen n uletma
ɛeggḍeɣ   fatiḥa  fatiḥa nuɣal-d  ur ttaggad ara  
tasusmi tuɣ yal amkan tessewḥac
qqimeɣ kra n ddqayeq ɣef umnar n utemmu akken ad aɣent wallen-iw tannumi d ṭṭlam yellan daxel-is
hatta tewweḍ-d yemma teḥerḥer tettɛeggiḍ treggem tettgalla deg-i
tḍegger lḥayek-ines teẓẓel ɣef ugertil akken ad d-terr nnehta
uẓaɣ ɣer wusu n uletma beddeɣ ttwaliɣ deg-s deg ṭṭlam kniɣ ɣef tfekka-ines brarḥent wallen-iw sdat n yir tugna yessefqaɛen i ttwaliɣ suɣeɣ
urǧin ad tennejli tugna-nni seg wallaɣ-iw
yal mi ara d-mmektiɣ addud-nni n tfekka yessuffuɣen laɛqel d wudem-nni usbik d wallen-nni yebrarḥen d uxbac-nni yeččan udem-is itezzi wallaɣ-iw
azgen n tfekka-ines tuɣ-itt berra n wusu tettuḍegger ɣef ugertil
truḥ-d yemma thucc-itt s ẓẓur d uɛeggeḍ maca tafekka-ines tuɣal d tasemmaḍt teqqur
nfaq tessuffeɣ terwiḥt mi tt-teṭṭef legrina
tḥebbi yemma yelli-s ɣer yidmaren-is temmermeɣ d imeṭṭawen tuɣwas ffɣen-d lǧiran seg yitemma-nsen uzzlen-d ɣur-neɣ ad walin acu i yeḍran
tameddit-nni yemmeɣ fell-aɣ leḥzen
aṭas i ttruɣ
ur ḥzineɣ ara i tmettant n baba am wakken ḥezneɣ i tmettant n uletma
ahat imi baba d amɣar taggara n yimɣaren d lmut
tules-iyi-d umbaɛd yemma belli baba d argaz-is wis sin asmi tt-yuɣ yeɣleb-itt yakan deg laɛmer
yebra-as urgaz-is amezwaru umbaɛd kraḍ n wagguren n zzwaǧ tuɣal-d s axxam s tadist n gma milud
tenna-yi-d yemma yeḥqer-itt mliḥ yezga yekkat-itt
tesber ledwar imezwura teccetka i temɣart-is maca taneggarut-agi tbedd d mmi-s tessuffeɣ-d accaren-is ɣur-s
ur tezmir ara ad tesber kter n waya
ṭṭfen-as tasawent imi d tagujilt rran-tt d taqeddact fell-asen
maca yemma ur telli ara seg tid ikennun
tbedd deg wudem-nsen
deg tazwara s wawal
yiwen n yiḍ yekker umennuɣ tekres tegnit yeddem urgaz-is aɛekkaz dayen ur teqbil yemma
tenna-as ur telli ara d taɣyult akken ad tt-wten s uɛekkaz
tḥudd ɣef yiman-is
tella tejhed tuɣ tannumi txeddem yakk lecɣal n uxxam seg temẓi
tessexdem iɣallen-is akken ad d-terr tiyita n urgaz-is
texbec argaz-is amesbaṭli tejreḥ leḥnak-is
yekker uhruḥu
ffɣen-d at uxxam d lǧiran
deg yiḍ-nni i teṭṭef yemma rray ad teffeɣ seg uxxam n urgaz-is
tuɣal-d s axxam n ɛemmi-s ɛerḍent snat n twaculin ad afent tifrat mi sent-yekkes zzɛaf maca tugi ad d-tuɣal s axxam n urgaz-is
teqqim yemma semmus n yiseggasen deg liḥala-agi d tamnafeqt
tuɣal tettwassen s yisem n  ɛica rajel 
amek ad tewwet argaz-is  yessefk ɣef tmeṭṭut ad taɣ awal wa ad teknu sdat n urgaz-is
baba d afeḥḥam d aberrani ɣef temnaḍt-nni
yella yezdeɣ weḥd-s deg yiwen n utemmu i d-yezgan tama-nneɣ
ixeddem lefḥem akken ad t-yessenz
d ɛemmi i iɛerḍen fell-as ad d-yaɣ yemma
tuɣ-it yugar yemma deg laɛmer
yella d igellil yezga yuḍen
teqbel yemma
tenna-d teqbel ɣef demma n mmi-s
akken ad terwel ɣef tuzzma n tmeṭṭut n ɛemmi-s d yessi-s deg kraḍet yid-sent i yeqqimen d tiɛezriyin kkatent deg-s la s-qqarent d kemmini i ɣ-yewwin nneḥs s axxam s lefɛayel-im
ass n tmunnent n tmurt yurez ɣer wass-nni amcum
yal mi ara beddren amezwaru s lefruḥ-is iɣumm-it wis sin s leḥzan-ines
yir ccfawat ttnernit ta nnig tayeḍ skecment deg wul-iw timussa d unezgum armi i yi-yuɣal kulci d aberkan dɣa ḥulfaɣ i tekref temmeɣ ɣef tfekka-inu
mi nemsefraq uɣaleɣ s axxam ttwaḥucceɣ
ẓẓleɣ ɣef wattag siɣeɣ tilibizyu ttneggizeɣ seg umaṭṭaf ɣer wayeḍ ttqellibeɣ ɣef usaru ara iyi-isettun imira-inu d yizri-inu armi i yi-tewwi tnafa
seg uzal-nni yugi ad iyi-yeṭṭixer yiwen n useqsi  d acu-tt taḥkayt-agi taqdimt i yerran tameṭṭut n racid ad tɣil aṭṭan i tt-yuɣen d tarrut ɣef yiwet n sseyya i texdem yiwen n wass  d acu-tt sseyya-agi  ameddakkel-iw yettwali-tt d taḥkayt taqdimt tɣumm-itt tatut aṭas aya
iban racid ur yettwali ara sseyya-agi am wakken i tt-twali tmeṭṭut-is mgaradent tmuɣliwin-nsen
deg ddurt-nni ttwaṭṭfeɣ qrib yal ass s temliliyin akken ad nwali amek ad nḥudd ɣef yimeɣnasen isertiyen i teṭṭef temsulta terra-ten deg lḥebs acku rẓan asaḍuf n ugdal n tmesbaniyin deg yiberdan  sudsen yiwen n unejmuɛ deg umraḥ n umenzu n mayyu akken ad bedden mgal tuṭṭfa n yiwen seg yiɣella-nsen i d-yemmeslayen deg yiwen n uɣmis afransiss ideg yenna belli anagraw n tmurt yenɣa yiwen seg yizumal n temgadla berra n tmurt
nuɣ tannumi nettemlili deg tnarit n umastan si nasser nettnadi ɣef yikalan iwulmen akken ad nexdem akken iwulem
d wagi i yi-d-yeǧǧan ad ttuɣ maḍi taḥkayt n racid d waṭṭan n tmeṭṭut-is  ur ruḥeɣ ad ten-ẓureɣ ur seqsaɣ ɣef liḥala-nsen snat n ledwar
ur ẓriɣ ara d acu i yi-yesmektan yis-s mi lliɣ tetteɣ imekli akked yiwen n umidaw deg usečču i iqublen axxam n teɣdemt
ahat d tamectarit-nni yettaken anzi ɣer tmeṭṭut n umeddakkel-iw i yeqqimen lmendad-iw
refdeɣ kan aqerruy-iw ɣef yiḍebsiyen armi ɣlint wallen-iw fell-as
tfaq ttmuquleɣ deg-s ur as-yaɛǧib ara lḥal tekker tbeddel amkan
sḥisfeɣ snat n tikkal
tamezwarut mi hewwjeɣ massa-nni nekk ur lliɣ ara seg wid yettazzalen deffir n tlawin
tis snat ɣef ustehzi-inu
amek i iruḥ racid seg wallaɣ-iw snat n ledwar yernu ẓriɣ tameṭṭut-is tuḍen mliḥ
dɣa ṭṭfeɣ rray ad seɣtiɣ lɣelṭa-inu
s tmara i tt-skecmeɣ ɣer ssbiṭar
ayɣer ur i yi-d-tenniḍ ara  tili ssawleɣ srid i uɣella n umeẓlu neɣ anemhal s timmad-is
tessneḍ-iyi mliḥ a si ɛebdelqader acḥal kerheɣ iberdan-a yezzin
kerheɣ tabenɛemmit acku temgarad mliḥ s wayen umneɣ
ma twaliḍ imdanen-nni imeɣban wid ukkud beddeɣ deg umennuɣ-nsen n yal ass mgal lbaṭal n tsuda d tmeḥqranit n yimeqqran deg tmurt-a tameɣbunt ttraǧun s ibeddi deg lesfuf ɛyan ttubahedlen suturen s tmuɣli-nsen deg yal yiwen yelsan tabanta tamellalt ad ten-iɛiwen wa ad taseḍ keččini d aneggaru mebla leḥya ad ten-tezwireḍ acku tessneḍ yiwen seg yimasayen
tigawin am tigi rennunt deg ddel n yimdanen snernayent deg-sen daɣen ddɣel
d tigawin am tigi i yesnernayen takriḍt deg tmetti sekrahent ula d tamurt i yimezdaɣ-is deg taggara ad qellben amek ad inigen ɣas ɣer unazir ur qebbleɣ ara tifula-agi ur ḥemmleɣ ara ad tent-xedmeɣ
ttḥarabeɣ ɣef yizerfan-iw am yizem maca ur rekḍeɣ ara izerfan n wiyaḍ
kečč tḥemmleḍ ad tessimɣureḍ temsal tagi ur telli d tabenɛemmit ur tettekkseḍ i walbaɛḍ izerfan-is
ayen yellan d asewzel deg umecwar acku aṭṭan n tmeṭṭut-ik yewɛer mliḥ yernu ilaq-as ad tt-tdawi s temɣawla
tura ad k-d-iniɣ tidet lbeɣḍ-inu i lḥukuma d unagraw aserti s umata yennerna ussan-a ineggura
iban-iyi-d ssbiṭar am uddaynin ucmit s rrwayeḥ-ines qessiḥen iɣef yerna ugudu yettnernin yal ass
ibduzen mebla aman tiwwura rẓent ulac tezdeg ulac leḥya
imuḍan ttawin-d yid-sen usu d tduli-nsen ula d učči-nsen d imawlan-nsen i sen-t-id-yettawin
sani ruḥen idrimen n usefrek  anda tella tɛessast  ad as-tiniḍ deg ssuq n  lḥerrac  i telliḍ terwi tebberwi ur tɛeqleḍ ara amejjay seg ufremli amsizdeg seg uɛessas neɣ wid yettawin yettaran din seg texxamt ɣer tayeḍ
ass amezwaru nesɛedda tasebḥit s lekmal-is nettraǧu akken ad ɣ-d-inin deg taggara ur nettɛedday ara ass-nni ilaq ad nuɣal ass niḍen
ur tettafeḍ ara yiwen d amasay d wumi ad temmeslayeḍ neɣ ad k-immel sani ilaq ad truḥeḍ
ttwaṭṭfen irkelli ur sɛin ara akud akken ad d-rren ɣef tuttriwin n yimuḍan neɣ n yimawlan-nsen
tazeqqa teččur s lɣaci wid ibedden ɣelben wid yeqqimen imsaɛfen ɣelben imuḍan
yernu ttcetkin irkelli am yixeddamen am yimẓuren
ma tesseqsaḍ tafremlit ad k-d-terr mebla leḥya mačči d nettat i yellan d tanemhalt
ma tqelbeḍ ɣef yiwen seg yimasayen iban d anabay i yella neɣ iruḥ ɣer unejmuɛ
ma terfiḍ neɣ tɛeggḍeḍ ad k-d-tas imir-n kan tririt  ruḥ ad teccektiḍ ɣer uneɣlaf neɣ ɣer uselway
d aɣerrabu ur nesɛi rrayes d ibeḥriyen yettnaɣen gar-asen ɣef wučči i d-yegran d nitni i t-yessulḥuyen amek i sen-yehwa
aselway am wakken mazal yesɛa uselway adabu gar yifassen-is
d taɛeljet i ttḥerriken ilemdimen ur nessin rreḥma wala leḥnana
amer ila uselway kra n lhiba tili urǧin neṭqen wigi s wawalen am wigi
aql-aɣ deg tmurt n war-tarrut n war-anqad d ustehzi ameqqran yernu ayɣer ad yelthu uselway d wid i as-yezzin s ssbiṭarat n lezzayer  ur ten-tteḥwijen ara
yal mi ara yewwet ubeḥri yiwen seg-sen neɣ seg twaculin-nsen ad as-heggin asafag ad t-yawin imir-n kan ɣer neɣ akken ad idawi deg ssbiṭarat imeqqranen s yidrimen n uɣref
d tagi d tamurt iɣef yennuɣ uɣref akken ad tawi tilelli-ines
ayen ibeddlen tura nezmer ad nesseglef wa ad nɛeggeḍ
maca d acu lfayda n ssuɣat nettɛeggiḍ deg lbir ur nesɛi lqaɛ 
imenzayen iɣef tettmeslayeḍ aṭas aya segmi ruḥen seg tudert-nneɣ
nekcem deg tbuciḍant n usaḍuf n teẓgi islem ameqqran itett islem ameẓyan ɣur-k adinar teswiḍ adinar tesɛiḍ taɛeqqayt n lleft azal-ik ihi d taɛeqqayt n lleft
ɣef waya ftiɣ tzemreḍ ad tesxedmeḍ timussniwin-inek i uferru n wuguren-inek maca mebla ma tḍurreḍ wiyaḍ neɣ ad teččeḍ izerfan-nsen acku wagi yettuɣal d lbaṭel d tmeḥqranit
nekkini am kečč kerheɣ lbaṭel tawuri-inu rriɣ-tt d allal s wayes ttḥudduɣ ɣef wid yettwaḥeqqren
maca ini-yi-d  amek i tettili nasira 
skecmeɣ-tt ass n wahad ɣer ssbiṭar mi ruḥeɣ ad tt-waliɣ ass n sem tenna-yi-d ulac win i d-yesfeqden fell-as neɣ idiwa-tt
ufiɣ-tt teqqim ɣef yiri n umeṭreḥ-ines tettru
tebɣa ad teffeɣ imir-n kan
 ssuffeɣ-iyi sya eǧǧ-iyi ad mmteɣ deg uxxam-iw  akka i teqqim la tettɛeggiḍ tegzem-iyi tasa-w
tɣaḍ-iyi mačči d kra zaɛfeɣ mliḥ ruḥeɣ ad qellbeɣ ɣef umejjay maca ulac ula d yiwen
ssbiṭar am tedbelt taggara n ddurt ulac win ad d-tafeḍ
yenna-yi-d ufremli i ufiɣ ass-nni belli timacinin xesrent ulac acu ad as-xedmen mebla rradyuyat
hedreɣ-as ɣef rradyuyat i tesɛa yakan yenna-yi-d ayɣer ur tent-id-wwiɣ ara akked tmuḍint
uɣaleɣ s temɣawla s axxam wwiɣ-tent-id yenna-yi-d yessefk fell-i ad rǧuɣ armi iɛedda umejjay amazzag ass n warim
ddurt s lekmal daxel ssbiṭar akken ad tt-iwali umejjay
amek ur treffuḍ ara 
amek ur k-yetteffeɣ ara laɛqel  yenna-yi-d ufremli ma bɣiɣ ad ɣiwleɣ i tujjya n umuḍin ilaq ad xedmeɣ rradyuyat berra n ssbiṭar
aql-iyi da ay ameddakkel ad k-iḥaseb rebbi ma teḥwaǧeḍ kra
ẓriɣ rradyuyat-agi ɣlayit mliḥ yernu tastaɣt-ik meẓẓiyet
deg tegnatin n ṭṭiq i tettbin tdukkli
ttxil-k ur ttsetḥi ara ur sekcam ara leḥsabat imeɛwuja gar-aneɣ
am wakken teẓriḍ anagar nekk d uqerruy-iw ulac wayeḍ yid-i tajernaḍt-inu tkeffu-yi
tanemmirt-ik a ɛebdelqader  ar iḍ-a tamayt i yakuc lḥemdullah yester-itt rebbi
ussan-nni zgiɣ d racid uɣal-as d tili
zgiɣ ttruḥuɣ yid-s ɣer ssbiṭar ttwaliɣ imejjayen d yifremliyen ttweṣṣiɣ-ten ɣef tmeṭṭut-is
maca simmal leḥḥun wussan simmal tettuɣal tezmert-is ɣer deffir yewwi-tt ihi ɣer tesga n deg ssbiṭar n musṭafa baca deg tmanaɣt yettuxessen deg waṭṭanen n ukunsir
din i as-xedmen tamzelt akken ad as-kksen tabbuct-is taẓelmaḍt
urǧin walaɣ ameddekkel-iw yuyes am wass n temzelt
nurǧa aṭas deg umraḥ n ssbiṭar
imir-n kan i as-faqeɣ d argaz urhif i yella d urnan tezmer yiwet n nnesma n waḍu asemmaḍ ad tt-id-tessafeg ɣer yigenni
ziɣ itteffer ddaw n wadduden-ines iquranen deg tedmi d tsertit yiwet n tmella neɣ rrehma talsant tameqqrant
aṭas i d-yemmeslay allen-is ččurent d imeṭṭawen i ixenqen tifyar-ines tugzimin i itteffɣen s tmara seg ccfawat-ines
zzwaǧ-ines d nasira yemxalaf ɣef wiyaḍ
yeḥmel-itt seg wul seg tnezzayt-nni ideg tt-iwala tleḥḥu ɣer ṭṭabla i yesefrak daxel n tesdawit akken ad tessekles iman-is deg tigawt n twizi n tegrest ilmend n tegrawla takerzant
taqcict tla snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen d taɣezfant acebbub-is ṭṭawes tezmummug s nniya ulac leḥsab yellan deg uqerruy-is telsa aserwal n ǧǧin n lmuda taneggarut
tenna-d srid mebla tazwert neɣ asgerfel 
tagi d tanarit n yinelmaden iwiziwen 
anɛam ansuf acu teḥwajeḍ a 
sliɣ tessudusem inigan ɣer sseḥra
d tidet maca mačči i uḥewwes
d tamuɣzelt i lfayda n tegrawla takerzant
yal ass d axeddim
ẓriɣ
ẓriɣ ula nekk d yelli-s n taddart uɣeɣ tannumi d tudert taqessḥant
nekk 
nekk d tanelmadt deg ugezdu n teglizit ẓriɣ seg kra n yinelmaden tetteffɣem ɣer tudrin tettmeslayem d yikerrazen tessefhamem-asen isuḍaf n tegrawla takerzant
nekk 
nekk ḥemmleɣ
bumedyen d tnemla bɣiɣ ad ffɣeɣ yid-wen deg yimuras n tegrest axir n tuɣalin ɣer taddart-iw d tɣimit deg uxxam
timlilit-a teṭṭef kra n ddqayeq kan maca tugna n
nasira tefses-ines d wamek tettmeslay melken racid yuɣal yettazzal deffir-s yeṭṭafar tili-s deg ddruj d tgennariyin n ugezdu n tsekla d tussniwin tilsanin
deg lkar i d-yewwin tarkeft n yinelmaden ɣer temdint n wergla yeqqim tama-s deg yikursiyen n deffir ihedder-as ɣef tmuɣzelt d tegrawla takerzant akked tnemla
teqqim la s-tsell kan tettserriḥ seg lweqt ɣer wayeḍ i ssuɣat n lewhama wa ad as-d-tefk iseqsiyen akken ad tefhem ugar
d taqcict i iḥemmlen tudert tḥemmel tamussni tleḥḥu s nniya
deg snat n ledwar ideg teqqim tezga nasira tessebgan-d lewhama-ines sdat n yidurar n yijdi awraɣ imedwan n tezdayin s tili d tiliwa-nsen
thedder mebla akukru i yifellaḥen i yesrusun i wallen-nsen seg leḥya d uqader ad cmumḥen wa ad seqsin anta tagi i d-yuzen bumedyen
akka i ttwalin timsal wehhmen daɣen deg tmussniwin-ines deg tfellaḥt ma tesserwes gar tfellaḥt deg ugafa d wayen xeddmen deg unẓul
leḥmala n racid i teqcict-a tennerna ladɣa mi tt-iwala amek i tettidir ur tessimɣur ara iman-is ur tcerriḍ ara ur tettɣunfu ara axeddim
tzewwir ɣer uxeddim txeddem lecɣal seg wul ugar n waya yezga uzmumeg ɣef yimi-s
akka i tt-yeglem racid allen-is ruḥent ɣer lfirmat-nni iwumi yecfa ar iḍ-a ɣef yismawen nsent  rwisat bni-tur
ḥasi ben ɛebdella ḥasi el fugaɛa ɛin naqa wadi
nexla
temlek ul-is d lejwareḥ-is deg tirza-nni i ifaq d nettat i d taḥbibt n laɛmer ulac tayeḍ
ɣef waya yexdem iwumi yezmer akken ad yesmil ul-is ɣur-syemmeslay-as-d ɣef yiman-is temẓi-ines tirga-ines d wayes yumen
acḥal i iferreḥ yettafeg seg tumert ma twufeq-it rray neɣ ad as-tini ula d nettat tɛac deg temẓi-ines tugnatin yettemcabin ɣer tid iɣef yettmeslay deg yiwet n taddart tameẓyant deg temnaḍt n tmurt n ufella
urǧin ad yettu iḍ-nni ideg yufa iman-is yid-s weḥd-sen kan deg tzeqqa tebra i ucebbub-is icenfiren-is d tameqqrant n usečču
yuɣ tannumi yettɛeẓẓir yesɛedday ssaɛa neɣ ugar deg tɣuri
ma ruḥen yinelmaden niḍen ɣer texxamin-nsen i usgunfu d yiḍes netta iḥemmel ad iruḥ ɣer usečču i d-yezgan deg tama niḍen n umraḥ ameqqran ad yeqqim ɣef ṭṭabla ad d-yessuffeɣ seg lǧib-is adlis wa ad yadef deg ugbur-ines
yiwen n yiḍ tessexleɛ-it mi tt-yufa tbedd nnig n uqerruy-is tesseqsa-t s taɣect-ines taḥlawant   d acu teqqareḍ   mebla ma terǧa tiririt teqqim sdat-s
aggur yemmed yeččur ul-is s tafat d tumert

turkya
yules-as s leḥya d tewzel taqsiḍt n tayri yellan gar
 memet  d tin i iḥemmel seg temẓi i yesserwel ɣer yidurar akken ad tt-yessemneɛ seg yifassen n umesbaṭli-nni
sakin yeɣra-as-d kra n tseddarin akken ad as-yekkes ukukru-nni
yečča-tt s wallen ad tɣileḍ d tajenniwt i t-id-yettqabalen
ayen yessewhamen ur as-d-tewwi ara ula yiwen n ufukel ɣef ssebba n tisin-ines ad as-d-tini amedya yeqreḥ-itt uqerruy-is teffeɣ ɣer umraḥ mi twala tafat deg tnawalt truḥ-d ad tsew aman neɣ ad d-taf ssebba niḍen
tusa-d teqqim-d amzun d tiɛad yesɛan yakan
telha teččur d nniya ur tessexdam ara tiḥerci neɣ taḥraymit
imir-n kan ifaq racid i umkan yexla ulac win yellan yezmer ad ten-iwali yiwen seg yinelmaden dɣa ad iɣil tella lḥaǧa gar-asen wa ad ten-yerdi d akken ttarran tamuɣzelt i wayen niḍen
racid yella seg yiɣellaten i yettḥaraben akken ur tteffɣent ara tmuɣzal ɣef ubrid iwakken ad rren talast lehdur n yisedmaren d i yineslemaẓra ama seg yinelmaden neɣ wiyaḍ i yekkaten deg tmuɣzal
gar lehdur-agi inigen-a deg tilawt d tagnit akken ad xedmen leḥram acku ɣer lmeɛsegga d yisduklanen tameṭṭut d ayla azday gar yirgazen
tullas-nni i yettekkan deg tmuɣzal d ticermuḍin ttqellibent kan ɣef lmeɛseyya
tikta-a grarbent ɣef wallaɣ n racid ɣef yiwen n ubrid
ad as-tiniḍ d azrem i t-yeqqsen ddaw n ṭṭabla
ibedd yerra talast i temlilit-nsen yewwi-d ssebba s yiḍes acku aṭas n lecɣal i ten-yettraǧun azekka-nni
banen-d urfan ɣef wudem n nasira i iɣilen d racid ur nebɣi ara ad yeqqim yid-s
tesrugmet  iḍ ameggaz  tejbed iman-is s laɛqel racid iletha s usexsi n teftilin n tnawalt
ur yerri ara racid lbal deg teswiɛt-nni i wurfan n
nasira
ifaq i temsalt-a azekka-nni mi ur as-d-terri ara yakk ccan
mi ara s-d-yemmeslay ad as-d-terr kan s tririyin tiwezzlanin
ussan-nni tessaweḍ tmuɣzelt ɣer taggara-s
racid yettwaṭṭef s tira n uneqqis ara yefk i yimasayen n lwilaya deg temlilit taneggarut
ifaq racid i ssebba i yerran tahuskayt izedɣen tirga-ines deg liḥala-nni
ur yufi ara tagnit anda ad yizmir ad yekkes asigna i yeɣlin gar-asen deg yiḍ-nni
deg lkar i ten-yerran tɣawel
nasira ad teṭṭef amkan i d-yusan deffir n unehhar
amkan-nni ttwalint-t yakk wid yellan deg lkar ur yezmir ara walbaɛḍ ad yeɛzel deg-s iman-is
ɣas akken yeqqim yettawi yettarra seg deffir ɣer sdat yettaf-d dima tisebbiwin akken ad yemmeslay d unehhar akked nasira ɣef yinig d tudrin d temdinin i zeggren
mi wwḍen tefsi
nasira am lmelḥ deg waman truḥ mebla ma tsellem fell-as
acḥal i ɣezzifit acḥal messusit wussan-nni i d-yegran seg yimuras
yeṭṭef rray asmi ara tt-iwali ad yekkes lemgarda ad as-yessefhem ayɣer i yexdem akken
ass n tuɣalin ɣer tesdawit ireyyes iman-is yelsa iselsa yelhan yerra leɛṭer yegla-d s ungal n  yecar kamal  akken ad as-t-yehdu wa ad tt-iweṣṣi ad t-tɣer
yeqqim yettraǧu tisin-ines s lḥir ameqqran yettalas deg wul-is tinfaliyin s wayes ad tt-imager yessugun amkan anda ara tili temlilit n umsaleḥ
tɛeṭṭel
tekcem-it tuggdi tecɛel deg wul-is times yebda yettazzal gar tgennariyin d tzeɣwa d tawwurt tagejdant n ugezdu
allen-is uɣalent am lkamira ulac acu ad zegglent
hatta tban-d am waggur n lɛid
tleḥḥu s laɛqel kan ur tḥar ara am wakken ur tebɣi ara ad d-tuɣal ɣer tesdawit seg wasmi i tennuɣna d racid
mi tt-iwala yennecraḥ ul-is iḥebbek yekkat am ṭṭbel yuzzel ɣur-s ad tt-imager yenna-as yettraǧu tisin-ines segmi teldi tesdawit tiwwura-ines
tiririt-ines tella am ucercur n waman isemmaḍen deg wussan n tegrest   ayɣer i yi-tettraǧuḍ 
yaxi ussan n tmuɣzelt kfan yal yiwen deg-neɣ ad yuɣal ɣer leqraya-ines 
ɛerqent-as i racid yebda asqewqew yakk tifyar tihuskayin i yeftel akken ad yekkes lemgarda i t-yenɣan ussan-a ineggura ufgent
maca ɣas akken yeṭṭef
ass-nni yeldi ul-is i nasira yesqir-as s tayri-ines
yessuffeɣ-itt seg tesdawit yelḥa yid-s deg uɣlad i d-yettakken ɣef tmersit yerra-tt ɣer yiḍ-nni yessemres yakk ayen i yessen akken ad tt-yecker wa ad yesnerni deg thuski-ines
yeglem-as-d amek i yesɛedda iḍ-nni umbaɛd mi msefraqen yeqqim yettmektay kan tiɣimit-nni i qqimen allaɣ-is yekcem imaḍalen n tayri
am wakken ineggura iɛeṭṭel umeslay ɣef uqelleq-ines ussan-a ixemmem ad iruḥ ɣer taddart-is wa ad iqelleb fell-as maca yuggad seg twacult-is d yinalkamen n tigawt am tagi
ssenden ɣef yiri n tɣalaḍt n wuzzal i iqublen aɣerrabu n yiminigen i yettraǧun ttesriḥ akken ad yeqleɛ ɣer marsilya yessuffeɣ-d akk tayri yeččuren ul-is i yelli-s n taddart yezmmumugen i tin yesɛan nnif
tcukk kan ur tt-iḥemmel ara tejbed iman-is s laɛqel mebla ssut mebla laɛyaḍ
yella yettmeslay yid-s mebla ma imuqel-itt
tamuɣli-ines truḥ ɣer yigli azegzaw i t-iqublen maca mi yebɣa ad as-ibuḥ s tayri-ines yessusem ciṭuḥ yezzi-d ɣur-s imuqqel allen-is yenna 
 ḥemmleɣ-kem a nasira 
ḥemmleɣ-kem seg wass amezwaru i kem-walaɣ
amen-iyi urǧin nniɣ-d imeslayen-a i teḥdayt niḍen am wakken laɛmer ad as-d-tsell teqcict-niḍen seg yimi-w tikkelt niḍen
ur tettɛedday ara ddqiqa mebla ma tɛeddaḍ-d gar wallen-iw 
tiḥnakin n nasira uɣalent d tizeggaɣin tessider i uqerruy-is ur as-d-tenni acemma
tessusem kra n lweqt
yerkeb-it ccek
kemmlen yimeɛcuqen aḥewwes deg yiberdan n lezzayer talemmast
sakin yedda yid-s armi taɣremt n tullas n ben
ɛeknun yeqqim ɣer tama n tewwurt n lemraḥ deg yiwet n teɣmert ugar n ssaɛa ur yecliɛ ara s tmuɣli n wid ur neɛǧib ara lḥal neɣ n wid i tenɣa tismin
iḥulfa racid i tfekka-ines fessuset ɣef rric n yitbiren yiwet n tiyita kan ad uɣalen yiɣallen-is d iferriwen ad t-ssafgen ɣer ṣa n yigenwan
ur iḥulfa i lweqt amek i yettazzal wala i laẓ amek i yeqqaz deg yiẓerman-is
ur skadben ara wid i d-yennan imeɛcuqen tetten tayri d ubeḥri
mi bedden akken tbuḥ-as-d nasira s leḥzen-ines d wayen i tt-iqerḥen
tenna-as tesɛedda iḍ-nni d imeṭṭawen s tsusmi ur teṭṭis ula d yiwet n ddqiqa
maca nnif-is yefka-as-d ssber s wayes ad tqabel uguren n tayri
tuɣal ɣer tesdawit teqqed ljerḥ-is
ur tebdir ara yakk awal n tayri lameɛna lehdur-nni sbeggnen i racid belli ul-is imal ɣur-s maca leḥya d laɛwayed ur tt-ǧǧin ara ad as-tbuḥ d tamezwarut s tayri-ines
akka i teḍra timlilit akka i tella tayri i yeqqimen sin n yiseggasen acekki-ten zgan yimeɛcuqen ttemlillin deg tesdawit ttawin-d awal ɣef yal asentel ttmeslayen-d ɣef tayri
tiɣimit deg sin yid-sen kan tɛumm-asen akken ad d-tekcem tumert ulawen-nsen
maca tafekka ɣur-s assaren-ines yewɛer ɣef umdan ad ibedd mgal-nsen
iɣwis agensay yeǧhed ɣef yiɣwis n laẓ d ssṭer anagar yusef i izemren ad t-iḥarben yernu s lemɛawna n yakuc
maca tiqsiḍin n yimazanen sɛant yiwet n tmeẓla temxalaf ɣef tmeẓla i yesselḥayen tudert n yimdanen
deg tazwara llan ttemlilin s tuffra deg tzeɣwa n ssinima ideg ɛerḍen i tikkelt tamenzut lbenna n usuden kan
ttɣimin akken iwumi zemren
yessawaḍ-itt armi d tawwurt n teɣremt n tnelmadin ad yeqqim yid-s deg yiwet n teɣmert tifekkin-nsen mqarabent mliḥ times tecɛel deg-sen rɣan tayri
ifassen-nsen myuṭṭafen iḍuḍan-nsen mcubbaken myeqraḥen ahat ad yessexsi ciṭuḥ seg tmes i yettnernin daxel n snat n tfekkiwin-a
timetti tettɛassa mliḥ timsal-a urǧin ad teǧǧ albaɛḍ ad iɛeddi tilisa ad yexdem ayen yettwagedlen ɛeynani
ma yebla-ken rebbi ṣṣret iman-nwen maca anda ara yeṣṣer umdan iman-is deg temdint-agi ideg iberdan zgan ččuren s yimenṭaren  assaɣ i ten-yezdin ur iɛedda ara aswir-a yeččuren s nniya d tayri tazedgant amer mačči d zzher tiderɣelt n wallen d wassaren n tfekka i iwaɛren ɣef umdan ad sen-yerr algam
racid ɣur-s yiwen n umeddakkel yesɛa axxam deg udcir  trular  ur yebɛid ara mliḥ ɣef tesdawit talemmast d ixxamen yettunefken i yinelmaden izewǧen
yiwen n ubrid yaɛreḍ-it umeddakkel-is i umulli n tmeṭṭut-is i yellan ula d nettat d tameɣnast deg umussu n tmuɣzelt n yinelmaden
iruḥ akked nasira ɣer tmeɣra ass-nni i yebda wassaɣ n tdukkli gar tmeṭṭut n umeddakkel-is d tin i iḥemmel wul-is
uɣalen ttemwalin deg tazwara seg lweqt ɣer wayeḍ umbaɛd mqarabent tmeẓra
yal tikkelt mi ara d-yaf racid iman-is daxel n uxxam ttimɣurent tirga-ines dɣa yebda yessaram ad yekseb ula d netta axxam am wa akken ad yidir d nasira deg yiwen n lɛecc aḥmayan ara yerren tirga-ines d tilawt
ur yecfi ara amek i zrin wussan almi yufa iman-is deg leɣyab n umeddakkel-is d tmeṭṭut-is ḥala netta d nasira deg uxxam akken ad sɛeddin iḍ n taggara n ddurt
zzin-d sin n yigḍaḍ-nni ɣef yiberdan n temdint n lezzayer ffren daxel n zzedwa n tmeddit n wass n wamhad ttneggizen seg tḥanut ɣer tayeḍ seg lejnan n  tlelli  ɣer usekwar n  sufya  sakin tzeqqa n ssinima ṭṭfen rray ad walin asaru deg
 dunyazad  d asaru amasri n ccna yettmeslay ɣef tayri d wuguren i tt-yettmagaren
rran iman-nsen deg umkan n yisebgaren imeɛcaq dɣa yennerna lebɣi-nsen akken ad rẓen ayen i ten-iferqen wa ad xedmen ayen ilaq akken ad ressin tayri-nsen yernu ḥala timlilit gar tfekwin yerɣan i izemren ad tressi tayri
uɣalen ɣer uxxam ferḥen mliḥ ad tɣileḍ deg yiḍ-nni zewǧen s tidet
thegga-d nasira imensi d afessas ɛawzen qqimen ttalsen i tmucuha yal yiwen seg yimeɛcaq yettraǧu taswiɛt-nni
mlalent-d tfekkiwin s laɛqel s ukukru s tugdi maca tayri i yuɣen aẓar sin n yiseggasen-aya leqfal mɛanaqen tifekkwin teṭṭef-itent tergagayt tasemmaḍt ara yessexsin irrij i yuɣen daxel-nsen
tafekka teččur s wuffiren tettawi bab-is ɣer kra n yimekwan mebla ma txemmem deg yinalkamen
deg yiḍ-nni i yesseɣres racid tindert n temddekkelt-is
tɛeggeḍ nasira tettru s tsusmi mi twala later n yidammen gar tmessaḍin-ines
tuẓ ɣer racid telseq deg-s am wakken tḥulfa i lehcaca n liḥala-ines
ihedden-itt racid yenna-as ad zewǧen deg wussan i d-iteddun ad iruḥ ad tt-yexḍeb sɣur yimawlan-is wa ad sɛeddin aggur n tament deg yiwet n temdint seg temdinin tihuskayin n yuruba
tirga ɣumment tudert-nsen tewwi-ten deg yiwen n yinig war taggara
tesseɣli-d yakk
seg yiḍ-nni uɣalen yimeɛcaq-agi ttfarasen yal tagnit ad d-afen akken ad semlilen tifekkiwin-nsen ad kecmen deg umaḍal niḍen
ẓeddmen am sin n uɛidiwen akken ad ɛerḍen i lbenna n tfekka alamma sekren
maca tumert ur d-tettas ara kan akka tesɛa ssuma am wakken tella deg tkesniwin tigrikiyin tettara talast i tirga tettara amdan ɣer tilawt-ines
yiwet n tsebḥit truḥ-d nasira s yiwen n wudem d awraɣ ur tezmir ara ad tenṭeq s yiwen n wawal mebla ma tebɣa ad teṭṭerḍeq d imeṭṭawen
uggadeɣ a racid  uggadeɣ ad iyi-ineɣ baba amer ad iẓer acu i yi-yeḍran
mraw n wussan nekk ttraǧuɣ yal ddqiqa  ulac  uɣaleɣ ur gganeɣ ur tetteɣ 
yestaɛref racid belli ur ifaq ara i ssebba i yerran taḥbibt-is deg liḥala-nni almi umbaɛd
yewwet iman-is s yibeqqayen
amek ur ixemmem ara i temsalt-a  amek i as-truḥ yeẓra yal assaɣ gar urgaz d tmeṭṭut ɣas s leqher igellu-d s urfad n tadist
d tabuciḍant i ten-yessuffɣen seg lǧennet n ɛaden am wakken teḍra i adam d ḥawa deg tazwara n talsa
anda-t yiblis i ten-iweswsen ad ččen seg tteffaḥ mebla ttesriḥ  ilaq ad yessekcem iman-is akken ad menɛen seg lefḍiḥa
maca deg tazwara ilaq ɣef racid ad yessenɣes seg lxelɛa d tuggdi i yeṭṭfen nasira
ur ttqelliq ara iman-im  d agellel kan deg tarda-inem

acu taderwict selbeɣ
