ass-nni i iwala i tikkelt tamezwarut udem uḍɛif n tmaɛcuqt-is
yettwali-tt uqbel d tin i ilan tugna tuntimt ur teclliɛ ara maḍi maca iwala-tt d tahcicant tɣelli sdat n ugur amezwaru ad tt-imagren
maca ɣas akken yefhem ssebba n tuggdi-ines acku tawaɣit i yeɣlin fell-as ma slan yis-s wiyaḍ ad teglu s uqerruy-is
ɣef waya yessefk fell-as ad iqabel tamsalt akken ilaq wa ad inadi ɣef tifrat ara iḥarben ɣef ccan d lɛerḍ n tmaɛcuqt-is
ass-nni yewwi-tt ɣer yiwen n usečču d urkid ulac acu ur yexdim ara akken ad tt-yesseqneɛ belli tamsalt ur berriket ara am wakken i d-teqqar
seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ yeqqar-as-d ad ibedd ɣer tama-s am wakken ad ibibb tamasit yid-s
maca amgired meqqer gar tirga akked lemɛahdat tiẓiḍanin d teqseḥ n tilawt
deg yiḍ-nni ixemmem racid i yal turda
ur yufi ula rrbeɛ n yiwet i yezmer ad yexdem
ixemmem mliḥ deg zzwaǧ maca am wakken i qqaren wid ijerrben zzwaǧ n yiwen n yiḍ aheggi-ines d aseggas ternuḍ ma yella kulci liḥala-ines d yewjed ulac uguren
tura ma nwala wassaɣen-ines d twacult-is ur nettaf ara kra yessefraḥen
zzwaǧ-ines ihi ilaq-as lqern neɣ ugar
d tazzla mgal akud
kra n ledwar wa ad d-tbin lefḍiḥa
tɣaḍ-it tmaɛcuqt-is d acu ad tt-yaɣen amer ad yeffeɣ wawal ad yaweḍ tawacult-is
iban ḥala idammen ara ssazlen yiɛeggalen n
ɣef tmenya n ssbaḥ tuɣ-it yesṭebṭib ɣef tewwurt n twacult-is
yeẓra amek i ttḥarabent twaculin ɣef tyeǧǧi n tlawin
ḥala idammen ara yessizdgen nnif
d wigi i d isuḍaf i ɣ-id-ǧǧan yimezwura-nneɣ ulac win i izemren ad ten-innal
yessefk fell-as ad yembiwel s temɣawla
yal ugur ɣur-s tifrat ulac asif ur nesɛi tiqenṭert qelleb ad tafeḍ
akka i yella yettxemmim
uxxam n umeddakkel-is zubir
tenna-as tmeṭṭut-is 
uqbel ma txedmeḍ kra ilaq ad tẓer nasira ma tella s tidet s tadist ahat d agellel kan
ɣef waya ilaq-as ad texdem tesleḍt ɣer umejjay
ass-agi ad ssiwleɣ i yiwet seg temdukalin-iw d tamejjayt tettekka yid-neɣ yakan deg umussu n temɣuzla txeddem deg ssbiṭar n bab el-wad
u ma yella s tadist i tella d acu ara nexdem 
ur zewwir ara temsal
yal tamsalt deg lawan-is
yesserwes racid lweqt n tgannit akken ad d-ffɣen yigemmaḍ n tesleḍt ɣer wakud n tmerǧiwt n yigemmaḍ n temzelt n tmeṭṭut-is deg tgemmi i iqublen tasga n
yusa-d yiwen n ssut yestewtiw-as-d seg lebɛid yeqqar-as-d tamsalt-a d asqecmeɛ kan tura ad yekkes wagu wa ad d-tuɣal yal taɣawsa s amkan-is
dɣa ad yefreḥ wul-is wa ad igal ur iseɛɛu ara assaɣen d tmaɛcuqt-is alamma frant yakk timsal n tmeɣra
iwala iman-is dayen iruḥ ad tt-yexḍeb imager-d baba-s i yesreḥben s urgaz n yelli-s yuqem tameɣra tameẓyant i kra seg yimeddukkal-is d kra seg watmaten-is sakin yewwi tajeǧǧigt-ines ɣer neɣ ruma akken ad sɛeddin aggur n tamemt
tugna-agi mazal ur temmid ara armi yesla i yiwen n ssut d azuran yerra-t-id ɣer terẓeg n tilawt-ines
dɣa iwala taɛebbuḍt tettcuffu am tkuret ara yesxesren tafekka n tmaɛcuqt-is
sakin ad grirbent fell-as twelfin yessefqaɛen tiwelfin n wudmawen n yiɛeggalen n twacult n nasira ddmen gar yifassen-nsen icaquren d tɛekzin i yessamsen nnif-nsen ara yazzlen
tergagi tfekka n racid yeqqim yetthuzzu aqerruy-is akken ad yesserwel seg wallaɣ-is yir tikta i t-izedɣen
yeqqim yettmuqqul ɣer yigli yettɛeggiḍ deg wudmawen n yizɣuɣen i as-yezzin 
 ur ken-ttaǧǧaɣ ara ad tnalem yiwen n unẓaḍ n teḥbibt-iw
ad tt-ḥamiɣ s tudert-iw ad tt-ḥebbiɣ ɣer yidmaren-iw wa ad afgeɣ yis-s ɣer tmurt ideg ur ɣ-yettḥasab yiwen ɣef tigawin-nneɣ tamurt i yettbaraken tayri tettḥarab fell-as 
ibedd yelḥa ɣer sdat sakin yuɣal-d s amkan-is
yeqbel s yigemmaḍ n tesleḍt s uzmumeg n usirem
iḥulfa i yiwet n tezmert tameqqrant i ikecmen ɣer tfekka-ines
d tazmert swayes yezmer ad yesseɣli yal yiwen ira ad inal tajeǧǧigt-ines
zrin wussan yufa iman-is akked tmaɛcuqt-is deg tmacint n yiḍ i yettawin ɣer wehran deg lǧib-is tansa n yiwen n umejjay i ixeddmen iɣrayen s tuffra
tadist tewweḍ ɣer ddurt tis semmuset ur ilaq ara ad iɛeṭṭel kter
ṭṭfen imekwan n deffir susmen taɛreq-asen ttxemmimen amek ad yili yimal-nsen
tenna-asen tmeṭṭut n zubir temmeslay d yiwet n tnelmadt i yesseɣlin tadist-ines ɣer umejjay-nni kraḍ n wagguren aya tefka-asen yakk isalen i sen-ilaqen
ulac acu ara aggaden
tamzelt teshel maḍi yernu amejjay yettwassen mliḥ isem-is yeffeɣ tilisa n tmurt ttruḥun-d ɣur-s tlawin seg yal tamurt akken ad d-sseɣlint tadist
d tidet azal n temzelt ɣlay mliḥ maca
racid yessaweḍ ad yejmeɛ idrimen mebla uguren
iḍ-nni n yinig ɣezzif mliḥ yesseɛya-ten
tennekmac
nesira ɣef yiman-is tɣumm aqerruy-is s lximar aqehwi teqmec allen-is teqqim tettxemmim deg twaɣit i yeɣlin fell-as
tettawi-tt tanafa seg lweqt ɣer wayeḍ kra n ddqayeq kan maca imir-n kan ad d-taki s usduqes texleɛ yeffeɣ-itt laɛqel am wakken d yir targit i turga
dɣa ad teckunṭeḍ deg yiɣil n racid ad tɣileḍ d timɣerreqt
racid ur yeṭṭis ara ula yiwet n ddqiqa yewwi-d tafat s wudem
yeswa tabakit n dduxan
yeɛreḍ ad yesɛeddi lweqt s tɣuri maca lbal-is ur thenni ara ur ssawḍen ara yisekkilen iberkanen ad t-jebden ɣur-sen
yecfa racid deg tafrara-nni n tegrest tban-as-d d tucmit d tamdint yesserwalen amdan bexlaf ɣef wayen ttmeslayen fell-as
ageffur ass-iwinaɣen ḥeznen nni yekkat s tinezduɣin d timeqqranin neddrent ddaw n yigenni aberkan i ixennqen lerwaḥ
deg tilawt allen n racid llant ttnadint kan ɣef yisem n uɣlad i yeqseḍ
ma d nasira tɣumm yakk aqerruy-is s lximar teckunṭeḍ deg yiɣil n win ara tt-yawin ɣer lfinga
mi tessawel tefremlit i yisem-is yerfed aqerruy-is s laɛqel yeseqsa s wallen-is kan ɛerqent-as
amejjay yebɣa ad k-iwali
tawwurt teǧǧa-t ad yekcem
mugren-it-id larkul d yisufar-niḍen iqesḥanen
ad yesɛu umejjay-nni ukkuẓet n tmerwin n ireyyes yeqqen nnwaḍer d yiseggasen d acaɛlal imẓerfen ad tɣileḍ d arumi yeqqim deffir n yiwet n tnarit tameqqrant  nasira tuɣ-itt tennekmac deg yiwen n wattag yezgan deg teɣmert tessider i uqerruy-is seg leḥya
iban texdem ugar n tezmert-ines akken ad tɛerri iman-is sdat n urgaz niḍen ɣas d amejjay ad as-d-tefk timessaḍin d uḥeččun-ines akken ad ten-yessames s yifassen-is
tenna-as ur as-yaɛǧib ara lḥal imi tɛerra iman-is sdat n umejjay amer tufa d tamejjayt ara s-yesseɣlin tadist
yenna-as umejjay 
tadist d tamagnut ulac acu tt-yuɣen
yekres yiles n racid ur yufi ara acu ad as-yerr
ikemmel umejjay deg wawal-is 
nesseɣlay tadist ḥala ma nwala liḥala n tyemmat neɣ n llufan tenṭer mliḥ
d acu-ten imeslayen-a  d abeqqa i yečča racid
yugi umejjay ad yexdem tamzelt akken ad yesseɣli tadist n
nasira  d acu ara yexdem ihi  inig-agi irkelli d usirem iɣef yeckunṭeḍ akken ad uɣalen deg taggara xaybin 
amek ara xedmen i tadist asmi ad ifut lawan 
nruḥ-d seg tmanaɣt  neqseḍ-ik-id keččini belxusus  d yiwet n teqcict i tdawiḍ kraḍ n wagguren aya i ɣ-d-yemmeslayen fell-ak
yesneḥneḥ umejjay imuqel racid seddaw n nnwaḍer-is 
ḥemḥem 
ur tezmirem ara ad teǧǧem tadist 
fhem liḥala-nneɣ a mass amejjay nekkni d inelmaden liḥala-nneɣ rqiqet mliḥ
uguren n zzwaǧ am wakken i teẓriḍ teḥwaǧ aṭas n lweqt tilemlekt awway n twaculin tameɣra i yettilin dima deg unebdu 
asmi ad wejdent tiwtilin-agi irkelli ad yelli llufan ilul-d yakan
amek ad tqabel tmeɣbunt tizzernent n twacult-is asmi ara slen terfed uqbel zzwaǧ  ɣef waya i d-nusa ɣur-k seg mebɛid akken ad ɣ-tesmenɛeḍ seg lefḍiḥa ara yeglun s yiqerra-nneɣ
sakin ad nesɛu yakk lweqt akken ad nheggi s laɛqel-nneɣ tameɣra
yirbeḥ yirbeḥ  tewwiḍ yid-k idrimen ilaqen i temzelt
mebla laɛḍil yekker racid s temɣawla yessuffeɣ-d seg lǧib n ubalṭu-ines rrezma n yidrimen yessers-itt sdat n umejjay
tanemmirt-ik a mass tanemmirt-ik a duktur  urǧin ad ttuɣ tajmilt-ik
yejbed umejjay idrimen-nni yerra-ten deg yiwen n leqjer sakin yekker yenna-as 
kkes aɣbel tamzelt ad tettwaxdem mebla akukru i  temddakkelt-ik
nettat ad teqqim ɣur-neɣ armi d rrebɛa n tmeddit
ma kečč d tagnit ad tẓureḍ tamdint n wehran
icebbeh-iyi rebbi i tikkelt tamezwarut ara tt-tẓureḍ
ad k-teɛǧeb mebla ccek
aṭas i yelḥa ddaw n ugeffur ur yumin ara taɛekkemt i ibubb ɣef tuyat-is acḥal n wussan aya ad tettwakkes deg kra n tsaɛtin kan
iḥewwes deg tzeɣwa yeččuren s lɣaci yekcem ɣer  tgennariyin ilan kraḍ n yinnagen yettderdib gar sselɛa yeččuren amkan
yuɣ-d snat n teqraɛtin n laɛṭer yiwet i tmaɛcuqet-is tayeḍ i yiman-is
yekcem ɣer leswaq iɣerfanen yecɣel iman-is s laɛyaḍ-nsen d umussu n usenz d tiɣin i as-yessettun i kra n lweqt kan lehmum-is
yeɣli s ugacur ɣer tirni n yillel i iqublen tamersit itekka ɣef uɣalaḍ yekcem ɣer umaḍal n tirga yelhan
yertaḥ seg yir-targit i t-ihewwjen ussan-a ineggura d tagnit ad yesgunfu ad iḥewwes ɣas deg tirga
yewwi yerra acḥal d abrid deg uṭrutwar n tirni n yillel
iḥulfa i laẓ ineqqer deg yiẓerman-is ixemmem ad yečč asundwič maca ulac acu i yexdem
ad yerǧu alamma teffeɣ nasira sɣur umejjay akken ad ruḥen jmiɛ ɣer usečču ad sfuglen s tuffɣa seg twaɣit anda ɣlin deg-s deg sin
yuɣal ɣer umejjay ɣef tlata n tmeddit
tewwi-t tefremlit-nni tazurant ɣer yiwet n texxamt i d-yezgan deg ṭṭerf ideg teṭṭes nasira akked yiwet n teqcict niḍen
yufa-tt teṭṭes maca yessers kan iman-is ɣef yiri n wusu teldi-d allen-is texleɛ
tessawal-as s yisem-is sakin teṭṭerḍeq d imeṭṭawen
anda telliḍ a racid  aṭas i tɛeṭṭleḍ
uɣeɣ awal n umejjay i yi-d-yennan ad teffɣeḍ ɣef rrebɛa
amejjay d agezzar mačči d amejjay
d agezzar
ih d agezzar d agezzar
teṭṭerḍeq d imeṭṭawen i tikkelt tis snat
yuẓa ɣur-s
racid yeẓẓem-itt ɣer yidmaren-is yenna-as s laɛqel kan 
ur ttaggad ara  kulci yekfa lmusiba ideg neɣli urǧin ad as-nales
nniɣ-ak-d d agezzar yeqreḥ-iyi mliḥ ur ẓriɣ ara acu i yessekcem deg tfekka-inu maca ḥulfaɣ i wallal d aqeḍɛan yettcerriq taɛebbuḍt-iw
ur am-d-fkin ara iɛeqqaren 
ih maca ssikran xfifet mliḥ
lliɣ ttḥulfuɣ u selleɣ maca ur zmireɣ ad mbiwleɣ ula ssuɣat-inu ur d-ffiɣent ara seg yimi-w
d ssikkis mi ara tḥulfuḍ i walbaɛḍ yetturar s tfekka-inek iqerreḥ-ik yernu keččini ulac acu tzemreḍ ad txedmeḍ
tella tettru deffir yal tafyirt
ur yufi ara racid awalen iwulmen akken ad tt-iwessi
iḥebbi-tt kan ɣur-s yesfeḍ imeṭṭawen-is s yiḍuḍan-is
ɣef rrebɛa tusa-d tefremlit tefka-asen taneglamt n yisufar sakin tessuter deg-sen ad ffɣen
s tmara i tbedd
nasiratefcel mačči d kra iḍarren-is kerfen amek ad tqabel tamdint  aṭas n yidammen i tḍegger aṭas n lweqt i as-ilaqen akken ad d-tuɣal am wakken tella
yessɣim-itt deg ddruj n uzaduɣ yebda anadi ɣef wayen ara ččen akken ad d-terr tazmert swayes ad tizmir ad tkemmel tikli
ilaq ad uɣalen ɣer tmanaɣt deg tmacint n yiḍ ara iruḥen ɣef tesɛa n tmeddit
sani ara ruḥen deg sswayeɛ-agi i sen-yegran deg usemmiḍ d ugeffur-agi  tečča tabwaḍt n lyawurt d tɛeqqayt n teffaḥt
s tmara i tbedd tettekka ɣef yiɣil n racid ad telḥu kra n lmitrat wa ad teqqim kra n ddqayeq armi wwḍen ɣer teɣsert n tmacinin
qqimen ɣef yiwen n ukersi ttraǧun
yebɣa ad tt-yawi ɣer yiwen n usečču n ukanaf maca tugi
aṭas n umbiwel yezmer ad yeglu s ssiq
iruḥ s temɣawla yuɣ-d tayaẓiḍt yewwan ɣas akken ur yeḥbis ara aḥawet deg-s ur tečči ara aṭas seg-s
deg taggara hata yewweḍ lawan n yinig
tebda kan tmacint ambiwel teẓẓel tessers aqerruy-is ɣef umessaḍ n racid tewwi-tt tnafa
s ṭṭul n yinig ur iḥerrek ara racid seg umkan-is akken ur tt-yessakay ara
teḥwaǧ ad testaɛfu
tuki-d deg teɣsert n lesnam mi teḥbes tmacint bdan yiminigen ttalin s lḥess d dderz tesseqsa acḥal ssaɛa  yerra-as racid  d lweḥda n ssbeḥ
tenna  ɣef wacḥal ad naweḍ  yerra-as racid  ṭṭes kan inig mazal ɣezzif
taɣuct-is d turkidt yettwakkes seg-s lxuf d ukukru
mi wwḍen ɣer teɣsert n laɣa yekra aṭaksi i tt-yewwin srid ɣer teɣremt n tullas mebla ma yettu tiɣin n yisufar seg yiwet n temsifert
sakin iruḥ ɣer texxamt-is yewwet-itt ɣef yiwen n yidis yeṭṭes yiwen n yiḍ d yiwen n wass s lekmal-is
yenna-d racid urǧin yexdim deg tudert-is inig ifuḥen am win i t-yewwin ɣer wehran
yuɣal ur iḥemmel ara tamdint-agi n wehran acku tesmektay-it-id dima s tedyant n uɣray
yella acu yerẓen gar-as d nasira iwumi iruḥ ucmummeḥ d unecreḥ-ines
udem-is yuɣal d aberkan
tigawin-ines uɣalent ččurent s tzernent
tettemlili d racid tettɣimi yid-s acḥal n tsaɛtin maca tugi ad qqimen weḥd-sen kan
tuɣal tettagi ad truḥ s axxam n yimeddukkal-nsen
yernu yiwen n wass tenna-as-t-id deg wudem-is d tamussni-nsen i d-yeglan s twaɣit i d-yeɣlin ɣef yiqerra-nsen
amer sebren rǧan ciṭuḥ tili ad ɛemren tameɣra tameqqrant am nitni am yimaɛcaq irkelli
tban-d tuzzma ɣef yiles-is tebda tselbiba tessexsar tumert-nsen
maca racid d argaz afeḥli ur tt-yeǧǧi ara
iḥemmel-itt s tidet yexdem iwumi yezmer akken ad tt-ihenni wa ad tt-yessefreḥ
kra n wussan umbaɛd wwḍen-d yimuras n tnasfa n useggas yunag ɣer taddart n nasira iwala baba-s yessuter-d afus-is sɣur-s
imuger-it-id baba-s n nasira s lferḥ ameqqran yenna-as ur yezmir ara ad ibedd deg wudmawen-nsen imi d yelli-s i as-yefkan tansa n uxxam-is anamek n waya teqbel
maca tilemlekt ur tezmir ara ad tili ḥala ma teḥḍer twacult-is wa ad ɣren lfatiḥa
d ayen ibanen am yiṭij d tigi d leɛwayed n medden mi ara fken tullas-nsen
maca racid yesɛa taɛdawt akked baba-s seg wasmi yekker umennuɣ gar-asen ɣef temsalt n tẓallit
baba-s am leɛwayed-is ijemmeɛ arraw-is asmi llan d imeẓyanen deffir-is akken ad ẓallen
racid yeḥbes taẓallit segwasmi yeffeɣ seg uxxam akken ad iɣer
yal tikkelt yettaf-d ifukal yeɛya ur yuɣ ara luḍu ad iẓal umbaɛd weḥd-s
maca yiwet n tikkelt iqubel-it baba-s s tidet 
ẓriɣ tḥebseḍ taẓallit yaxi teẓriḍ win i yettaǧǧan taẓallit ɣur-neɣ yettwaḥsab d amṭurni d akafriw
nekk ur bɣiɣ ara ad yili mmi d akafriw acku taggara-s d anazir ad aɣ-yenǧu rebbi
ɣef waya aql-ik sdat sin n yiberdan  ama ad d-tuɣaleḍ ɣer laɛqel-ik dɣa ad d-tuɣaleḍ ɣer tẓallit am keččini am watmaten-ik neɣ kečč mačči d mmi ur k-ssineɣ ara ternuḍ učči-inu d leḥram fell-ak
racid yerfa ibedd deg wudem n baba-s i yeḥseb d ameqqal
yenna-as lǧennet d unazir d asnulfu n yimdanen ur sɛin ara assaɣ d tidet
baba-s yerfa mliḥ yessaɛseq-it seg uxxam
seg wass-nni ur d-yuɣal racid s axxam n yimawlan-is ḥala snat n tikkal yeqqim deg-sent kra n tsaɛtin kan iqesser deg-sent akked yemma-s d kra seg watmaten-is
deg yal tikkelt tessuter deg-s yemma-s ad yessuter ssmaḥ seg baba-s tuɣ-it yerfa mi as-ffɣen wawalen-nni yernu asumer-ines d aggaz kan iɣil ad yuɣal ɣer laɛqel-is
ur ixemmem ara irkelli ad yeǧǧ axxam i lebda
deg tẓallit-ines yezga ideɛɛu-as s tuɣalin ɣer ubrid amaɣud
amek ad yuɣal s axxam umbaɛd n yiba n ukkuẓ n yiseggasen neɣ ugar mačči d tujjma i ten-yejjem d lemzeyya ad sen-yessuter  ad as-xeḍben tameṭṭut
ad ikellex i uḍeggal-is  ad yawi yid-s kra seg yimeddukkal-is d yiwet n temɣart ara yestaɛemlen iman-is d yemma-s d yiwen n umɣar ara yerren iman-is d baba-s  ugur atan deg racid ur iḥemmel tamaɛmult ur iḥemmel astaɛmel
deg yiwen n wass deg wussan n rebbi yeṭṭef lkar yuɣal ɣer taddart-is
tmuger-it-id yemma-s s yimeṭṭawen d tuzzma
seddis n wagguren mi yewweḍ baba-s laɛfu n
rebbi yemmut umbaɛd aṭṭan i t-yuɣen kra n ledwar
ulac acu i as-nnan acku baba-s yugi maḍi yenna-asen urǧin ad yessuref i win ad t-ixebbren la deg ddunit wala deg laxert
yefren umelɛun abrid-is ad iḍebber aqerruy-is ihi
ṭṭaɛa n yimawlan d lferḍ deg usɣan-nneɣ yeṭṭef amkan amezwaru deg lfuruḍ imeqqranen n lmumen
ɣef waya i yugi i watmaten-ik ad k-id-xebbren s waṭṭan-is neɣ s tmettant-ines
tessuter deg-s yemma-s ad yeqqim armi d azekka akken ad iẓur aẓekka-ines
yestaɛref racid ur yeḥzin ara i tmettant n baba-s
ur iḥulfa ara yella kra n wassaɣ yelhan gar-asen
assaɣ i ten-yezdin seg temẓi d win n mass d wakli-ines
baba-s yettamer racid yettaɣ awal
ur yecfi ara i yiwet n tikkelt deg tudert-is ideg yemmeslay-as-d s leḥnana
tisunḍiwin aɛeggeḍ tuzzma d wigi kan i yessen arraw-is yessefk fell-asen ad as-aɣen awal terwi teberwi ɣef win ara t-iɛassen
aɛekkaz i win yeffɣen abrid d netta d mass ameqqran ur iqebbel ara win ara ibedden deg wudem-is
yemma-s n racid d tameɣbunt ur tesɛi rray wala awal acḥal d abrid i as-yefka ibeqqayen sdat n tarwa-s acku taɛreḍ ad as-d-terr awal
yemma-s lyaqut twala laɛǧeb yesserwa-as urgaz-is amesbaṭli tameḥqranit
ur tettaf tilelli-ines ḥala deg leɣyab-is
ad yekcem kan ad d-tuɣal d azɣuɣ amedlul tettazzal am uqziḥ akken ad as-d-taɣ awal ɣef wayen yessutur
iruḥ ad iẓur aẓekka n baba-s am wakken i as-tessuter yemma-s maca ur yeḍlib deg-s ssmaḥ am wakken i as-tenna
yenna-as ur t-yeḍlim ara
taẓallit d tamsalt i yi-yaɛnan gar-i d rebbi
d baba-s i t-yesɛesqen seg uxxam
ur yebɣi ara racid ad t-yennaɣ i tikkelt tis snat ɣef waya ur d-yuɣal ara
deg tirzi-nni yeqqim d yemma-s kraḍ n wuḍan yemmeslay yid-s ɣef lumur n twacult d ddunit uqbel ad tt-ixebber s temsalt n tilemlekt n yiwet n teqcict i yessen deg tesdawit
tefreḥ yemma-s s tekti maca tecreḍ fell-as alamma iɛedda useggas akken ad yaɛmer wurar
yerra assaɣ d yimawlan-is yuɣal irezzu ɣur-sen seg tallit ɣer tayeḍ ulac win i as-yemmeslayen ɣef temsalt n tẓallit
akka zrin wussan yewwi racid yemma-s d kra seg watmaten-is d yessetma-s ad as-xeḍben taqcict-nni
ddurt umbaɛd yuɣal akked sin seg yimeddukkal-is d inigan i usekles n warra n zzwaǧ deg tɣiwant n yiḍulan-is akken ad yessuffeɣ tadlist n twacult wa ad yenjer abrid n tlelli-ines akked tmaɛcuqet-is tamezwarut d tneggarut
yettu racid ussan-nni n lmerta
yebna d nasira yiwen n lɛecc ibedd ɣef tumert
maca tiwuɣa ḍefrent ɣer taggara n ddunit-is
teqqim tadyant n uɣray teffer deg warukan n
nasira teṭṭerḍeq ɣer berra asmi tuḍen s waṭṭan n ukunsir n yidmaren
ddunit-is tenneqlab tuɣal-as-d d ddnub iɣef ilaq ad tettuḥaseb deg ddunit uqbel laxert dɣa tekcem s amaḍal n usɣan tezga tettezzem deg yiman-is d ayen i yesxerben assaɣ n tayri i tedder d racid
racid ur iḥemmel ara ad ibuḥ s lehmum-is ḥala ma neqqim weḥd-neɣ kan
mi ara nili deg terbaɛt akked yimeddukkal yettmeslay kan ɣef temsal n tsertit tussna d yiwenniten ɣef wayen yeɣra deg yidlisen d yiɣmisen neɣ ayen iwala deg tiliẓri neɣ ayen yesla deg rradyu
mačči am rrabiɛ amedyaz mi ara nemmeslay kan ɣef tezmert ad yessekcem tameṭṭut-is d tamejjayt n tuɣmas txeddem i yiman-is neɣ ɛebdella yal tikkelt ideg nebder deg-s awal n uɣerbaz d uselmad ad yessidef tameṭṭut-is yernu ayen i d-tenna d tidet d tanemhalt n uɣerbaz
ma d caɛban yenɣa-aɣ s yisalan n mmi-s i ixedmen d ajenyur deg yiwet n tnaremt n unadi deg fransa
deg tgannit-nni taɣezzfant nasira mazal-itt teẓẓel lemwas n umejjay nnig n uqerruy-is iserreḥ racid i wallus n lehmum-is ladɣa wid yerzan amgired-ines d tmeṭṭut-is
tuɣalin n tmeṭṭut-iw ɣer usɣan d uẓam-ines n waggur n remḍan
tewwi-d ssebba s tmidawin-ines deg tesnawit ttuẓument irkelli ma faqent-as ur tettuẓum ara ad tt-muqlent s yir tiṭ
wagi irkelli yebda-d asmi d-tban tumant n useḥjeb ɣer tlawin i d-wwin watmaten inselmen yefrurxen deg yiɣerbazen
ur telsi ara lḥiǧab maca tebda s laɛqel teṭṭeggir yakk iselsa imiranen tuɣal tettɣummu tafekka-ines irekelli anagar aqerruy-is
deg wussan isemmaḍen tettezzi i uqerrruy-is d temgerḍt-is yiwen n lximar
wwḍen wat-yiččumar ɣer daxel n tneɣriyin
ur yessetḥi ara yiwen n unelmad seg wat-yiččumar-agi yewweḍ armi i tt-yesseqsa ayɣer ur tettlusu ara lḥiǧab am tlawin niḍen n yinselmen
amer ur as-d-terri ara s leqseḥ ur tɛeggeḍ ara fell-as tenna-as amer ad ikemmel deg ubrid-a ad yessekcem iman-is deg tudert-is ad teccetki yis-s ɣer unemhal tili ur neẓri ara acu ara yexdem
am wakken teẓriḍ a si ɛebdelqader ur ttamneɣ ara s rebbi wala s usɣan n yinselmen ur tẓummuɣ ur tẓallaɣ
ɣas akken ur as-nniɣ ara ur ttuẓum ara cerḍeɣ-as kan yiwen n ccerḍt  ad iyi-teǧǧ ad ččeɣ ur selleɣ ara i yisemtar-ines akken ad uɣaleɣ s abrid n usɣan
s tidet urǧin sugneɣ ad tbeddel tikli i tudert-is ad d-taɣ abrid niḍen
nekk ɣileɣ tumen mliḥ s tikta timiranin acku urǧin i yi-d-temmeslay fell-asent
ad k-d-iniɣ tidet tella tettheggi-yi imekli deg waggur n remḍan mebla ma yuli-as awal
nekk daɣen seg tama-w xedmeɣ iwumi zemreɣ akken ad sisehleɣ uẓam-ines
ur as-ssawaleɣ ara akken ad teṭṭes yid-i deg uzal am wakken xeddmeɣ deg wagguren niḍen
walaɣ tamsalt-a d tamagnut ur i yi-taɛni ara taɛna-tt kan nettat
maca ur i yi-yaɛǧib ara lḥal mi tt-walaɣ tettlussu lḥiǧab wa ad theggi iman-is i tẓalit dɣa mmektaɣ-d temẓi-inu d uqhar n baba
maca ɣas akkenni ur zmireɣ ara ad beddeɣ deg wudem-is neɣ ad as-iniɣ amek i ilaq ad telḥu
ur ḥemmleɣ ara iqehharen ɣef waya urǧin sugneɣ iman-iw ad d-yas wass ad lseɣ aqendur-nsen wa ad ṭṭfeɣ gar yifassen-iw ajelkaḍ swayes ad wwteɣ wiyaḍ
tikkelt-a mmeslayeɣ yid-s ɣef temsalt-a
nniɣ-as taẓallit d ddaɛwat i yakucen i zedɣen igenwan d lɛadat tiqburin yesnulfa-ten umdan asmi yella d uḍɛif d ljahel ulac acu yessen
ass-a amdan yewweḍ ɣer yigenni maca ur yufi iyakucen ur yufi igenwan wala amkan n lǧennet d unazir ini-yi-d ihi iwumi tettẓallaḍ iwumi tettuẓumeḍ  amer yella
rebbi s tidet tili tɣaḍ-it liḥala n talsa tili isellek lmumnin tuget-nsen d inselmen seg lḥif d lbaṭel
yuruba tuɣal d lǧennet s lfeḍl n uxeddim n umdan mačči s ddaɛwat i
rebbi acku rran asɣan deg ṭṭerf seg tallit n tafat
ma d nekkni mazal ur neffiɣ ara seg tallit n ṭṭlam nessugun
rebbi-agi d amɣar azemni yeṭṭef gar yifassen-is tisura n i lǧennet d unazir tezzi-as-d taredsa n lmalaykat yesseklasen deg yizmamen imeqqranen adduden d yimeslayen n yal amdan yeddren deg umaḍal
nettidir deg yiwet n tmetti tameqqalt selḥayen-tt timucuha leǧhel d lḥif
imdanen ckunṭeḍen deg tẓallit am usirem aneggaru ara sen-yeldin tiwwura n tudert niḍen ama tagi ideg ttidiren tezzi-asen s waɛrur
am wakken i d-yeqqar umddakkel-nneɣ amedyaz mazal-iten deg yiswiren addayen
zzin-as-d i umrar n rebbi ckunṭuḍen deg-s ttganin melmi ad ten-yawi ɣer lǧennet i sen-yeṛgem
ayen i yi-yeswehmen tameṭṭut-iw ulac acu i yi-d-tenna
tesla-iyi deg tsusmi sakin tekker ad tkemmel leqdic-ines
teẓra reffuɣ s sshala ɣef waya tugi ad i yi-tluɛej s umeslay
acḥal d abrid i nennuɣ ɣef kra n temsal icudden ɣer uxxam mebla lmaɛna ur ttfiqiɣ ara armi ufiɣ iman-iw ttɛeggiḍeɣ
dɣa ad tessusem ad tejbed iman-is
maca din-din ad uɣaleɣ ɣer laɛqel-iw ad as-ssutreɣ ssmaḥ ɣef wayen xedmeɣ
iwakken ad as-sbegneɣ nniya-inu yesfan ad azzleɣ ad as-d-aɣeɣ asefk
imennuɣen-nneɣ d tiɛejjajin d tifessasin ur ttaṭṭafent ara ugar n kra n tsaɛtin
maca tuɣal seg wass ɣer wayeḍ tjebbed iman-is fell-i tɛezzel iman-is
ameslay gar-aneɣ yuɣal itezzi-d kan ɣef temsal n uxxam d warraw-nneɣ
nettat ur nessin deg tutlayt taɛrabt ḥala isekkilen tuɣal tettawi-d idlisen iwraɣen ara tɣer
ɣas akken urǧin i yi-d-tenna d acu i teqqar ccil n yiseqsiyen-inu
yiwet n tikkelt tenna-iyi-d   d tagi d lumur n usɣan keččini ur tettamneḍ ara s temsal-agi
d acu d lfayda ma teẓriḍ d acu i qqareɣ ihi   teẓdeq ur teɣliḍ ara d acu lfayda ara afeɣ deg tmussni i d-yusan seg tallit talemmast  akken ad tt-namreɣ wa ad tt-rreɣ ɣer ubrid-iw  hatta ass-a tuḍen s waṭṭan-a amcum ad as-tiniḍ tettkacaf teẓra ad tehlek dɣa tezwar i wallalen-a imakunen imi teẓra tamejjayt d tussna ulac acu ad as-fell-as zgiɣ d xedment
ɣef waya imeṭṭawen ɣef liḥala-inu d wayen i yi-yuɣen
tayri d lemɛacra-nneɣ ṭṭfent kraḍet n tmerwin n yiseggasen ɣlint deg kra n lweqt kan ad as-tiniḍ d iɣrem n yijdi mebla ma nla gar yifassen-nneɣ tifrat swayes nezmer ad t-nessemneɛ seg uɣelluy deg wanu lqayen ur nesɛi lqaɛ 
awezlu neɣ tamsalt n umerḥum n mmi-k yekres a si
racid
racid yeqqim tama-w metwal n yiwet n tnarit tahrawant
yessers ukumisar n temsulta si aḥmed akaram i yeṭṭef gar yifassen imuqel mliḥ deg wallen n baba-s n uqcic iwumi yeffeɣ laɛqel
ḥusseɣ tella lḥaǧa ur nessefraḥ ara deg temsalt-a
ur as-ssawlen ara i racid benɣusa akken ad mmeslayen yid-s kan
aqcic meskin yemmut atan tura ddaw n tmedlin d acu i tebɣa temsulta ɣer baba-s  ikemmel ukumisar lehdur-is s yiwet n taɣect tazurant 
sbegnen-d yisestanen-nneɣ belli tameẓyant i nufa deg ufus n mmi-k d ayla n umsaltu yettwanɣan ukkuẓ n wagguren aya deg ssuq n  miksik 
d wagi d ifri n yizerman ihi  anwa ad ɣ-yessuffɣen seg-s 
yenna-d racid 
nniɣ-ak-d iḍelli iqjan-a nɣan-t ǧǧan tameẓyant gar yifassen-is baɛmada
tura neẓra ssebba
ad sefḍen timenɣiwt n umsaltu deg-s u nutni ad d-ffɣen seg-s am unẓaḍ seg urukti
lexbar  aṭas i d-temmeslay-d
ugur atan deg umejjay iwalan tafekka
ɣur-s tamettant-ines teqreb ɣer tinɣi n yiman wala ɣer tiyita sɣur walbaɛḍ niḍen
tettemcabi ɣer temsalt n umsaltu-nni yenɣan iman-is ɣur-neɣ acḥal n wagguren aya
ahat fell-as yewweḍ-iken tɣamsa tra ad tessebgen i lɛamma tiderwect d tselbi yuɣen tamsulta seg wasmi yebda umennuɣ akked yirebraben d wayen i t-iḍefren seg uṭaxer seg uxeddim d tenɣiman
yerra-as-d racid s wurfan i d-ibanen deg tergagayt n yiḍuḍan-is 
nekk ur umineɣ ara s temsalt-a n tenɣiman  mmi ur yenɣi ara iman-is
teɣli-d tsusmi gar-aneɣ
yenna ukumisar 
irebraben ḥwaǧen mliḥ leslaḥ
ad snegren lɛerc s lekmal-is ɣef derra n yiwet n tmekḥelt n ssyada
amek ad ǧǧen tameẓyant tatumatikt seg nnuɛ aneggaru yelhan ternuḍ teččur s tersasin  nekkni nettwali belli mmi-k d timenɣiwt i yenɣa iman-is
maca urɛad ur neẓri ara ssebba
mi ara nwali iselsa-ines yettbin-d d win yettekkan deg trebbuyaɛ tinselmin
ssawleɣ-ak-d akken ad iyi-temmeslayeḍ ɣef mmi-k
d acu tessneḍ fell-as  ɣef wassaɣen-ines  ɣef yimeddukkal-is  ad nceggeɛ tarbaɛt n yimsulta ad tqelleb deg leḥwayej-is ahat yeǧǧa kra n warraten ara ɣ-yalen deg tsestant-nneɣ
yessider racid i uqerruy-is yenna-d ddaw n teɣmest 
 d ahdum d tawaɣit  ɣer taggara n laɛmer-iw ad yuɣal mmi d arebrab  axxam-iw d aglat n yirebraben

skecmeɣ iman-iw nniɣ-asen 
mačči d wagi i d-nenna
nebɣa ad nwali amek i tewweḍ tmeẓyant n umsaltu yettwanɣan ɣer mmi-k  nessutur deg-k ad aɣ-tɛiwneḍ
a si aḥmed ssneɣ tawacult n racid aṭas n yiseggasen aya ur cukkeɣ ara tesɛa assaɣ d yineḍliben-agi
anwa i yerdan tawacult s lḥaǧa  nettmeslay kan ɣef mmi-tsen yemmuten yewwḍen laɛfu n rebbi
ayen nebɣa d isallen ara ɣ-yessawḍen ɣer wid yenɣan amsaltu
ayen yaɛnan tameẓyant d lxiḍ ayiwan i nla imir-a
yallah a si racid mmeslay-d
umbaɛd n tsusmi taẓayant yenna-d ukumisar 
hder-iyi-d ɣef yimeddukkal n mmi-k  bɣiɣ ad d-iniɣ imeddukkal-is seg wat-yiččumar
imeddukkal at-yiččumar  ur ten-ssineɣ ur bɣiɣ ad ten-issineɣ
s laɛqel kan xemmem ciṭuḥ  ahat
yessider racid i uqerruy-is ixemmem kra n tsanin 
ah d tidet yella yiwen d awezzlan d imsibrek mliḥ yelsa tacacit d ubalṭu nnig n uqendur
walaɣ-t yiwen n ubrid ibedd sdat n tewwurt n uɣerbaz alemmas
ad tili ssaɛa qrib d setta n tmeddit
seqsaɣ-t acu yeḥwaǧ
yenna-yi-d yettraǧu deg nabil
imuqel-iyi-d ddaw n tiṭ am wakken tella lḥaǧa deg wul-is
tameddit-nni seqsaɣ mmi fell-as
yenna-yi-d  d ameddakkel-iw
nniɣ-as  yeqqar yid-k deg tesdawit  yenna-yi-d  ulac acu i k-yaɛnan d ameddekkel-iw d aya 
melmi teḍra temlilit-agi 
ɣur-s kra n wagguren kan
twalaḍ-t umbaɛd 
ala  maca yiwet n tikkelt mi d-uɣaleɣ s axxam tameddit tenna-yi-d tmeṭṭut-iw ad iɣib nabil kra n wussan seg uxxam
mi tt-seqsaɣ ɣef ssebba tenna-yi-d iruḥ d yasin ad iẓur jidda-s seg yemma-s deg temnaḍt n
tubiret
dɣa seqsaɣ-t ɣef yasin-agi
tenna-d  akeḥluc-nni i d-yettassen ɣur-s tikwal ad iqelleb fell-as
nniɣ  tessneḍ-t 
tenna  walaɣ-t yiwet n tikket d nabil
tuɣ-it yettraǧu-t deg umraḥ n uɣerbaz mi d-heggaɣ yiwen n yimekli yelhan nniɣ-as ad as-yessiwel ad yefter ɣur-neɣ
yuli-d yečča imekli d nabil deg tnawalt
d netta i as-d-yettawin idlisen n usɣan
yettbin-d d ukyis d uḥdiq
tameṭṭut-iw tameskint tettwaxdeɛ s sshala tettak aṭas n wazal i ssifa n berra
seg wasmi tebda taẓallit ma twala albaɛḍ yelsa aqendur d tcacit yettuɣal deg wallen-is d agellid
ur teẓri ara ula d ccwaṭen ifuḥen ttasen-d s talɣa n lmalayek
anamek n wawalen-ik ilaq ad nawi imeslayen-ik d wid n tmeṭṭut-ik daɣen
ad ɣ-ɛiwnen deg tsestant-nneɣ
ahat maca nekk ilaq ad ẓreɣ amek i yemmut mmi
tameddit-nni yugi racid ad yuɣal s axxam
nniɣ-as ad nruḥ ad neṭṭef tiɣmert deg yiwet n tberna ideg ulac win i ɣ-yessnen
maca yugi daɣen
yessuter deg-i ur ḥebbseɣ ara tikli
yeṭṭef-aɣ ṭṭlam nekkni mazal-aɣ deg ubrid arurdan yettawin ɣer unafag
ṭumubilat qlilet tisergal n temsulta ṭṭuqtent
nuɣal seg ubrid n yillel
acḥal i cebḥen yiberdan n tmanaɣt deg yiḍ ma yilin d ilmawen  tiftilin ttmecbariqqent ṭumubil tettecrurud s laɛqel am wakken d afug i tettafeg deg walun
deg tazwara yessusem racid ad as-tiniḍ tafat tettara algam i yiles-is akked talast i ccfawat-ines
mi d-yeɣli yiḍ iɣumm ṭṭlam igli tettwakkes tyersi i yiles-is yuɣal ɣer umeslay
 ah a nabil terẓiḍ-iyi deg temɣer-inu nekk i k-iḥesben d asalel-inu asmi ara grarben yis-i wussan
telliḍ dima d aqcic d imsetḥi ur tessuguteḍ ara awal bexlaf uletma-k tameqqrant i iheddren aṭas tin i yettalsen i tudert-is s yifetusen
meqqret fell-ak s ukkuẓ n yiseggasen tbedd ɣur-k asmi meẓẓiyeḍ armi i k-tessenteḍ kra n tigawin n tullas
ur tettnaɣeḍ d warrac n uɣerbaz wala d warraw n lǧiran
d aqcic uḥdiq d anelmad uḥric deg leqraya-inek
tezgiḍ d amezwaru deg yikayaden  almi d anebdu-nni amcum
temmut yemma tameɣbunt nruḥ ad neḥḍer i tenṭelt-ines dihin deg taddart n ulad-musa
ǧǧiɣ-k ɣer laɛmum-ik akken ad tesɛediḍ ayen i d-yegran deg yimuras
d nitni i yebɣan ula d kečč tebɣiḍ ad teqqimeḍ
ayɣer i qebleɣ  maca nniɣ-as d tagnit ad tissineḍ tawacult-ik d tudert n tudrin
ad taẓleḍ ciṭuḥ deg lexlawi deg yisaffen  ad tuɣaleḍ d argaz
ɣelḍeɣ
ttuɣ maḍi leɛwayed-nni tiqburin mebla lmeɛna nniɣ-as ruḥent d bab-nsent
maca ur rriɣ ara tidmi i wayen iḍerrun sdat-i yernu ḥareɣ ad uɣaleɣ ɣer uxxam ɣef waya ur walaɣ ara timerna n yiqendyar ticaciyin d yiččumar yeččuren d aɣebbar n wid i ḥeḍren i tenṭelt
tisneslemt tuɣ yal amkan deg taddart tennerna ɣef zik
ǧǧiɣ-k deg yirebbi n yiḍiɛi uɣaleɣ s axxam-iw ad kemmleɣ taɣuri n yidlisen n tfelsuft d uɣmis timetti-inu tbeddel irkelli nekk lhiɣ kan s wayen i yi-yettassen seg utaram s nnfaq ɣef leɛwayed tiqburin n tmetti am tlelli n tmeṭṭut tiǧǧin n yirgazen d tlawin zzwaǧ s laɛqed uɣalen ttidiren jmiɛ mebla ma zewǧen
tilelli n usɣan tewweḍ armi sbedden tiddukla n wid ur nettamnen ara s rebbi d tdukkliwin n yisɣanen imaynuten am  isiyuntulijiyen  d tarwa n yiṭij d wiyaḍ
zzwaǧ gar tlawin kan d yirgazen kan
yal tanezzayt ttwaliɣ imaṭṭafen n tilibizyu n fransa akken ad ẓreɣ timetti-nni taneflit i leḥḥun ɣer lǧennet yellan deg lqaɛa  dderɣleɣ ur walaɣ ara ayen iḍerrun sdat-i am tuɣalin s yiɣil ɣer tudert n zik ɣer tmettiwin n tazwara n umezruy
imezdaɣ n timettiwin-agi ttraǧun kan ayen ad sen-yeɣlin seg yigenni seg tmucuha d twuɣa timaganin d yihellilen imazdayen i usuter seg yigenni ad sen-yefk ureɣ d uẓref yernu akal-nsen d wayen yellan ddaw-as yeččur s lxir nrekkeḍ-it s yiḍarren n yiderɣalen ddeɣlen wa ad nkemmel abrid-nneɣ ad tɣileḍ ulac ayen yellan
ǧǧan medden tayerza n wakal kecmen ɣer leǧwameɛ ssuturen deg yigenni ssbeḥ tameddit ad sen-yefk aɣrum d waman
yiwen n wass yefka-asen yiwen n uylel annect ilat  walan isem n allah yettafeg deg yigenwan
d tiderwect yessefqaɛen tessegrareb imdanen deg yiwen n wanu mebla lqaɛ
imi ur d-tusi ara lǧennet-nni i ctaqen refden lesyuf ad myigzamen yiqerra saɣen times deg wayen yegra seg yigran d tzeɣwa
seg lǧennet neɣli deg unazir ulac aɣref yeddren taluft-a uqbel-nneɣ yernu ur cukkeɣ ara ad yili uɣref niḍen ad tt-yidir umbaɛd-nneɣ
akka a mmi skecmen-k ɣer wanu n waylellen tuɣaleḍ-asen d asegdel d tnassabt mgal baba-k u ɣer taggara mgal iman-ik
ula d nekk tuɣ-iyi deg wanu n tmucuha timeqqranin asmi umneɣ nettemcabi ɣer yiɣerfan n yuruba
umneɣ nezmer ad nebnu lǧennet nnig n tmurt-nneɣ tahuskayt
ladɣa asmi ɣlint tkubbaniyin n ddula tanemlayt akked tsertit n useɛreb n uselmed s yisem n umennuɣ mgal ayen d-tessegra temharsa wa ad nuɣal ɣer yiẓuran-nneɣ
aseɛreb yezzuɣur dima yid-s tineslemt
timettiwin tiɛrabin niḍen sɛant agadir asnaktan deg yidles-nsent aɛrab am wakken tiwaculin-nsent lant llsas iseḥḥan deg usɣan ɣef waya arraw-nsen ur sen-tteffɣen ara afus s sshala
ɣur-neɣ tamharsa thudd lsas n yidles aɛrab d lfiqh n usɣan ineslem
ffɣent twaculin seg ṭṭlam n temharsa maca ur ffiɣent ara seg lǧehl ur ssinent ad arunt wala ad ɣrent
tuɣalin ɣer taɛrabt d tneslemt teḍra s lḥir
dɣa uɣalen medden ttwalin yal asekkil aɛrab d uɣris uɣalen daɣen ttamnen s yal ddiɛaya yelsan taɛmamt d uqendur i sen-d-yusan seg tmura n usammer aɛrab mebla ma walan nniya-s ma tesfa neɣ xaṭi
deg tallit-nni n usgunfu amagday i iḍefren timesbaniyin n wurfan n tuber tuɣal yal tama tettsuɣu s tidet-ines
maca tidet tayiwant i izemren i ujbad n yiwen i iɣerqen deg waluḍ d tamkarra
ckunṭuḍen yimdanen ɣer temkarra n yiderwicen uɣalen irkelli ttmuqulen ɣer yigenni
maca igenni yeqqim d aggugam
dɣa yeḍra-d wayen iɣef nebna
yeḍra-d wayen ur nlaq ara ad yeḍru
ayen yeḍran ɣur-neɣ ulac aɣref i t-yeddren
rǧiɣ ass n tuɣalin-inek s tumert tameqqrant
nniɣ-as tura ad iyi-yeḥku ɣef taddart n temẓi-inu d yiberdan-is yeččuren s uɣebbar d rrwayeḥ n yisaffen-ines d yimɣan-is
maca tuɣaleḍ-iyi-d d uḥzin terriḍ kulci daxel n wul-ik ad tɣileḍ d ajenniw i yukren rruḥ-ik
allen-ik zgant rewwlent fell-i iles-ik yuɣal d amecḥaḥ ur ineṭṭeq ara s yiwen n wawal alamma tcarweḍ-tt merriɣet
acu yeḍran 
teqqimeḍ yid-neɣ kra n ddqayeq tessuffɣeḍ sakin seg tbalizt-inek tameẓyant tasejjedt dɣa tkecmeḍ taxxamt-ik ad tẓalleḍ
acu xedmen i wallaɣ-ik ameẓyan  ǧǧiɣ-k d imnecreḥ tuɣaleḍ-iyi-d d amɣar
slemden-ak aqrur taẓallit
tuɣaleḍ tettẓallaḍ yal ass
mmeslayeɣ yid-k ɣef temsalt-agi maca yemma-k tewwet-iyi s yifukal-inu
taẓallit d tiferni tamsismant terza bab-is kan
imi lǧameɛ ur yebɛid ara ɣef uxxam tezgiḍ deg-s ssbeḥ tameddit
ur cliɛeɣ ara ussan-nni acku tuɣ-iyi d amaswaḍ zgiɣ berra n uxxam
ṭṭfeɣ kraḍet n lwilayat baɛdit irkelli yernu xeddmeɣ iwumi zemreɣ akken ad waliɣ yakk iɣerbazen-is deg usemmiḍ neɣ deg uzɣal deg uzaɣar neɣ deg udrar
mebla ṭumubil ttaṭṭafeɣ lkar d tmacint gganeɣ deg usagan n yinelmaden
d tawuri-inu xedmeɣ-tt seg wul-iw
ǧǧiɣ-k i yizerman ɛerken-k am wakken bɣan rran-k d lbumba swayes ad wwten imsulta
lḥaǧa tamezwarut i ibeddlen deg-k d iselsa-inek d uččamar i tugiḍ ad tseṭṭleḍ
igemmaḍ-inek iɣurbizen deg ukraḍyur amezwaru d tawaɣit
tesɛeddayeḍ akud-inek s lekmal-is deg lǧameɛ
tettakiḍ mi ara d-yedden ladan amezwaru n lefjer akken ad truḥeḍ ɣer ljameɛ sakin ɣer tesnawit
tameddit twalaḍ
deg yiseggasen yezrin tettuɣaleḍ s axxam umbaɛd tikwal tettɛeṭṭileḍ mliḥ berra n uxxam
mi ara k-seqsiɣ ɣef ssebba n ugellel anagar yiwet n lliɣ d yimeddukkal-iw deg lǧameɛ
zzmeɣ-k acḥal n tikkal sfehmeɣ-ak lfayda n leqraya d wazal n unefḍis swayes ad teččeḍ aɣrum d azedgan
ɣas akken tulseḍ i useggas-inek
tesseɣtaḍ igulen-inek maca ugur ur yelli ara deg leqraya
amdan yezmer ad yidir s lḥerfa n uzebbal neɣ d aḥemmal deg leswaq
urǧin ad ttuɣ tasebḥit-nni ideg nennuɣ deg-s s tidet
ass-nni d ass amezwaru n waggur n remḍan
mi iyi-twalaḍ deg tnawalt tesseɣ lqehwa-inu tɛeggḍeḍ lxelɛa tban-d ɣef wudem-ik ad as-tiniḍ d aɛefrit bu-sin n wacciwen tuɣ-ik tettesseḍ yid-i lqehwa mebla ugur
tenniḍ   atmaten-ik irkelli ttẓummun ttẓallen nella nettemlili irkelli deg yiwen n ssef akken ad nẓal deg tarbaɛt
nella s tidet d tawacult 
tessusmeḍ ciṭuḥ tenniḍ sakin   ayɣer ur tessutureḍ ara ssmaḥ deg sidi rebbi deg wass-agi amezwaru n waggur n remḍan ad tessucfeḍ wa ad truḥeḍ ɣer lǧameɛ ad tẓalleḍ am keččini am yinselmen irkelli  
akka i yuɣal mmi i ssekreɣ seg temẓi-s ɣef tikta n tafat d tlelli seg tikta timakunin  yenneqlab fell-i yuɣal yettak-iyi-d timsirin umbaɛd mi yeqqim kra n wussan deg yiwet n taddart i d-yezgan deg lqern n ddunit mazal-itt ar tura tettiddir deg lǧhel d lḥif deg tallit n tmucuha
ɛeggḍeɣ fell-ak nniɣ-ak urǧin ad talseḍ i nnhayat-a tungifin
lḥaǧa tamezwarut i txedmeḍ tḥebseḍ učči yid-i
tuɣaleḍ tettraǧuḍ-aɣ alamma neffeɣ seg tnawalt akken ad teqqimeḍ weḥd-k
tezgiḍ berra n uxxam
anda tettiliḍ 
deg lǧameɛ d yimeddukkal-iw
axxam-ik d twacult-ik tamaynut
ma d axxam-nneɣ yuɣal d asagan d asensu i yiḍes kan
ssawaleɣ-ak-d tikwal sɣamayeɣ-k tama-w dɣa ad k-d-mmeslayeɣ ɣef tudert tidmi taɣerma tamirant d umezruy
tettaraḍ iman-ik tettḥessiseḍ kra n lweqt sakin tettafeḍ ifukal s wallus n temsirin-inek dɣa ad tekreḍ ad iyi-teǧǧeḍ weḥd-i
tennerna tiṭṭurfa-inek segmi tkecmeḍ ɣer tesdawit
deg tallit-nneɣ tella tesdawit d afiken i tmussni d wallaɣ d tikta n tafat ass-agi tuɣal d ifri i tiṭṭurfa lǧehl d tmucuha tiqburin mebla n lmeɛna
deg tlemmast n useggas amezwaru asmi tkecmeḍ fell-aneɣ s uqendur n afɣanistan d tamart n uqelwac walaɣ-k mliḥ ur umineɣ ara acu ttwaliɣ sdat-i nniɣ-ak   d acu-t ukarnafal-agi   tenniḍ s zzux   wagi d aselsu ineslem 
nniɣ-ak  wagi mačči d aselsu n yinselmen d aselsu amensay n yifɣaniyen
yernu acḥal i nebɛed ɣef tmurt n yifɣaniyen
inselmen mzerbɛen deg umaḍal yal tamurt tesɛa aselsu-ines amensay
ulac aselsu iwumi nessawal ineslem maca yella uselsu axaliǧi irani amalizi abakistani amerrakci  tmuqleḍ-iyi s yir tamuɣli tekkreḍ truḥeḍ ɣer texxamt-ik terriḍ tasurt i tewwurt tesfehmeḍ-aɣ-d dayen tmedleḍ yakk tiwwura n uskasi
d acu xedmeɣ akken ad yennerni deg wul-ik ddɣel-agi i walaɣ ass-nni deg wallen-ik  ddɣel mgal-iw mgal iman-ik ddɣel i k-yessawḍen ad terreḍ talast i tudert-ik
ɣelqen fell-ak yakk tiwwura n tudert armi tt-tkerheḍ  seg wansi i i k-tt-id-yefkan  d-tewwiḍ tameẓyant-nni  anwa seg
tuɣaleḍ d aneḍlib mebla ul kečč i yellan d imsetḥi  ah tuttriwin war qrib ad yeṭṭerḍeq uqerruy-iw tiririyin

yezga racid itezzem iman-is ur yessaweḍ ara ad yessemneɛ mmi-s seg uɣelluy deg yifri n tiṭṭurfa
d baba-s yessefk fell-as ihi ad ibedd tama-s ad yefhem ssebba n uneqleb n mmi-s ad yeskasi yid-s mebla tiṭṭurfa d uɛeggeḍ mebla lmeɛna
yufa iman-is yettalles i wayen ixeddem baba-s zik
baba-s yella d uqsiḥ yeqqur am yicekran yellan deg yidurar yezzin i taddart n ulad
mussa
ur yessin ara abrid i tleqaqin i yesserwas ɣer tmeṭṭut
d ul n tmeṭṭut i yettelqiqen yettiḍɛif yettaǧǧa seg lḥeqq-is
dɣa yexser mmi-s i lebda
yemmut mebla ma iwala-t tikkelt niḍen
iban yeḥzen mliḥ ɣer taggara n ddunit-is
yezzem mliḥ iman-is ɣef wayen yexdem d mmi-s am wakken ixeddem ass-a racid
tasa n yibabaten qessiḥet mliḥ yewɛer ad yessexsi walbaɛḍ times-ines ɣas ma ibabaten ɣur-neɣ ur ttqirrin ara s wayen yellan deg wulawen-nsen
ttwalin-t d aḍɛaf d asenɣes seg truggza-nsen
yewɛer ɣef baba-s ad yejbed taqejjirt ɣer deffir
amer yexdem-itt tili yessenɣes seg lhiba-ines ɣur-s netta s timmad-is uqbel ma tenɣes lqima-ines deg wallen n warraw-is d tmeṭṭut-is
maca limmer yuɣ racid awal n yemma-s iruḥ iwala baba-s akken ad ibeddel addud-ines s tenfaliyin n umtawa tili ad yeḥnin wul n baba-s wa ad yuɣal ɣef ccerṭ-is uqsiḥ
racid yexdem anemgal n wayen yexdem baba-s
yecreḍ fell-as baba-s ad iẓall neɣ ad yeffeɣ seg uxxam
ula d netta yecreḍ ɣef mmi-s ad yeǧǧ taẓallit ɣas s laɛqel
netta tugna-s d tuntimt yernu ɛiwnent kra n tegnatin akken ad yessemneɛ aqerruy-is wa ad yeslek
maca mmi-s tugna-s d tuḍɛift ugar n waya yesseɣli-t zzher-is deg yifri n yizerman
asatel n tmetti deg yiseggasen n ṣat n tmerwin yemxalaf ɣef win n tmetti n yiseggasen n tẓat n tmerwin yewwi-t waḍu ihudd-it netta urɛad ur iɛeddi ara i snat n tmerwin d semmus n yiseggasen deg tudert-is
maca ssneɣ mliḥ racid
ssneɣ teqseḥ n wadduden-ines amer llant deg tallit-ines trebbuyaɛ timselḥin timarksiyin iban ad yeddu yid-sent mebla axemmem ula yiwet n ddqiqa
anda yella umgared ihi gar teqseḥ n baba-s yekren deg taddart win ur nessin anagar kra n tsurtin n leqran d kra n yimenzayen n usɣan d teqseḥ n mmi-s i yeɣran tafelsuft deg tesdawit 
ayen ssneɣ tiṭṭurfa teddukkul d leǧhel d lqella n tmussni ma tamussni n tidet tettak i bab-is ssber d tsura swayes yezmer ad yegzu wa ad yefhem amek ttxemmimen wiyaḍ
maca deg tilawt tamsalt-a tekres ɣef tasint-a mebla lmeɛna
ilaq ad nadi deg ṭṭbiɛa n yimdanen d usatel ideg kkren  am wakken ilaq ad nwali amek i ttwabnant tugniwin-nsen deg temẓi-nsen
acekki-tt temẓi-inek a racid
tufiḍ nnig n uqerruy-ik tasmert tuntimt am ujeɣlal i k-yesmenɛen seg laẓ d usemmiḍ tbedd deg wudem n leqher n yinazmaren 
amer ufiɣ ad idireɣ ddaw n leqher n yiwen n ubabat am wa  tili qebleɣ yakk ccuruṭ-is ad rnuɣ sɣur-i akken ad iyi-iḥemmel ugar
ayen ssneɣ seg baba ḥala tugna-nni yessefqaɛen yeẓẓel ɣef ugertil amerku yeččuren d tilkin d tẓeddem ɣer sdat d nettat lxuf seg tusut-nni tuqsiḥt i igedlen fell-i iḍes  d ameḥbus deg ṭṭlam yenɣa-yi lweswas kemceɣ ɣef yiman-iw deg teɣmert n utemmu-nni asemmaḍ ttergigiɣ am ugḍiḍ iwumi rẓen yiferrawen ddaw n ugeffur
yemma d i yettakken tabergazt tisunḍiwin mebla akukru yettbin-d ɣef taɣect-is d nettat i iḥekkmen
urǧin walaɣ kennu deg tikli n yemma neɣ leqher ɣer baba
asmi d-uɣaleɣ seg tmeqbert ḥusseɣ i ufrad yessewḥacen
kra n wussan umbaɛd mi walaɣ yiwen n urgaz yeṭṭef deg ufus-is yiwen n uqcic ameẓyan yeskerkir-it deffir-is ččurent wallen-iw s yimeṭṭawen ḥulfaɣ i wul-iw yettneqbaḍ
uɣaleɣ srid s axxam ḍeggreɣ iman-iw deg yirebbi n yemma
maca yemma ur tettsewwiq ara ur tḥedder ara i tmeɣriwin ur tettḥewwis ara gar yizenqan
ula d zzyarat-nni i lawliya d ssalḥin akked wid yeqqaren leqran teḥbes-itent
ahat tekfer ula nettat s lkaramat-nsen acku ur smenɛent ara argaz-is seg tmettant
gma ameqqran itteffeɣ seg uxxam seg tafrara ur d-yettuɣal ara armi d lmeɣreb
tuɣ-it ixeddem deg kra n lfirmat baɛdit ccwiya nettraǧu tuɣalin-ines am waggur n lɛid
ma d-yekcem ad as-tejleq yemma taqeft seg yifassen netta urɛad yekkis irkasen-is ad yesgunfu  ad tesmir ayen yellan deg-s ɣef ugertil tettqellib ɣef lxeḍra yellan i usewwi
asafar ayiwan i yezgan deg uxxam  d aɣrum
yernu d nekk iɣef teɣli tmasit ad awiɣ irden neɣ timẓin ɣer tsirt n ɛmer uɛelluc yiwet n tikkelt deg ddurt
tettɛawan-iyi yemma akken ad serseɣ tacekkart ɣef tayet-iw tikli ɣef uḍar tettaṭṭaf-iyi ugar n ssaɛa akken ad awḍeɣ ɣer tlemmast n taddart ideg tella tsirt
acḥal ferrḥeɣ mi ara sleɣ i ssut n umseddu seg lebɛid uqbel mi ara bduɣ tikli deg tsawent i d-yettawin ɣur-s
ma yessusem lmeɛna-ines d aḥbas i yeḥbes umseddu-nni dɣa ad neqqim din ad nerǧu melmi ad t-yexdem ɛemmi ɛmer tikwal nettaf iman-nneɣ nettuḥettem ad neǧǧ ticekkarin-nneɣ din armi d azekka-nni
ad lḥuɣ yakk amecwar-nni aɣezzfan mebla asgunfu mebla ma subbeɣ tacekkart-nni seg tayet-iw
anwa ara iyi-iɛiwnen akken ad tt-rreɣ ɣef tayet-iw  ad tt-skerkreɣ deg ubrid ad tt-rreɣ deffir n yicekkaren i tt-yezwaren taɣuct n ɛemmi ɛmer tettɛeggiḍ fell-i akken ur sseɣraseɣ ara tacekkart-nni
deg zzedwa-nni aɣebbar n ssmid yeččur amkan
ameẓẓaḍ arqiqan yeččur s uɣebbar amellal taɛmamt-is tetteɛluluq ɣef tuyat-is yettali yettsubbu deg tsirt-ines
yettaddam s sin n yiɣallen iɛeryanen d untimen yeččuren s yinẓaden tacekkart seg lqaɛa wa ad yali yis-s asellum ameẓyan ad tt-yesmir sakin deg yimi n tsirt
uqbel ad d-isubb ad yessefqed taɣara n ssmid i d-iɣellin am ucercur daxel n tcekkart
nekk ttɣimiɣ deg uṭrutwar i d-iqublen tisirt akken ad d-rreɣ nnehta
tuɣalin s axxam tettili s laɛqel ẓẓayet ugar ɣezzifet ɣef rrwaḥ acku tettili dima ddaw n yiṭij aqesḥan ugar n waya atemmu-nneɣ yezga ddaw n tizi yulin ɣef tlemmast n taddart
tissin tettili ɣef yiwet n tkessart i yi-yettɛawan mliḥ deg tikli
ma d alluy yettiḥwiǧ tazmert
maca nekk yenɣa-yi laẓ selleɣ i yiẓerman-iw mi ttɛeggiḍen
abrid yeččur s yixejḍan idɣaɣen d uɣebbar deg unebdu s waluḍ deg tegrest
neccarew-iten merriɣet akken ad d-nawi imi n uɣrum
yemma telmed deg temɣer-ines ad tesneɛ timedwazin
uɣaleɣ ttedduɣ yid-s ɣer umadaɣ i d-yezgan tama n tizi akken ad neqleɛ awri
nettawi-t s axxam yemma tettarra-t d timedwazin i tesnuzu i lǧiran
ma ur nessaweḍ ara ad tent-nessenz i lǧiran tettara-tent yemma d tazdemt ttawiɣ-tent ad tent-senzeɣ deg ssuq n taddart
 senz-itent s zzuǧ duru
ma ur tessawḍeḍ ara ad tent-tessenẓeḍ deg ssuq sṭebṭeb ɣer yixxamen kečč mazal-ik meẓẓiyeḍ tilawin ur ḥeǧbent ara deg-k ɛreḍ ad tent-tessawmeḍ ur ttsetḥi ara
yakk ixxamen tteḥwiǧin imezziren ad tafeḍ win ad d-yaɣen fell-ak yiwen neɣ sin 
akka i txeddem yemma ad iyi-tesseḥfeḍ tamsirt wa ad tessers agerruj ɣef tayet-iw
seg usennan ɣer tmellalt uɣaleɣ ttekleɣ ɣef yiman-iw am wakken uɣaleɣ ḥemmleɣ tudert
tuɣal ṭṭabla-nneɣ tameẓyant tettaččar s wučči yemma tuɣal tettɛeggiḍ fell-i akken ad kfuɣ lmakla i d-yegran deg uḍebsi-nni ameqqran n ufexxar
 ad aɣ-iḥaseb rebbi ɣef uḍegger-agi n wučči yezmer ad aɣ-yekkes lxir-agi 
yemma tesɛa tawant maca tettaggad tuɣalin n wussan-nni n laẓ d lḥif dɣa ad tt-tafeḍ tjemmeɛ ayen iwumi tezmer wa ad tseddeq ɣef win yenḥafen fell-aneɣ
 rḥem wid yellan deg lqaɛa ad k-yerḥem win yellan deg yigenwan
xdem lxir ad t-tafeḍ
xdem ccer ad t-tafeḍ 
acḥal i telha tmuɣli n yemma
tesselmed-as ddunit belli ussan ttneqlaben yiwen n wass aql-ik iwsawen wayeḍ ad d-tafeḍ iman-ik tegrarbeḍ ukessar
ayen i ɣ-yuɣen asmi yemmut gma umbaɛd mi nɣil ussan-nni n lḥif ruḥen war tuɣalin d anza ɣef tuggdi-ines
werteɣ sɣur-s tuggdi seg wussan n lḥif d lmiziriya
cfiɣ mliḥ ɣef uzal-nni mi d-yuɣal gma lmilud zik s axxam mačči d leɛwayed-is
uɣaleɣ-d seg tsirt skerkireɣ iḍarren-iw deg tsawent-nni i d-yettawin s axxam-nneɣ tafekka-inu tnedder ddaw n taẓayt n tcekkart n ssmid
ur as-faqeɣ ara armi ḥulfaɣ i tcekkart-nni tettwakkes ɣef tayet-iw s ẓẓur
ɣileɣ d amakar i yebɣan ad iyi-yaker lqut n twacult-iw iḍuḍan-iw ckunṭeḍen deg tcekkart nwiɣ ɣef umennuɣ ad mmteɣ akken ḥuddeɣ ɣef ugerruj-inu
maca mi sliɣ i ssut-is theddneɣ
 awi-d ɣer dagi  ẓriɣ taɛyiḍ yernu yenɣa-k laẓ

yerfed tacekkart s yiwen n ufus yerra-tt ɣef tayet-is
gma yejhed mliḥ yuɣ tannumi ixeddem lecɣal iwaɛren
yefka-yi-d yiwet n tcekkart tameẓyant yellan deg ufus niḍen sakin nkemmel alluy n tsawent-nni
tertaḥ tfekka-inu tekcem tumert tameqqrant ul-iw
teɣli-d fell-i lemɛawna am waggur n lɛid i ɣ-yessufuɣen seg laɛtab n wussan n tuẓumin deg tsemhuyin tiḥmayanin
ttwaliɣ gma d ameqqran annect ilat yezmer ad iyi-ibibb ula d nekk ɣef tayet-is tis snat
tekcem tudert tafekka-inu ḥulfaɣ i tezmert-is tettazzal deg yiẓuran-iw dɣa yufeg laɛtab-iw ḍefreɣ-t s zzux
lḥaǧa tamezwarut i ijebden tidmi-w d aselsu-ines azedgan i yettlusu ḥala deg wussan n teswiqt
mačči seg uxeddim i d-yuɣal ihi
sani iruḥ yernu ass-a mačči d taswiqt
mazal ur yezgir ara amnar n tewwurt armi isuɣ 
a yemma  d ayen qeblen-iyi
teǧǧa yemma ayen yellan gar yifassen-is tbedd tserreḥ-as i tiɣratin
d acu-t usali-agi i yesferḥen akka yemma  tɛenneq-it 
mebruk fell-ak a mmi melmi ad tkecmeḍ ɣer lkaẓirna 
lkaẓirna  gma ad yuɣal d aserdas
u yemma teẓra
lmilud yebɣa ad yuɣal d aɛeskriw
yessers gma tacekkart n ssmid yessuter deg-i ad as-fkeɣ tacekkart-ines tameẓyant
ḥemdet rebbi  wagi d ass ameqqran ilaq ad t-nesfuggel
sya sin n wussan ad iliɣ deg blida
anda d-tezga blida-agi  iban ad iɛeṭṭel leɣyab n gma
fecleɣ ɣef yiwen n ubrid tazmert-nni i yi-izedɣen mi d-magreɣ gma deg tsawent-nni tufeg ulac d acu i d-yeqqimen deg-s
walaɣ iman-iw d awḥid ḥala nekk d yemma ad as-tiniḍ d akelbun d yemma-s tuḍɛift i yesseglafen yal mi ara tsell i ssut tɣil yella kra n yimihi i itezzin ɣef mmi-s
yeqqim gma udem-is yettfeǧǧiǧ seg lferḥ yeldi tacekkart-nni yessuffeɣ-d seg-s iḥricen n leḥlawat imud-iyi-ten 
ečč a qeddur  tagi ssawalen-as neɣ tiɣrifin s tament  ur cliɛeɣ ara
amer deg tegnatin niḍen i d-tusa tili d asebleɛ ad tent-sbelɛeɣ
ččurent wallen-iw d imeṭṭawen rewleɣ ɣer berra
iluḥeq-iyi-d gma yekkes ɣef lxaṭer-iw
s kra n wawalen yesuneɣ-iyi-d i aɣ-yettganin umbaɛd anekcum-is ɣer lɛesker
ur nettɣimi ara deg utemmu-agi
ad ngaǧ ɣer taddart yezmer lḥal ɣer temdint wa ad tudert yelhan kecmeɣ ɣer uɣerbaz
sefḍeɣ imeṭṭawen-iw ččiɣ 
seg wass-nni yal mi ara d-yers ɣef ṭṭabla ttuɣalent-d ccfawat-inu ɣer uzal-nni n tumert d leḥzen
tudert-nneɣ tbeddel s tidet umbaɛd unekcum n gma ɣer lɛesker
iɣab acḥal n ledwar ulac acu neẓra fell-as
kemmleɣ snuzuyeɣ imezziren ttawiɣ irden d temẓin ɣer tsirt ttseggideɣ igḍaḍ
yal mi ara seqsiɣ yemma ɣef ssebba n uɛeṭṭel-ines ad iyi-thedden  qrib ad d-yuɣal incallah
banen-iyi-d wussan war taggara
yernu yal mi ara d-uɣaleɣ ɣer taddart ad bduɣ tikli deg tsawent-nni i d-yettawin ɣer uxxam-nneɣ acḥal d abrid i d-zziɣ ɣer deffir limmer ad t-waliɣ iteddu s yiselsa n yiserdasen yesɛan lhiba
mugreɣ-d acḥal n tikkal kra n yiserdasen deg tezniqin n taddart dɣa ttmuquleɣ-ten s tuffra ttsuguneɣ gma deg umkan-nsen
hata yuɣal-d
d aɣelluy i d-yeɣli fell-aneɣ mebla ma neẓra
taddart-nneɣ mazal ur tessin ara deg tallit-nni tibratin neɣ amaway n tebratin
yewweḍ-d umbaɛd lmeɣreb
seg wasmi iruḥ gma nuɣal nettarra tawwurt mi ad yeɣli yiṭij ad nsiɣ tacemmaɛt ad nečč imensi wa ad neṭṭes
teɣli-d fell-aneɣ taɣuct-is d taḥmayant ad as-tiniḍ d izenẓaren n yiṭij n tnezzayt
negzeɣ ad ldiɣ tawwurt
yenna-d s uqesser 
tegganem akked tyuẓaḍ tura 
yettbin-d deg uselsu-ines n userdas am umnay izedɣen tirga-inu
yessers tabalizt-ines tameqqrant ɣef umnar n tewwurt nemsalam s yiwet n leḥrara yesseḥmayen ulawen
yufeg leḥzen iruḥ ṭṭlam d tsusmi n utemmu
yesseɛya-yi yinig yernu laẓ igezzem iẓerman-iw
tenna-d yemma s ciṭuḥ n leḥya 
ur neẓri ara ad d-taseḍ ass-a a lmilud a mmi nečča ayen d-yegran  maca ssber kan rrbeɛ n ssaɛa ad kreɣ ad ak-ɛerkeɣ tamtunt am wakken tḥemmleḍ
ur ssaɛyu ara iman-im a yemma
wwiɣ-awen-d imensi izad
amek ad d-uɣaleɣ s axxam umbaɛd leɣyab n sin n wagguren s yifassen d ilmawen 
yeldi tabalizt yessufeɣ-d seg-s ḥala lqut yelhan  aɣrum n ubulunji d amellal tayaẓiḍt yewwan mazal-itt akken teḥma aguglu azemmur ččina taqarɛet n lgazuz d lḥelwa n 
nessaɣ-d tacemmaɛt niḍen neččur ṭṭabla s wučči-nni aẓiḍan neqqim nettqessir urǧin neqqim tiɣimit am ta
yessuffeɣ-d sakin iselsa imaynuten i ɣ-d-yewwi i nekk d yemma
lsiɣ-ten s zzux suguneɣ iman-iw leḥḥuɣ deg yiberdan n taddart aqerruy-iw deg yigenni tikkelt-a ur ttsetḥiɣ ara s yiselsa-inu mačči d iqdimen-nni yeččuren s tfawtin deg tgecrar neɣ deffir n userwal-iw
iḍ-nni ṭṭseɣ yis-sen s tumert ḥulfaɣ i yiman-iw d afug i ttafgeɣ ɣef usigna i yetthuzu yiwen n waḍu d afessas
yeqqim gma yid-neɣ mraw n wussan
i tikkelt tamezwarut mi ara d-akiɣ tanezzayt ttafeɣ-t deg uxxam
nruḥ jmiɛ ɣer ssuq n taddart neqqim ntezzi gar lɣaci d sselɛa yersen ɣef tmurt am wakken xeddmen yirgazen s zzux d nnefxa
aṭas n tɣawsiwin i d-nuɣ  leḥwal i tnawalt lxeḍra kraḍ n yikilugramen n ttmer semmuset n litrat n zzit n uzemmur d tebwaḍin n leḥelwa n ssenf n
mi d-nuɣal yeḥka-yi-d kra n ttfasil ɣef tudert-ines deg lkazirna  isluɣma deg wannar tiyita s leslaḥ imeddukkal d temdint n blida tameqqrant ideg yezmer ad yaɛreq umdan deg yiberdan-is
yenna-yi-d tikkelt-a mi ara yuɣal kan ad yelmed tanhert n ṭumubil
qqimeɣ kan ttḥessiseɣ deg-s asugen-inu yebda yessenfal awalen-nni d tugniwin i ttwaliɣ sdat n wallen-iw mi nuɣ tasawent-nni yernu ldiɣ allen-iw mliḥ almi brarḥent akken ad tent-waliɣ s tidet sdat-i
seqsaɣ-t s lḥir 
ad d-taɣeḍ ṭumubil 
ih ayɣer ara lemdeɣ tanhert ihi
maca ṭumubil ur tezmir ara ad telḥu deg tsawent-agi yernu ur tettaweḍ ara armi d axxam-nneɣ
anda ad tt-teǧǧeḍ 
anwa i ak-d-yennan dagi ara neqqim  qrib ad neggaǧ ɣer taddart
ǧǧiɣ ttewsaya i yiwen seg tmussniwin-inu ad aɣ-iqelleb ɣef uxxam din
yettazzalen deg tlemmast n ubrid aruradan
maca anurẓem n gma yekfa s temɣawla
nuɣal nekk d yemma ɣer tudert-nneɣ tuḥzint n yal ass
ad ruḥeɣ yal tanezzayt ɣer zzawiya n ccix ad lemdeɣ leqran akked tarbaɛt n warrac i zedɣen tama-nneɣ
yemma ur tuɣal ara ɣer lxedma n yimezziren acku yeǧǧa-aɣ-d gma aṭas n yidrimen
myiqrabent tirza n gma
yettaweḍ tikwal ɣer lmeɣreb wa ad ɣ-yeǧǧ ɣer tafrara maca yettawi-d yid-s dima
sugneɣ iman-iw qqimeɣ tama n gma daxel n ṭumubil i lqeḍyan i ɣ-yessuffɣen s tidet seg lḥif i ɣ-yesberken ussan-nneɣ
yiwen n wass deg wussan n rebbi deg tnafsa n wass yekcem-d fell-aneɣ am tbuciḍant n yijdi yumeṛ-aɣ ad nejmeɛ lqecc-nneɣ akken ad neggaǧ
ṭumubil tettraǧu-aɣ ddaw n tsawent
yemma tesgerfel deg tazwara
tebda aseqsi deg-s
sani ad neggaǧ  iwumi ad neǧǧ atemmu-nneɣ 
ad nawi yid-neɣ yakk ayla-nneɣ  maca mi nwala gma yefreḥ iḥerres deg-neɣ ad neffeɣ neddem iwumi nezmer neḍfer-it mebla ma neẓra sani
axxam-nni tuɣ-it d ameẓyan ila snat n texxamin d umraḥ leḥyuḍ-is bnan s yidɣaɣen ssqef-is s zzenk i yemmug
yezga deg tlemmast n tegrumma tameẓyant n yixxamen i d-yezgan deg yizenqan nnig n tsirt
mi nɛedda kan sdat-s ssarmeɣ ur yettili ara uxxam-agi yebɛed fell-as akken ad thenniɣ seg tikli-nni n umecwar aɣezzfan tacekkart n yirden ɣef uɛrur-iw
axxam-nneɣ amaynut yesɛa tasafut i d-yesskecmen lḥamu ɣef wuḍan-nneɣ u tesnejla fell-i tuggdi d uneqbaḍ n wul i yi-xenqen yal mi ara d-yeɣli ṭṭlam
am wakken nethenna seg wabbu n tmes n yisɣaren d wuguren i tettmagar yemma akken ad tessiɣ times s usuḍu ɣef yirrij alamma yuɣal wudem n tmeɣbunt d aberkan s yinbuxen
yuɣ-aɣ-d gma taqarɛet n lgaz n lbuṭan d ufurnu d ameẓyan bu-kraḍ n yikanunen
deg wussan imezwura n tudert-nneɣ tamaynut tezga yemma tettalas awalen-a  tneɣriyin n yimaglalen

nella nettwamḍel a qeddur a mmi
tamettant-nneɣ tif tudert-nneɣ
ad yesseɣzef rebbi laɛmer n lmilud i ɣ-d-yessuffɣen seddaw n wakal ɣer tafat
nɛac deg uxxam-nni deg tumert
kecmeɣ ɣer uɣerbaz sɛiɣ qqareɣ deg imeddukkal seg warrac n udcir netturar jmiɛ nettnaɣ tikwal maca amennuɣ ur yettɛeṭṭil ara dɣa ad nuɣal ɣer uhruḥu-nneɣ deg tlemmast n yiberdan d yizenqan n taddart
yemma ur tɛeṭṭel ara tufa amkan-is deg taddart
teqqen assaɣen d waṭas n tǧiratin ttembaddalent tirza tettɣimi yid-sent tettawi yid-sen ameslay ɣef yal asentel
atan yecreq-d yiṭij fell-aneɣ u tezmummeg ddunit deg wudem-nneɣ
maca ulac lḥaǧa i yettɣamayen deg umkan-is
yir-lbext yerra-aɣ gar wallen-is yettɛassa deg-neɣ
mazal ur neffiɣ ɣef wannar n tmuɣli-s iḍegger fell-aneɣ ifassen-is yejbed-aɣ ɣur-s
tanezzayt n yiwen n wass aɣemɣam ffɣeɣ seg uxxam tuɣ-iyi leḥḥuɣ ɣer tsirt ɣef tayet-iw tacekkart n yirden teḥbes yiwet n tmerkabt n yiserdasen deg yiwen n umkan ur nebɛid ara ɣef uxxam-nneɣ
isubb-d yiwen n userdas yebda ittezzi ur ẓriɣ ara ɣef wacu i yettnadi
ul-iw yebda yekkat am ṭṭbel
yal mi ara ɣlint wallen-iw ɣef userdas-nni walaɣ ssifa n gma s uselsu-ines adal yesɛan lhiba sdat-i
d netta i d-yusan  seg lebɛid iserdasen irkelli ttemcabin
beddeɣ deg umkan-iw ḥekkreɣ deg-sen heggaɣ-d iman-iw ad serseɣ tacekkart n yirden
tura meqqreɣ zemreɣ ad ddmeɣ wa ad serseɣ tacekkart s sshala
iwala-yi userdas-nni yelḥa-d ɣur-i amzun d lḥaǧa ɣlayen i d-yufa sdat-s
ay aqcic ruḥ-d
serseɣ tacekkart uẓaɣ-d ɣur-s s ukukru
ayɣer ad aggadeɣ  d aserdas am gma
ahat d gma i t-iweṣṣan ad iɛeddi ɣef uxxam-nneɣ  maca win i d-yusan d amestul am wid i nettmagar deg ssuq
dagi i tzedɣeḍ 
ih
anda d-yezga uxxam n userdas lmilud ǧennadi 
nniɣ-as s yiwet n taɣect d tazurant zuxxeɣ mačči d kra riɣ ad as-beggneɣ d nekk i d gma-s n milud iɣef ttnadin yiǧadarmiyen ɣef uxxam-is wehhaɣ-asen ɣer tewwurt 
dagi nekk d gma-s
ruḥ siwel-as i yemma-k ini-as nebɣa ad tt-nwali
uzzleɣ 
a yemma  a yemma  d iǧadarmiyen yuzen-iten-id gma ɣur-m
teffeɣ-d yemma tefqeɛ ad as-tiniḍ tcumm i twaɣit
yuẓa ɣur-s umestul
tewweḍ-iyi-d taɣuct-is maca ur fhimeɣ ara d acu i as-yeqqar
imir-n kan tuɣwas yemma tebda tiyitwin deg yidmaren-is s yifassen-is
uzzleɣ ɣur-s s tuffɣa n laɛqel

lmilud
yeqqim umestul deg umkan-is yeqqur
iluḥeq-it-id umeddakkel-is i yeqqimen deg  yuẓa ɣer yemma 
ur tettru ara a yemma  wagi d lmektub n rebbi
maca yemma tɛuẓẓeg tsell kan i yimeṭṭawen-is
tessawal i mmi-s s yiwet n taɣect i igezzmen ula tasa n urumi
ḍeggreɣ iman-iw deg yirebbi-s serḥeɣ-as ula d nekk i yimeṭṭawen
truḥ-d tǧaret-nneɣ lalla xayra teṭṭef yemma seg yiɣil tesker-itt-id s laɛqel tessekcem-itt ɣer daxel n umraḥ n uxxam tessuter deg-s ad tesber wa ad teqbel s tikci n sidi rebbi
kra n lweqt umbaɛd mi yeffeɣ lexbar-a yessefqaɛen yeččur uxxam-nneɣ s tlawin n udcir i d-yusan ad ɛezzint yemma
kra n yirgazen seg lǧiran bedden sdat n tseqsayen kan s wallen-nsen acu akka i yeḍran
yuẓa ɛemmi muḥ bab n tḥanut tayiwant n udcir ɣer yiwen n yimestal 
amek i yemmut lmilud 
deg tazwara yessusem umestul sakin yerra-as-d s tewzel 
nnan-aɣ-d d yiwen n uggullu i d-yenneqlaben fell-as deg uslaɣmu
yurǧa bab n tḥanut d yirgazen niḍen yellan yid-s ad ikemmel awal-is maca yessider umestul i uqerruy-is yessusem
kra n lweqt umbaɛd yenna 
tafekka n umerḥum ad d-taweḍ azekka
nessawel i yiɛeggalen n tɣiwant akken ad heggin lumur n tenṭelt
yenna bab n tḥanut 
ad t-yerḥem rebbi d ilemẓi yelhan medden yakk ḥemmlen-t
yuli-d yiwen n ssut ɣef yiwen n ubrid  amin
kra n yimawen bdan stewtiwen i tsuret n lfatiḥa
uqbel n ttnasfa n wass yewweḍ-d ukamyun n yiserdasen deg-s i yella usenduq ideg yeẓẓel gma
mmeslayen-d yimestal-nni kra n lweqt akked lǧiran-nneɣ uqbel ad sidren asenduq ad t-sersen deg umraḥ n uxxam
tneggez yemma ɣef usenduq n usɣar tebɣa ad as-tekkes aɣummu-ines maca semmren-t

tisunḍa n lɛesker a yemma ur nezmir ara 
yessusem userdas ur ikemmel ara awal-is
wallaɣ i uqerruy-is allen-is ččurent d yeqqim ibedd sdat n usenduq
yettwamḍel gma neɣ asenduq-nni i ɣ-d-nnan deg-s i tella tafekka n lmilud deg uzal-nni
ur ṭṭaxren ara yiserdasen i usenduq ula d ddqiqa armi t-rran ddaw n wakal deg tmeqbert n taddart
rekben sakin akamyun-nsen uɣalen seg wansi i d-usan
imezdaɣ n udcir bedden yid-neɣ
yeqqim uxxam-nneɣ yeččur s lɣaci ugar n ddurt
iɛeggalen n twacult n yemma wwḍen-d s ugellel ur ten-yewwiḍ ara lexbar armi zrin sin n wussan armi d ass n teswiqt
ma tawacult n baba ur nessin ula yiwen seg-s
ɣef wawal n yemma baba yella ixeddem lefḥem seg wasmi imeṭṭawen
yessider ttazzalen d tezweǧ yid-s ur teẓri ara ma yesɛa tawacult neɣ ur yesɛi ara
tenna-yi-d lasel-is seg temnaḍt n ssɛida d tazzla deffir n uɣrum i t-yessawḍen ɣer yidurar-agi
asmi d-iruḥ ad tt-id-yexḍeb tesɛa yemma sin n yiseggasen mi tennebra lmilud yid-s i yella u tezdeɣ ɣur ɛemmi-s
ɛemmi-s-agi yemmut uqbel ma yeṭṭef urgaz-is baba rray ad yinig wa ad ɣ-yawi yid-s ad nezdeɣ deg utemmu-nni ideg sɛeddaɣ temẓi-inu tamezwarut
tamettant n gma d ahdum i d-yeɣlin ɣef yiqerra-nneɣ
teɣli yemma am teckirt-nni tameqqrant yettwagezmen imeṭṭawen fell-as
