urǧin teḥbes
lmilud iḍ d wass
am wakken tuɣal tettḥulfu i sster deg uqerruy-is tettaɛraḍ ad tekkes leqriḥ-nni s ucuddu n unyir-is s umendil i tessebzag s lxell d lqares
ur zrin ara kra n wussan armi yewweḍ yiwen n usali 
lmilud yettwanɣa deg yiwen n umerẓi i yeḍran deg tama n blida gar yisafagen n hewwari bumedyen d yiggulluyen n kra n yikulunalen n lɛesker i bɣan ad t-seɣlin akken ad rren ttar i ben bella iwumi yekkes
bumedyen adabu yerna yessekcem-it lḥebs
d tikkelt tamezwarut i sliɣ i yismawen n bumedyen d ben bella
lehdur-agi sliɣ-asen ɣer bab n tḥanut
ufiɣ yiwen n urgaz yettmeslay ɣef temsalt-a mi i iy-iwala kan yessusem
maca ɣas akken ukreɣ asali
seqsaɣ yemma
maca amek ara tẓer tmeɣbunt
ula d nettat tesla ayen sliɣ
tenna   d acu lfayda seg waya  lmilud yemmut lmeyyet urǧin ad d-yuɣal wid i t-yenɣan leḥsab-nsen ɣer rebbi nekkni d imeɣban ulac acu nezmer ad t-nexdem d acu yellan gar yifassen-nneɣ ḥala ddaɛwat i sidi rebbi 

yemma tessusem twekkel lamer-is i sidi rebbi maca nekk ala
bɣiɣ ad ẓreɣ acu s-yeḍran i gma
deg wussan-nni lliɣ ṭṭafareɣ timsirin n yiḍ tekcem s ul-iw leqraya d tira
tigawt tamezwarut i xedmeɣ uɣeɣ-d aɣmis n limmer ad afeɣ asali i yettmeslayen ɣef ṭṭrad-nni i yenɣan gma
ulac acu ufiɣ ɣef usentel-a
isebtar-ines ččuren s tewlifin d wawalen n hewwari bumedyen aselway n useqqamu n tegrawla
ulac ula yiwen n wawal ɣef ben bella neɣ ɣef wid yebɣan ad as-kksen adabu
kra n lweqt umbaɛd uɣaleɣ ur t-id-ttaɣeɣ ara
yuɣal iqerreḥ-iyi ciṭuḥ lḥal mi ara waliɣ bumedyen yettezmummug yerfed afus-is ɣer yigenni ma d gma atan snat n lmitrat ddaw n wakal
yernu deg uqerru-iw fran-t ttuqenɛeɣ daxel-iw belli d netta i t-yenɣan
yiwen n wass ǧǧiɣ armi tefreɣ tḥanut n ɛemmi muḥ dɣa seqsaɣ-t 
ɛemmi muḥ d tidet ayen sliɣ gma yettwanɣa deg ṭṭrad yeḍran gar bumedyen d ben bella 
tembawel tcacit-is allen-is brarḥent 
anda tesliḍ i yimeslayen-agi ay amcum 
dagi i sliɣ i yiwen n urgaz ihedder belli isafagen n
bumedyen wwten iggelluyen i iteddun ɣer tmanaɣt aṭas n yiserdasen i yemmuten gar-asen gma
yessussem ɛemmi muḥ yesneḥneḥ dɣa yenna  imuqqel yeffus ẓelmaḍ
susmeɣ kkreɣ ffɣeɣ
ɛemmi muḥ ttqadaren-t yirkelli
sell mliḥ a mmi ur ttamen ara acu i d-qqaren wigi yessuguten awal ccɣel-nsen ḥala awal mebla lmeɛna kečč meẓẓiyeḍ timsal-agi meqqrit fell-ak
gma-k yemmut wagi d lmektub n sidi rebbi
ma yewweḍ lajel n walbaɛḍ teččur-as dayen
ɣas mgaradent tsebbiwin tamettant d yiwet kan
ɣef waya ad k-weṣṣiɣ ur nebbec ara ur ttɛawad ara ad tesseqsiḍ iseqsiyen am wigi
lethu kan s leqraya d uxeddim-inek bedd ɣef yemma-k tameɣbunt
d keččini i d asalel-ines ayiwan
sliɣ tuḍen
ad as-yefk rebbi ccfa
aɣ awal-iw a mmi
ur yettmeslay ara aṭas maca awalen-is weznen d ureɣ
grarben yis-neɣ wussan
win i ɣ-yettawin aɣrum iruḥ dayen
tuɣal yemma ɣer lxedma n yimezziren
tugi ad tt-ɛiwneɣ deg tukksa n uwri neɣ ad t-senzeɣ  wagi d ccɣel n tlawin
ma d kečč kker ad tnadiḍ ɣef uxeddim n yirgazen
 tuɣal tettenkar zik tettruḥu ɣer utemmu-nneɣ aqdim tqelleɛ awri weḥd-s kan tettaǧǧa-t din mi zrin kra n wussan ad d-tuɣal ɣur-s akken ad tesneɛ yimezziren deg umkan-nni
tikwal ttlaḥaqeɣ-tt ɣer din akken ad tt-wanseɣ ad bibbeɣ rrezma n yimezziren wa ad uɣaleɣ s laɛqel kan ɣer uxxam-nneɣ i d-yezgan deg taddart
timsirin n tmeddit beddunt seg lxemsa n tmeddit armi d tmenya
dɣa ttɣamayeɣ ass s lekmal-is mebla ccɣel
kra n lweqt xedmeɣ deg lfirma n yimjuhad d axeddim n tsemhuyt kan ikeffu s ujmaɛ n lɣella
tajernaḍt d tamecṭuḥt maca ttuɣaleɣ-d dima s kra n lxeḍra d lfakya
axeddim yewɛer yessamas yernu ulac deg-s imal
ur ẓriɣ ara amek i yi-d-tusa tikti n unekcum ɣer lɛesker
hedreɣ-as i yemma
tsuɣ ad tɣileḍ d azrem i tt-yeqsen
 tebɣiḍ ad iyi-tenɣeḍ  ur tesqenɛeḍ ara s wayen yeḍran i gma-k  ad yenɛel rebbi idrimen-nsen
ad yenɛel
rebbi ass-nni mi yekcem lmilud ɣer lkazirna tigullelt tif tagnit ideg ddreɣ tura
tiggullelt ur tneqq ara
nekkni d imeɣban nqenneɛ s wulac
kkes tikti-a seg uqerruy-ik 
kkseɣ tikti-agi s tidet seg uqerruy-iw
ssakint-iyi-d tiyitwin tifessasin ɣef tewwurt
ṭṭurceɣ i tmezzuɣin-inu akken ad kkseɣ ccek
d asṭebṭeb s tidet neɣ d ayen i d-yegran seg yir targit i urgaɣ  uḍan-inu ineggura uɣalen-iyi-d d ɛeggu deg tazwara d iḍes ixerben deg tlemmast d yir-tirga yessefqaɛen ɣer taggara
ssut n tyitwin yennerna
mseḍfarent d tifessasin am wakken win i yesṭebṭuben ur yebɣi ara ad yessaki lǧiran
ḍeggreɣ taduli akin ttekkaɣ ɣef tqeffalt n umesbaḥ muqleɣ s wallen imedlen ɣer ssaɛa n lḥiḍ
zzuǧ u rrbeɛ n ssbeḥ
srugmteɣ s wurfan   acu yeḍran akka  d timenɣiwt niḍen i yeḍran  ur yezmir ara bab n twaɣit-a tamaynut ad yerǧu alamma yuli wass  
ɣef tewwurt tessekref-iyi lhejna tesdubbez iles-iw
ccil n ṭṭlam i yemmɣen ɣef umkan ɛeqleɣ yusef ɛeyyaci win iɣef ttḥudduɣ d netta i irewlen ass n uẓdam s leslaḥ ɣef tkamyunt n temsulta
qqureɣ deg umkan-iw ur s mmeslayeɣ ur xdimeɣ kra
ucmummeḥ sakin yenna-yi-d s usqewqew 
suref-iyi a si ɛebdelqader  yettuḥettem fell-i ḥwaǧeɣ-k
anda telliḍ ay amcum  d acu txedmeḍ  tegreḍ iman-ik deg yiwet n twaɣit tameqqrant
imuqel-iyi-d kan
mačči d nekk d tamara a si ɛebdelqader d tamara i yi-rran asmi ad k-d-ḥkuɣ ad iyi-tfehmeḍ wa ad iyi-tɛawneḍ
kcem tura teḥkuḍ-iyi-d taqsiḍt-ik
ala mačči dagi
els iselsa-inek ddu-d yid-neɣ
yid-wen  anwa-ken  yaɛni mačči weḥd-k i telliḍ 
ur ttaggad ara a si ɛebdelqader bɣan ad mmeslayen yid-k kečč d amastan d abugaṭu tamsalt tekres ugar ɣef wayen tɣileḍ
sani ad dduɣ yid-k 
ɣer yiwen n umkan ur yebɛid ara mliḥ syagi
xemmemeɣ kra n lweqt i usumer-agi yessewhamen
ran kan ad iyi-yessuffɣen akken ad iyi-nɣen  ala nekk d amastan ur sɛiɣ ara taɛdawt yid-sen
ttqadaren imastanen acku ḥudden ɣef lecyux-nsen asmi ten-yerra udabu aserdasan deg lḥebs yernu lliɣ yiwen deg-sen
iban ḥwaǧen amastan ara iḥudden fell-asen
maca acu yezmer ad yexdem umastan umbaɛd n tmenɣiwt n seddis n yimesulta  tamsalt-a tezzuɣur deffir-s uffir bɣiɣ ad ẓreɣ d acu-t
nniɣ 
kcem a yusef kra n ddqayeq ad iliɣ ɣur-k
ad k-ibarek rebbi a si ɛebdelqader
ad k-rǧuɣ kan dagi
sin n yirgazen s leslaḥ ɣummen udmawen-nsen tuɣ-iten ttraǧun-aɣ deg ubrid
nessers kan iḍarren-nneɣ ɣef ubrid yeččuren s yixjuḍen nserreḥ-as i tazzla ad as-tiniḍ nerbeḥ
yiwen deg-sen d yettmuqqul seg lweqt ɣer wayeḍ ɣer deffir akken ad iẓer i nebɣa ad timsizzelt ma yella win i ɣ-yeṭṭafaren
ṭṭlam atellis yemmeɣ ɣef udcir
acḥal d abrid i mmeslayeɣ i uselway n tɣiwant i iɛeddan akken ad tesbedd tɣiwant imesbaḥen deg ubrid
yenna-d yefka yakan i lwilaya yiwen n usenfar yemmed ɣef useqɛed n yiberdan d wusu-nsen s ugudrun tiririt n ukarlaj i uṭrutwar d teftilin deg yiberdan
maca lwilya ur texdim acemma
lwilaya  d tiɣremt yerkan tessalay leḥyuḍ-is s usemnenni n yikamaren ḥekkmen-tt yisuḍaf n leqher d usali n leswar s yiɣallen laman d yiɛessasen deg yal annag
tsemmin i yikalan-agi tibiruqraṭiyin lhiba n uwanak
wagi d arebrab n uwanak uḍɛif ur nessaweḍ ara ad yessuffeɣ tamurt seg tggunẓit d twernaḍt ccil n lxir yessemnennin deg tmurt d yimiḍanen lbankat n iwadmayen n lbanka
yeḥfeḍ uselway n tɣiwant taɣect yuɣal yal mi ara t-smektiɣ s lemɛahdat-ines ad d-iyi-tt-yettalles
maca seg wasmi yettwanɣa budyaf ameɣnas-nni arumansi bu-nniya i suffɣen yiseḥḥaren seg talwit n temɣert-is akken ad yerr tamacint-nsen s abrid d uṭerḍerq n ṭṭrad-agi ur nessaweḍ ad as-naf isem iwumi nbubb ɣef yiferrawen-is yeččuren d idammen yakk ibriren d ddɣel-nneɣ
nekkni nuɣ tannumi nettarra llum ɣef wiyaḍ nekk d agellid wiyaḍ d ccwaṭen ulamma d gma neɣ d mmi-s n lɛerc-inu ttmagareɣ-t ssbeḥ tameddit gar lɣaci deg ssuq neɣ ad beddeɣ tama-s deffir n ccix n lǧameɛ sbedden wayeḍ ɣef uqerru n tɣiwant qqaren-d d amestul yewwin tastaɣt-ines ḥebsen yakk isenfaren
tura ur i yi-teɛni ara temsalt
nuɣ tannumi s waluḍ ixjuḍen n waman d ṭṭlam
nuɣal nettnadi kan amek ad nesseḥbiber ɣef tudert-nneɣ
awi-d kan ad nidir yuɣal-aɣ d raslmal aɣlayan isettu-aɣ talwit n tudert tamirant i aɣ-d-tefka tatiknulujit d usnulfu ussnan
d tuɣalin ɣer deffir i ɣ-yerran ɣer tudert n tallit n temharsa
nuɣal nḥemmed
rebbi iḍ d wass imi mazal ulawen-nneɣ kkaten wa tameddit ɣer yixxamen-nneɣ nemneɛ
nettuɣal yal
tettbin-iyi-d liḥala simmal tettiwɛir uɣalent twuɣa ttlaḥaqent-aɣ s ixxamen-nneɣ
mmi-s n umeddakkel-iw yettwanɣa ɣef umnar n uxxam nekk ad iyi-suffɣen deg tlemmast n yiḍ akken ad iyi-zzuɣren ur zriɣ sani
ad yester rebbi wa ad tt-yessuffeɣ ɛla xir
lḥiɣ acḥal n tmerwin n lmitrat mebla ma walaɣ acemma sdat-i
kecmen yiḍarren-iw deg tlemmast n yixjuḍen n waman d waluḍ qrib i yi-d-seɣlin
ageffur yeḥbes maca asemmiḍ mazal iteqqes
ur ttaggadeɣ ara ṭṭlam ur yessekcam ara deg wul-iw ccek s lmeqlub yettɣummu-yi ṭṭlam s yiwet n talwit yettarran talast i wallen n yiɛdawen
uɣent sakin wallen-iw tannumi d ṭṭlam uɣaleɣ leḥḥuɣ mebla uguren ttneggizen ɣef yiɛerriḍen i ttmagareɣ deg ubrid-iw
yelseq
yusef ɛeyyaci deg-i ad as-tiniḍ yuggad ad as-rewleɣ
inebbeh-iyi-d acḥal d abrid akken ur ɣelliɣ ara deg yixjuḍen n waman
yezga-d udcir ɣef yiwen n ugni d awesɛan ad k-id-tmager sakin yiwet n tkessart
ixxamen teɣli-d fell-asen tsusmi
amur ameqqran deg-sen ur ttwazdɣen ara acku urɛad yekfi lebni-nsen
ddaw n leḥyuḍ yettemḍeggar yijdi d yibeɛɛayen i ssexdamen i uheggi n ubiṭun
bedden sin-nni iɣummen udmawen-nsen ɣer tewwurt n lemraḥ n yiwen n uxxam mazal ur yekfi ara seg lebni yesɛa sin n yinnagen
yessuffeɣ-d yiwen deg-sen amesbaḥ n tsafut yessaɣ yis-s abrid
deg wannag amezwaru tama taẓelmaḍt tban-d ciṭuḥ n tafat deg taggara n tgennarit
yiwet n tzeqqa newrent-tt snat n tcemmaɛin sersen-tent ɣef lqaɛa n ssima deg snat n tɣemmar mqabalent daxel-is llan ukkuẓ n yirgazen qqimen ɣef tzerbiyin ttmeslayen
wwḍen-iyi-d leswat-nsen mi ttaliɣ ɣef usellum
tuɣ-iten ttraǧun deg-neɣ
mi newweḍ bedden sellmen fell-aneɣ
 ansuf s  ustad -nneɣ 

ɛiwden-as i tenfalit-a acḥal d abrid
yiwen deg-sen iwehha-yi-d anda iaq ad aɣeɣ amkan
sgerfleɣ deg tazwara acku issebbaḍen-iw bezgen s waluḍ
kkseɣ-ten rniɣ iqaciren ibezgen ḍeggreɣ sakin iman-iw ɣef wusu
tessaɛya-yi tikli
icebbeh-iyi rebbi dayen bdiɣ ttimɣureɣ ttuɣaleɣ d mmi-s n temdint uɣaleɣ ur zmireɣ ara i tikli mačči am zik
iluḥeq-iyi-d yusef yuɣ amkan tama-w
qqimeɣ rǧiɣ
sidreɣ i uqerruy-iw kra n lweqt akken ad ffreɣ tuggdi-inu
d nitni i yi-d-ssawlen d nitni ihi ara yebdun ameslay
refdeɣ allen-iw muqqleɣ deg udmawen-nni iɣef temɣi tamart tseqsayeɣ iman-iw 
anwa i irewlen seg lḥebs anwa i iẓedmen ɣef yimsulta 
acu yeḍran i umejjay  amek ad ddukklen deg wudmawen-agi tewɛer n tmenɣiwt d ucmummeḥ d taḍsa swayes i yi-d-mmagren  d imellayen gar-asen d iwɛiren ɣef yicenga-nsen
anwa-ten icenga-nneɣ s tidet  fell-as mačči taẓallit n rebbi
yesneḥneḥ yiwen n urgaz tamart tečča yakk udem-is yerreẓ tasusmi-nni
isemma yules-d i tenfalit n userḥeb yis-i
a nettɛuzzu-k mliḥ acku tbeddeḍ d amastan n lecyuxat-nneɣ imeqqranen
nwala tabɣest-inek mi ten-tḥuddeḍ ccil n wuguren imeqqranen i tmagreḍ d uqhar n yiqehharen i iḥekkmen deg tmeggraḍ n uɣref-agi lmumen ameskin
ahat tesseqsaḍ iman-ik ɣef ssebba i ɣ-yeǧǧan ad k-id-nawi armi d amkan-a  acku yeḍmen yernu nezmer ad nemmeslay amek i ɣ-yehwa
nessawel-ak-d akken ad k-nessenɛet tidet
tidet i iḥemmel sidi rebbi d umazan-ines tikerkas n yimesbaṭliyen-nni n yimsulta d lɛesker ara tečč tmes n
unazir ad ɣ-yessemneɛ rebbi seg-s
nekkni nessawal i lxir ur nḥemmel ara takriḍt
maca d adabu amesbaṭli i iḥettmen fell-aneɣ ad nerfed leslaḥ deg wudem-is
wagi d azref i ɣ-d-yefka rebbi akken ad nḥudd ɣef yiman-nneɣ
win yebdan d netta i iḍelmen
sɛeddaɣ mraw d ukkuẓ n wagguren deg unarraz deg sseḥra
yir amkan awer t-twaliḍ awer t-yessin ukafriw acu ad d-nini ɣef lmumen
tamnaḍt mazal ar tura deg-s later n lbumba tabelkamt i tesṭerḍeq fransa tamharsant yernu yezmer ula yir-izenẓaren-is udfen tafekka-nneɣ
izenẓaren i yeshelken imezdaɣ n temnaḍt-nni s waṭṭan n ukunsir
yessusem ciṭuḥ yebda aslaf i uččamar-is s ufus-is
sendeɣ aɛrur-iw ɣef lḥiḍ skecmeɣ iḍarren-iw cekkleɣ-ten am wakken xeddmeɣ asmi lliɣ d aqrur ameẓyan lemdeɣ leqran deg zzawiya ttqellibeɣ ɣef waddud iwatan heggaɣ iman-iw i usebleɛ n tidet-agi ara iyi-iḍegger umeqqran-nsen
ikemmel deg wawal-is 
maca ur d-usiɣ ara ɣer dagi ad mmeslayeɣ ɣef yiman-iw acku fkiɣ-tt d asfel i unezmar win i tt-ixelqen
tiɣawsiwin n ddunit uɣalent war azal ɣur-i
cceɣl-iw irkelli yuɣal d aḥebber amek ad rreɣ azal i tmurt-agi tamejruḥt i ḥekkmen iqehharen imṭurniyen yuklalen times n unazir ad ɣ-yessemneɛ rebbi seg-s
newwi-k-id ɣer dagi akken ad k-nemmeslay ɣef umeddakkel-nneɣ
yusef iɣef telliḍ d amastan ad t-iɛin rebbi wa ad t-yessuffeɣ seg twaɣit ideg yella
anagar netta i tesɛa yemma-s tamuḍint baba-s ad t-yerḥem rebbi yella deg terbaɛt-nni n umeɣras buyaɛli yesɛedda acḥal n yiseggasen deg lḥebs uqbel ad yemmet seg lɣiḍ d lḥesra ɣef tmurt-agi yeffɣen ɣef ubrid n rebbi
asmi yura yusef d i yukren amerḥum ameɣras ɛebdelkrim
buɛebdellah d nitni i t-yenɣan ḍeggren sakin tafekka-ines deg terga ur nebɛid ara ɣef wasif n sefsafa yenna-d tidet ur yeskadeb ara
d tidet i d-yenna acku d nekkni i as-tt-id-yefkan
ilaq ad teẓreḍ a ɛebdelkrim ur yelli ara seg yiserdasen-nneɣ
yella d amsenzu yeṭṭafaren ilugan n usɣan
gma-s i k-iqublen gma-tneɣ ɛebdelḥamid d tidet seg yirgazen-nneɣ ma d gma-s xaṭi
tura ad t-ǧǧeɣ ad k-d-yales taqsiḍt seg tazwara akken ad k-d-tbin tidet n yiqehharen-a yerran lmumnin yelhan ddaw n yiḍarren-nsen lbaṭel ɣef yimelsanen senkaren imdanen mgal dduɛat lmumnin am ttkellixen imsulta srusun lɛibad nekkni
yallah a gma ɛebdelḥamid mmeslay-d ales-as i ayen akk i tessneḍ
yembawel urgaz-nni i yeqqimen ɣer tama tazelmaḍt-ines iseggem tiɣimit-ines akken ad yebdu ameslay
d ilemẓi d uḍɛif tamart-is n kra n wussan kan
iseṭṭel aqerruy-is allen-is kecment ɣer daxel aɣenjur-is d aɣezzfan yettemcabi ɣer win n ufalku
yelsa aserwal n yiserdasen d ubalṭu n uglim yessers ɣef tgecrar-is tamekḥelt seg ssenf n kalacinkuf
seqsaɣ iman-iw leslaḥ-agi wwin-t-id seg uẓḍam-nni i xedmen mgal takamyunt-nni i d-yewwin imeḥbas  susmeɣ
acu lfayda ma seqsaɣ-t 
muqel a  ad k-d-iniɣ tidet ḥala tidet seg tazwara armi d taggara
ayen i d-yessuffeɣ yusef deg uɣmis d tidet meyya ɣef meyya
d imsulta i yenɣan gma
karim ad as-yeɛfu rebbi
ahat ad iyi-tiniḍ sken-iyi-d lberhan-ik ma tsedqeḍ
ɣur-neɣ anza nesɛa inigan
nekk yiwen deg-sen
aṭas yellan seg wat n udcir
tqebleḍ kečč d wigi iɣef tettmeslayeḍ ad tbeddem sdat n unezzarfu ad d-tefkem taggwa-nwen ass n ccreɛ 
yessekcem umeqqran-nsen yiwen n uzmumeg n usqecmeɛ ɣef yicenfiren-is 
ṣelli ɣef nnbi a
srugemteɣ tanfalit  taẓallit n rebbi fell-as  s laɛqel kan ulac win i as-yeslan
nessusem kra n lweqt dɣa ikemmel awal-is  iman-is yenna-yi-d s
sḥebseɣ-t nniɣ-as 
tettamneḍ taɣdemt n yiqehharen-agi  anezzarfu ameɣbun d taɛeljet kan deg yifessen-nsen
ad yeḥkem s wayen ara s-inin nitni
ɣas ṭṭuqten lehdur ɣef lbaṭel n teɣdemt deg tmurt-nneɣ maca ma ddukklent ccuruṭ n ustan yelhan anzaten d inigan yessefk ɣef unezzarfu ad yeḥkem s usaḍuf mačči s tsunḍiwin
yenna-d ɛebdelḥamid s wurnan 
 a  eǧǧ-iyi ad k-d-alseɣ d acu yeḍran s tidet gar gma d umsaltu fateḥ ben slama yellan d mmi-s n udcir-nneɣ yernu d ameddakkel n temẓi
gma yella d aḥeddad n lfeṭṭa isenneɛ yesnuzzu isɣunen n wureɣ d uẓref
deg tazwara yella d axeddam ɣer yiwen n uḥeddad n lfeṭṭa deg tama n umraḥ n yimeɣrasen deg tmanaɣt sakin yeffeɣ sɣur-s yekra-d yiwen n lmaḥel deg ssuq n lmiksik
seg wass-nni yeldi fell-as rebbi tiwwura n lxir tennerna tjara-ines s uxeddim yelhan i ixeddem yernu yeẓwer mliḥ deg lḥerfa-agi seg wasmi meẓẓey
yuɣal d asalel n twacult-nneɣ nnaɛma d lxir n sidi rebbi bdan tettbin-d fell-aneɣ limer mačči yir amdan-nni bu uɛebbuḍ i yeskecmen izerman ɣer wayla-nneɣ
ass-nni tuɣ-iyi daxel n lmaḥel mi d-yekcem ɣur-neɣ fateḥ akked yiwen n urgaz yenna-d d ameddakkel ɛziz fell-as lasel-is seg tmurt n leqbayel ixeddem yid-s d amsaltu
iṭij qrib ad yeɣli d lmeɣreb nhegga-d iman-nneɣ ad neɣleq taḥanut
mi yeqqim fateḥ yettqessir d gma karim walaɣ tawwurt yeldin ciṭuḥ ameddakkel-nni-ines yemdel
banen-d wurnan ɣef wudem-is
yenna-d fateḥ   wagi d ameddekkel ɛziz fell-i mliḥ yemma-s tewweḍ laɛfu n
rebbi teǧǧa-d deffir-s isɣunen iqdimen yebɣa ad ten-yessenz akken ad yessenfeɛ tawacult-is s yidrimen-is
dɣa nniɣ-as tanezzut-agi ḥala aḥbib-iw karim i yi-tecrek yid-s tagella d lmelḥ seg temẓi i as-izemren
nekkni ur nessin iqqiḥ ɣef wazal d ssuma n wureɣ d taẓeyt-ines
nuggad ma nruḥ ad nwali aḥeddad n lfeṭṭa niḍen ad ten-yaɣ fell-aneɣ s uzgen n ssuma n ssuq
ɣef waya i d-nezwar deg-k
kečč d argaz afeḥli d asendid ur tḥemmleḍ ara leḥram 
imir-n kan yessuffeɣ-d urgaz-nni seg lbalṭu-ines n uglim amendil yessers-it ɣef ukunṭwar n usɣar
iwala gma sselɛa yersen sdat-s  timeqyasin tizrarin timengucin d yiwen n uzrar qlilit tura lxedma-nni n zik
kra seg yisɣunen mazal-iten ttemcaɛalen d ijdiden ma wiyaḍ iban d iqdimen lsan-ten yakan
kra seg-sen yerreẓ neɣ yeɛwej
yenna-asen gma   tasmekta-a meqqret yernu nekk am wakken tezriḍ a fateḥ ttreqqiɛeɣ isɣunen ur ten-ttaɣeɣ ur ten-snuzuɣ 
yessekcem umeddakkel-nni iman-s yenna   ur k-d-nniɣ ara efk-iyi-d azal-nsen tura
s lɣerḍ-ik kan senz-iten sakin ad nemsefham
kečč d bab n wawal ur txeddɛeḍ ara
irgazen i yirgazen
d ameddekkel-iw fateḥ i yi-d-yewwin ɣur-k kečč tesneḍ-t mliḥ
ulac acu iḥaren ttruḥuɣ ɣer twacult-iw yiwet n tikkelt deg waggur ma zemreɣ 
yessusem gma kra n lweqt iɣezz icenfiren-is akka i ixeddem yal mi ara yettxemmim dɣa yenna-as   nemtafaq
efk-iyi-d ciṭuḥ n lweqt
sefqed-d fell-i seg tallit ɣer tayeḍ
yal mi ara senzeɣ kra deg-sen ad k-in-fkeɣ azal-nsen
akka i mtafaqen deg tazwara
urǧin i ɣ-yewwi ccek belli ureɣ-nni i sersen ɣer lwert maca d aglaf n tkurḍiwin n gma mačči d yixxamen

wehmeɣ mi sliɣ i yimeslayen-agi
qrib i sutreɣ seg
ɛebdelḥamid ad-iyi-yales tafyirt taneggarut
maca ulac acu xedmeɣ
s laɛqel kan a ɛebdelqader  iḍ mazal-it ɣezzif yernu mazal ad tesleḍ i yisallen ara k-yeswehmen
ǧǧiɣ-t ad ikemmel taqsiḍt-is 
ur tezzi ara ddurt tikkelt-nni ulac-iyi d gma i yi-d-yennan uɣalen-d yimsulta-nni deg sin yid-sen yedda-d yid-sen wis kraḍ yewwi-d yid-s amendil yeččur s yisɣunen n wureɣ d wuẓref
yenna-as-d fateḥ argaz-nni wis kraḍ yebɣa ad yessenz isɣunen n ɛemti-s d taǧǧalt i yenwan ad tẓur axxam n rebbi
imir-nni yebda ccek ikeccem gma
tameddit-nni yeḥka-yi-d ɣef uḥettet n fetḥi akken ad yejmeɛ gma ɣur-s isɣunen-nni ɣas ma mazal ur yessenz ara imezwura-nni i sen-yeǧǧa
yewwi-d ifukal ulac laman deg yisaganen n lkazirna n temsulta yezmer ad t-akren yernu isɣunen-a d lamana deg temgarḍt-is d ayla n yiwet n temɣart yessawḍen sat n tmerwin n yiseggasen deg laɛmer-is tebɣa ad tessizdeg iɣsan-is s lḥiǧ ɣer uxxam n rebbi
tebɣa ad tfareq ddunit-a wa ad tmager bab-is d tazedgant mebla ddunb
ɣas akken gma yumen taqsiḍt-nni yeǧǧa isɣunen-nni ɣur-s
yuɣal fateḥ d imezgi deg tḥanut
ad yessuget awal mebla lmeɛna sakin ad yesseqsi ɣef lamana i ǧǧan ɣer gma
karim d bab n wawal ur yessin ara lekdeb
d gma ssneɣ-t mliḥ
d netta i d ameqqran deg twacult-nneɣ d netta i d amedya-ines deg lewqama
kra n wussan umbaɛd yessaweḍ ad yessenz kra n yisɣunen yessuter deg fateḥ ad ixebber bab-is ad d-yas ad yawi azal-nsen
maca fateḥ yebɣa ad yessaweḍ idrimen-nni s timmad-is yewwi-as-d afukel tuffɣa seg lkazirna tuɣal tewɛer ɣef ẓẓedmat i iḍerrun mgal imsulta
yefka-as gma idrimen-nni mebla ma truḥ-d ɣer tidimi-s ad yeǧǧ ɣur-s lbayan d fateḥ i ten-yewwin
yuɣal-d fateḥ acḥal d abrid yettawi idrimen xas ma yella mačči d lḥaǧa meqqren
yiwen n wass usan-d yirgazen-nni mebla ma yedda yid-sen fateḥ sutren deg-s ad sen-d-yefk idrimen n wayen yenzan yakan
yenna-asen gma d amidaw-nsen i ten-yewwin
ur t-yumin ara uqbayli-nni
yessuter deg-s idrimen d areṭṭal ara yekkes umbaɛd mi isɣunen niḍen
yenna-as yeḥwaǧ mliḥ ara yessenz idrimen
yewwi-d afukel s yinig ɣer taddart-is deg tmurt n leqbayel u netta ulac acu yesɛa deg lǧib-is ulac ula adinar yernu tajernaḍt urɛad d-tekcim
s nnig n wul-is i yeqbel
yefka-as qrib yakk idrimen i yesɛa ass-nni
tameddit-nni yewweḍ-d s axxam yerfa ireggem deg
fateḥ
neffeɣ ad nadi fell-as deg uxxam-nsen
yenna-aɣ-d gma-s ur yekcim ara s axxam ugar n ddurt
tekres taluft yufa gma iman-is deg uwaɣiw
yeffeɣ-d wawal ussan-nni d akken aṭas n yixxamen i yettwakren deg yiḍ
imakaren-nni ttɣummun udmawen-nsen sexdamen timeẓyanin akken ad ḥettmen ɣef yimawlan n yixxamen ad sen-fken yakk ayen sɛan ama d idrimen neɣ d ureɣ
idrimen d yisɣunen d aya ayen yellan d afessas kan ɣlay wazal-is yernu yeshel i tuffra
yeḥka-yi-d gma ɣef uqelleq i t-yettaṭṭafen yal tikkelt mi ara ten-yesken i yimectariyen
yuggad ad mmeslayen medden ɣef lasel n yisɣunen-nni
iles n medden am tmes ur yettferriq ur iferren
tiyita deg yimdanen ɣef yilsawen-nsen tettazzal am tament deg ugerjum
sneɣseɣ seg tuggdi-ines nniɣ-as isɣunen yellan ɣur-s nessen imawlan-is  d imsulta
kkes aɣbel ur ttqelliq ara iman-ik
ɣelḍeɣ seg tazwara armi d taggara
kra n wussan umbaɛd s ugacur ɣef lɛecra n ssbeḥ mi ɛeddaɣ sdat n uxxam n twacult n fateḥ walaɣ-t yeffeɣ s temɣawla xmat-xmat s tuffra kan am wakken ur yebɣi ara ad imager ḥed deg ubrid-is
mi i yi-iwala ɛerqent-as yessekcem aqerruy-is gar tuyat-is yezmummeg azmumeg n ukaɛeb yuzzel-d ad iyi-iɛenneq yenna-yi-d acḥal i yefreḥ mi i yi-d-imuger
hedreɣ-as ɣef wayen i d-yekkan sɣur sin n yimeddukkal-is sutreɣ deg-s daɣen ad i yi-yessefhem ayɣer ur sen-yefki ara idrimen-nsen
yerra iman-is yewhem yeggul s uqerru n yemma-s tamuḍint belli lamana tewweḍ imawlan-is yewhem deg wayen yeḍran
maca ad ten-iwali kan ad yerr talast i wugur-a s temɣawla
sakin yewwi-d afukel s rrwaḥ-ines ɣer lkazirna dɣa nemfaraq
tikerkas banent ɣef wudem-is
ɣas akken umneɣ-t nniɣ-d gar-i d yiman-iw mačči sɣur-s ad d-yekk lexdeɛ d ameddakkel n temẓi-nneɣ d mmi-s n udcir-nneɣ
ahat ur yemsefham ara akked sin n yiberraniyen-nni
tameddit-nni iwala fateḥ gma deg tḥanut-is yessuter seg-s ssmaḥ ɣef wayen yexdem umeddakkel-is i yettmagaren aṭas n wuguren deg twacult-i is
ass-nni yeṭṭef gma rray ad yerr isɣunen-nni yimawlan-is
maca yesseqneɛ-it fateḥ ad ten-yeǧǧ ɣur-s yewweḍ armi i as-yessuter ad yurar amek i as-yehwa s ssuma-nsen
yenna-as yezmer ad yekkes ayen i as-yehwan seg ssuma n yisɣunen
sin n yirgazen-nni ur ssinen ara azal n wureɣ ihi yezmer ad yekkes ayen i as-yehwan seg yidrimen n tnezzut
ikemmel yenna-as ur yessin ara sin n yirgazen-nni ɣur-s netta d imidawen kan deg uxeddim ihi ur yeẓri ara ma tseḥḥa teqsiḍt-nsen ɣef lasel n wureɣ neɣ xaṭi
maca d tagnit i karim akken ad yerbeḥ ugar
tunzin d tiɣin d tanezzut u llsas n tnezzut d rrbeḥ
lmuhim fateḥ axabit yelsa talaba n umahaḍ yexdem ayen yezmer akken ad iqenneɛ gma ad ikemmel ccɣel yid-sen
yeṛgem-it ad as-yernu isɣunen-niḍen
d tidet ula d gma yewwi-t ciṭuḥ n ṭṭmeɛ ur yeẓri ara gar wuccanen i d-yeɣli
yuɣal netta i yettwassnen s leqniɛa iẓeṭṭ yir aẓeṭṭa
yessawel i wid yessen yakan seg yiḥeddaden n lfeṭṭa d wureɣ yebda yesnuzu-asen sselɛa yemyussaden deg usenduq-ines
yuɣal fateḥ yettas-d qrib yal ass ɣer tḥanut yettawi idrimen akken ad ten-yefk i yimawlan-nsen
lamana d ddin deg temgerḍt n yineslem
uccay-nni amḥili yuker lamana
nekk d gma nella neṭṭes ɣef sin n yimeẓẓuɣen-nneɣ ur nfaq s tidet almi i iɛedda lawan asmi d-yusa uqbayli-nni yessutur lḥeqq-is seg yidrimen
yusa-d s wurfan yennuɣ-aɣ tban-d ɣef wudem-is taɛdawit seg wasmi yezger amnar n tewwurt
yenna i gma   kečč teqqareḍ tefkiḍ idrimen i uxabit-nni netta yettgella ur yeṭṭif ula yiwen n udinar
anwa deg-wen i d-yeqqaren tidet  wagi d anguz mgal-i txaḍem-tt deg sin yid-wen
maca win ilaɛben yid-i ad ireɣ s tmes 
yessuffeɣ-d tameẓyant-ines yuggez-it s lmut ma ur as-yefki ara azal n yisɣunen deg yiwet n ddurt
yessuffeɣ-d gma tazmamt n leḥsabat yesken-as-d i uqbayli acḥal n yidrimen i as-yefka i fateḥ akken ad as-ten-yawi
yeggul urgaz-nni belli fateḥ ur as-yefki acemma
ɣas akken yefka gma i umsaltu-nni ayen i yesɛa ass-nni deg yidrimen akken ad as-yeṭṭixer wa ad as-yefk lehna am wakken iyi-d-yenna
sin n wussan umbaɛd yuɣal-d d urgaz wis kraḍ i d-yeɣlin fell-as s rregmat d waggaz s lmut
cerḍen fell-as sin n yirgazen-nni ad awin lḥeqq-nsen seg wazal n yisɣunen
yerra-d gma ɣef yiman-is yessuffeɣ-d ayen i as-yegran seg yisɣunen seg usenduq-ines yessuter deg-sen ad ten-awin
iberraniyen-nni ugin deg sin
ugar n waya yuggez uqbayil-nni gma yenna-as ad t-yessekcem ɣer lḥebs ɣef tkurḍa n yisɣunen
yenna-as aṭas n yiɣermanen i d-yusan s axxam n temsulta ccetkayen ɣef tkurḍa n yixxamen-nsen
bdan yisestanen akken ad ẓren anwa-ten yimakaren-agi
ad nwehhi kan akka ɣur-k alamma ẓeḍmen yimsulta ɣef tḥanut wa ad tt-qellben irkelli
acu ad asen-tiniḍ tasmekta-agi imir-n ma ufan ɣur-k tameqqrant n wureɣ  tameddit-nni yekcem-d karim s axxam yettergigi seg tuggdi
yeḥka-yi-d yakk ayen i as-yeḍran
sdat-s snat n ledwar kan akken ad yerr i sin n yirgazen-nni ayen yakk i as-ttallasen
d acu ara nexdem 
nxemmem ad neɣleq taḥanut alamma nwala fateḥ ahat yezmer ad ten-yerr ɣer ubrid
iḍ-nni nfaq belli ureɣ-nni d takerḍa i yettwaker u sin n yimsulta-nni akked fateḥ d nitni i d imakaren
summreɣ ɣef karim ad iruḥ ad iwali akumisar n temsulta ad as-yales kulci
maca mi nxemmem mliḥ nufa asummer-agi ur iwulem ara
kraḍ n yimsulta ad bedden mgal-nneɣ
awal-nsen mgal awal-nneɣ
ugar n waya isɣunen yellan ɣer gma deg tḥanut d anza mgal-is
d ayen yenɣa-t ccreɛ
neɣli deg yiwen n uwaɣiw ameqqran ur neẓri ara amek ad nefsi lexyuḍ-is
yeṭṭef karim rray ad yessenz isɣunen-nni ɣer wid yessen seg yiḥeddaden neɣ imsenza n wureɣ ur nesɛi lekwaɣeḍ yettilin deg kra n yizenqan n tmanaɣt
kraḍ n wussan d tazzla deg leswaq-nni uffiren
sselɛa teɣleb imsaɣen
ureɣ ur yettnuz ara s sshala labaɛda win yettwaxedmen yakan win ur nesɛi ara ṭṭabeɛ neɣ win ur nesɛi tifaṭurin i ɣ-d-yemmalen seg wansi i d-yusa
iqelleb daɣen ɣef tenmeslin n yiḥeddaden akken ad sen-yessenz isɣunen i usefsi-nsen iwakken ad sen-ɛiwden ṣṣenɛa s wadda
maca ur yufi ara amsaɣ ɣas ssuma-nnsen rxiset
am wakken yeṭṭuqet unadi deg tserglin n yimsulta i d-yennernan s waṭas uɣalent d amihi ɣef win yettawin yid-s isɣunen mebla tifaṭurin
yenna-yi-d acḥal d abrid i yemneɛ s lqeḍra n
rebbi
ttalin yiɣallen n laman ɣer lkar ad bdun aqelleb deg tbalizin n yiminigen
ad sidren seg lkar wid ideg yella ccek ttawḍen alamma nudan acu yellan deg lejyubat-nsen
maca karim yesɛa zzher yesɛa ssifa yettlus mliḥ yetseṭṭil tamart-is yal tasebḥit
d leɛwayed i yelmed asmi yella d axeddam ɣer yiwen n uḥeddad i as-yesḥefḍen amek ilaq ad yemmeslay d yimsaɣen d wamek ilaq ad ten-imager tuget deg-sen d tilawin ɣef waya ur ttarran ara i ɣur-s lbal mi ara bdun anadi
sin n yimsulta-nni zgan-d ttasen-d ɣer tḥanut-is yal tikkelt ttemyuṭṭafen deg wawal tirdayin d waggazen simmal ttimɣuren
fateḥ ur iban ara irkelli ad as-tiniḍ tessebleɛ-it lqaɛa
nettruḥu qrib yal ass s axxam n twacult-is
yenna-aɣ-d yiwen seg lǧiran-is yuɣal ixeddem deg temnaḍt n bumerdas yettas-d s axxam s tuffra yettɣimi kan kra n tsaɛtin deg uzal neɣ deg yiḍ
tewweḍ tifidi s iɣes yekfa-as ssber i karim
mi yeḥma wawal gar-asen iqubel-iten s tidet taqerḥant
yenna-asen  d kunwi i d imakaren i iẓedmen ɣef yixxamen n medden deg yiḍ tettakrem isɣunen
ulac acu ad wen-d-fkeɣ anagar sselɛa yettwakren teǧǧam ɣur-i
hatta yessuffeɣ-itt yessers-itt ɣef ukunṭwar n usɣar
awit-tt xedmet yi-s acu i wen-yehwan
ayen yaɛnan idrimen n yisɣunen i ssawḍeɣ ad senzeɣ ad ten-tafem ɣer umidaw-nwen fateḥ
d netta yellan gar-aneɣ msefhamet yid-s
nekk gar-i d sidi rebbi kulci yesfa
fkiɣ-as yakk idrimen
ad yeched rebbi ḥala amur-iw i yi-d-isaḥen seg tnezzut i wwiɣ la kter wala aqel
maca d wumi tettmeslayeḍ  rdin gma belli yettemsefham d mmis n udcir-ines fateḥ
yenna-as gma fateḥ iɣab irkelli ɣef udcir atan tura deg lkazirna yid-sen
imir-n i as-nnan tidet uznen-t ɣer temnaḍt-niḍen ur ẓrin ara amek ad awḍen ɣur-s
yenna-asen gma  i tura tebɣam ad t-sseɣliɣ seg yigenni  yerra-as-d yiwen seg sin n yirgazen-nni  ḍebber aqerruy-ik nekkni d i nebɣa
yenna gma  awit idrimen-nwen aneft-iyi neɣ ma ulac ad ggalleɣ s rebbi ad ruḥeɣ ɣer uwkil n tegduda ad ccetkiɣ yis-wen
isuɣ idrimen-nneɣ fell-as umsaltu-nni aqbayli yestaɛref deg wawal-is s wayen yellan   tura imi teẓriḍ tidet aql-ik imir-a d acrik yid-neɣ s usenz n wureɣ yettwakren
ma teldiḍ imi-k ad k-nekkes seg ddunit-agi uqbel mi ara tebdu tsestant yid-neɣ
ur tettu ara d imsulta i nella yewɛer ad ɣ-tesbibbeḍ tikurḍa yezmer ur tettafeḍ ara yiwen ad k-yamnen
keččini ur tesɛiḍ ula yiwen n wanza mgal-neɣ
nekkni ur k-nissin ur nesɛi yid-k assaɣ
sdat-k sin n yiberdan ulac wis kraḍ  ad aɣ-d-tefkeḍ idrimen-nneɣ neɣ ad k-neṭṭef atiki deg yinig amezwaru yettawin ɣer unazir
ur netturar ara s tudert-nneɣ ɣef yiɣsan-a ur nqebbel ula aqjun amellaẓu
ad nuɣal ɣur-k azekka tameddit ad t-neḥseb d alɣu aneggaru
sakin ad taɛqel faḍma argaz-is 
 azekka-nni ur yeldi ara karim taḥanut-is
yunag ɣer tmanaɣt limmer ad yaf tifrat ɣer yiḥeddaden i yessen
mebla lfayda
yuɣal-d tameddit-nni yaɛya yuyes
yeẓra aggaz n yimakaren-nni mačči d awal i yettawi waḍu ladɣa mi ifaq i uffir-nsen d waggaz-ines ad ten-yekcef i lɛamma
neffeɣ deg tlemmast n ṭṭlam neqseḍ axxam n
fateḥ
ur t-nufi ara
yuɣal ur yettẓuru ara aṭas tawacult-is
yexdem-itt ufuḥan yedreg ɣef wallen
deg tallit-nni tennulfa-d tarbaɛt tamezwarut n tradsa tineslemt i usellek deg udcir n  brarik 
lliɣ yiwen seg yimeltaɣen-ines
nella taserdasant tamezwarut akken ad nerr ɣef uqhar n terbaɛt n yiserdasen i iḥekmen tamurt d yiqeddacen-ines i iḍeggren atmaten-nneɣ deg yinarrazen n sseḥra
ussan-nni bdan iwumi sserḥen dɣa ttawḍen-d tigawt-nneɣ imezwura nettheggi imeḥbas imir-n ḥekkun-aɣ-d ɣef yir tegnatin n ddel i ɛacen deg leḥbus-a imenɛulen
tiṭ s tiṭ tuɣmest s tuɣmest win i ibdan d netta i iḍelmen
tusa-d tegnit i nettgani
dɣa xemmemeɣ amek ad rreɣ ttar n gma karim
ilaq ad nneɣ sin n yimsulta-nni
ad nawi ttwab berdayen ma yebɣa rebbi
ad nekkes seg lumma-nneɣ sin n yiqehharen d sin n yimakaren
ma d fateḥ ad nesɛu yid-s imeslayen niḍen
mmeslayeɣ-d d watmaten-iw deg lbaḍna dɣa nemsefham ad asen-nendi tacerket i sin n yimsulta-nni deg uḥanu n uzniq ideg tella taḥanut n karim
qenɛeɣ gma ad yeldi taḥanut-ines wa ad yefk ttiɛad i sin n yirgazen-nni ɣer lmeɣreb
ssneɣ yakan yiwen deg-sen ad t-ɛeqleɣ s sshala
qqimeɣ din ttawiɣ ttarraɣ gar lɣaci ttrajuɣ tisin-nsen
ssuq n  lmiksik  yezga yeččur s yimsaɣen
ddmeɣ yid-i tameẓyant tutumatikt ffreɣ-tt deg lǧib n ubalṭu-inu
sɛeddaɣ lɛesker-inu ssneɣ amek ad sxedmeɣ leslaḥ
ur nesɛi ara zzher d aqbayli i d-yusan iman-is
ɛeqleɣ-t seg tmuɣli tamezwarut
ileḥḥu s laɛqel ulac acu yuggad deg umkan-nni
deg uḥanu n uzniq yeqqim yettmuqul sselɛa yettufesren deg tḥuna neɣ ɣef ubrid
frant deg uqerruy-is ad yawi iferren tiɣawsiwin ara d-yaɣ
ḍefreɣ-t seg deffir ibedd sdat n yiwen n uɛemmur n yirkasen inaddalen yersen ɣef yiwen n ugertil d amerku yekna yeddem-d tayuga tamellalt seg ssenf n  adidas  yedba yettmassa yettqellib deg-s s yifassen-is sakin yesseqsa umsenzu ɣef ssuma-s
fuṛseɣ tagnit-a mi yella yettmeslay suffɣeɣ-d tameẓyant qqerseɣ fell-as snat n tersasin deg waɛrur ɣer tama n wul am idrimen sɣur gma yebda yakan wakken i yi-iweṣṣa gma-tneɣ ɛebdeljebbar
yessusem ciṭuḥ imuqel ɣer tama n umeqqran-nsen i yebdan awal deg temlilit-nneɣ dɣa faqeɣ d netta i yeqseḍ
ssut n tersasin yessefqeɛ imsewqen
iɛedda fell-asen kan uzaylal faqen i wayen yeḍran yekker uhruḥu bdan medden tazzla ɣer yal tanila
imsenza-nni n ubrid bdan jemmɛen sselɛa-nsen s temɣawla rewlen irkelli ɣef ssuq
ula d nekk ur ɛeṭṭleɣ ara
tebteɣ yemmut umsaltu-nni kkseɣ-as tameẓyant-ines d rrsa yellan ɣur-s ɣawleɣ s tazzla ɣer umkan iɣef nemsefham yakan deg timlilit tuffirt
deg yiḍ-nni ur nsiɣ ara deg uxxam
maca azekka-nni yenna-aɣ-d yiwen seg yimeltaɣ n tuddsa-nneɣ wid yettɛassan u jemɛen isallen belli taḥanut n gma teqqim teɣleq s ṭul n wass
deg yiḍ nefdeɣ s axxam-nneɣ akken ad weṣṣiɣ gma ad yuɣal ɣer uxeddim akken ur tcukkun ara deg-s
aɣlaq n tḥanut ad yeslal ccek ɣur medden
maca yessefhem-iyi karim mi iyi-d-yenna xedmeɣ yiwen n ugul d ameqqran acku yiwen n umsaltu kan i nɣiɣ mačči deg sin yid-sen
wis sin mazal-it yedder
sɣur-s ad yekk ccer
ad iɛas iman-is acku yeẓra seg wansi i d-tusa tiyita
iban ḥala ttar ara d-yerr
turda-agi teffeɣ yakk aqerruy-iw
ad staɛrfeɣ belli mi qrib ad jebdeɣ ɣef umsaltu-nni ur xemmemeɣ ara ula ddqiqa ɣer temsalt n gma bɣiɣ kan ad sferḥeɣ el-amir-nneɣ ɛebdeljebbar
d netta i iqeblen ad xedmeɣ tuɣḍaḍt-a tuɣdimt ɣef waya yessefk fell-i ur ttuɣaleɣ ara xayeb skerkireɣ deffir-iw lihana n truẓi
uɣaleɣ aqerruy-iw deg yigenni zzuɣureɣ tarennawt akken ad skecmeɣ tarbaɛt-nneɣ deg trebbuyaɛ n tredsa reffun reggmen
ttɛeggiḍen tineslemt ittḥerkilen deg wannar
zrin kra n wussan d urkiden
umbaɛd n leɣyab n kra n wussan ɣef uxeddim imi ulac win i yesteqsan fell-as ula d imsulta ur zzin ara yakk ɣef tḥanut-is yeldi karim taḥanut-ines
yuggad seg tririt n ttar
deg tallit-nni uɣaleɣ ur gganeɣ ara deg uxxam n yimawlan-iw
yuɣal-d uẓḍam-nni n yiḍ ɣer udcir-nneɣ
imsulta  imestal  azgen deg-sen ɣummen udmawen-nsen yewɛer ad ten-tɛeqleḍ
ttnadin ɣef watmaten-nneɣ
ttqelliben ixxamen seqsayen iɛeggalen n twaculin
ayen yessewhamen ur ḥbisen ara maḍi ɣer uxxam-nneɣ
ur lliɣ ara d aferdis amihaw yettwassnen ɣur-sen
urǧin kecmeɣ lḥebs
gma yettaṭṭaf kan taɛebbuḍt-is seg ẓẓeḍmat-a n yiḍ
tikwal yesmenyif ad yeṭṭes deg tḥanut-is
acḥal d abrid i ixemmem ad yinig ɣer temdint niḍen ad yeldi taḥanut i usenzi n wureɣ deg tmanaɣt neɣ deg blida
maca azal n lekra n tḥuna yewweḍ s igenni times-ines tesraɣay seg lebɛid
ziɣ tuggdi n gma tebna ɣef sseḥ
yiwen n yiḍ tusa-d tarbaɛt n yimjelkaḍen n unagraw tewwi-t yid-s
ur nudan axxam ur seqsan ula yiwen deg-neɣ
sutren deg-s ad yeffeɣ
wekkden-aɣ yiɣbula-nneɣ deg udcir mačči d tamsulta i t-yewwin deg yiḍ-nni am wakken ur tekcim ula d yiwen n uxxam
tekcem ṭumubil tunsibt n temsulta ɣer udcir ɣef ṭnac n yiḍ teḥbes sdat n uxxam-nneɣ
ffɣen-d seg-s sin n yirgazen lsan iselsa n terbaɛt n unekcum aruradan ɣummen udmawen-nsen s yini aberkan
yenna-d baba deg tazwara yesla i tiyita s zzur ɣef tewwurt n wuzzal sakin yesla sin n yiberdan i yisem n ɛebdelkrim
buɛebdellah
bedden yirgazen-nni ɣef umnar n tewwurt ur kcimen ara daxel
walan kan karim yeṭṭef-it yiwen n umsaltu seg yiɣil ad as-tiniḍ yessen-it yakan idegger-it daxel n ṭumubil yesrugmet kra n waggazen
yewweḍ-iyi-d lexbar tanezzayt n uzekka-nni
imir-n kan faqeɣ takerḍa-ines ur tesɛi ara assaɣ d umennuɣ mgal n rrebrab am wakken i d-qqaren acku ad qellben fell-i ula d nekk
ma d karim d amsenzu n wureɣ yebɛed mliḥ ɣef umennuɣ aserti
ayɣer ad t-ddmen deg yiḍ  ɣef temsulta ad truḥ kan ɣer tḥanut-is ideg yettɣimi s ṭul n wass wa ad t-tawi sdat n medden
maca ur texdim ara akka acku niyya-ines ur tesfi ara
walaɣ baba deg tazwara n uzal sutreɣ deg-s ad iruḥ ad yesseqsi fell-as deg uxxam n temsulta
nnan-as-d ur ṭṭifen ara albaɛḍ s yisem-agi
yuɣal-d xayeb
baba d ameɣbun teqher-it ddunit
yesɛedda ddunit-is d axemmas deg lfirmat yettaɣ tajernaḍt tamecṭuḥt maḍi
anagar taɣiwant i yessen seg tedbelt
ɣef waya ulac acu i d-yenna i umsaltu i as-yennan ur sḥebsen ara albaɛḍ s yisem i yebder
ukkuẓ n wussan umbaɛd usan-d yimsulta deg ṭumubil tunsibt ɣer uxxam-nneɣ ɣef lɛecra n ssbeḥ ttnadin ɣef karim buɛebdellah amsenzu n wureɣ
ḥala yemma i yellan deg uxxam
tenna-asen mmi-s karim atan d ameḥbus ɣur-sen tusa-d temsulta tewwi-t deg yiḍ
deg tazwara yewhem umsaltu-nni sakin yenna-as temsulta ur tettawi ara imdanen deg yiḍ ḥala ma llan d ineḍliben imerwalen
yessefhem-as ttnadin ɣef ɛebdelkrim buɛebdellah d aḥeddad n lfeṭṭa deg tlemmast n temdint
ruḥen deg tazwara ɣer tḥanut-ines maca ufan-tt teɣleq dɣa usan-d ad nadin fell-as deg uxxam-is
ḥwaǧen-t deg yiwet n tsestant ɣef tkurḍa n yisɣunen
tenna-asen yemma i tikkelt tis snat tusa-d yakan yiwet n terbeɛt n temsulta am nitni deg tlemmast n yiḍ tewwi-t yid-s
seg yiḍ-nni ur iban ara lexbar-is
amsaltu-nni yeǧǧa-as kan taseɣra ɣef yisem n gma yenna-as yessefk fell-as ad iruḥ s temɣawla ɣer uxxam n temsulta
yemma ur tefhim acemma
mi ruḥeɣ ad tt-waliɣ deg yiḍ-nni ufiɣ-tt tettwanɣeḍ ur teḥbis ara seg yimeṭṭawen
anwa-ten wigi i yewwin karim ma mačči d imsulta  tamsulta tebḍa d tirebbuyaɛ
wid i d-yusan deg uzal ttgensisen tuddsa tunsibt
ma d iminigen n yiḍ ttekkan deg terebbuyaɛ iwumi ssawalen tirebbuyaɛ n umennuɣ mgal rrebrab i ṭṭafaren taɣellist taserdasant
deg tnezzayt n uzekka-nni tuɣal-d tarbaɛt-nni s timmad-is tnuda yakk axxam
ulac acu ufan
sutren tisura n tḥanut
tqelleb fell-asent deg leǧyub n yiselsa n karim tefka-asen tisura-nni
kra n tsaɛtin umbaɛd uɣalen-d s axxam wwin-d yid-sen imsulta niḍen nudan-t i tikkelt tis snat s telqi
baba tuɣ-it deg uxxam imir-n wwin-t yid-sen
neẓra umbaɛd mi nudan taḥanut n karim ufan ayen d-yegran seg yisɣunen yettwakren
yuɣal gma d amaker n yisɣunen neɣ d amɛiwen n yimakaren imi d netta i ten-yesnuzun
deg lmeɣreb sserḥen-as i baba usan-d ad nadin fell-i
mi ur iyi-ufan ara weṣṣaɣ-ten ad inin ruḥeɣ ɣer fransa ad xedmeɣ wwin deg umkan-iw gma ameẓyan ur nessaweḍ ara mraw d semmus n yiseggasen deg laɛmer-is
yesɛedda umeɣbun aḥric ameqqran n yiḍ deg tririt ɣef yiseqsiyen-nsen
bɣan ad ẓren ma iwala kra n yimdanen ttruḥun ɣer karim neɣ ma yella acu i as-ǧǧan
gma ameẓyan yeltha kan s leqraya-ines ur yeẓri tigert ɣef lecɣal-nneɣ nekkni s yimeqqranen
azekka-nni wwin yemma d uletma tameqqrant akken ad tent-seqsin s ṭul n wass
nnan-as i yemma ufan deg tḥanut n mmi-s isɣunen yettwakren
sseknen-ten i yimawlan-nsen i ten-ɛeqlen d ayla-nsen
asali-agi yesṭenṭen yemma ɣas akken ur tekni ara sdat n waggazen-nsen
maca tuɣal-d s axxam tettwanɣeḍ allaɣ-is yerwi
amenzu-ines win swayes tettzuxxu s ttrebga-ines tunnigt yuɣal d amakar yesnuzu isɣunen yettwakkren  tugi ad tamen s usali-agi
ur as-nniɣ ara tidet
qenɛeɣ-tt mi s-nniɣ ahat kellxen-as i karim
ahat d yiwen n umdan i yeǧǧan ɣur-s isɣunen-nni akken ad ten-yessenz
imsulta ur ḥbisen ara ahewwej d uluɛej deg twacult-iw
usan-d acḥal d abrid ama deg yiḍ ama deg uzal
tikwal seqsayen kan ɣef gma yellan d amerwal deg wallen-is tikwal ttnadin axxam ladɣa deg yiḍ
ulac acu zemreɣ ad xedmeɣ
uɣaleɣ deg tama niḍen beddeɣ mgal-nsen
uggadeɣ ma ruḥeɣ ad sen-mmeslayeɣ ɣef sin n yimsulta-nni ladɣa win i ssneɣ i nɣan deg yiwen n umkan ur nebɛid ara ɣef tḥanut n gma ad d-tuɣal tiyita-nni fell-i
yuzzel wawal deg udcir karim ittekka deg tkurḍa n yixxamen
bdan yilsawen snulfuyen timucuha sɣur-sen suffuɣen-d turdiwin
anwa ara yilin d acrik-is ma mačči d gma-s ɛebdelḥamid  d nekk i yuɣalen d amaker deg wallen n wat udcir-nneɣ timsulta tuɣal tettqellib fell-i tezga tẓeddem ɣef uxxam-nneɣ
mi sen-yenna baba ɣer fransa i unageɣ ulayɣer ad nadin fell-i yerra-as yiwen n umsaltu   ur skidib ara fell-aneɣ d amɣar i telliḍ d lɛib fell-ak
amek ad yinig mmi-k ɣer
fransa netta ur yesɛi ara arrat n yinig neɣ
ur nufi ara isem-is deg uzmam n warraten n yinig
ɣur-neɣ nekkni mmi-k ɛebdelḥamid yuli s adrar akked gma-s
karim yedda d yirebraben
jemɛen idrimen akken ad ten-fken i trebbuyaɛ timselḥin i tiɣin n leslaḥ d tmenɣiwt n yimelsanen
maca ur ttɛeṭṭilen ara ad ɣlin gar yifassen-nneɣ yessider baba i uqerruy-is yessusem
d acu yezmer ad d-yini sdat n tmacint-a i imeḥqen kulci sdat-s yernu ulac acu yeffren  kra n wussan umbaɛd yeɣli-d fell-aneɣ usali am ssaɛqa
ufan-d karim yettwanɣa tafekka-ines tettuḍegger deg yiwen n umdun deg wasif n
ssefsaf
tafekka-ines tentuter
d yiwen n ukerraz i tt-yufan s ugacur
nekk ẓriɣ d amsaltu wis kraḍ s lemɛawna n fateḥ i yewwin karim nɣan-t ḍeggren sakin tafekka-ines deg umkan-a
imir-n kan ṭṭfeɣ rray ad nɣeɣ fateḥ ɣas yeffer deg uɛebbuḍ n yemma-s
ad t-nɛass yal ass sani ara iruḥ  ad t-nessuffeɣ seg tiṭ n yiblis wa ad as-nsew ilili n lexdeɛ
karim yella d amsenzu aḥesbi yettɛawan tawacult-ines yettẓalla lewqat-is sakin yekcem-d fell-as
yiblis-nni ad t-yessames wa ad yessames isem n twacult-nneɣ deg taggara ad t-ineɣ yir tamenɣiwt
uɣalen medden heddren yir lehdur ɣef twacult-nneɣ tettwaḥqer
ulac lɛib deg tgullelt maca takerḍa d teḥraymit d lɛar ara tezzuɣreḍ i lebda
uliɣ s adrar ḍefreɣ abrid n lǧihad akken ad saliɣ ccan-is maca tardayt-a n uẓḍam ɣef yixxamen d tkerḍa n yidrimen d yisɣunen tessames isem n twacult-nneɣ deg wallen n wat udcir
bɣiɣ seg teqsiḍt-agi i k-d-ḥkiɣ ad rreɣ azal i yisem n gma d twacult-iw ad as-yaɛfu rebbi wa ad t-yessekcem ɣer lǧennet-ines
yusef yewǧed akken ad ttemɛawanen wali d acu ad ɣ-tessumreḍ
kečč d amastan aqdim tuɣeḍ tannumi tettafeḍ tiwwura i temsal iwaɛren 
yeḥbes ɛebdelḥamid seg wallus n teqsiḍt n gma-s
nessider yakk iqerra-nneɣ yal yiwen sani i iruḥ uqerruy-is
ad staɛerfeɣ wehmeɣ seg wayen sliɣ ɣas ma ẓriɣ yakan deg twuri-inu ayen yessewhamen ugar
maca taddukkli n yimsulta akken ad sbedden tarbaɛt n yimakaren i iẓedmen ɣef yixxamen mačči d lḥaǧa s wayes nezmer ad namen s sshala
ẓriɣ imsulta ur llin ara d imdanen izedganen i yettḥaraben ɣef usaḍuf mačči d tagi i d tamuɣli-inu tuget deg-sen d ilmeẓyen ffɣen i ubrid xeddmen kra n tigawin zemrent ad glunt s yiqerra-nsen
ẓran seg tazwara tawuri n temsulta mačči d tin isehlen zemren ad ǧǧen ula d tirwiḥin-nsen
tikti-agi tebɛed fell-i am wakken tebɛed lqaɛa ɣef yigenni
ttwassnen yirgazen-a s yidrimen irebḥen s iberdan niḍen am tukksa n yidrimen sɣur yimawlan n yikumya yettawin sselɛa d yinehharen n lkiran d yiṭaksiyen mebla lekwaɣeḍ neɣ awway n yidrimen mgal tiririt n wuragen n tenhert i sen-ttekksen yimidawen-nsen ma xedmen agul deg ubrid
kra ttawḍen ttḥuddun ɣef yimsenza n lehyuf ama d lbarunat neɣ yimsenza imeẓyanen mgal tajɛelt
ayen yaɛnan takerḍa n yixxamen ur nesli ara yis-s uqbel
ɣas akken
iɣawel ad iyi-d-yerr ad as-tiniḍ ihegga-d tiririt-ines friɣ-tt d yiman-iw ad kemmleɣ tasestant-inu akked ukumisar n temsulta
iban ɣur-s kra n yisallen ur ten-itteffer ara ɣef umeddakkel-is amastan
yessak-iyi-d umeqqran-nsen mi d-yenna 
acu d-tenniḍ 
refdeɣ tamuɣli-inu ɣur-s huzzeɣ aqerruy-is s laɛqel dɣa nniɣ-as 
tamsalt tekres mliḥ lexyuḍ-is d izerman i izemren ad ɣ-qqsen
yakan 
ur tettruẓu ara aqerruy-ik s gma-tneɣ ɛebdelḥamid
d yiwen seg yiserdasen-nneɣ
nekkni abrid-nneɣ nefren-it yakan neẓra ama ad nerbeḥ neɣ ad nemmet
maca nebɣa ad tesbeggneḍ i lɛamma inɣayen n yimsulta mgal n yimelsanen
neqqen sakin sefḍen inɣayen-nsen deg yiččumar-nneɣ
keččini tḥuddeḍ yakan ɣef lecyuxat-nneɣ teẓriḍ d acu lbaṭel i d-sseɣlin fell-asen d tirdayin i sen-selsqen ttuḍeggren tura deg leḥbus-nsen deg lbaṭel
nezmer ad nessuffeɣ alɣu ideg ad nini d imjelkaḍen-agi i yenɣan ɛebdelkrim buɛebdellah maca ulac win ara ɣ-yamnen
nekkni d aḥric deg umennuɣ-a ayen ara d-nini ad yettwaḥseb d ddiɛaya akken ad nessames icenga-nneɣ
maca keččini ay amastan mi ara tbeddeḍ deg teɣdemt wa ad temmeslayeḍ s ttbut ad tales tɣamsa i yimeslayen-ik bɣiɣ ad d-iniɣ taɣamsa tagraɣlant mačči isebtar-a yumsen i ɣ-ferrqen yal tanezzayt
aɣmis aneggaru yesɛan leqder d win anda yella ixeddem yusef maca gedlen tuffɣa-ines ɣelqen tiwwura-ines umbaɛd n usuffeɣ n umagrad-nni
nettwali nezmer ad nexdem aya u lfayda-ines ma yebɣa
rebbi ad d-tuɣal fell-aneɣ irkelli s lxir ameqqran
imuqel-iyi-d s yiwet n tmuɣli tuqsiḥt d uzmmumeg n trennawt
yessusem yurǧa tiririt
tasusmi tɛeṭṭel tikkelt-a mačči am tikkal niḍen
sidreɣ i uqerruy-iw qqimeɣ ttxemmimeɣ ẓriɣ allen-nsen irkelli ɣur-i i ttmuqulent imeẓẓuɣen-nsen ttraǧun kan acu ad d-iniɣ
deg taggara refdeɣ allen-iw i tikkelt tis snat ɣer ɛebdeljebbar-agi nniɣ-as 
am wakken i wen-d-nniɣ yakan tamsalt-a tekres akken ad as-naf tifrat tlaq-aɣ tazrawt s telqi
wali tamsalt-a s laɛqel-ik a  siwel i yusef d
ɛebdelḥamid melmi i k-yehwa akken ad k-d-fken isallen i teḥwaǧeḍ
ṭṭef lweqt i k-ilaqen maca efk-aɣ-d tifrat iwulmen
lmuhim ɣur-neɣ ad d-tbin tidet
taflest n tredsa-nneɣ deg-k d tameqqrant
yesneḥneḥ ibedd s laɛqel kan isenned ɣef tmekḥelt-is
tekfa temlilit yewweḍ-d lawan n umfaraq
beddeɣ ula d nekk senndeɣ ɣef aɣrab
ḥulfaɣ i uḍar-iw ayeffus i ttiɣ yedubbez
qrib i ɣliɣ
isellem fell-i s leḥrara yeffeɣ ḍefren-t yirgazen-is umbaɛd mi iweṣṣa ɛebdelḥamid ad iyi-yessaweḍ
yerǧa-yi uneggaru-agi i yeqqimen d yusef armi lsiɣ iqaciren d yissebbaḍen-inu dɣa neffeɣ seg umkan-nni
yekkes ṭṭlam tban-d tafat n tefrara i d-yusan s umured
nelḥa acḥal n tmerwin n lmitrat deg tsusmi sakin yefka-yi-d yusef ɛeyyaci yiwet n tuttra ahat tessenejla fell-as iḍes i ucḥal n wuḍan 
d acu tenniḍ ma ruḥeɣ ɣer temsulta ad randiɣ
ḥebseɣ tikli
beddeɣ lmendad n yusef ṭṭfeɣ-t seg tuyat-is nniɣ-as 
ruḥ-d ɣur-i azekka neɣ seldazekka s axxam ad nwali jmiɛ tamsalt-a
ikemmel awal-is am wakken ur yesli ara i tririt-inu 
ad sen-iniɣ wid iẓeḍmen ɣef tkamyunt n yimeḥbas d nitni i yi-yeṭṭfen ɣur-sen s yiɣil s ṭul n wussan-a
acu tenniḍ a  ad amnen taqsiḍt-inu mebla ma sɛeddan-iyi deg ssikkis am wakken i yi-xedmen tikkelt yezrin 
tban-d tuggdi deg tergagayt n taɣect-is d tmuɣli-ines
ɛerḍeɣ ad t-id-heddneɣ s wawalen iɛeddan ɣef uqerruy-iw
deg tilawt lliɣ ɛyiɣ nuɣnaɣ bɣiɣ ad qqimeɣ weḥd-i
sɛiɣ tura kra n yisallen imihawen zemren ad glun s uqerruy-iw ma kecfeɣ-ten
ssneɣ irebraben ẓriɣ anda ttilin
am wakken ẓriɣ anwa i yenɣan amsaltu-nni
deg usaḍuf ma ur bdireɣ ara ismawen-nsen yettwaḥseb d tirmeggit zemreɣ ad kecmeɣ ɣer lḥebs ɣef waya
ma ur yefḍiḥ ara walbaɛḍ ɣef wanɣa yettwaḥseb d anɣa
ḥulfaɣ i uqraḥ n uqerru i yessneɣsen seg yiẓri-w am wakken yessexreb tikta-inu
ulseɣ-as i yusef akken ad d-yuɣal ɣur-i s axxam sakin sutreɣ deg-sen ad uɣalen ɣer uglat-nsen nekk kemmleɣ abrid-iw ɣer uxxam-inu s yisuraf iẓayanen deg tidmi-w ttemyewwatent tikta am lemwaji deg ugaraw iḥecren
ɣas akken bɣiɣ ad ṭṭseɣ allen-iw ugint ad qemcent
tikta-inu tesluɣ-itent tuggdi i yi-kecmen
suliɣ aṭas n yisinaryuten ẓẓmeɣ asugen-inu akken ad sen-d-afeɣ taggara yessefraḥen neɣ ma ulac maḍi ur tettili ara lexsara tameqqrant
sɛiɣ zzher ass-nni d anurẓem n taggara n ddurt
deg uzal ad laḥqeɣ iḥbiben-iw akken ad nesseɣreq lehmum-nneɣ deg tewraɣt-nni yettaran rruḥ tin i yessekcamen tumert ɣer wulawen-nneɣ mi ara tsubb deg tgerjumin
mmektaɣ-d ameddakkel-iw racid
tezri tura ugar n ddurt seg wasmi nemḍel nabil ameɣbun
qqaren-d ulac ayen iwaɛren ɣef ubabat am tmettant n mmi-s ulac tiyita i iɣelban tiyita-a
racid yeḥwaǧ ssber n
ayub d tezmert n ferɛun akken ad yeffel i lmeḥna i t-yuɣen
maca zemren wussan ad ṛmun tirgin n lqerḥ ddaw n temɣer tamezwarut n umdan tettili deg tezmert swayes yezmer ad iḍaweɛ wa ad ibedd deg wudem n yal tagnit tamaynut ulamma qessiḥet
yettmeslay urgaz-a ɣef tirmit-ines deg wannar aserti i t-iḍeggren ɣer unazir n leḥbus n sibirya
tamettant n nabil teqqim d uffir i yi-yeswehmen ar tura
ɣef racid ad yefru daɣen leḥsabat-ines d ccfawat-ines tuqriḥin
ur t-walaɣ ara seg wasmi neffeɣ ad nḥewwes tatut
yenna tɣiɣdin n deg yiḍ deg yiberdan n tmanaɣt
d acu yellan d amaynut  imir-n kan truḥ-d ɣer tidmi-w ad rzuɣ ɣur-s
walaɣ ssaɛa yettuɛelqen ɣef lḥiḍ
d lɛecra u rrbeɛ
ssaɛa-agi twulem mliḥ
d tagnit daɣen ad kkseɣ lxiq i yemmɣen ɣef wul-iw
iḍal-d racid am leɛwayed-is seg ubalkun yessuter-d deg-i ad aliɣ ɣer uxxam-is
imuger-iyi-d s uzmumeg uḥzin d yiwet n tefyirt n userḥeb tawezzlant
imir-n kan ẓriɣ ddeq i yečča mazal yebrek ɣef yidmaren-is
teɣli-d gar-aneɣ yiwet n tsusmi taẓayant i kra n lweqt
mebla ma faqeɣ ufiɣ iman-iw ttmeslayeɣ ɣef lmektub d teqseḥ-ines ɣef yimdanen
ameslay d azrar awal yezzuɣur wayeḍ am wakken i d-nnan yimezwura
nekk s timmad-iw kerheɣ ad qqimeɣ d walbaɛḍ d asusam
ɣef waya ad iyi-tafeḍ deg temliliyin am ta zewwireɣ ɣer umeslay s wayen yuzzlen ɣef yiles-iw ẓriɣ ad yili d tasarut i uskasi wa ad yejbed wiyaḍ ɣer umeslay
maca win yessnen racid yeẓra belli yid-s yezga yella umaynut
imuqel-iyi-d s tmuɣli-nni n umusnaw ɣer uɣerda-ines yellan deg lqefs yekker ɣer wadar n yidlisen yellan deg teɣmert n usalun yeddem yiwet n tezmamt taqehwit imuqel isebtar-ines s laɛqel uqbel ma ad tt-id-yefk
wagi d aɣmis abaḍni n nabil
aɣmis abaḍni  anda i t-id-tufiḍ 
deg texxamt-is tettuḍ acu i yi-yenna ukumisar n temsulta yenna-yi-d ad yazen irgazen-ines ad qellben lqecc-is limmer ad afen kra n yisallen ad ten-ɛiwnen deg testant-nsen
ah ih
suref-iyi kan ay ameddakkel ussan-agi ineggura ttwaṭṭfeɣ mliḥ
ad k-d-ḥkuɣ umbaɛd laɛǧeb i yi-yeḍran
maca ufiɣ kan kra n lweqt usiɣ-d srid ɣur-k
tagi mačči d tuzzma d aɛeggen kan
lecɣal n ddunit tamelɛunt ur ttfakkan ara
ula d nekk tewweḍ-iyi-d iḍelli yiwet n tebrat yessewhamen
ad k-tt-id-ssikneɣ umbaɛd
tagi d tazmamt n mmi nabil ufiɣ-tt deg tlemmast n yidlisen-ines
yella yettaru deg-s ayen i yettɛeddayen ɣef uqerruy-is
am wakken teẓriḍ ffreɣ-tt ɣef temsulta
d si
aḥmed i yeskecmen tawekka deg uqerruy-iw dɣa uɣaleɣ-d srid qellbeɣ taxzant-is
teqqim texxamt-is am wakken i tt-yeǧǧa
la nekk wala yemma-s ur nesɛi tabɣest ad neqɛed lqecc-is
yemma-s tettɣimi ɣef umnar n tewwurt tesmektay ccfawat-ines akked tasa-ines am wakken i as-tsemmi ma yeqreḥ-itt mliḥ lḥal tettaẓ asurif ɣer sdat ad teṭṭef aselsu amezwaru ara d-tmager ad t-tessenṭeḍ ɣer wudem-is ad tebdu sakin imeṭṭawen d unedder
ulac acu ad d-iniɣ neɣ ayen zemreɣ ad xedmeɣ
ula d nekk deg wussan imezwura amer mačči d tiruggza i yi-yefkan tabɣest tili glalzeɣ deg lqaɛa wwteɣ agejdur ad as-serḥeɣ i teɣwisin ara yessakin lmeggtin
kečč ur tesɛiḍ ara dderya ahat ur tezriḍ ara acu taẓayt i ttaǧǧan deffir-nsen mi ara ruḥen
kečč tessneḍ-iyi mliḥ ur cetkayeɣ ara ɣef tlufa n zzman xas ma ddunit tewɛer yid-i
maca tikkelt-a rẓeɣ ɣliɣ teḍra yid-i am uẓru-nni i yessegrareb ucercur am wakken i d-yenna umedyaz n tallit taqburt
d tiyita i yebḍan adrar ɣef sin ur cukkeɣ ara ad d-yas wass ad as-ḥluɣ
d tidet mmi yemmut yewweḍ laɛfu n rebbi ur tenfiɛ tiyita n ugejdur ur tenfiɛ tselbiba
uraren yis-s yiderwicen ifuḥanen wwin-t srid ɣer wanda ur yettuɣal ara
hatta tezmamt-is bɣiɣ ad teɣreḍ ayen yellan deg-s ad tafeḍ deg-s kra n lemqirrat tuqsiḥin ɛnant-yi ɛnant daɣen tawacult maca keččini d ameddakkel-iw teẓriḍ acu yellan daxel n tasilt
deg-s daɣen aṭas n yifutas ɣef wassaɣen-is d yiderwicen-nni
aṭas-aya mi s-ččan allaɣ-is nekkini ur ɛlimeɣ
ad steɛerfeɣ tura belli d lɣelṭa tameqqrant i xedmeɣ asmi qebleɣ tawuri n umaswaḍ amatu
ṭṭuqten yibaten-inu
iḍaɛ mmi s ssebba-w am wakken tḍaɛ yelli
d tidet tessemneɛ iman-is tura tettidir deg tmurt n kanada
maca teǧǧa-d deffir-s ilem d ameqqran
ur tteffreɣ ara fell-ak yal mi ara tt-mmektiɣ yettruḥu-yi naddam ikeccem wul-iw leḥzen lfuruḥ n ddunit ur zmiren ara ad t-kksen
ɣas akken ugiɣ ad tt-xebbreɣ s tmettant n gma-s
ini-yi-d deg laɛnaya-k d acu ad texdem deg tmurt n yineḍliben  teqqar-iyi-d deg tebratin-ines attan terked deg uxeddim-is deg yiwet n tnaremt tabyulujit yettwassnen deg umaḍal tetthenna daɣen deg tudert-ines tamaynut
d ayen i yeskecmen talwit deg wul-iw d wul n yemma-s
wali ma yella deg tezmamt-a kra ara yallen yimsulta deg tsastant-nsen
kečč d amastan tuɣeḍ tannumi teqqareḍ ikaramen
s lferḥ ameqqran ara ɛiwneɣ tamsulta akken ad tessenger imṭurfa-agi iẓuran-nsen seg ddunit-agi neɣ ad ten-tenfu ɣer sseḥrawehmeɣ ayɣer i sen-ttserriḥen tura  amer mazal budyaf yedder tili yessenger-iten irkelli ur yeǧǧi ula d yiwen deg-sen ineḍliben wa ad teqleɛ
truḥ-d temsulta akken ad tnadi 
truḥ-d tnuda kulci maca ulac acu i d-tufa
ttiɣ tazmamt-nni deg yifassen-iw
taduli-ines temmečč deg yidisan
ini-nni aqehwi ɣumment wunuɣen d usxerbec yuran s uberkan d uzegzaw
d taswast n tkubanit taɣelnawt n tsafut d lgaz
asebter i yal ass seg wussan n useggas
semmus n yiseggasen i iɛeddan fell-as
tuget n yisebtar d ilmawen
k ra deg-sen kan ččuren s yiwet n tira ur necbiḥ ara yernu meẓẓiyet maca ɣas akken tettwaɣer tura s waṭas n yiniten
aṭas n yisebtar ččuren s yiluɣma n tusnakt d teɣrasna akked yisefra d yinzan yettwakksen seg yidlisenfusen
yenna racid 
cfiɣ mliḥ asmi i as-fkiɣ tazmamt-nni tuɣ-it imir-n deg useggas wis sin n tesnawit aseggas n nneḥs d ubrir
ruḥeɣ ad xelseɣ tafaṭurt n tsafut mmugreɣ-d yiwen n unmalay d ameddakkel aqdim yessekcem-iyi ɣer tnarit-ines nemmeslay ɣef waṭas n yisental
mi nemfaraq yekker yeddem-d seg yiwet n texzant yiwet n teswast tameqqrant terqem d snat n tezmamin n ssenf-a
ǧǧiɣ yiwet ɣur-i ttaruɣ deg-s ttiɛadat-inu n umaswaḍ tis snat fkiɣ-tt i mmi nabil
nella deg taggara n waggur n yennayer
cfiɣ ɣef uzemz acku unageɣ umbaɛd srid ɣer
leɣwaṭ lwilaya tamaynut i yi-d-rnan nnig n lwilayat n
lemdiya d lǧelfa
d amenẓaw s lekmal-is  ɛum baḥrek  ay amaswaḍ ameɣbun
ulac ṭumubil ara k-yawin wala isensa yelhan ad k-yeddarin
lkar am kečč am  lɣaci  d yisaganen n yiɣerbazen ilemmasen yeččuren s uɣebbar
ma tesɛiḍ zzher ad k-yeɛreḍ yiwen n unemhal neɣ yiwen n uselmad s axxam-is
deg yiseggasen-nni ẓriɣ liḥala n tidet ideg tettiddir tmurt
uɣaleɣ kerheɣ ugar adabu i ɣ-iḥekmen
mi i as-nniɣ i umeddakkel-iw aqdim d acu-tt tawuri-inu tamaynut yerra nnehta yenna-yi-d amerzg-iw
d tagnit akken ad yinig walbaɛḍ  ad ibeddel amkan d wudmawen wa ad yerwel seg tudert-a n tnarit yeččuren s rrḍuba d uɣebbar n yikaramen

baṭṭuṭa  d
neɣ i tira n tkatutin  ur k-d-tusi ara tikti ad tent-teskelseḍ 
kečč d ameɣnas aqdim deg yiwen n ukabar uffir tkecmeḍ lḥebs tɛaceḍ ssikis
rnu ugar n waya tzemreḍ ad tgelmeḍ lezzayer talqayant
d taggwa ara inefɛen tisuta i d-iteddun
mazal-ik tettarguḍ belli tamurt-a tezmer ad tissin yiwen n wass taneflit d tenkelwit  d tirga i ɣ-yeskerkren yiwen n wass neckuṭeḍ deg-s am uɣriq-nni i yeckunṭḍen deg telwiḥt yemmeččen iɣil deg uɣerrabu n nuḥ i yeṭṭef
wali kan sdat-k aql-aɣ nekcem daxel n tgennarit mebla tafat ulac tawwurt yessufuɣen ɣer berra
eǧǧ-aɣ tura seg tekta-inek tiberkanin
tenniḍ-iyi-d tura teṭṭfeḍ yiwet n tebrat yessewhamen
ah tesmektaḍ-iyi-d
yuɣal ɣer wadar n yidlisen yeddem-d yiwet n tjellabt yefka-yi-tt-id
truḥ-d seg tenmehla n usegmi
d acu bɣan ɣur-s  bɣan ad yuɣal ɣer uxeddim-is  mi ɛeṭṭleɣ ur ldiɣ-ara tejellabt-nni yenna-yi-d racid 
ɣer akken ad teẓreḍ s wallen-ik d acu teswa tamurt tamurt-a iwumi mazal tessarameḍ lxir
ldiɣ tajellabt ddmeɣ tabrat bdiɣ taɣuri
refdeɣ aqerruy-iw wehmeɣ 
d acu-t waya 
am wakken tettwaliḍ bɣan ad iyi-yessuffɣen seg uxxam i yeddarin tawacult-iw umbaɛd ugar n kraḍet n tmerwin n yiseggasen n uxeddim
ini-yi-d tura deg leɛnaya-k amek i tebɣiḍ ad ḥemmleɣ ulamma ciṭuḥ kan tamurt-a 
tardayt s usuffeɣ seg uxxam tban am yiṭij
 nessutur deg-wen ad teǧǧem imir-a axxam awuran acku teḥwaǧ-it tenmehla n usegmi akken ad zedɣen inawaren imaynuten 
tawaɣit niḍen i d-yeɣlin ɣef uqerru n racid ameɣbun
tamsalt-a teffeɣ yakk allaɣ-iw
nniɣ 
yernu ur tesɛiḍ ara axxam niḍen ad k-yeddarin
s laɛqel-ik kan ay ameddakkel tebɣiḍ ula d kečč ad iyi-tessuffɣeḍ uqbel lawan
tura ma yella uxxam-agi s tidet d axxam awuran yeshel maḍi ɣef tenmehla n usegmi ad d-tawi aɣtas n usuffeɣ seg uxxam n teɣdemt
imir-n ulac acu tzemreḍ ad txedmeḍ anagar tuffɣa seg uxxam s lebɣi-k neɣ s yiɣil
yiwen n wass ṭṭfeɣ yiwen n uwezlu i t-yecban
bab-is d amagaẓ amatu ɣur-s zzher yexdem deg yiwet n tesnawit ugar n snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen yessers yiwen n ukaram yessuter deg-s tikci n uxxam deg tɣiwant-ines taneslit
ussan-nni aselway n tɣiwant yeɣli-d yiwen i as-yettilin dɣa yefka-as yiwen n uxxam asmi ferrqen yixxamen am teckarin n uyefki
maca tura umbaɛd mraw n yiseggasen n tezɣent tadamsant d uṭerḍeq n ṭṭrad aɣarim i ihudden kulci yakk isenfaren n lebni ḥebsen ula d lebni n yizadaɣen yeffɣen yakan seg wakal yeḥbes
sani truḥeḍ ma yesɣer unemhal n usegmi aqerruy-is yessaweḍ tamsalt s axxam n teɣdemt  yernu mačči d aqesser
ssneɣ yiwen n ufesyan i yewwin tastaɣt-ines yesɛedda anebdu s lekmal-is netta d twacult-is deg umraḥ deg uzaduɣ ideg yezdeɣ yakan deg wannag wis ukkuẓ ugar n mraw n yiseggasen
ulac tanarit i yeǧǧa ulac tawwurt uɣur yesṭebṭeb ara iwala acḥal n yimasayen akken ad tiḥnin tasa-nsen fell-as maca ulac win i as-yufan axxam
mi d-yewweḍ lawan n usemmiḍ d yigefran yejmeɛ yiruka-ines yuɣal s axxam n yimawlan-is i d-yezgan deg yiwet n taddart tebɛed mliḥ yeqqim acḥal n yiseggasen ur tt-iwala ara
ayɣer tḥesbeḍ-iyi d bu-nniya ur ẓriɣ ara asaḍuf yaɛnan ixxamen iwuranen
axxam-agi d awuran u mačči d awuran deg yiwen lweqt
akken ad yettwaḥseb yiwen n uxxam d axxam awuran ilaq ad yezg deg tlemmast n uɣerbaz wa ad yesɛu yiwet n tewwurt n lemreḥ kan sexdamen-tt inawaren d yimezdaɣ
ayen yaɛnan ukkuẓ n yixxamen i d-yezgan deg wannag wis sin sɛan tawwurt n lemreḥ weḥd-sen
tamsalt mačči n wass-a
tagi d tacerket tamaynut i yenda udemmas-nni amaynut i d-uznen ɣer uɣerbaz alemmas ɣef ssebba n yir asefrek-ines wid yeẓran acu yeḍran s tidet qqaren-d yerda s uḍegger n yidrimen n lɛamma deg yiguta n tnezzut mduɣlet
qqaren-d daɣen yekseb ssraya deg temnaḍt n blida
mraw n yiseggasen aya asmi d-yeffeɣ usaḍuf i d-yewwin ɣef tuǧǧin n wayla n ddula nɣawel nessers akaram ɣer yimeẓla ideblanen yaɛnan s tnezzut
neldi tawwurt seg deffir tessuffuɣ-aɣ srid ɣer ubrid nessali daɣen ssur gar-aneɣ d umraḥ n uɣerbaz alemmas
akka uɣalen-d yixxamen-nneɣ d ilelliyen yeɛna-ten usaḍuf n tiǧǧin n wayla n ddula
truḥ-d yiwet n tesmelt tuzzigt twala amkan teqbel tikti n tiɣin n yixxamen
maca tabiruqratit tɛeccec deg tedbelt-nneɣ dayen i iɛeṭṭlen ferru n temsalt
maca yettbin-d am wakken llan kra n yifassen udrigen xeddmen amek ad skeflen tamsalt s wadda ṭṭamaɛen ad ɣ-sɛesqen wa ad ḥewṣen ixxamen-a
d tidet nɛawed neldi tawwurt-nni tagensayt i d-yettakken ɣer umraḥ n uɣerbaz
d anemhal amaynut i yerẓan iqerra-nneɣ yewwi-d ifukal dayen ara yessisehlen axeddim-ines labeɛda mi tluɣ liḥala n tmurt maca am wakken i d-yeqqar umeddakkel-nneɣ caɛban
 dagi ara yemmet qasi 
tettmeslayeḍ ɣef ukkuẓ n yixxamen imawlan-nsen ṭṭfen tibratin akken ad ffɣen ula d nitni 
ayen i ẓriɣ tura anagar nekk i yeṭṭfen tabrat am ta
i wiyaḍ mazal-iten deg uselmed 
tanezduɣt i d-yezgan ɣer tama tayeffust-inu teɣleq semmus n yiseggasen aya neɣ ugar
tesneḍ mliḥ bab-is
yella seg yiselmaden imezwura deg uɣerbaz-agi uznen-t ɣer fransa ad yeselmed tutlayt taɛrabt
deg yiseggasen imezwura tuɣ-it yesɛedday imuras n unebdu gar-aneɣ ɣur-s tura sin n yiseggasen ur d-yusi ara ɣer tmurt
iban d tiɣimit i yeqqim i lebda deg fransa
yernu ur yeɣliḍ ara d acu ara yexdem deg tmurt-a i yessuffuɣen ixeddamen-is mi ara wwḍen ɣer tastaɣt
ma d tanezduɣt i d-yezgan ɣer tama tazelmaḍt yers ɣef yisem n yiwet n tselmadt taɛezrit tewwi-d yakk tawacult-is mi yemmut baba-s tettidir tura akked yemma-s d wukkuẓ n watmaten-is
ma d tanezduɣt tis ukkuẓet yeṭṭef-itt unemhal i d-yusan deffir-i amagaẓ amatu aqdim n uɣerbaz alemmas-a seqsaɣ-t yiwen n wass fell-ak yenna-yi-d ur k-yessin ara
ahat yewweḍ-d umbaɛd n uṭixer-inek
ǧǧiɣ aɣerbaz alemmas qrib azgen n lqern tura ay aḥbib anwa ara yecfun ɣef yiwen n udinusur qrib ad yenger 
lḥasun ad k-weṣṣiɣ ad tḥerkeḍ akken ad d-tafeḍ tifrat i wugur n tnezduɣt-ik uqbel ad ifat lḥal
ɣur-i kra n tmussniwin deg wayla n ddula
ad nruḥ jmiɛ ad nesseqsi ɣef ukaram n tnezduɣin-nwen
ad ɛeddiɣ ddurt-a ad waliɣ ad k-xebbreɣ s wayen yellan
sakin ad nwali acu i ilaq ad t-nexdem
ayen yebɣu yili ulac win i izemren ad iyi-yessuffeɣ sya skud ddreɣ
imir-n kan teṭṭal-d tmeṭṭut-is seg tewwurt n usalun tesṭerḥeb yis-i
tella temtuttel deg yiwen n lximar d aberkan allen-is cuffent seg yimeṭṭawen d ɛawaz udem-is yuɣal d awraɣ am tɛeqqayt n lqares
beddeɣ seqsaɣ-tt ɣef liḥala d tezmert-ines
ur tessaweḍ ara ad tenṭeq s snat n tefyar armi walaɣ allen-is ččurent s yimeṭṭawen dɣa tessusem
tessider aqerruy-is kra n lweqt sakin truḥ tettru
tegzem tasa-w fell-as sutreɣ deg racid ad i yi-yessuref ad ruḥeɣ wwiɣ-as-d ifukal s ttiɛadat n uxeddim i yi-yettganin ffɣeɣ seg uxxam n umeddakkel-iw ddaw n teɣruḍt-iw tazmamt-nni  lḥir yečča-yi bɣiɣ ad tt-ɣreɣ akken ad ẓreɣ ayen yellan daxel-is
sem  seg furar
acu ad xedmeɣ s tezmamt-agi  yenna-yi-d baba 
 ad k-tenfeɛ i yiluɣma n tusnakt d teɣrasna 
tusnakt d teɣrasna  kerheɣ leqraya tasnawit iselmaden kerheɣ kulci
ula d baba bdiɣ kerrheɣ-t
ayɣer ur yettẓalla ur yettuẓum am netta am lbaqi n yinselmen  ur yuggad seg ssikis n uẓekka d tmes n unazir  deg wass n sem yezrin mi yebda limam amennay igellem deg ssikis n uẓekka d lɛezla n lmegget d tuggdi-ines seg ɛeẓrayen aneglus n tmettant u netta weḥd-s kan isell i yisurifen n wid i t-imeṭṭlen yettenɣas ssut-nsen ttbaɛden fell-as tergagi tfekka-inu seg tuggdi
ur kfiɣ taẓallit-inu armi uɣaleɣ d ulac
ttẓallaɣ s ṭul n yiḍ am wakken ttẓallaɣ deg lawan steɣfireɣ rebbi ssbeḥ tameddit akken ad iyi-yessuref
yenna-yi-d yasin rebbi iseffeḍ yakk ddnub ma yuɣal umdan s abrid amaɣud
nettemlili yal ass deg lǧameɛ deg tẓallit n lefjer akked tin n lɛica
ssaɛa qrib ad taweḍ d ṭnac n wass
d lawan ad ruḥeɣ ɣer lǧameɛ i tẓallit n lǧumuɛa
yasin yettraǧu-iyi
iḥettet fell-i ad n-awaḍeɣ zik acku ccix meḥfuḍ ad ɣ-d-yas seg blida akken ad ɣ-yessiwel inaw n wass n lǧumuɛa
yasin yebɣa ad neqqim deg lesfuf imezwura
aram  seg furar
yessuffeɣ-iyi ass-a uselmad n teɣrasna akked kraḍ n yimidaw-inu seg tneɣrit
mi s-nenna i umagaẓ amatu tuɣ-aɣ deg lǧameɛ yessusem yeǧǧa-aɣ ad nali ɣer wannag wis sin
ma d aselmad n teɣrasna amenɛul mi nekcem ɣer tneɣrit isuɣ fell-aneɣ ad as-tiniḍ d aɛefrit i iwala
yeɛreḍ yasin ad as-yessefhem mačči d urar i netturar d lwajeb-nneɣ i nxeddem maca ur as-yeǧǧi ara tagnit ad yenṭeq
yessuffeɣ-aɣ yerra tawwurt deffir-nneɣ s ẓẓur
cukkeɣ iga am baba d icenga n usɣan d izduklanen ur nettamen ara s rebbi
maca walaɣ-t yiwet n tikkelt deg wass n sem deg umraḥ n lǧameɛ umbaɛd n tẓallit
taẓallit n yixabiten ass n sem d lɛid kan
nuɣal ad nwali amagaẓ amatu maca yenna-aɣ-d aselmad n teɣrasna iẓeyyer mliḥ d ameqsuḥ ur iḥemmel ara win i yessekcamen iman-is deg uxeddim-is
yessumer yasin ad t-nerǧu berra n tesnawit akken ad as-nessefhem addud-nneɣ
mi t-nemmuger kan yenna-aɣ s wurfan   ur cliɛeɣ ara deg wuguren-nwen neɣ s wayes tettamnem
win yebɣan ad iɣer yas-d deg lweqt
ad ttuɣ ayen yeḍran ass-a
tikkelt i d-teddun ma ur d-tusim ara deg lawan ad ken-sɛesqeɣ seg tneɣrit-inu i lebda
xemmemt-as mliḥ 
sakin iruḥ s tazzla
ma taselmadt n taɛrabt ulac acu i ɣ-d-tenna
tessusem armi nuɣ tkemmel tamsirt ur as-d-yuli ara wawal
d tidet ur tettlusu ara lḥiǧab maca d taselmadt ifazen yezga uzmumeg ɣef yimi-s ma d asmures ɣur-s yeḍmen seg tazwara
amek ad imekwan-nneɣ sakin nexdem akken ad nqader lawan n tẓallit ladɣa tin n ṭṭhur d tin n lɛesr  ur ẓriɣ ara
d yasin ara ɣ-d-yafen tifrat
arim  seg meɣres tmenya nemlal-d deg umraḥ n
tasebḥit-a ɣef tesnawit
mi yesṭenṭen nnaqus uzzlen kra n yinelmaden ad bedden deg lesfuf i unekcum ɣer tneɣriyin maca tarbaɛt-nneɣ tbedd mgal-nsen
ulac leqraya ass-a
iruḥ-d umagaẓ amatu ad iwali d acu ssebba n waya nenna-as nebɣa ad nemmeslay d unemhal kan
umbaɛd rrbeɛ n ssaɛa yusa-d unemhal s tazzla tban-d lfeqɛa ɣef uqadum-is
yuẓa ɣur-s yasin idmaren-is cuffen yehder yid-s ad tɣileḍ d netta i iḥekkmen   nessutur deg-k ad ɣ-teldiḍ tazeqqa i tẓallit daxel n tesnawit 
yessider unemhal aqerruy-is kra n lweqt iɣeẓẓ icenfiren-is yewhem kan imuqqel ɣer yinelmaden i as-yezzin d aqusis ḥaren irkelli ttrajun acu ad sen-d-yini
deg taggara yenṭeq yenna 
 ɣef waya i txedmem asunded  tamsalt teshel maḍi ur teḥwaǧ ara ccwal-agi irkelli
kecmet ɣer tneɣriyin-nwen tura ad waliɣ temsalt u ma yebɣa rebbi ad as-d-naf tifrat i wugur-nwen 
newhem mi yeqbel s temɣawla asuter-nneɣ dɣa neḥbes asunded
yesɛedda yasin ass yefreḥ mačči d kra
d tarennawt tameqqrant
tura ad nessali isem n rebbi deg tesnawit am wakken i t-ssulin daxel n leǧwameɛ
sed  seg meɣres
ass-agi suffɣen-aɣ irkelli bɣiɣ ad iniɣ wid yesɛan aččamar
ɣef tmenya n ssbeḥ nufa-d anemhal d umagaẓ amatu bedden ɣer tewwurt n umraḥ n tesnawit
ldin tawwurt tameẓyant kan sakin bdan afran
gedlen anekcum ɣef yal yiwen yesɛan aččamar ur nettlusu ara tabanta
yenna-d unemhal   wagi d aɣerbaz ɣur-s asaḍuf iɣef ileḥḥu
ilaq ad tseṭṭlem tamart wa ad telsem tabanta
tasnawit-a mačči d ssuq win i d-yusan ad yekcem 
sakin rran tawwurt
iban lliɣ seg wid ssuffɣen berra ɣef tamart d uqendur i lsiɣ
aččamar d ssuna i ɣ-yeǧǧa umazan ur nezmir ara ad tt-neǧǧ
nebda aɛeggeḍ nettalas i tenfaliyin tisertiyen neɣ timasɣanin d tinfaliyin i nsell deg tmesbaniyin i nettwali seg lweqt ɣer wayeḍ deg yiberdan n temdint
truḥ-d temsulta
yusa-d yiwen n ufesyan yesɛan sin n yitran ɣef tayet-is
yenna-aɣ-d deg lfayda-nneɣ ma nquder asaḍuf u nuɣal ɣer leqraya-nneɣ
ur yebɣi ara ad ihud imal-nneɣ ma yessekcem-aɣ ɣer lḥebs
tardayt s lḥebs tessekcem tuggdi deg wulawen n yinelmaden
ḥala yasin i ibedden deg wudem-is s yiwet n tebɣest yessewhamen
ur sɛiɣ ara tabɣest-ines
iɛeggeḍ yenna-as ur yettaggad leḥbus-nsen ur yettqadar isuḍaf-nsen acku ur ddin ara d wayen yellan deg ccariɛa wala deg uṣaḍuf n rebbi
imir-n kan yessuneḍ ufesyan ad t-ṭṭfen
ẓedmen fell-as sin seg yimsulta skecmen-t s yiɣil daxel n ṭumubil-nsen
nuzzel nerwel
yal yiwen deg-neɣ yekcem s axxam-is
maca tameddit-nni ufiɣ yasin deg lǧameɛ
yenna-d ṭṭfen-t armi d rrebɛa n tmeddit
hanen-t sɛeddan-t deg yixef n tsegnit
amer ur skecmen ara iman-nsen kra seg watmaten yesɛan tamussni tili yesɛedda iḍ deg bu-yikurdan
izuxx yasin s wayen yexdem
deg yiḍ-nni neqqim tama n lǧameɛ nsell i yasin yettales-aɣ ifutas n uḥbas-ines
sem  seg meɣres
nugi ad nseṭṭel ičamaren-nneɣ anemhal yugi ad ɣ-yeǧǧ ad nekcem
mačči irkelli
kra n yibabaten ḥettmen ɣef warraw-nsen ad uɣalen ɣer uɣerbaz dɣa uɣalen am tullas s tbanta d wudem iseṭṭel
sɛiɣ zzher ussan-nni baba iɣab ugar n ddurt
teɛreḍ yemma ad iyi-tbeddel rray ad ṭṭixreɣ i taɣart n uqerru maca ur as-sliɣ ara
ula d nettat d taselmadt maca deg tesnawit ibaɛden
tetteffeɣ ɣef ssebɛa ur tettuɣal ara armi d lmeɣreb
ur as-d-yewwiḍ usali n usuffeɣ-nneɣ armi d ass wis kraḍ
tbeṭṭel axeddim tessuki-yi-d zik tessuter deg-i ad heggiɣ iman-iw ad nruḥ yid-s ɣer tesnawit
qqimeɣ deg wusu ugiɣ ad as-aɣeɣ awal
tuggez-iyi s baba
tenna-yi-d ad yesseɣli axxam ɣef yiqerra-nneɣ ma kemmleɣ deg ubrid-agi
yenna-d yasin tadyant-agi d tikci sɣur rebbi akken ad iẓer sani tewweḍ taflest-nneɣ u ma neṭṭef s tidet deg usɣan-nneɣ
yessefk fell-aneɣ ad nesber wa ad nezbu am wakken zban asaḍen n usaru 
ur ṭṭaxren ara i usɣan-nsen ɣas akken hanen-ten sɛeddan-ten deg ssikis
ilaq ad neḍfer abrid-nsen wa ad zuxxen yis-neɣ
ass-a d ass amezwaru iḍelli tameddit
n yimuras n tefsut
baba yuɣal-d
yewweḍ-d yaɛya yeṭṭes zik
tura selleɣ i ssut-is deg tnawalt
iban yella acu i as-d-tenna yemma
ur bɣiɣ ara ad t-waliɣ
ẓriɣ d acu ad iyi-d-yini
yekreh atmaten inselmen neɣ  ixwanǧiyen  am wakken i sen-yessawal
maca ɣas akken d baba ur zmireɣ ara ad t-ɛṣuɣ
yessuneḍ-aɣ rebbi ad naɣ awal n yimawlan-nneɣ
maca yenna-yi-d yasin ur nettaɣ ara awal i umdan deg uɛsay n rebbi ulamma d yiwen seg yimawlan-nneɣ
yasin ur yesɛi ara baba-s yettidir akked yemma-s kan
tella txeddem d tamsizdegt deg uɣerbaz alemmas sakin tuḍen dɣa teḥbes axeddim
yezdeɣ mebɛid deg udcir  lebrarik 
ur tettseqsi ɣer leqraya-ines neɣ ɣef yiba-ines seg uɣerbaz
ixeddem acu i as-yehwan
ulac win ad ibedden deg ubrid-is
yesɛa zzher
ur yesɛi baba-s ad t-id-yaggez s uxnaq neɣ s usuffeɣ seg uxxam
ad qqimeɣ deg wusu almi yewweḍ lawan n tẓallit n lǧumuɛa
ur tetteɣ ara imekli
ad ččeɣ sseksu ara ferqen ɣef yimeɣban deg umraḥ n lǧameɛ
sed  seg meɣres
tekker tenger ddunit
ɛeṭleɣ baɛmada ssarmeɣ ad afeɣ baba yeṭṭes
maca ufiɣ-t yettraǧu deg-i
ufiɣ s uzekrun
yessewḥec-iyi wudem-is ufiɣ-t d aberkan yerfa
bɣiɣ ad ruḥeɣ srid ɣer texxamt-iw maca yeskerker-iyi ɣer tzeqqa n usired yesuneḍ-iyi ad seṭṭleɣ aččamar-inu
ihegga-yi-d yakk allalen n useṭṭel
d acu ara xedmeɣ  sidreɣ aqerruy-iw ssusmeɣ
iserreḥ-as umbaɛd i ucercur n nnhayat d yir tikta i yekkaten deg terbaɛt-nneɣ yessenɣasen deg wazal-ines
maca ɣelqeɣ imeẓẓuɣen-iw rriɣ ɣer tidmi-w tugna n lqiyamma tawwurt teɣleq iḍelli
zayd i ineddren ddaw n taẓayt n uẓru ameqqran yersen ɣef yidmaren-is
d nnuba-w tura ad zbuɣ
refdeɣ aqerruy-iw nniɣ   kečč d akafriw ur ilaq ara ad k-aɣeɣ awal 
dɣa yewwet-iyi s ubeqqa qrib i yi-yesseɣli ɣer lqaɛa
iremmez yiwen n urmaz yerfa mliḥ yebɣa ad iyi-yewwet i tikkelt tis snat amer ur tessekcem ara yemma iman-is i yeqqimen deg berra tettraǧu kan melmi ad teḍru tawaɣit iman-is
idegger-itt baba s zzur yenna-as   eǧǧ-iyi ad rebbiɣ amcum-agi uqbel ad ifat lḥal 
yeggul ad iyi-yessuffeɣ seg uxxam ma ugiɣ ad seṭṭleɣ aččamar-iw wa ad uɣaleɣ ɣer leqraya
ttwaṭṭfeɣ ur ẓriɣ ara acu ara xedmeɣ
seṭṭleɣ aččamar-inu nnig n wul-iw jerḥeɣ amayeg-inu acḥal n tikkal
sakin yesɣimi-yi lmendad-is deg usalun yehder-iyi-d s tentala niḍen temgarad teččur s lḥenna d tizeḍt
sidreɣ kan i uqerruy-iw ur nṭiqeɣ ara s yiwen n wawal
inaw aɣezzfan ɣef leqraya imal tiṭṭurfa tamasɣant ikabaren yessexlaḍen gar usɣan d tsertit tamasit n yimawlan deg urebbi n dderya-nsen d temsal niḍen
deg tilawt ur as-sliɣ ara lliɣ ttxemmimeɣ deg waddud n yasin asmi ad i yi-iwali seṭṭleɣ aččamar-iw
iban ad yerfu fell-i wa ad ɣliɣ deg wallen-is
ṭṭfeɣ rray ad qqimeɣ deg uxxam alamma kfan imuras
yernu ẓriɣ seg tura ass n tuɣalin ɣer tesnawit d baba ara yawin s timmad-is ɣer tesnawit
sem  seg yibril
anagar yasin i yugin ad iseṭṭel aččamar-ines yugi daɣen ad yuɣal ɣer leqraya
uɣaleɣ ur t-ttwaliɣ ara s waṭas
yuɣal baba yettɛassa mliḥ tigawin-inu
yegdel fell-i ad ruḥeɣ ɣer lǧameɛ
yeǧǧa-yi kan ad ruḥeɣ ad ẓalleɣ taẓallit n lǧumuɛa
ibedd ɣef uqerruy-iw ssbeḥ tameddit yeseqsi ɣef temsirin-inu
ibaten-ines uɣalen wezzilit
tbedd uletma farida tanelmadt deg tesdawit ɣer tama-s
tuɣal ula d nettat tettas-d yal taggara n ddurt tettɛawan-iyi deg uheggi n yiluɣma n tusnakt d teɣrasna
maca ulac acu i fehmeɣ
yenna uselmad n teɣrasna i baba belli ḍeggreɣ aseggas s lekmal-is yewɛer fell-i ad sɛuɣ aswir iwatan
ḥemmleɣ mliḥ uletma farida tesnefcic-iyi txeddem-iyi ayen bɣiɣ seg wasmi lliɣ meẓẓeyeɣ
deg unebdu yezrin yeḍra gar-aneɣ umgared amezwaru asmi tessuter deg-i ad dduɣ yid-s ɣer yillel am wakken uɣeɣ tannumi xeddmeɣ yakan
teṭṭerḍeq s taḍsa mi s-nniɣ d leḥram ɣef tmeṭṭut ad truḥ ɣer yillel
tenna-d   ula d kečč tuɣaleḍ tfettuḍ
deg tmurt-agi yuɣal yal yiwen ifettu i yiman-is
nekk ad iniɣ lɛumm deg yillel d leḥlal ɣef tmeṭṭut 
bɣiɣ ad as-sfehmeɣ maca thuzz tuyat-is teffeɣ
baba yefka-as tilelli
ur tt-yesseqsi sani truḥ neɣ anda tella
ḥala yemma i as-yeqqaren ur ilaq ara ad tɛeṭṭel wa ad d-tuɣal s axxam uqbel n lmeɣreb
uletma txeddem kan acu yellan deg uqerruy-is u baba yedda yid-s
amhad  seg yunyu
assa-a ttekkaɣ deg yiwet n temsbanit tameqqrant deg yiberdan n tmanaɣt
ur ruḥeɣ ara ad ɣreɣ ddiɣ zik d
yasin
ffreɣ aqendur-inu deg uqrab uggadeɣ ad i yi-iwali baba
skud yella deg uxxam ur ttafeɣ ara iman-iw
d tamnaḍt n
yasin i yeffren aqrab ɣer musa aḥeffaf i iɣelqen taḥanut-is yedda yid-neɣ ula netta
lsiɣ aqendur rriɣ tacacit tamellalt ɣef uqerruy-iw neṭṭef imekwan-nneɣ deg lkar gar yimezwura
inig baṭel awwaḍ tuɣalin i yal win yebɣan ad yettekki
ɣas akken meqqret lkar teččur armi dayen wid i d-yusan umbaɛd ur ufin ara amkan
amraḥ n umenzu n mayyu anda tebdu tamesbanit ara iruḥen armi d amraḥ n yimeɣrasen yeččur s lmeyyat n lkiran i d-yusan seg yal tmurt
luluf n yimeɣnasen s yiččamaren lsan iqendyar inselmen
seḍḥaɣ seg wudem-iw ur nesɛi tamart
melmi ad afeɣ tilelli akken ad serḥeɣ i uččamar-inu am watmaten inselmen niḍen  nufa ugur ad nembiwel
yezzuɣer-iyi yasin deg tlemmast n lɣaci-nni akken ad iyi-yesken lmacayex
nwala-ten seg mbaɛid
bɣan irkelli ad ten-walin wa ad selmen fell-asen
maca nufa sdat-neɣ aɣrab n yiɛessasen uzmiren i ɣ-gedlen aqerreb ɣur-sen
yeɛreq-iyi yasin deg tlemmast n lɣaci-nni ufiɣ-t ugar n ssaɛa umbaɛd
yenna-yi-d yewweḍ ad yedderdeb armi i yewweḍ ɣur-sen isellem fell-asen
yasin yesɛa zzher ɣur-s daɣen tabɣest tameqqrant
aṭas i nelḥa neqqim nettales i tenfaliyin swayes tettɛeggiḍ yakk lɛamma
fell-as ad nidir fell-as ad nemmet  ccariɛa ccariɛa 
ulac tamendawt ulac arakwal  leqran
leqran  igduden-a d tazmert tameqqrant zemren ad refden idurar ma numeṛ-iten s waya  am wakken i d-yenna yiwen seg lmacayex deg yinaw-ines deg umraḥ n yimeɣrasen
ass-nni faqeɣ mačči weḥd-i i lliɣ
yeččur wul-iw s tumert d nnefxa s wayen xeddmeɣ ɣas ibedd lxilafa ad tegzem baba deg wudem-iw
mi d-nuɣal yenna-yi-d yasin ad tili yiwet n tmesbanit tameqqrant niḍen deg wussan i d-iteddun deg umraḥ n yimeɣrasen ad teqqim alamma sbedden lxilafa tineslemt
yernu qrib ad tt-sbedden ma yebɣa rebbi
ad nefreḥ irkelli wa ad nessenger icenga n usɣan
xemmemeɣ ɣef taggara n baba d uletma d umkan-nsen deg lxilafa-agi
s tidet d icenga n usɣan  yessefk fell-i ad sqenɛeɣ baba ad yeǧǧ abrid n tezdukkla wa ad yekcem ɣer tneslemt
ilaq ad xedmeɣ aya uqbel n usbeddi n lxilafa
ur bɣiɣ ara ad yeḍru wayen n dir i baba d iqerra n uletma
yenna-d yasin yikafriwen d tlawin mebla lḥiǧab
ilaq ad sqenɛeɣ uletma akken ad d-tels lḥiǧab wa ad teḥbes rrwaḥ-ines ɣer yillel
attan tura deg tesdawit
imuras qrib ad d-awḍen nettat tuɣ tannumi tessucuf deg yillel akked yirgazen
ya rebbi all-iyi akken ad ten-rreɣ s abrid amaɣud
aram  seg yunyu
suref-as a rebbi i baba mi itett remḍan
ẓriɣ ur yettuẓummu ara
maca tasebḥit-agi mi t-walaɣ deg tnawalt itess lqehwa-ines nekkni deg waggur asaɛdi yettubarken ur ṭṭifeɣ ara iman-iw ɛeggḍeɣ fell-as nniɣ-as kečč d akafriw ad k-yessekcem rebbi ɣer unazir
ass-nni yennecraḥ
yessewhem-iyi ass-nni ur yerfi ara am zik
yessuter deg-i ad qqimeɣ yebda ad i yi-yessefhem tafelsuft-ines ur nettamnen ara s rebbi
iban ur sliɣ ara i wayen yettmeslay
ur selleɣ ara i lweswas n cciṭan
d cciṭan amelɛun i yettmeslayen s yiles-is
netta yettmeslay nekk ttalseɣ s tsusmi tasuret n  elmuɛwidateyn 
sakin furseɣ tagnit mi yessaɣ agarru yeddem afenǧal ad isew lqehwa beddeɣ wwiɣ-d ssebba s rrwaḥ-inu ɣer tesnawit ɣas akken nekfa akradyur-nneɣ u nesɛa azref ur nḥedder ara i temsirin
uggadeɣ ad as-gezmen aqerruy-is asmi ara tbedd lxilafa
all-iyi a rebbi akken ad ldiɣ ul-is i sburren yifyar n cciṭan 
acer  seg yunyu
d acu-tent twuɣa-agi i iɣellin ɣef uqerruy-iw  deg yiḍ yezrin tuɣ-iyi weḥd-i deg usalun qqareɣ yiwen n udlis
baba d anabay ulac-it deg uxxam
yenna-d ad iruḥ ɣer
leɣwaṭ deg tirza n tesweḍt taneggarut
uletma attan deg uɣrem asdawen deg tmanaɣt
yemma teṭṭes deg texxamt-is
ɛyiɣ deg tɣuri ur nuddmeɣ ara
saɣeɣ tiliẓri bdiɣ ttbeddileɣ deg yimaṭṭafen limmer ad afeɣ asaru ara yessedhun
ɛlaɣila thucc-iyi yiwet n tugna n usaru n wuzuf
tameṭṭut tecbeḥ mliḥ tcerreɛ i yimessaḍen-is tefka aḥeččun-is i yiwen n ubbuc ibedden ikeccem deg-s s zzur
tafekka-inu teṭṭef-itt tergagayt
yiwet n taɣect i d-yekkan seg daxel-iw tettɛeggiḍ teqqar-iyi-d  d leḥram  sens-itt sexsi-tt  maca tafekka-inu tekref tugi ad d-terr awal
tugna-nni teɣli-d fell-i am ssiɛqa
urǧin walaɣ tameṭṭut ɛeryan neɣ amek i ixeddem urgaz tayri i tmeṭṭut
deg kra n lweqt kan ḥulfaɣ i uzɣal yettaɣ yakk tafekka-inu ḥusseɣ daɣen i ubbuc-iw yettenkar
tessewhem-iyi tugna-nni tareqmant yellan sdat n wallen-iw yebrarḥen
uggadeɣ ad yessaki unazeɛ n tmeṭṭut-nni yeččuren asalun yemma
ṭṭfeɣ  atilikumund  sneɣseɣ-as i ssut maca ur ufiɣ ara daxel-iw tazmert ad beddleɣ amaṭṭaf
tafekka-inu irkelli teṭṭef-itt tergagayt deg tazwara seg tuggdi sakin ḥulfaɣ i tergagayt n ccehwa
aḍegger n ẓẓel yaɛǧeb-iyi am wakken yeqreḥ-iyi deg yiwen n lweqt qrib i ssuɣeɣ am tcermuḍt-nni n tiliẓri
ɣliɣ umbaɛd ɣef wattug ḥerḥreɣ ad tɣileḍ uzzleɣ amecwar aɣezzfan
argaz-nni mazal iteqqu tameṭṭut-nni yeṭṭef-itt deg yiwen n waddud n yiɣersiwen am yiqjan
yeṭṭef-itt seg uqerqur ad ɣ-yessuref
rebbi
kkreɣ s temɣawla senseɣ tiliẓri-nni
sakin uzzleɣ ɣer tzeqqa n usired akken ad slileɣ tubezgin-nni tamelɛunt
luḍu amecṭuḥ drus
zriɣ wid izewǧen siriden yakk tifekkiwin-nsen
dɣa sardeɣ yakk tafekka-inu s ssabun
sakin slaleɣ taserwalt-inu akken ad kkseɣ rriḥa-nni n ẓẓel i ilesqen deg-i tezmer ad iyi-tessenz
uɣaleɣ ɣer usalun steɣfreɣ rebbi sutreɣ deg-s ad yessuref lɣelṭa-inu
ddmeɣ nnesxa bdiɣ taɣuri
maca tugna n tmeṭṭut-nni taɛeryant tezga gar wallen-iw tɣumm fell-i ifyar n leqran ur iyi-teǧǧi ara ad ɣreɣ
qemceɣ allen-iw leɛneɣ cciṭan amelɛun
ɣas akken teqqim tugna-nni gar wallen-iw ad as-tiniḍ yella win i tt-yeslesqen ɣef wallen-iw
imir-n kan mmektaɣ-d mi senseɣ tiliẓri ǧǧiɣ-tt ɣef umaṭṭaf-nni n cciṭan
amer ad tsiɣ yemma azekka tiliẓri ad d-teɣli srid ɣef umaṭṭaf-nni dɣa ad tẓer tawaɣit i xedmeɣ
siɣeɣ tiliẓri i tikkelt niḍen
ur trewwu ara tmeṭṭut-agi seg wuqu 
akka d ahdum sin n yirgazen i tt-yeṭṭfen amezwaru seg uḥeččun ma d wis sin seg uqerqur
ad yenɛel rebbi tameṭṭut-nni wa ad yenɛel rebbi sin n yirgazen-nni
maca lɛar d ixeddem tiẓiḍanin snejlayeɣ-tent ɣas akken ur beddleɣ ara amaṭṭaf
yekker-d ubbuc-iw i tikkelt niḍen ḥulfaɣ i tergagayt n ccehwa tettaɣ tafekka-inu i tikkelt tis snat
maca tikkelt-a ṭṭfeɣ iman-iw beddleɣ amaṭṭaf sakin senseɣ tiliẓri
d wagi d amaṭṭaf n yiblis iɣef leḥram ttmeslyen kra n yimidawen-inu
d ameqqran win lmeɛsegga t-yettwalin i tameqqrant
kkreɣ ẓulleɣ snat n rrekɛat sutreɣ deg rebbi ad iyi-yessuref
ɣas akken allaɣ-iw ur yelhi ara s tẓallit
mazal tugniwin n tmeṭṭut-nni d uɛray-ines ttɛeddin ɣef tidmi-w d tikwal tikwal ẓeddment fell-i
kecmeɣ s usu senseɣ tafat dɣa ẓedment fell-i tugniwin-nni i tikkelt niḍen uɣent yakk lejwareḥ-iw almi ufiɣ afus-iw mebla ma faqeɣ isub ɣer ubbuc-iw aḥmayan i d-yekkren dɣa ẓẓmeɣ-t d tuẓẓma armi i ḥulfaɣ i tfekka-inu tettergigi s yiwet n ccehwa i tt-yeskerfen
kummceɣ daxel n wusu urǧin ḥulfaɣ i lbenna am ta
beddeɣ deg wudem n taɣect i d-yekkan seg daxel-iw tesuneḍ deg-i ad kkreɣ ad sizdgeɣ iman-iw seg ubluleɣ d wammus
lliɣ gar targit d tukin
ur ẓriɣ ara amek i yi-yerna yiḍes
maca ur ṭṭiseɣ mliḥ
cfiɣ tugniwin-nni huccent-iyi s ṭul n yiḍ
mi ldiɣ allen-iw ufiɣ tafat tuɣ yal amkan deg texxamt-iw
qqimeɣ ɣef umeṭreḥ allaɣ-iw yemmekta-d yakk ayen yeḍran laɛca-nni
setḥaɣ terkeb-iyi tuggdi ḥulfaɣ daɣen s ddnub
amek ad qableɣ ass 
amek ad ffreɣ ayen i yi-yeḍran  ad tɣileḍ zemren medden ad ɣren lefḍiḥa i yi-yeḍran ɣef wudem-iw mi ara ffɣeɣ kan s abrid
dderdbeɣ ɣer tzeqqa n usired ssardeɣ iman-iw ɛerḍeɣ amek ur xeddmeɣ ara ssut iwakken ur iyi-tsell ara yemma
ur uɣeɣ tannumi ttsucufeɣ zik
yezmer ad tcik deg kra
sakin swiɣ lqehwa-inu s temɣawla ffɣeɣ
ur ruḥeɣ ara ɣer tesnawit
nudaɣ ɣef
yasin maca ur t-ufiɣ ara
qqimeɣ ttezziɣ tama n lǧameɛ armi d-iban
ḥkiɣ-as ayen i yi-yeḍran
yenna-iyi-d aṭas i yesla ɣef umaṭṭaf-agi n yiblis maca ur t-iwala ara
deg uxxam-is ḥala amaṭṭaf n lezzayer i yettaṭṭaf
nniɣ-as baba yessuli yiwet n taska swayes yezmer ad yeṭṭef imaṭṭafen ifransiyen
baba iḥemmel mliḥ tasertit
yezga yeqqar iɣmisen neɣ tisɣunin yeṭṭafar daɣen iskasiyen deg yimaṭṭafen n tiliẓri neɣ n rradyu
yessuter deg-i yasin ad as-alseɣ akk ayen yeḍran
mi heggaɣ iman-iw ad mmeslayeɣ ɣef tugniwin-nni ḥulfaɣ i lḥamu yettali ɣer yimuyag-inu ḥusseɣ daɣen i ubbuc-iw yettenkar
setḥaɣ deg yiman-iw uggadeɣ ad iyi-ifaq yasin
nniɣ-as kan walaɣ-tt kan kra n lweqt sakin beddleɣ amaṭṭaf
yenna-yi-d amer deg umkan-iw tili yerreẓ taska-nni
sfehmeɣ-as ɣliɣ ɣef umaṭṭaf-nni s ugacur ur bniɣ ara fell-as maḍi
yernu amer ad rẓeɣ taska-nni ad ihudd baba axxam ɣef uqerruy-iw
netta ur yessin ara baba ɣef waya i ihedder lehdur-agi
yemma-s ur teɣri ara tuḍen ixeddem ayen i as-yehwan
yugi ad iseṭṭel aččamar-ines wa ad yuɣal ɣer leqraya ulac acu i as-d-tenna
mi t-seqsaɣ yenna-yi-d ur tesli ara maḍi s wayen yeḍran
ɣur-s ar tura mazal-it yeqqar
yernu d igellilen ur sɛin acemma
amer mačči d xalti-s i yetseddiqen fell-asen tili mmuten seg laẓ
tadyant-nni yufa-tt d tagnit akken ad yeṭṭixer seg leqraya wa ad inadi ɣef uxeddim
yufa-t ɣer yiwen n umdan yesɛan yiwen n useddari neɣ agaraǧ ideg ixeddem tikeryas
d yiwen seg yineslemaẓra yettwassnen
yezmer lḥal ad yebdu axeddim deg wussan i d-iteddun
sem  seg yulyu
seg yiḍ-nni tbeddel tmuɣli-inu ɣef tlawin
uɣalent wallen-iw fellunt iselsa-nsent sugunent talɣa n tfekka-nsent ladɣa tibbucin timessaḍin d wayen yezgan ddaw n tmiḍt
s tidet tura sɛiɣ ugur
ɣef waya i ɣ-yumeṛ rebbi ad neqqen allen-nneɣ ur nettemsalam ara d tmeṭṭut am wakken yumeṛ tameṭṭut yumnen s tlusi n lḥiǧab akken ur tǧebbed ara tafekka-ines lwelha n urgaz
ugur-inu yennerna seg wasmi d-tuɣal uletma s axxam deg yimuras n unebdu
uletma farida ur as-tuqiɛ ara maḍi
ḥala iselsa ifrawanen d iwezzlanen i tettlusu  tuyat-is d yiḍarren-is ttɣimin ɛeryan
tseḍḥiɣ ad muqleɣ ɣur-s neɣ ad qqimeɣ sdat-s
uɣaleɣ ur heddreɣ ara yid-s rewwleɣ fell-as
d tidet azɣal n unebdu ixenneq amdan maca acu ad nexdem  mi ara i yi-tessumer ad nales i kra n yiluɣma n tusnakt d teɣrasna ttagiɣ
afukel i as-ttakeɣ yesɛa anamek
imi qabel ad ɛiwdeɣ i useggas ayɣer ad seɛyuɣ iman-iw seg tura
qabel ad sɛuɣ aseggas aɣurbiz s lekmal-is akken ad ɣreɣ akken ilaq
maca ssebba n ṣṣeḥ  uɣaleɣ ur zmireɣ ara ad qqimeɣ tama n tmeṭṭut ɣas ulamma d uletma
ugar n waya uɣaleɣ seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ ɛezzleɣ iman-iw deg tzeqqa n usired kkateɣ abakur ɣas akken ẓriɣ d leḥram yernu tamernut ɣer sidi rebbi qessiḥet
sakin ad sirdeɣ iman-iw wa ad stuqteɣ deg tẓallit
bdiɣ ttnadiɣ deg yidlisen n lfiqh ɣef waddud n usɣan seg temsalt-agi yerzan yal ilemẓi
summren irkelli tikti n zzwaǧ
maca amek ad zewǧeɣ u nekkini urɛad ɛeddaɣ mraw d ṭam n yiseggasen deg tudert-iw mazal ur kfiɣ ara leqraya-inu
uẓam llan kra summren tuẓamin
bdiɣ ttẓumuɣ
maca tuẓamin deg unebdu mačči d ayen isehlen ussan ḥman mliḥ d tirɣi yernu ɣezzifet zemren ad ɛeddin mraw d ukkuẓet n tsaɛtin
ḥesleɣ ur ẓriɣ ara d acu ara xedmeɣ
uɣaleɣ ttaggadeɣ ad waliɣ isura ulamma deg tiliẓri azzayri
mi walaɣ argaz ibedd tama n tmeṭṭut neggzent ɣer tidmi-w tugniwin-nni timelɛunin
