tifrat attan deg usṭuqet n tɣuri n leqran akked tẓallit
tazmamt-nni yunag wallaɣ-iw qqimeɣ ttxemmimeɣ deg wugur n nabil ameɣbun
ugur-ines tuɣ-it yiwen n wass d ugur-inu ula d nekk
ula d nekk ssneɣ d acu iwumi qqaren i ccehwa n tfekka s ugacur kan
asmi i d-yezgan ɣef ugni-nni ngguǧ seg utemmu-nneɣ amelɛun nruḥ ad nezdeɣ deg taddart n sidi ɛmer
yiwen n wass temmeslay-as-d yiwet n tǧaret i yemma ɣef yiwen n lḥemmam i d-yezgan deg tama niḍen n taddart dɣa tuɣal tettruḥu ɣur-s
yiwen n wass tessuter deg-i ad ɛeddiɣ fell-as deg lḥemmam akken ad awiɣ yid-i s axxam tabalizt n yiselsa d tserbiḍin acku ass-nni tenwa ad truḥ d yiwet n tǧaret ɣer tmeɣra
ussan-nni tuɣ-iyi d aqcic uḍɛif wezzileɣ deg lqedd ɣef waya ur i yi-tegdil ara temɣart i sdat-i tlawin tifekkiwin-nni n yessefraken lḥemmam anekcum ɣer tzeqqa tameqqrant ideg sgunfuyent tlawin u ttbeddilent iselsa-nsent
takunt n wass-nni tettak anzi ɣer tuqqsa
tifekkiwin n tlawin cebḥent mačči d kra ttemḍugarent sya u sya
qqureɣ deg umkan-iw allen-iw brarḥent deg tlawin-nni ssikideɣ deg tgelmatin timellalin tiwerdiyin d txemriyin ɣumment mnasef kan zemreɣ ad iniɣ tura mebla ma ɣelṭeɣ labaɛda deg temɣer-inu ideg tafekka n tmeṭṭut ur iyi-d-tuɣal ara d uffir umbaɛd mi jerrbeɣ yal ssenf u yal laɛmer n tlawin belli tuget n tfekkiwin-nni llant d tiɛeryanin irkelli
neɣ akka i d-tressa tugna-nni deg ccfawat-inu
ar tura mazal ttwaliɣ tihuskayin yettembiwilen s nnefxa d zzux
yal tameṭṭut tettzuxxu s thuski-ines umbaɛd mi tmekken tafekka-ines acḥal n tsaɛtin i uzɣal n tzeɣwa tiḥmayanin d usizdeg s yal ssenf n ssabun
ḥemmlent tlemẓiyin ad serḥent i umzur-nsent aberkan aɣezzfan ad t-mecḍent umbaɛd ma ad t-ssuffɣen seg lḥebs n lximar i iɣummen iqerra-nsent s ṭul n useggas
tugna-agi n tlawin turez-iyi ɣur-s qqureɣ kan ula d ssut n yemma i yi-yessawalen ur as-sliɣ ara armi i yi-teqqes temɣart-nni yessefraken lḥemmam deg umayeg-inu tɛeggeḍ fell-i
sakin mi ddmeɣ tabalizt qesdeɣ tawwurt ad ffɣeɣ sliɣ-as thedder i tmeṭṭut niḍen tenna-as 
 imecṭaḥ-agi d ccwaṭen mazal ur ffiɣen ara seg lqaɛa maca allen-nsen d allen n yirgazen
acḥal d abrid i gguleɣ ur ttaǧǧaɣ yiwen n umecṭuḥ ad yezger amnar maca ɣas akken tettuɣ iman-iw ttaǧǧaɣ-ten ad kecmen 
ula d nekk teqqim tugna-nni teṭṭafar deg-i acḥal n wussan d nettat i yessakin ccehwa n tfekka-inu dɣa uɣaleɣ ḥebbkeɣ deg  ɛmimer  yal mi ara yectaq aḥbak yernu acḥal i yelha uḥbak-nni mebla ma ḥulfaɣ i ddnub deg wayen xeddmeɣ
deg tallit-nni tamussni-inu deg usɣan ur tɛeddi ara almad n kra n tsurtin n leqran
ula d sidi lmulud aselmad n leqran ihedder-aɣ kan ɣef yisental yerzan almad n tefyar d tsurtin ur yuɣ ara tannumi yettmeslay yid-neɣ s waṭas
yeqqar-aɣ-d kan uqbel ma nekker ad neffeɣ sɣur-s ilaq ad naɣ awal i yimawlan-nneɣ ad nbaɛɛed ɣef tkerkas d tkerḍa
tuẓulin-a qqiment deg-i
ur skidibeɣ ɣef yiwen ur ttemɣeɣ ɣef wayla n wayeḍ ɣas ulamma ḥwajeɣ neɣ yettawwi-iyi ṭṭmeɛ
deg tallit-nni llan
 yixammen imeqqranen  deg tuget n temdinin
ma iḥulfa yilemẓi i tfekka-ines tebɣa ad tmass tameṭṭut abrid yettawin ɣer tullas n  uxxam n tquḥbit  yeshel i tifin
cfiɣ mliḥ ɣef tikkeklt tamezwarut ideg ṭṭseɣ akked tmeṭṭut
d ameddakkel-iw lǧilali i yi-yewwin ɣer din
lliɣ deg uɣerbaz n usileɣ n yiselmaden deg xmis
melyana sɛiɣ snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen jehdeɣ aglim-inu imal mliḥ ɣer tebrek kemmlen-as yinẓaḍen n cclaɣem d tamart ɣef waya lliɣ ttbineɣ-d meqqreɣ ugar
kukraɣ ciṭuḥ mi kecmeɣ ɣer ubraḥ ahrawan yeččuren s tid yesnuzuyen tayri yal yiwet tefser tafekka-ines tahuskayt maca tabɣest n lǧilali i ifernen tameṭṭut i yiman-is yerna tayeḍ i nekk tsellek-iyi
ḍefreɣ tameṭṭut-nni ɣer texxamt-is xeddmeɣ iwumi zemreɣ akken ad snejliɣ akukru-nni
temdel kan tawwurt tenna   yallah kkes aserwal-ik 
sakin teṭṭes tinegnit ɣef umeṭreḥ tcerreɛ mliḥ i yiḍarren-teṭṭef-iyi is tenna   ɣiwel 
yekref wallaɣ-iw mi yesla i lehdur-a
d tikkelt tamezwarut ideg ṭṭseɣ akked tmeṭṭut
ɛerḍeɣ ad waliɣ agerruj uffir yellan sdat n wallen-iw maca tafat ur tejhid ara ur walaɣ ara aṭas
tekcem-iyi tasmuḍi tessenɣes seg tezɣel n tfekka-inu ḥulfaɣ sakin i ubbuc-iw yettuɣal d asellaw d alexlux
maca mi ḍeggreɣ iman-iw ɣef tfekka n tcermuḍt tuɣal-iyi-d cihwa-nni
skecmeɣ abbuc-iw deg uḥeččun-ines aḥmayan ur ɛeddant ara kra n tsinin armi ḍeggreɣ ẓẓel tergagayt
tdegger-iyi akin twehha-d ɣer yiwet n teɣmert tenna   hatan ssṭel d waman sired iman-ik

ur iyi-ɛǧiben ara lehdur-is
mačči akka i tettmeslay tmeṭṭut ulamma d tacermuḍt
ffɣeɣ syin ul-iw yenneqbaḍ
ndemmeɣ rfiɣ mliḥ
mi as-ḥkiɣ i
lǧilali ayen i yi-yeḍran d tcermuḍt-nni yeṭṭerḍeq s taḍsa yenna-yi-d   d acu lqeḥba yesnuzuyen aḥeččun-ines  ad k-tɣer isefra n niẓar
qebbani neɣ tasuret n  lmuɛwadateyn   wagi d amkan n wuqqu d aya 
ur whimeɣ ara seg lehdur n umnir-inu i yi-yemlan abrid yettawin s  axxam n tquḥbit  yettwassen s yimeslyen n yihwah
ur yezmir ara ad yenṭeq s yiwet n tefyirt mebla ma yerna-as yir awal itezzin ɣef uktawal n wayen yellan ddaw n tbaggust
yir lehdur zgan sexdamen-ten yirgazen d yilmeẓyen armi nuɣal d ayen neqbel-iten
maca mi ara azzlen wawalen-a yumsen ɣef yiles n tmeṭṭut d tamsalt tamaynut fell-i tessewhem-iyi mliḥ
yernu ar tura mazal ur ibeddel ara uxemmem-inu
ɣas akken tirmit tamezwarut ur iyi-taɛǧib ara maḍi qrib i yi-tessekreh iḍes d tlawin maca ufiɣ iman-iw kra n tettraǧuḍ seg imectariyen
kra steqsayent ɣef wussan umbaɛd leḥḥuɣ deg uzniq-nni uḍyiq
uɣaleɣ yiwet n tikkelt snat n tikkal kraḍet ukkuẓet armi i yi-yexleḍ leḥsab
faqeɣ belli tid izedɣen deg lḥebs-nni n ccehwa mxalafent amek ttmagarent d wamek ttmeslayent liḥala-inek akked tazmert-ik tamurt-ik d twuri-inek tikkwal steqsayent ma tzewǧeḍ neɣ xaṭi
ulac leqbaḥa neɣ awal n yihwah deg lehdur-nsent neɣ tuffɣa seg leɛwayed
kra deg-sent ttawḍent alamma sirdent abbuc-ik s waman yeḥman wa ad k-ɛiwnent ad telseḍ iselsa-inek amedya s uqfal n tqeffalin
iḍes d tlawin yemxalaf seg tmeṭṭut ɣer tayeḍ mačči am wakken i d-yeqqar umeddakkel-iw lǧilali
mačči d asmiri n wayen izaden seg ẓẓel
ma yella akka tiyita n ubakur tɛumm
yal tacermuḍt ɣur-s tarrayt i usuffeɣ d usnerni n ccehwa-inek yal yiwet deg-sent daɣen tessumer addud i wuqqu
ɣef waya wid yuɣen tannumi ttẓurun tullas-a qessḍen yiwet n tcermuḍt kan yal yiwen anta i yebɣa ɣas ma ufan aṭas n tullas d tilelliyin ttraǧunt d uḥettet n temɣart-nni yessefraken axxam akken ad ɣiwlen ad fernen yiwet d acu truḥ-d ad txedbeḍ  neɣ asewsen i tid ibedden d tid yeqqimen
hatta sselɛa sdat-wen fren yiwet ma tzemreḍ ma telliḍ s tidet d afeḥli
deg tazwara ur iyi-yaɛǧib ara uggani-nsen sakin faqeɣ i wuffir tekkes-iyi lewhama dɣa uɣaleɣ am nitni ttraǧuɣ s laɛqel kan alamma teffeɣ-d tin i bɣiɣ
maca ẓriɣ yakk temsal-a asmi i yi-yerḍel ɛemmar  d amidaw niḍen nesberweḍ jmiɛ acḥal n yiseggasen yewweḍ laɛfu n rebbi mi yewweḍ ukkuẓet n tmerwin n yiseggasen umbaɛd aṭṭan i ɣ-t-yewwin deg kra n wagguren kan
adlis  tibḥirt n laɛṭer 
 annefzawi  ar tura mazal cfiɣ ɣef tefyirt tamezwarut swayes yebda udlis-ines   tamayt i yakuc i yerran lbenna tameqqrant n yirgazen deg yiḥeččunen n tlawin yerra-tt daɣen i tlawin deg yibbac n yirgazen 
asmi qqareɣ adlis-a ssneɣ zehra tasṭayfit tamidawt-inu deg usensu amerku ideg zedɣeɣ deg yiseggasen-nni mi lliɣ d aselmad
amer ur telli ara d tacermuḍt yerna ẓran irkelli acu txeddem tili rriɣ-tt d tamaɛcuqt-iw
maca amek i yezmer urgaz am nekkini yetturebban deg tmetti yebnan ɣef leɛwayed i yettwalin tameṭṭut yeznan tumes ɣef yilef ad yaɣ yiwet seg ssenf-a
yal mi ara ixaq wul-iw ad aliɣ ɣer wannag wis semmus aneggaru
ur iyi-terri ara ula d yiwet n tikkelt ɣer deffir ɣas ma tesɛa tarda
teẓra amek ad tessismeḍ ccehwa-inu s uslaf d umcaḥ n uferḍas
acḥal d abrid tusa-yi-d ccehwa ḍeggreɣ ẓẓel-inu deg yimi-s
ur treffu ara
ad d-tekker ad tessired iman-is wa ad tessired i bu-yiwet n tiṭ sakin ad teqqim ad tkemmel tiḥkayin-ines ur nkeffu
ɣur-s aɛemmur n teḥkayin ɣef medden tawacult-is d temẓi-ines
nettat seg temdint n  lɛelma  neɣ am wakken i as-teqqar
aswir-ines deg ulmad ur iɛedda kra n yiseggasen deg uswir amenzu
am nekk kif-kif teǧǧa-tt tmacint n uselmed
amgared gar-aneɣ nekk ssawḍeɣ ad qeḍɛeɣ ayen i yi-ruḥen s lfeḍl n uselmed n yiḍ akked gma lmilud
tawacult-is tusa-d seg tudrin umbaɛd timunent n tmurt truḥ am waṭas n twaculin ɣer temdint
asmi tewweḍ mraw d sa n taddart yiseggasen deg tudert-is yetɛedda fell-as yiwen n userdas
yeṛgem-as ad tt-yaɣ maca seg wasmi iruḥ ur d-iban ara
asmi d-yusa yiwen seg twacult-ines yettidiren deg taddart ad yessuter afus-is tugi maḍi tettru ulac acu ur texdim ara armi knan yimawlan-is ladɣa baba-s ur negzim ara assaɣ d taddart-is yettruḥu ɣur-s s ssebba neɣ mebla ssebba
tamezwarut tuggad lefḍiḥa d yinalkamen-is ara yeglun s ddel i nettat d twacult-is s lekmal-is
tis snat tugi ad d-tuɣal ɣer tudert n taddart d leqdic n uxxam iwaɛren mliḥ asizdeg n uddaynin asewwi n wučči d uɣrum ɣef usɣar mačči s lgaz am wakken yella ɣur-sen deg temdint
nniɣ-as tesɛa lḥeq deg ufukel wis sin acku tudert deg tura tewɛer s ttmektayeɣ lḥif n yemma d wurfan-is seg yir lefḥem asɣar ibezgen d wabbu i itetten allen
kra n wagguren umbaɛd tessen yiwen n userdas niḍen i d-yusan seg
ɛennaba
tella tettruḥu yid-s ɣer temdint n seṭṭif ideg ikerru taxxamt deg yiwen n usensu tettɣimi yid-s ass s lekmal-is
sakin tuɣal tesɛedday yid-s uḍan teskiddib ɣef leqraya-ines yimawlan-is tlemmed daɣen lexyaḍa
aserdas-nni yewɛer yid-s ladɣa ma ad yeṣkeṛ
yewweḍ armi tt-yessuffeɣ deg tnasfa n yiḍ seg texxamt yeglem-itt s yir lehdur  tacermuḍt tafuḥant takeḥluct d taxemrit mliḥ tamerkut teǧǧa-t truḥ ɣer tmanaɣt
mi izad fell-as lḥal teḥwaǧ idrimen tebda txeddem tawuri taqdimt yellan deg umezruy am wakken i qqaren
lliɣ yid-s d uɣdim ulac acu i as-ṛegmeɣ
ttakkeɣ-as azal n usmuzget-inu ɣas akken tettaggi
tezga teqqar-tidet mazal ar teqqar-asen tettkemmil fell-as tettaṭṭaf nnefs kan iyi-d   nekkni d lǧiran lǧar yettwaḥseb am yiwen seg yimawlan nettɛawan-it mebla lexlas 
sakin ad tkemmel awal s teḍsa yeččuren s teḥraymit   kečč d aselmad ameɣbun jmeɛ idrimen-ik ad k-nefɛen i lebni n uxxam 
teqqar-iyi-d
ma semṭeɣ leǧyubat-ines ččuren yakan s yidrimen i tessekcem sɣur yimsaɣen imerkantiyen
xedmeɣ yid-s aṭas n wadduden n wuqqu i d-wwiɣ seg udlis n  annefzawi  uqbel ma ad d-ffɣen yidlisen n tugniwin n wuqqu sakin isura n i d-yeɣlin fell-aneɣ am ucercur s ubrid n yimaṭṭafen n tiliẓri ɣas akken aṭas n medden i ibedden mgal n waya
ma deg lbaḍna ayen iḍerrun deg tuffra ḥala rebbi i yeẓran uffiren-ines
yeṭṭuqet uɣway ulac allalen ara ibedden deg wudem-is dɣa ɣerrqen medden deg yiberdan iwernenniyen i itetten tudert-nsen seg daxel am twekka
uɣalent ass-a temsal n uheǧǧu d yinɣayen yerzan tuzzuft ttaččarent isebtar n yiɣmisen d tgennariyin n yixxamen n teɣdemt
ahuǧǧu n warrac imeẓyanen d tumant tamaynut ur tettwassnen ara uqbel
ula d sbiṭarat tura ttaččaren s yiḥḍiḍen
ula kra n yixxamen n yigujilen i nesɛa ur zmiren ara tura ad ten-awin akken ad ten-rebbin
ma d wid nettaf daxel n tecekkarin ttuḍegren deg yiguduyen d wid yettwaxenqen neɣ wid yettwgezmen d iwezwazen d ayen yesserfayen ɣef waya ilaq ad nemmeslay ɣef wugur-agi
aɣlaq n yixxamen n tquḥbit d lɣelṭa tameqqrant i yexdem udabu i yeslan i yinaw amasɣan ameṭṭarfu
inaw-agi amasɣan ur yufi deg wuguren i ttmagaren yimdanen ḥala ixxamen n tquḥbit imezdaɣ-is ur ssawḍen ara yiwen seg lmeyya seg tmetti maca tessemneɛ luluf n yimdanen seg yinɣayen i ɣelben zzna
mebla ma nemmeslay ɣef waṭṭanen izfanen yettanṭaḍen
acḥal d abrid i d-mčaqlaleɣ d yimidawen-inu imastanen deg tgennariyin n uxxam n teɣdemt ɣef yinɣayen izfanen dɣa sumreɣ fell-asen ad nezwir ad nessuter deg tmetti akked ddula ad ldin ixxamen n tquḥbit
d ccer ilaqen d ccer yellan deg yal timetti
yernu timura tineɣram xeddment isuḍaf d leqwanen i twuri-agi akken ur tteffɣent ara afus-nsent
ma d nukkni nessemras tasertit n unhil ungif nɣil nezmer ad nɣumm iṭij s uɣerbal
neckunṭeḍ deg yiwen n yinaw anazzam amakun yebna ɣef teḥkayin tiqburin tuget deg-sent d asnulfu i tent-id-snulfan usant-d seg yiwen n umaḍal yebɛed ɣef tilawt-nneɣ am wakken yebɛed yigenni ɣef lqaɛa
d acu-t waful neɣ lmektub n yigiman n warrac yettwattun deg yixxamen n yigujilen  mačči d lbumbat ara yesseqwun tinnɣi d tiṭṭurfa ad d-yas wass ad ṭerḍqent fell-aneɣ irkelli  ugar n waṭṭanen izfanen yettanṭaḍen d yinɣayen izfanen yettnernin seg wass ɣer wayeḍ yetthuddun timetti seg daxel zemren ma tkemmel akka ad hudden kulci ulac acu ad ǧǧen deffir-nsen
tamsulta teṭṭafar kan irgazen d tlawin yettilin deg yimekwan izuyaz neɣ deg yisensa s yisem n ṭṭrad mgal  d usizdeg n tmetti seg lebla-a yuɣen timetti
nessekcam-iten ɣer leḥbus am yineḍliben
ḥuddeɣ s timmad-iw ɣef waṭas n yirgazen zewǧen s leqder-nsen ur uklalen ara lefḍiḥa d ddel-nni maca d tignatin i ten-ḥettmen ad sɛun assaɣen ffɣen i ubrid n lqanun
assaɣen-inu d tlawin ur bnin ara kan ɣef tuzzuft d ccehwa n tfekka ula d aḥemmal n tayri yewwi-yi ɣerqeɣ daxel-is ɛerḍeɣ deg-s tiẓeḍt d terẓeg
tin i yessaɣen deg-i tayri d yiwet n tmastant taqbaylit d tacelhabt mugreɣ-tt i tikkelt tamezwarut deg uxxam n teɣdemt n yiɛeẓẓugen anda ṭṭfeɣ yiwen n uwezlu n lwert n yiwet n twacult yekres mačči d kra
ussan-nni lliɣ xeddmeɣ deg tnarit n
si nasser uqbel ma ad ldiɣ tanarit-inu
xedmeɣ yid-s ugar n seddis n yiseggasen
ass-nni d tikkelt tamezwarut ideg rziɣ ɣer tizi-uzzu yernu imir-n kan i bdiɣ tanhert n ṭumubil
yewwet wul-iw mi tt-walaɣ deg tnarit n uwkil n tegduda faqeɣ d nettat i yettḥuddun ɣef yixsimen n win iɣef ttḥudduɣ
nembadal kra n tenfaliyin n lekyasa sakin truḥ
tameṭṭut-nni d talemmast deg laɛmer d talemmast deg lqedd teččur maca ur zuret ara d ayen i iḥemmel wul-iw
kerheɣ tesmektayent-iyi s yemma d tlawin timeɣbunin n taddart-nneɣ
imi-s yuneɣ am ugazi  acebbub-is d awraɣ yettinig d waḍu ad as-tiniḍ d  lɛandalib al-asmer  yeččuren tudert-iw deg tallit-nni i icennun
terra tezweɣ ɣef yicenfiren-is d ayen yernan deg thuski-ines
sutreɣ awexxer n uzaraf akken ad semmdeɣ akaram-inu
maca iswi-inu uffir d timlilit yid-s tikkelt niḍen
imi tamsalt taɛna tawacult sumreɣ fell-as ad nwali ma nezmer ad naweḍ ɣer tifrat ara yeqbel yal yiwen deg yixsimen
nemtafaq ad nheggi timlilit n wahil
nemsefham ɣef yiwen n ttiɛad nniɣ-as d nekk ara yasen tirqaqanin acku ɣer tnarit-ines i d-yezgan deg tlemmast n temdint n
yiɛeẓẓugen
umbaɛd ukkuẓ n ledwar newweḍ ɣer yiwet n tifrat yesdukklen yixsimen
ɛaceɣ deg ledwar-nni yiwet n tergit tzad mliḥ
nella deg tsemhuyt n tefsut lḥal ur yeḥma ara iṭij yuɣ igenni mebla ma yeqreḥ allen n umdan
tafsut deg tmurt n leqbayel d tasemhuyt yelhan teɣleb tisemhay niḍen maca ur tettɛeṭṭil ara aṭas
ma d inessef waggur n mayyu ad tecɛel tmes n unebdu i itetten tizegzewt i d-yettarran rruḥ wa ad tt-terr d aɣebbar i iregglen wanzaren yeskawayen igerjumen
amecwar yellan gar lezzayer tamanaɣt d temdint n yiɛeẓẓugen iɛedda mya n yikulimtren ɣas akken urǧin ɛyiɣ urǧin kecmen-iyi timussa d unezgum
taqbaylit-nni tacelhabt tezga yid-i deg usugen-inu dɣa bdiɣ ssalayeɣ isinaryuten ara deg
mi ara nemlil deg uxxam n teɣdemt ɛerḍeɣ dima ad ffɣeɣ seg yifutas n umezlu i ɣ-yessemlalen akken ad mmeslayeɣ ɣef temsal i yi-yaɛnan ahat ad d-temmeslay ula d nettat ɣef tudert-is
maca texdem iwumi tezmer akken ad teqqim kan deg usatel n twuri tettaf-d dima ifukal s lecɣal niḍen ɣas akken teqqim targit-inu tettimɣur seg wass ɣer wayeḍ am ugersal-nni yerwan aman d yiṭij
yiwen n wass mi nemtafaq ɣef yifutas n tifrat n umezlu-nneɣ sdukkleɣ tabɣest yellan deg-i ldiɣ-as ul-iw sutreɣ-tt i zzwaǧ
tusa-d tririt-ines am usucef s waman isemmaḍen deg tlemmast n tegrest tenna-yi-d kra n temsal ur ten-ssineɣ uqbel
tenna-yi-d tawacult-is seg lecraf n tmurt n leqbayel iwumi neqqar imrabḍen
deg yeswehmen wid d-yessuffuɣen isura ttakkent tullas-nsent twaculin-agi leɛwayed n i yimrabḍen am nitni kan
ɣef waya ur tettxemmim ara ad tesɛu assaɣ d urgaz ur nelli ara d aqbayli amrabeḍ
tkemmel awal-is tenna   ur k-ugiɣ ara kečč s timmad-ik acku walaɣ deg-k ḥala lxir d ssifa n urgaz yelhan yettqadaren
d tagi d leɛwayed n lejdud-nneɣ ilaq ad ten-qadreɣ wa ad ḍefreɣ abrid-nsen
nekk ttqadareɣ-k ur walaɣ ara deg-k kra n lɛib ara ibedden deg ubrid n lebni n twacult yumren maca tawacult-iw urǧin ad teqbel ad d-tefk yelli-s i yiwen d aɣrib
ur bɣiɣ ara ad nnaɣeɣ d twacult-iw 
ɛerḍeɣ ad qenɛeɣ tacelhabt-inu tuzzyint mmeslayeɣ-as ɣef wassaɣen n usɣan d leɛwayed yettemcabin
wwiɣ-d awal daɣen ɣef tetrarit ɣef uselmed ɣef tmurt tayiwant i ɣ-yesddukklen iɣef mmuten leqbayel d waɛraben maca mebla lfayda
tenna-yi-d daɣen tameṭṭut taqbaylit ur tezmir ara ad teɛsu imawlan-is
ma texdem-itt taggara-s d aseɛseq d unfay
yernu ad tt-id-awin deffir-s yezmer ad tt-nɣen
ur serseɣ i yifassen-iw s sshala suffɣeɣ ayen sɛiɣ seg yifukal akken ad as-beddleɣ rray-is ad iyi-teǧǧ ad waliɣ baba-s
maca terra talast i uskasi tenɣa-yi s yiwet n tiyita mi iyi-d-tenna tettwaxḍeb yakan seg wasmi meẓẓiyet i yiwen i as-yettilin yeqqar tura deg fransa tawacult-is tettraǧu kan ad d-yekcem akken ad frun tamsalt-a wa ad ɛeqden fell-asen
mi sliɣ i yimeslayen-agi uqsiḥen yeggugem yiles-iw
uɣaleɣ xayeb ttnadiɣ ɣef yisufar ad yesneɣsen seg leqriḥ i yi-yuɣen
qqimeɣ acḥal n wagguren d amuḍin ur umineɣ ara s wayen i yi-yuɣen
uɣaleɣ ɣer usensu-inu amerku
seg wass-nni gguleɣ ur ḥemmleɣ ara tameṭṭut niḍen
ttnadiɣ ɣef zahra tasṭayfit
ula d nettat teǧǧa asensu ulac win yeẓran sani truḥ
ḥala d ticermuḍin i ufiɣ d asafar i waṭṭan-inu
uɣaleɣ mi ad yeɣli yiṭij ad zziɣ s ṭumubil-inu ɣef yiberdan n tmanaɣt akken ad refdeɣ yiwet seg-sent ad tt-ɛerḍeɣ ɣer yimensi sakin ad tt-awiɣ ɣer uxxam-inu ajdid iruḥ-d ɣur-i uneɣmas amerwal yusef
ɛeyyaci
ur ḥbiseɣ ara axemmem deg uwezlu-ines rǧiɣ tisin-ines seg yiḍ ɣer wayeḍ
icebbeh-iyi rebbi yella yettɛassa deg-i
unageɣ ɣer tmanaɣt ur d-uɣaleɣ ara zik tɛedda lɛecra n yiḍ mi kecmeɣ s axxam
kkseɣ kan iselsa-inu lsiɣ aselsu-inu n waddal i smenyifeɣ ɣef yakk yiselsa n yiḍes ulamma s leḥrir yesfan armi sliɣ i tyitwin tifessasin ɣef tewwurt
faqeɣ d netta
ahat iɛedda-d kan akka s ugacur neɣ ahat yugi ad iɛeddi lawan n yiḍes akken ur iyi-yessakay ara am wakken yexdem tikkelt yezrin
iruḥ-d weḥd-s
ulac acu i as-nniɣ
mi d-ldiɣ tawwurt ɛerḍeɣ-t ad yekcem yudef mebla akukru
ur rriɣ ara tawwurt srid rǧiɣ ad t-id-yeḍfer walbaɛḍ niḍen ahat wis kraḍ
ziɣ ulac aɛessas yeffren deg ṭṭlam yuɣ yiwet n teɣmert yettɛassa amkan
iban-d ukukru deg tigawin-ines
imuyag-ines d timeqqranin banent mliḥ ccil n uččamar awezzlan i iɣummen amur ameqqran seg wudem-is
skecmeɣ-t ɣer usalun sutreɣ deg-s ad yesgunfu skud ad d-tewǧed lqehwa ara yessenjlin fell-aneɣ nnadem d ɛeggu
seqsaɣ-t ma yebɣa ad yečč yenna-yi-d tura kan i yečča imensi
yeskef tajɣumt tamezwarut s ssut aɛlayan yessers afenǧal ɣef ṭṭabla imuqqel-iy-d mliḥ iɣeẓẓ icenfiren-is iḥukk tamgerḍt-is s yicerr n uḍaḍ-is sakin yenna 
aql-iyi ɣerqeɣ deg yiwet n twaɣit ḥala rebbi i yeẓan acḥal tekres yaɛreq-iyi cedd n uyeddid uɣaleɣ ur semgaradeɣ ara gar uqerruy-iw d uḍar-iw
iḍelli tameddit lliɣ ɣer yemma tameɣbunt
tegzem tasa-w s yimeṭṭawen d ucetki-ines
tezga tettḥawat deg-i ad ruḥeɣ ɣer temsulta ad randiɣ
teṭṭef-iyi ccil-iw ɣur-s armi d tafrara nettat tḥekku-d tettru
yal mi ara mbiwleɣ akken ad ruḥeɣ tzewwir-iyi ɣer tgallit akken ad qqimeɣ ɣur-s  sani ad truḥeḍ deg tlemmast n yiḍ  anda tegganeḍ anda tetteḍ 
eǧǧ-iyi ad rwuɣ tamuɣli-inek
tezmer ad k-tawi tmettant bɛid ccer ad iyi-teqqimeḍ d tirget yerɣan deg wul-iw
dɣa ad tt-smektiɣ belli tamsulta tettqellib fell-i yezmer ad teẓdem ɣef uxxam seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ am wakken i texdem acḥal n tikkal
maca terra-yi-d gar snat n nnehtat 
 ad ssutreɣ deg sidi rebbi ad yazen imir-a kan tamsulta ad k-tawi lḥebs wala tamettant
tif ad rzuɣ ɣur-k yiwet n tikkelt deg ddurt ad d-mmeslayeɣ yid-k ulamma semmus n ddqayeq ul-iw yeččur s usirem n tuffɣa-inek yiwen n wass ad iyi-d-tuɣaleḍ ad k-ɛemreɣ urar ad k-zewǧeɣ wa ad ddreɣ ussan-inu ineggura d warraw-ik wala ad ẓureɣ aẓekka-inek yal ass n sem
ur bɣiɣ ara ad uɣaleɣ seg tmeqbert uyseɣ seg ddunit kkaweɣ am uyeddid aqdim 
mazal ssut n yimeṭṭawen-is yettzenzun deg yimeẓẓuɣen-iw 
 tebɣiḍ ad k-nɣen s rrsas am baba-k keččini mazal-ik meẓẓeyeḍ  baba-k ad fell-as yaɛfu yerḥem yeqqur uqerruy-is ur isell i ḥedd
dɣa yečča aqerruy-is netta mazal ur yessaweḍ ara kraḍet n tmerwin n yiseggasen yeǧǧa-aɣ deg sin akked yemma-s tamuḍint nettidir deg yiwen n lḥif d aberkan ur ilaq ara ula i yiqjan 
teḥka-yi-d jidda-k belli argaz-is yettwanɣa deg ṭṭrad yeḍran deg temnaḍt n tmurt n leqbayel i d-yekkren srid umbaɛd timunnent
yiwen n wass teḥka-yi-d jidda-k taqsiḍt s lekmal-is
tenna   yuli urgaz-iw aḥmed s adrar yedda d tmunnent yimjuhad ukkuẓ n yiseggasen uqbel n yesɛedda amur ameqqran deg-sen deg tmurt n leqbayel
nella nezdeɣ deg yiwen n lḥuc d aqdim yebna s wakal d zzenk deg ulad raḥmun deg temnaḍt tataramt neɣ taɣerbit n temdint n tniya neɣ am wakken i as-ssawalen deg tallit n fransa
deg unebdu n tmunnent asmi bdant trebbuyaɛ n yimjuhad ttsubunt seg yidurar yuɣal-d ɣur-neɣ am yizem yelsa aselsu aserdasan yesɛan lhiba yerra ɣef tayet-is tamekḥalt n ssenf n mat 
negguǧ nekk d yemma-s ɣer yiwen n uxxam n urumi
nefreḥ s tmunnent nenna-d hatta tudert n lḥerma d tenkelwit i ɣ-yettraǧun
maca ya ḥasrah tudert-nni ur tɛeṭṭel ara aṭas
ayen yellan d targit yuɣal-aɣ d buberrak iberken ɣef yidmaren-nneɣ yerra-aɣ ɣer tudert-nni n zik tekres ɣef tudert ddaw n temharsa
yekker ṭṭrad deg tmurt n leqbayel yeddem urgaz-iw tamitrayit-ines yeḍfer imeddukkal-is i ɣ-yettawḍen ɣef yimennuɣen yettilin deg tqucac d tizza n tmurt n leqbayel mgaraden
nella nettwali yal ass tirkaf n yiserdasen s yigelluyen d yikumya leḥḥun ɣer ǧerǧer
kra n wagguren umbaɛd yeḥbes ṭṭrad nefreḥ neqqim tikkelt niḍen imjuhad
isallen nettraǧu tuɣalin n urgaz-iw aḥmed
nurǧa aṭas ulawen-nneɣ ččuren s usirem maca ur d-yuɣal ara
yessawel gma-s i kra n yimjuhad n tizi-uzzu maca ula d yiwen ur as-yenni acemma
neqqim nessarem tuɣalin-ines mebla lfayda
kra n wagguren umbaɛd bdan ttawḍen yisallen n ṭṭrad-nni
nesla d akken lɛesker n lkulunil huwari
bumedyen rnan lɛesker n lkulunil muḥend ulḥaǧ yenɣa lmeyyat deg-sen ttwameḍlen mebla ma ẓẓulen fell-asen mebla ma ẓran ismawen-nsen am yiɣersiwen yuḍnen s waṭṭan n tburdit
nuyes seg tmerǧiwt-ines neɣra fell-as lfatiḥa
amer dagi kan i teḥbes temsalt tili neḥmed rebbi neqbel s tikci-s
tamettant tettgani yal amdan yal yiwen s lmijal-ines
nella nezdeɣ deg uxxam-nni ucbiḥ i as-yezzin tferranin yemma-s mmi ɛebderrezzaq d nekkini akked gma-s nasser i ɣ-ileḥqen s tmeṭṭut-is d warraw-is akken ad ɣ-iḥudd deg leɣyab n gma-s am wakken i ɣ-d-yenna
yiwet n tsebḥit tusa-d tarbaɛt n yirgazen nnan-aɣ-d d imjuhad seg uxxam
yessefhem-asen uslif-iw nasser ula d argaz-iw d amjahed d netta i ɣ-d-yewwin s axxam-agi
yenna-as yiwen deg-sen 
 win i ken-d-yewwin s axxam-agi ur yettwaḥsab ara d amjahed acku yexdeɛ tagrawla d yimeɣrasen asmi yerfed leslaḥ deg wudem n tredsa n teslullit taɣelnawt tura yettwaḥseb seg yiḥerkiyen d yicenga n tegrawla d tmurt 
ffɣeɣ ɣur-sen ttruɣ ḥiwteɣ-ten maca ulawen-nsen qquren am yiẓra
suffɣen-aɣ s ddreɛ
nasser ameɣbun ur yufi acu ad yexdem
yerra-aɣ ɣer utemmu-nneɣ aqdim
nasser cekklen yifassen-is
yella yettqudur ssutren deg-neɣ ad neffeɣ seg uḍar aẓelmaḍ yettaf uguren deg tikli
yuɣal ixeddem deg lfirmat i d-yezzin i 
nekk daɣen yečča-yi lḥif uɣaleɣ xeddmeɣ deg lfirmat i yuɣalen d ayla n yimjuhad
acḥal i ttruɣ acḥal i yi-tɣaḍ tejhelt n urgaz-iw
amer yeqqim yid-neɣ deg uxxam-nni ucbiḥ tili mazal-it yedder yekseb ula netta yiwet n lfirma d tamsirewt
deg tallit-nni tteffreɣ isem-iw d lasel-iw uggadeɣ ad iyi-yessuffɣen seg uxeddim
d nnhaya n uslif-iw
asmi yuli baba-s s adrar yedda d tegrawla mmi ɛebderrezzaq yella yesɛa imir-n seddis n yiseggasen deg laɛmer-is
kra n yiseggasen umbaɛd timunnent yuɣal d ilemẓi yejhed am baba-s
dɣa ur iyi-yeǧǧi ara ad xedmeɣ iruḥ ad yexdem ula d netta deg lfirmat
tseggem tudert-nneɣ ciṭuḥ
nuɣal meqqar ur nessin ara laẓ nettaɣ iselsa imaynuten
maca ddaɛwessu teḍfer-aɣ tikkelt niḍen
asmi bdan medden deg tallit n bumedyen ttmeslayen ɣef ujmaɛ n yiɣsan n yimeɣrasen akken ad ten-meḍlen deg tmeqbrin-nsen weḥd-sen wa ad fken lbaga i tuǧǧal-nsen d warraw-nsen yebda mmi ɛedberrezzaq yettḥerrik akken ad iẓer acu yeḍran i baba-s
meqqer yuɣal ifehhem deg tsertit
yebda yettnadi yesteqsay ɣef wayen yeḍra
ur yeḥbis ara tikli ur yeǧǧi ara amkan iwala yakk wid yeẓran acu yeḍran deg ṭṭrad-nni tamelɛunt
yeẓra tidet am wakken i yeqqar
sakin yebda ireddu deg lɛesker n bumedyen d nitni i yenɣan baba-s
iruḥ ɣer lqasma n yimjuhad iqdimen yessuter deg-sen ad skelsen baba-s ɣef wumuɣ n yimeɣrasen
ugin nnan-as ur semlalayen ara iḥerkiyen d yimeɣrasen deg yiwen n umkan
yennuɣ-iten yergem-iten yergem ula d huwari bumedyen yenna-d fell-as d aneḍlib d netta i yenɣan ɛebban remḍan d lkulunil
caɛbani
seg wansi i d-yettawi mmi isallen-agi ɣef tegrawla  lemdeɣ sɣur-s aṭas n temsal urǧin sliɣ yis-sent ɣas akken ddreɣ tallit n tegrawla
mi ara d-yekcem s axxam yettuɣal-d s wurfan
kra n wussan umbaɛd kecmen yirgazen n tɣellist taserdasant s axxam-nneɣ deg yiḍ wwin mmi
qrib i mmuteɣ deg wussan-nni qellbeɣ fell-as deg lkumisaryat n temsulta ɣer temsetla qqaren-iyi-d irkelli ulac acu ẓran fell-as
nnan-iyi-d kra ahat d tarbaɛt n yineḍliben i t-yewwin ɣef temsal yerzan tanezzut n sselɛa yettwagedlen
ṭṭfen-t ɣur-sen ugar n waggur
mi s-serḥen yuɣal s axxam qrib ur t-taɛqil ara imi aṭas i ibeddel
ɣlint-as snat n tuɣmas seg wuglan unnigen iselsa-ines rkan qersen irkelli
yuɣal-aɣ-d d imirqiq am usɣar
yeqqim deg uxxam ur yeffiɣ ara irkelli acḥal n wagguren yezga ireggem yettgalla ad d-yerr ttar
yugi ad ɣ-yales d acu s-yeḍran deg lḥebs
maca mi ara nwali ddɣel i yesɛa mgal yal yiwen yesɛan assaɣ d unagraw n bumedyen ad neḥsu kksen fell-as sser sbehdlen-t sɛeddan-t deg ssikkis fransa ur t-tesɛeddi ara ɣef yizzayriyen
yenna-as ɛemmi-s ad yinig ɣer umkan niḍen ibaɛden ideg ulac win i t-yessnen wa ad yeḥbes tirdayin-ines acku bumedyen d anezmar ɣur-s imjelkaḍen teqqur tasa-nsen
tikkelt-a yezmer ur itteffeɣ seg bu-yikurdan-nsen ḥala ma yuɣal d tafekka taqqurant neɣ d amaɛḍur ur yezmir ara ad yelḥu
iɣab mmi kra n ledwar sakin yuɣal-d yiwet n tsebḥit s ukamyun yewwi-aɣ ɣer udcir-a n lebrarik
ɣiwleɣ ɣer zzwaǧ-is akken ad terked tnefsit-ines wa ad yeḥbes deg unbac deg umezruy i nebɣa ad nesfeḍ irkelli seg ccfawat-nneɣ 
tkemmel yemma tenna   maca ɣas akken ur yessers ara baba-k i yifassen-is
yeqqim yesteqsay yettnadi wa ireddu deg
bumedyen belli d netta i yenɣan baba-s d lmeyyat n yimjuhad deg ṭṭrad n tmurt n leqbayel d wacḥal n yisertayen am xiḍer d krim belqasem d uneḥbus n tmerwin n waggagen i yewwten deg useɣli n yiserdasen n leḥkem n ben bella
yebder-d aṭas n yismawen maca ur cfiɣ ara fell-asen irkelli
am wakken teẓriḍ a mmi nekk ur kcimeɣ ara ɣer uɣerbaz ur ssineɣ ara ayen tessneḍ keččini
ɣef waya yewɛer fell-i ad fehmeɣ imennuɣen iɣef yella yettmeslay baba-k
ula d netta ur yeɣri ara aṭas am wakken itteffeɣ i yi-d-yeḥka
maca netta d argaz yettemlili d medden ilemmed
ugar n waya yeqqar iɣmisen d yidlisen
ma d nekk d tabujadit tameɣbunt kemneɣ deg uxxam ccɣel-iw d asewwi asired n yiselsa d urebbi-inek acku imir-n mazal-ik d llufan
ad staɛerfeɣ tura lliɣ ḥemmleɣ tugna n bumedyen i yekreh baba-k ireddu-t d netta i yenɣan baba-s yewweḍ ɣer udabu s yiɣil d yiserdasen
ma iyi-d-yaf selleɣ i yinawen-ines i d-yettɛeddayen yal ass deg rradyu ad t-yessens wa ad yebdu rregmat ur ẓriɣ ara ma d nekk i yeqseḍ s rregmat-nni neɣ d axsim-is
mi d-iban umussu n nnfaq n buyaɛli i yeṭṭfen iɣawel baba-k yedda d yimnafqen
yuɣal yettɣibi acḥal n wussan ma seqsaɣ-t yeqqar-iyi-d d ttar n baba-s i yettarra
hedreɣ yid-s yiwen imudaɣ n tablaḍt n wass fkiɣ-as rray-iw nniɣ-as cukkeɣ deg trennawt-ines ɣef yiserdasen n bumedyen yerfa fell-i yenna-yi-d kemm d tameṭṭut yeččuren d nniya acku ttamneɣ s lekdubat d tkerkas n uneḍlib-nni
dɣa yebda yettmeslay kra n lehdur meqqrit ɣef uswir-inu ur fhimeɣ deg-sen iqiḥ
sakin yessuter deg-i ad ɣbuɣ sser ur ttbuḥuɣ ara yis-s i walbaɛḍ niḍen
ma yesseqsayi-d walbaɛḍ ad as-iniɣ argaz-iw ixeddem deg ɛennaba
ɣas akken acḥal d abrid i newwi nekk d yemma-s awal ɣef usentel-a
nenna-as nuggad ad as-teḍru am baba-s ad ɣ-yeǧǧ snat n tlawin d llufan ameẓyan mebla asalel ara ɣ-iḥudden
tesmekta-t-id yemma-s s tedyant n usuffeɣ-nsen seg uxxam ucbiḥ n urumi ideg zedɣen umbaɛd timunnent d wamek uɣalen ɣer tudert n lḥif umbaɛd mi ssnen tudert n tenkelwit
yezmer ad ɣ-yaɣ kter n win yezrin
maca d wumi ad temmeslayeḍ  yezmer ad k-isell uɛeẓẓug ad k-iwali uderɣal ma d baba-k ur isell ḥala i wayen s-yeqqar uqerruy-is aqquran ur yettwali ḥala ayen yebɣa ad iwali netta
tesɛiḍ imir-n sin n yissagasen
nesla sakin s tmenɣiwt deg wass n lɛid tameqqrant n yiwen n umsaltu deg uɣerbaz n temsulta i d-yezgan deg ssumɛa
baba-k yella d anabay
kra n wussan umbaɛd teẓḍem-d temsulta ɣef uxxam-nneɣ tnuda-d snat n texxamin d tnawalt tardest tardest nnan i jidda-k baba-k yenɣa yiwen n umsaltu yuker leslaḥ-is ahat yeffer-it deg uxxam-is
wwin-aɣ ɣer uxxam n temsulta seqsan-aɣ acḥal n sswayeɛ
baba-k urǧin d-yuɣal s axxam
nnɣan-t s rrsas deg tqucac n ccriɛa
wwin-d tafekka-ines ḍeggren-tt ɣef umnar n tewwurt
kkren-d kra seg lǧiran ad t-meḍlen deg tmeqqbert tazayezt
aṭas i tettru jidda-k ɣef tmettant tucmit n mmi-s yemmut urgaz-is ur as-tessin ar tura aẓekka ad tẓur deg laɛyud wa ad tɣerr fell-as lfatiḥa
ur tefriḥ ara tmeɣbunt ula yiwen n wass deg ddunit-is
temmut kra n wagguren kan umbaɛd seg lɣiḍ
hatta twaɣit tluḥeq-aɣ-d tikkelt niḍen
tuɣeḍ abrid i yuɣ baba-k tḍefreḍ tirebbuyaɛ n yimnafqen
taggara-inek am tin n baba-k d jeddi-k  ad temteḍ s rrsas wa tettwameḍleḍ d aɣrib
ɣef waya ad sutreɣ deg-k a mmi ad txemmeḍ mliḥ akken ad tesmenɛeḍ iman-ik seg lmut
kra n yiseggasen deg lḥebs kan ad teffɣeḍ umbaɛd
kečč teɣriḍ yeshel fell-ak ad tafeḍ axeddim yelhan ara k-iɛiwnen ara ɣ-yesbaɛden ɣef twuɣa i d-yesseɣli baba-k ɣef yiqerra-nneɣ 
akka i temmeslay yemma tameɣbunt tegzem tasa-w ttruɣ yid-s
umbaɛd kra n lweqt n tsusmi ikemmel yenna 
 ruḥeɣ-d ɣur-k a akken ad iyi-d-tafeḍ tifrat ad iyi-yessuffɣen seg twaɣit-a ideg ɣliɣ 
sussmeɣ ula nekk
tesmekta-yi-d teqsiḍt n baba-s s teqsiḍt n gma lmilud yettwanɣan ula d netta deg yiwen n ṭṭraḍ ideg yella daɣen bumedyen
ar tura mazal ssut n ukabural ɛemmar i d-mugreɣ kra n yiseggasen umbaɛd mi yuɣaleɣ d amastan itezzi daxel n ccfawat-inu 
 xedɛen-aɣ ad ten-yexdeɛ rebbi
nnuɣen ɣef ukesri ẓẓuɣren-aɣ yid-sen ɣas ulac acu i ɣ-icerken yid-sen la taɣaḍt la tixsi wala tayaẓiḍt
milud yella seg yimidawen-inu ɛzizen fell-i
akken i nelmed tanhert d usexdem n yigelluyen deg ḥasi beḥbeḥ deg temnaḍt n lǧelfa
nella nettzuxxu s twuri-nneɣ deg lɛesker d tjernaḍt i nettaɣ yal aggur
tawacult-iw ula d nekk d tigellilt seg sidi laɛǧel tesliḍ yis-s yakan
d taddart yettwattun deg tegrest ḥala asemmiḍ d waḍu i iqellɛen isekla deg unebdu yettuɣal waḍu-nni d urɣu deg ḥertadem d aẓḍam n ujrad
ur cukkeɣ ara tella ɣef lkarṭa n lezzayer
d aɣrum i yi-yewwin ɣer lɛesker
ur ttaggadeɣ ɛeggu ur ttaggedeɣ asemmiḍ neɣ azɣal
nekkni d tarwa n ṭṭrad n teslullit nuɣ tannumi d laẓ fad akked tuɛrin
nufa deg lɛesker iselsa yeḥman učči mebla cceḥḥa d laman
nella nettak-d ulac akken ad nessefreḥ iɣella-nneɣ nlemmed seg wul amek ad neqres s leslaḥ amek ad nexdem iluɣma-nneɣ iserdasanen akken ad nḥudd ɣef tmurt-nneɣ iɣef fkan amelyun d uzgen n umelyun n yimaɣrasen tudert-nsen d asfel akken ad ssuffɣen tamhersa seg tmurt-a
mi ara ɣ-d-fken ttesriḥ ntteffeɣ ɣer temdint
nleḥḥu iqerra-nneɣ deg yigenni nettzuxxu s yiselsa-nneɣ i yettḥaraben fell-aneɣ
nella nettwali tismin deg wallen n wid d wumi nettmeslay
neqbel ad ɣ-awin ɣer unazir mebla urfan neɣ urnan acku numen d nekkni i d imḥaddan n tmurt am wakken i ɣ-slemden
imaɣrasen wwin-d tilelli i tmurt-a s yidammen-nsen kunwi d ixulaf-nsen d kunwi ara iḥudden ɣef tmurt-agi seg yimnekcamen iberraniyen
d tanfalit i nsell ssbeḥ tameddit
aḥuddu ɣef tmurt d tamsit tameqqrant i nbubb ɣef tuyat-nneɣ
d wagi i nexdem mi telmatin
gezmen yigelluyen-nneɣ
yenna-aɣ-d ufesyan   tamanaɣt n tmurt attan deg umihi ignan d irusiyen tečča times-nsen ilaq ad nɣiwel ad tt-nsellek 
neḥma nɣiwel nruḥ ad tt-nsellek
nuɣ awal i yiɣella-nneɣ
nelḥa s yigelluyen armi newweḍ ɣer yiwen n ugni ur yebɛid ara ɣef temdint n
lɛefrun nerǧa awwaḍ n lemɛawna ad ɣ-d-yasen seg utaram azzayri
tuɣ-iyi d gma-k daxel n yiwen n ugelluy
ur neẓri ara nruḥ d asfel n ṭṭmeɛ i yewwin kra n yifesyanen n tegrawla s timmad-nsen iswi-nsen aseɣli n
bumedyen akken ad aɣen amkan-is
deg tefrara mi nwala isaffagen n ṭṭrad ɣummen igenni bdan aḍegger n lbumbat fell-aneɣ ur tteffreɣ ara fell-ak suggneɣ-ten d isaffagen ifransiyen i d-yuɣalen ad ṭṭfen tamurt
neɛreḍ ad nḥudd ɣef yiman-nneɣ maca igelluyen
yettwawet ugelluy-nneɣ s lbumba tecɛel deg-s tmes
lmilud yettwanɣa daxel-is
ḥuzant-iyi kra n tceqqfin deg tama tayeffust deg yiɣil d uḍar
s tmara i ffɣeɣ seg ugelluy
seḥnunḍeɣ iman-iw deg tlemmast n tmes ur ttwaliɣ acemma gar wabbu d ssut n lbumbat
ttsuɣun ttazzalen
ur neẓri acu i ɣ-iḍerrun
wa yemmut wa yettwajreḥ wa yerwel lḥasun terwi tebberwi
ur nufi ara anwa ad ɣ-yinin acu ilaq ad nexdem deg tegnit am ta
nekkni d iserdasen nettembiwel s tsunḍiwin kan
qqimeɣ deg umkan-iw nnedreɣ deg tsusmi
ur zmireɣ ara ad ḥerrkeɣ
ur newwiḍ ara d ṭnac armi ɣ-d-zzin yiserdasen seg yal amkan
d izzayriyen am nekkni
kra deg-sen ɛeqlen imeddukkal-nsen iqdimen i ssnen deg lkazirnat
nerrunda
bdan yimdanen heddren neẓra tidet
nruḥ d asfel n umennuɣ gar yimasayen ur ɣ-yaɛni ara maḍi
d imeslayen-agi i d-nniɣ i yiwen seg yifesyanen n tɣelllist taserdasant i d-yusan ad iyi-yesseqsi mi lliɣ deg ssbiṭar
ur iyi-yesɛeddin ara deg ssikkis
sliɣ aṭas n yifesyanen i sɛeddan deg ssikis
llan qerben i yiqerra imeqqranen i iḍebbren tiyita-agi iban ẓran kra n wuffiren ɣef wayen yeḍran
mliɣ-as ayen ssneɣ deg temlilit tamezwarut
nekk kecmeɣ ɣer lɛesker ur ssineɣ taɣuri wala tira
ulac acu fehmeɣ deg tsertit
lethaɣ kan s useggem n yigelluyen d usizdeg-nsen
qqimeɣ kra n wagguren deg lḥebs sakin sserḥen-iyi rran-iyi ɣer lkazirna
uznen-iyi ɣer tinduf deg sseḥra
ẓriɣ tidet kra n wagguren umbaɛd
amek nɣan lkulunil saɛid ɛbid nnan-d umbaɛd d timenɣiwt i yenɣa iman-is mi yesla amussu-nsen ur yewwiḍ ara ɣer yiswi-s
amek yerwel lkulunil
ṭaher zbiri d wid yeddan yid-s ɣer tunes umbaɛd mi ɛeddan ɣef tizi-uzzu jijel skikda d temnaḍt n wawras
d amennuɣ gar yikulunalen n tegrawla umbaɛd timmunent
yal akulunil yettwali iman-is d netta i ilaqen ɣef uqerru n tmurt-a
imi d iserdasen tutlayt n leslaḥ kan i ssnen ɣef waya anagar asexdem n yiɣil iwumi zemren
nufa iman-nneɣ nekkni s iserdasen imeẓyanen nettunefk d asfel
lmeyyat n yiserdasen i yemmuten seg tiyita-nni n yisafagen aṭas daɣen i yuɣalen d imaɛḍuren mebla ma nebder ifesyanen-nni i yesɛeddan acḥal n yiseggasen deg leḥbus neɣ d imenfiyen berra n tmurt
lliɣ seg wid yesɛan zzher menɛeɣ seg lmut ḍeggren-iyi ɣer sseḥra ttun-iyi ugar n snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen
ur uɣaleɣ ara d akabural armi yewweḍ cadli benjdid i yessurfen i wid ibedden mgal bumedyen 
lezzayer n bumedyen mačči d lezzayer n tegrawliyin n tfellaḥt n temguri n yidles n tmejjayt d uselmed baṭel kan
d lezzayer daɣen n uqhar n yikabaren isertiyen uffiren n lemɛessegga n yinelmaden i useɣli n udabu d umennuɣ gar watmaten iɛdawen i d-yeglan s luluf n lmeggtin n yimejraḥ d yimeḥbas
aṭas n twaculin yettwalin deg tmunnent d taggara n lḥif n tuggdi d unemṭer uɣalent ttidirent deg leḥzen
 ɛemmar ablandi  am wakken i as-semman imidawen-ines deg lkazirna yesɛedda ugar n snat n tmerwin d sat n yiseggasen deg tlemmast n yigelluyen
yelmed tamikanikt armi i as-yuɣal umseddu d alelluc n warrac gar yifassen-is izuranen
maca yeffeɣ seg lɛesker am umseddu aqdim yemmečč irkelli  am wakken iyi-d-yenna mi iyi-d-yettmeslay yal aḥric seg tfekka-ines yeqreḥ-it  ssker tussda n yidammen sster deg uɛebbuḍ-is d uḍar-is ayeffus maca ɣas akken yezga yennecraḥ ur iḥebbes ara allus n teqsiḍin n yiseggasen i yesɛedda deg lɛesker d uneqqel-ines gar lkazirnat n sseḥra d tsila n ufella
lliɣ ttruḥuɣ ɣur-s ttzuruɣ-t yal mi ara sɛuɣ ccɣel deg blida ideg yezdeɣ asmi yewwi tastaɣt-ines
yuɣ akal yebna axxam n sin n yinnagen i d-yezgan berra n temdint
asmi t-sseqsaɣ ayɣer i yefren blida  yenna   tebɣiḍ ad meḍleɣ iman-iw akked twacult-iw deg tlemmast n yifri n ujrad anda luleɣ 
jerbeɣ ssehra d tsila n ufella ad k-d-iniɣ tidet tudert berra n temdinin n ugafa tewɛer yernu ur tesɛi ara lbenna
yemma i iɛeddan sat n tmerwin n yiseggasen deg laɛmer-is tin i yesɛeddan tudert-is deg sidi laɛǧel tufa iman-is dagi tuɣal tekreh tuɣlin ɣer taddart-is ulamma i kra n wussan kan yernu deg tazwara-nni tella tettagi ad d-teddu yid-i acḥal d abrid i ɛerḍeɣ ad tt-qenɛeɣ ad teqqim ɣur-i umbaɛd tamettant n baba 
ɣur-k tifrat a 
yessak-iyi-d yusef ɛeyyaci seg uxemmem-inu
ulac asif ur nesɛi tiqenṭert
xemmemeɣ aṭas deg temsalt-a
yemma-k ur teɣliḍ ara
yessefk fell-ak ad truḥeḍ ɣer temsulta
nesla ussan-a ɣef yiwen n usaḍuf i ttheggin iwsawen yettak-d taseglut i yirebraben ara yessersen leslaḥ i refden mgal ddula d tmetti wa ad randin i yiɣallen n laman
yezmer ad tesfaydiḍ seg tseglut n usaḍuf ara d-yeffɣen ussan-a am wakken sliɣ sɣur yinezzurfa deg uxxam unnig n teɣdemt
qebleɣ
melmi tebɣiḍ ad randiɣ  ad ruḥeɣ weḥd-i neɣ ad tedduḍ yid-i 
ur tettḥiri ara
tamsalt ur teshil ara am wakken tɣileḍ
amer tamsalt tcudd kan ɣer temsulta tili d ayen isehlen maḍi
akumisar n ɛin-el-kerma d ameddakkel-iw ad k-iɛiwen mebla ccek
maca asennan yettuseččan d tɣellist taserdasant i tuffirt yettaṭṭafen timsal am tigi
irgazen-is qessiḥet tasa-nsen ur xeddmen ara amgared gar umeddakkel d ucengu xeddmen s yismawen uffiren ula d imekwan n uxeddim-nsen d tiɣermin n ṭṭrad sɛeddayen deg-sen deg ssikkis yakk wid ibedden mgal adabu neɣ wid ur ḥemmlen ara
d tidet tagnit tbeddel ciṭuḥ umbaɛd timesbaniyin n tuber
 maca deg tilawt ulac acu ibeddlen
suffgen kra n tamihawt d nettat tirmest-agi yiqerra yettwassnen skecmen kra n ubeddel deg tuddsa n termest-a snulfan-d ismawen imaynuten maca imdanen iɣef tbedd d tarrayin i sexdamen qqimen kan d nitni ulac acu i ibeddlen
teḍra-as am wurar n cciṭranǧ beddlen initen d talɣa n yiguntar beddlen daɣen yiwen neɣ sin n yimyuraren maca ilugan n wurar qqimen d nitni kan
ugar n waya ur cukkeɣ ara ad yeqbel udabu ad yexdem iqbalen am wigi kan akka
yernu ur tettu ara tettekkaḍ deg tmenɣiwt n seddis n yimsulta
maca ur ten-nɣiɣ ara ulac acu xedmeɣ d amelsan i lliɣ
tuɣ-iyi d ameḥbus daxel n tkamyunt aẓḍam yeḍra seg berra wwin-iyi yid-sen s nnig n lebɣi-w
uggadeɣ ad iyi-yenɣen
amer qqimeɣ daxel n tkamyunt tili nɣan-iyi yimsulta
ur lliɣ ara d amasay ɣef tmettant-nsen
wagi d asegzi-inek keččini maca yezmer ad yekker walbaɛḍ niḍen ara yefken asegzi niḍen i tedyant
anef-aɣ ad as-nxemmem mliḥ i temsalt-a
ur ten-ttraǧu ara ad k-mmagren s yijeǧǧigen wa ad k-rren ɣer lḥebs am wakken ulac acu yeḍran
iban ad k-sseqsin ɣef wayen yeḍran yernu ad k-ẓẓmen alamma tefkiḍ-d ulac
ad k-ḥersen akken ad sen-tefkeḍ yakk isalen i tesɛiḍ  ismawen n yimdanen d wumi telliḍ imekwan ideg tteffren d kra n temsal urǧin ɛeddant ɣef uqerruy-ik
amek ara k-twali terbaɛt timselleḥt mi ara ten-tessenzeḍ 
ɛyiɣ kerheɣ tudert gar terbaɛt-agi
ass-a usiɣ-d ɣur-k mebla ma ẓran
bɣan irkelli ad refdeɣ leslaḥ wa ad tekkiɣ yid-sen deg tmenɣiwin d uhuddu
tthuddun mebla ssebba
deg wussan-a yezrin sserɣen yakk ikumya d lkiran n tɣiwant n wad-rruman
anda tella lfayda seg waya  sbeggneɣ-d i el-amir belli ur iyi-yaɛǧib ara wayen xeddmen
el-amir-nni yettili-iyi yessen yemma yessen daɣen taqsiḍt n baba
ḥala netta i yugin ad kecmeɣ ɣer trebbuyaɛ n umennuɣ
yettwali zemreɣ ad ten-ɛiwneɣ s ubrid n tɣamsa
d yiwen seg terbaɛt n watmaten inselmen iqdimen yekcem ɣer lḥebs umbaɛd tidyanin n tuber  ittekka deg yimenɣan yeḍran gar yineslemẓra d yiɣallen n laman
yesɛedda aseggas d uzgen deg lḥebs n serkaǧi din i yessen imeḥbas seg terbaɛt n melyani yiwen seg yirfiqen n buyaɛli
asmi kecmeɣ lḥebs iwala yemma tegzem tasa-s fell-as
ɣef waya yebɣa ad iyi-iɛiwen
yenna ula d netta ibedd mgal n uhuddu d usexreb maca ilaq ad t-nexdem acku d ccer ara yeglun s lxir i umussu deg kra n yiseggasen d afella
d tasetratijit yebnan ɣef umesḍuḍeɛ n termisin n ddula takafriwt iwakken ad ssigden yirgazen-ines wa ad sen-sbeggnen zemren ad ten-wwten melmi d wanda i sen-yehwa
maca yessuter deg-i ad ssusmeɣ ur ttakkeɣ ara rray-iw mgal ayen txeddem tarbaɛt-nsen akken ur seɛɛuɣ ara taɛdawt d yirgazen-is
yenna-iyi-d 
 ṭṭrad-nneɣ d ṭṭrad yumsen mgal adabu n lɛesker yal allal ara nessexdem d leḥlal ula d tid yeffɣen ccreɛ
ayen ad nessedrem ass-a ad as-nales lebni asmi ara neṭṭef leḥkem wa ad nebnu lxilafa tineslemt 
umnen irkelli belli lxilafa-agi qrib ad tettwabdedd
melmi d wamek 
ḥala rebbi i yeẓran
ɣur-i nekkini ulac acu yettbinen deg lxilafa-a neɣ melmi ad d-teffeɣ ɣer tafat
lxilafa neɣ n ddula tineslemt d tikti taṭubawit ur tban ara mliḥ d acu yellan deg-s aṭas n medden i yettmeslayen fell-as maca ulac win ad k-d-yinin d acu-tt s tidet teḍra-as am lbanka tineslemt
iswi n lbankat d yiwen  lfayda
mgaradent kan deg tarrayin
ɣas mgaraden yismawen ttmeslayen irkelli ɣef yiwet n tɣawsa  awwaḍ ɣer udabu d tseglut i d-itteddun yid-s
d aya kan
lmuhim a  ur d-usiɣ ara ɣer dagi ad mmeslayeɣ ɣef usbeddi n lxilafa tineslemt
bɣiɣ kan ad afeɣ tifrat i wugur-inu
ih ih am wakken teẓriḍ awal yezzuɣur wayeḍ
uɣaleɣ-d ɣur-i deg kra n wussan ad iliɣ jemɛeɣ isallen ɣef usaḍuf-agi amaynut yezmer ad naf tifrat yessefraḥen i uwaɣiw-a i d-yeɣlin fell-ak
ibedd beddeɣ yid-s
ddiɣ yid-s armi d tawwurt allaɣ-iw yeččur s kra n temsal i yi-yeɛnan
selmeɣ fell-as nniɣ-as ad nemlil deg wussan i d-iteddun
imir-nni ur ẓriɣ ara d tikkelt taneggarut ideg ad t-waliɣ deg-s
tamsalt n urandi-ines i temsulta tesseɣbel-iyi mliḥ uggadeɣ ugar asbeddi-ines deg lluleb
iban ad sen-yini acu yessen
ad sen-d-yemmeslay ɣef temlilit yeḍran gar-i d terbaɛt-ines deg yiḍ-nni
nekk d amastan yegdel fell-i usaḍuf ad sɛuɣ assaɣen d yimnafqen i xedmen afernas deg lɛibad deg wussan-a yezrin
yessefk fell-i ad ten-senzeɣ mi d-uɣaleɣ srid sɣur-sen
abeggeɛ anamek-is d lexdeɛ tamernut n lexdeɛ d lmut
tura ma ur ten-beggɛeɣ ara yettwaḥseb fell-i ddiɣ d yineḍliben taggara n wanɣa-agi d lḥebs
ufiɣ iman-iw deg lmerta ur ẓriɣ ara amek ad ffɣeɣ seg-s
uɣaleɣ ɣer usalun allaɣ-iw yexreb
ɣlint wallen-iw ɣef tezmamt n nabil ddmeɣ-tt ttiɣ isebtar-ines bdiɣ taɣuri 
sed  seg ctamber
ass-a wwḍeɣ ɣer lebɣi-w umreɣ mačči d kra fkan-iyi-d taxxamt-iw deg teɣremt tasdawant
deg-s ukkuẓ n yimṭerḥen
anagar yiwen seg wid ara yilin yid-i i walaɣ
yekcem s temɣawla yessers tabalizt-is yeffeɣ
iban d anelmad aqdim yessen amkan
zziɣ ciṭuḥ gar yizadaɣen iwumi yezzi uɣrab aɛlayan yeččur s uleẓwi
kif-kif am tesnawit-nneɣ
kecmeɣ ɣer lqehwa n teɣremt ur iyi-teɛǧib ara
lḥess ameɣriw abbu d yimdanen ur ssineɣ ara
dayen thennaɣ seg lɣemm n twacult-iw
yuɣal baba am umestul nnig n uqerruy-iw
seg wasmi d-yewwi tastaɣt-ines uɣaleɣ ur ttemsefhameɣ ara yid-s mliḥ
yesɛedday ussan-is yelseq deg usalun yettwali deg tiliẓri neɣ yeqqar aɣmis
sani ad truḥeḍ  anda telliḍ  ad as-tiniḍ mazal-iyi d aqrur amecṭuḥ
uletma farida ur tt-yettḥasab ara maḍi
tetteffeɣ tkeččem tettɣib tettinig tettruḥu ɣer yillel
d tilellit am urgaz
nekk yellan d argaz ttwarzeɣ am umeḥbus
amer mačči d yemma tameɣbunt tili dagi ad qqimeɣ alamma wwḍen imuras n unebdu
tweṣṣa-iyi ur ttɣibiɣ ara aṭas
tuḍen yir aṭṭan i zemren ad yeglu yi-s
ur tt-sseqsaɣ ara
ẓriɣ yakan
sliɣ ayen i as-d-yeqqar deg ledwar ineggura mi tt-yettawi ɣer ssbiṭar wa ad d-yuɣal yennuɣna yerfa
yemma tameɣbunt ayɣer fell-as i d-yeɣli waṭṭan-a  telha yernu d lmumen
amer d lebɣi aṭṭan-a ad yeɣli ɣef ukafriw-nni n baba
d netta i yuklalen tamernut am ta
ahat ad d-yuɣal s abrid amaɣud ad yuẓum wa ad iẓall
baba iɣil iman-is d ferɛun ulac acu ara t-yaɣen deg ddunit-a
ɣef waya ur yeḥwaǧ ara ad yamen s kra neɣ ad yessuter lemɛawna sɣur rebbi
tura ad kkreɣ ad ẓalleɣ snat n rrekɛat ad ssutreɣ seg rebbi ad yeseḥlu yemma wa ad yesseɣli tamernut tameqqrant ɣef
ferɛun-nni n baba
ad ssutreɣ seg-s daɣen ad t-yehdu s abrid amaɣud
ɣas yuɣal d aqehhar yewɛer yid-i maca ad yeqqim d baba
rebbi subḥanu iweṣṣa ɣef yimawlan
aram  seg tuber
tumert-inu ur tɛeṭṭel ara aṭas tdumm kra n wussan kan
irfiqen-iw deg texxamt d inelmaden seg tmurt n
leqbayel ttmeslayen gar-asen s yiwet n tutlayt ur fhimeɣ deg-s iqiḥ
yernu ur ttẓallan ur ttqadaren win yettẓallan
deg wussan imezwura lliɣ ttenkareɣ zik akken ad ẓalleɣ lefjer d ssebḥ deg texxamt
maca yiwen deg-sen isuɣ-d fell-i yenna-yi-d taxxamt tettwaxdem i yiḍes mačči d lǧameɛ
rfiɣ mliḥ maca ulac acu i d-nniɣ
nitni deg kraḍ yid-sen nekk weḥd-i kan
ḥebseɣ taẓallit deg texxamt
ugar n waya ttasen-d ɣur-sen yimeddukkal-nsen ad tterren i uɛeggeḍ ttqessiren s tutlayt-nsen alamma tɛedda ṭnac n yiḍ
dɣa ur zmireɣ ad alseɣ i temsirin-inu neɣ ad ɣreɣ kra seg leqran
ur ḥemmleɣ ara ad naɣeɣ akka i giɣ
maca ilaq-iyi ad rewleɣ ɣef yir-irfiqen-a
uɣaleɣ ur tteffɣeɣ ara seg lǧameɛ n teɣremt din i ssneɣ kra n yimeẓẓula hedreɣ d yiwen seg-sen d yiwen n bu-uččamar nemlal-d yiwen n wass s ugacur hedreɣ-as ɣef tarbaɛt-nneɣ wurfan-inu mgal irfiqen-inu d wumi zdiɣ taxxamt
yerra-yi-d srid   ad tzedɣeḍ yid-neɣ d acu d-tenniḍ   nniɣ 
 uggadeɣ ad ken-hewwjeɣ
 yenna   ala tettbiniḍ d ilemẓi yumnen seg tḥedqeḍ yernu watmaten inselmen yeṭṭaffaren awal n rebbi 
qebleɣ imir-n kan
kulci ibeddel s temɣawla
ufiɣ ayen ttnadiɣ aṭas aya
yakk irfiqen n texxamt-inu tamaynut ṭṭafaren ccreɛ n rebbi  aččamar ɛla ḥaseb n ssuna n nnbi aqendur iwatan aqader n lewqat n tẓallit daɣen yal askasi i d-nettawi ur itteffeɣ ara ɣef leqran d ssuna
uɣaleɣ daɣen ḥeddreɣ i lḥelqat timesɣanin i suddusen deg lǧameɛ seg lweqt ɣer wayeḍ
tikwal ttasen-d kra n yimennayen seg berra n teɣremt ad ɣ-d-fken timsirin
d imussnawen d inelmaden deg lɛulama meẓẓiyet deg yiseggasen ineggura maca macallah iqerra-nsen ččuren s tmussniwin timesɣanin s umezruy n ssuḥaba d wayen nnan yimussnawen n usɣan
lemdeɣ aṭas n yilugan ur ssineɣ ara yakan
yiwen n wass sseqsaɣ yiwen deg-sen yerra-yi-d s leḥdaqa allen-is ččant-iyi irkelli
d wigi d lmumnin n tidet lmumen ur yettaggad kra seg-sen
ad mmeslayeɣ fell-asen i yasin
ẓriɣ ad iḥir ad ten-yissin
sem  seg duǧamber
sɛeddaɣ imuras n taggara n ddurt deg ɛayn-el-kerma
jemmeɣ aṭas yemma
aṭas i tettru tezzem-iyi ɣef ugellel-inu 
 tmeqqreḍ tura dɣa tettuḍ yemma-k  i yi-tettales nettat tseffeḍ imeṭṭawen-is
ma d baba deg umkan ad yesserḥeb yis-i ad iyi-yesseqsi ɣef leqraya-inu yebda laɛmer d yettmesxir ɣef yiselsa d tamart-inu  aselsu n yiderwicen d tamart n uqelwac
heggaɣ iman-iw ad as-iniɣ wwḍeɣ tura snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen ɣur-i imir-a tilelli ad ferneɣ aselsu i yi-yehwan maca uggadeɣ ad nemyuṭṭaf deg wawal i tikkelt niḍen
sidreɣ kan i uqerruy-iw ffɣeɣ seg uxxam
ruḥeɣ ɣer umeddakkel-iw yasin
ixeddem deg ugaraǧ n useqɛed n ṭumubilat
neqqim deg lqahwa i d-yezgan metwal n ugaraǧ-nni mebda aqesser d umeslay
ula d netta yezzem-iyi ɣef ugellel-inu
yenna-yi-d amer mačči d ccɣel i t-yeṭṭfen tili iruḥ-d ad inadi fell-i deg tesdawit
yemmesla-yi-d ɣef tefranin ara yilin deg snat n ledwar i d-iteddun
deg wussan yezrin yeḥma wawal gar watmaten teɣremt n inselmen ɣef usentel-a deg yinelmaden
yenna-yi-d yasin yessekles isem-iw deg tɣiwant akken ad iyi-ssuffɣen takarḍa n uferran
yerẓa aqerruy-iw akken ad iliɣ ass n tefranin iwakken ad ferneɣ umuɣ n lmacayex
mi as-nniɣ yezmer lḥal ur ttiliɣ ara yerfa fell-i yumeṛ-iyi ad iliɣ acku aful n tneslemt ibedd ɣef tefranin ara inejren abrid i usbeddi n lxilafa tineslemt
umbaɛd n tẓallit n lǧumuɛa yedda-d yid-i armi d timersit n lkiran
yenna-yi-d leɣyab-inu ad yesɛu inelkimen ɣef tdukkli-nneɣ ad t-iwali am lexdeɛ d ibeddi ɣer yidis n yicenga n usɣan
ur i yi-yeǧǧi ara armi s-ṛegmeɣ ad d-uɣaleɣ
aram  seg meɣres
iḍ yezrin teẓḍem temsulta ɣef teɣremt n yinelmaden teɣleq lǧameɛ terra ssnasel n wuzzal ɣef tiwwura-ines
tewwi daɣen ccix n lǧameɛ d anelmad i yettẓallan yisdaɣen timsirin
d ilemẓi acekki-t neɣ yettak-aɣ-d yeḥdeq ur fhimeɣ ara ayɣer i t-ḥebsen
ahat mi ibedd mgal aselway amaynut i d-wwin seg tmurt n lmerruk
sliɣ-as acḥal d abrid yekkat deg-s deg temsirin-ines yenna fell-as d yiwen seg yizduklalen iqdimen wid i t-yessersen ɣef ukersi d imakaren d imesfesden
nekk ur t-ssineɣ ara urǧin sliɣ s yisem-is
yettales baba i yismawen n kra n yizduklanen maca isem-a urǧin i iɛedda ɣef umeẓẓuɣ-iw
ɣriɣ deg yiwen n uɣmis d yiwen n umǧahed d ameqqran d netta i yessekren ṭṭrad n teslullit u yewwi-d timmunent i tmurt
aṭas n temsal i nelmed deg temsirin n umezruy ɣef tegrawla n wunbir d wid yellan ɣef uqerruy-is
mmuten irkelli d imeɣrasen tenɣa-ten taredsa tafransisst
urǧin i ɣ-d-mmeslayen yiselmaden n umezruy ɣef urgaz-agi
anda yezga yifri-agi anda i t-ufan  s tidet d yiwen seg yimeqqranen i d-yessekkren tagrawla n tmunnent  d azduklan am wakken i d-yeqqar ccix n lǧameɛ  ur ẓriɣ ara
aṭas n temsal i ibeddlen daxel n teɣremt tasdawant iɛessasen ɣef tewwurt n umraḥ
ilaq ad
sbedden nessebgen takarḍa  aqelleb deg lqecc-nneɣ  ur nezmir ara ad nekcem umbaɛd n lɛecra n yiḍ
sɛeddaɣ ddurt s lekmal-is weḥd-i deg texxamt
ɣaben yimeddukkal-iw wa deffir wa
farid anelmad-nni i yi-yesmenɛen seg terbaɛt-nni tamelɛunt wwin-t ɣer lḥebs mi yekker ccwal ɣer tewwurt n tesdawit
ass-nni bɣan yinelmaden ad ffɣen ɣer berra tbedd temsulta deg wudem-nsen maca rẓan tasergelt lḥan deg ubrid
aṭas i yeɣlin gar yifassen n temsulta wwin-ten irkelli ɣer lḥebs
farid d yiwen yellan gar-asen
ass-nni ḥeḍreɣ i wayen yeḍran maca qqimeɣ deg lesfuf ineggura ttwaliɣ kan
mi ẓeḍmen yimsulta ɣef yinelmaden bdan kkaten deg-sen s tɛekkzin kecmeɣ daxel n tzeɣwa n leqraya
rǧiɣ armi terked liḥala uɣaleɣ ɣer teɣremt
kerheɣ takriḍt yernu uggadeɣ ad ttwajerḥeɣ
ma walaɣ idammen tteffɣen seg tfekka-inu tettaṭṭaf-iyi tergagayt itezzi laɛqel-iw zemreɣ ad fesxeɣ
ma d
musṭafa arfiq-iw wis sin deg texxamt seg temdint n
lexdariya yenna-aɣ yiwen seg watmaten belli iserdasen ruḥen s axxam n yimawlan-is ddmen-t syin ar tura ulac win yeẓran sani t-wwin
ma d sid ɛli arfiq wis kraḍ netta seg cercal yeḥbes leqraya iletha s usefrek n tḥanut n baba-s yebɣa ad yessemneɛ aqerruy-is am wakken iyi-d-yenna yiwen n wass mi d-yusa ad yejmeɛ lqecc-is
ma d
 d netta i iqellben fell-i daxel n tesdawit akken ad as-jemɛeɣ ayen yeǧǧa daxel n texxamt ama d lqecc ama d idlisen
yenna-yi-d iɛessasen n teɣremt ur t-ǧǧin ara ad yekcem acku ur yelli ara seg yimezdaɣ unsiben am wakken i sen-neqqar
d anelmad deg ugezdu n tussna n uselkim ur yesɛi ara azref ad yeṭṭef taxxamt acku yezdeɣ deg belkur i d-yezgan deg tlemmast n lezzayer tamanaɣt
yezga yeccetkay seg ṭṭiq n uxxam n yimawlan-is  snat n texxamin ideg ttidiren mraw d yiwen n yimdanen
gma-s ameqqran i yewwḍen ukkuẓet n tmerwin n yiseggasen deg laɛmer-is yezweǧ yewwi-asen abalkun-nni ideg yella yeggan netta d sin seg watmaten-is ǧǧan taxxamt tis snat i semmus n watmaten-nsen niḍen
anda ad yeṭṭes ihi  deg tnawalt  sdat n tewwurt n umraḥ  iɣab ugar n ddurt
ɣileɣ yettwaṭṭef ula d netta
yeḥka-yi-d amek i yennuɣ d yiɛessasen i as-ssutren takarḍa tunsibt n unekcum
yesɣar aqerruy-is yebɣa ad yekcem s yiɣil
ssawlen-d i temsulta tusa-d tewwi-t tḍegger-it deg txeddem akked lḥebs am wakken yimakaren d yisekranen
yenna-d yesɛedda yiwen n yiḍ deg yiwen n bu-yik urdan yettriḥi s rriḥa n yiriran d yibeccan
yeggul ad yeǧǧ tamurt ma yufa tagnit iwatan
inig d tifrat i wugur-ines
newwi-d awal ɣef yirfiqen-nneɣ deg texxamt yenna-d d imeɣnasen deg tirni tineslemt i usellek fis aselway amaynut yewwi-tt-id deffir-nsen
yewwi luluf seg-sen ɣer leḥbus deg sseḥra
yenna-yi-d s wurnan   liḥala n tmurt ur tessefraḥ ara
attan ɣef yimi n ubulkan yezmer ad yeṭṭerḍeq ɣef yiqerra-nneɣ irkelli seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ
tifrat tayiwant i d-yegran i win yebɣan ad yidir ur t-ɣeddren ara s tersast neɣ ad teccenqer tfekka-inek d iwezwazen s uṭerḍeq n lbumba d inig ad ibeɛɛed ɣef tmurt-agi tamelɛunt s usedger n sebɛa n lebḥur am wakken i d-teqqar jidda
win iɣilen yezmer ad ibeddel kra s leslaḥ d targit i yettargu ulac acu yessen ɣef yiserdasen yesselḥayen tamurt-a s wuzzal 
yennurna ihedder s laɛqel yessider i taɣect-is yettwali ayeffus aẓelmaḍ ma yella win i as-isellen
tban-d tuggdi fell-as
iban iḍ-nni i yesɛedda deg bu-yikurdan amaɛfun yeǧǧa-d deg-s ddeq i as-yeskerhen tamurt-a
yiwen n wass sliɣ-as i baba mi yettmeslay akked umeddakkel-is amastan ɣef lemṛar n lḥebs d lewɛara n ssikkis
ula d netta yessen lḥebs deg temẓi-s
ɣef waya yekreh lḥukuma lɛesker yakk d wayen yesɛan assaɣ d yiɣallen n laman
mi sliɣ i wawal n lḥebs tettcirriw tfekka-inu
ur ẓriɣ ara ma zemreɣ ad sebreɣ i ssikkis-ines ma ttwaṭṭfeɣ yiwen n wass  iban ad rreɣ talast i tudert-iw deg yiḍ amezwaru
ɛyiɣ deg tɣimit weḥd-i deg texxamt
ahad-agi ad ruḥeɣ ad ẓureɣ yemma

yasin
ur ẓriɣ ara anda yezdeɣ deg udcir n  lebrarik 
tikkelt-a ad ruḥeɣ srid s axxam-is
ḥebseɣ taɣuri
mmektaɣ-d taqsiḍt n umeddakkel-iw
racid d yifutas n uḥbas-ines asmi yeqqar deg tesdawit iqeddec deg unmalu n yinelmaden
cfiɣ ɣur-s i lliɣ deg uxxam
ɣef waya yewweḍ yinaw-ines ɣer yimeẓẓuɣen n
nabil
mazal taɣuct-ines yeččuren s wurfan d ddɣel tettezzi deg yimeẓẓuɣen-inu ad as-tiniḍ tura kan i as-sliɣ
 amek i tebɣiḍ ad ttuɣ aqhar d ddel i d-sseɣlin fell-i imjelkaḍen n bumedyen s ṭul n snat n ledwar deg lḥebs uffir
refden-iyi seg teɣremt tasdawant n ben ɛeknun ɣef leḥdac n yiḍ
deg yiḍ-nni qqimeɣ ttqessireɣ d kra n yimeddukkal-iw deg tberna n
 abi nuwwas 
neswa newwi-d awal ɣef tsertit ladɣa ɣef usunded n yinelmaden i yeskerfen tasga ugar n waggur d usenfar n usnulfu n tdukkla n yinelmaden tilellit ɣef udabu
deg useggas-nni ur terkid ara tesdawit  tewwurt n umraḥ n aneḥbus ɣef leqraya igrawen yal ass daxel neɣ berra n tzeɣwa aneɛruḍ akken ad ffɣen ɣer ubrid amennuɣ gar yinelmaden
tisnaktiwin yemgaraden ttnaɣent gar-asent akken ad ṭṭfent aqerru n unmalu n yinelmaden  izduklanen itruteskiyen wid yekkaten ɣef tmaziɣt tuget deg-sen seg tmurt n leqbayel ibaɛtiyen irefden taɛlamt n useɛreb atmaten inselmen drus deg-sen deg tallit-nni d annar n umennuɣ terwi tebberwi
ddiɣ d umussu aẓelmaḍ azduklan maca ur kcimeɣ ara ɣer ukabar-ines
arfiq-iw deg texxamt yella d ameɣnas n ukabar
faqeɣ i waya s ugacur cfiɣ ass-nni d ageffur
uɣaleɣ-d ɣer texxamt ad d-ddmeɣ ssiwan-inu ufiɣ-t yettara aɣmis
 taɣuct n uɣref   ssawt ccaɛb  daxel n tjellabin akken ad t-yefreq
ɣriɣ yakan kra n wuṭṭunen i yesɛa
yenna-yi-d d ameddakkel-is yeqqaren deg tesga n tussna n tmetti i as-ten-id-ireḍlen
mačči d lḥaǧa yessewhamen aṭas n tesɣunin d yidlisen yettwagdlen nettaf-iten ɣer yinelmaden n tesdawit am udlis  ṭṭrad n lezzayer  n s wukkuẓ n yiḥricen i yessuffɣen ɣer tafat uffiren yessefqaɛen n ṭṭrad n teslullit tura ssnen-ten irkelli
maca tasebḥit-nni faqeɣ-as iwala-yi kan yaɛreq-as ccedd i uyeddid yeɛreḍ ad ten-yeffer ddaw n yidlisen i yeṭṭef gar yifassen-is
imir-n ur d-nniɣ acemma
rriɣ iman-iw ulac acu walaɣ ddmeɣ kan ssiwan-inu ffɣeɣ
maca tameddit-nni d netta i yezwaren ɣer umeslay ɣef usentel-a yessefhem-iyi belli ittekka deg ukabar uffir axeddim-is  afraq n kra n wuṭṭunen n tesɣunt-nni
deg tilawt anelmad-nni ɛaziz ma ur ɣliḍeɣ ara yella d inselmen tteffren daxel n asusam ur yettmeslay ara aṭas urǧin yehder neɣ yefka-d rray-is deg temliliyin n yinelmaden
yettaṭṭaf kan amkan aneggaru yettferriǧ deg wayen iḍerrun
ɣef waya ulac win ad icukken deg-s ittekka deg ukabar uffir ibedden deg wudem n unagraw
ma d nekk lliɣ ẓeddmeɣ kan
sumreɣ-as ad t-ɛiwneɣ deg ufraq n tesɣunt
uɣaleɣ ttawiɣ yid-i deg uqrab-iw kra n wuṭṭunen yal mi ara mmeslayeɣ d unelmad neɣ d tnelmadt ufiɣ tikta-nneɣ mqarabent fkiɣ-as yiwen seg wuṭṭunen
acḥal d abrid i yi-inebbeh umeddakkel-iw ad ɛasseɣ iman-iw
irgazen n tɣellist taserdasant ččuren tasdawit leḥḥun s usɣum ad ten-tafeḍ lsan iselsa n yizduklanen n yitruteskiyen n yibaɛtiyen d watmaten tuddsiwin n yinelmaden akken ad tent-selḥun neɣ ad tent-rẓent
maca ttrebga-inu n taddart terna-yi
ayen yellan deg wul-iw ad d-tafeḍ ɣef yiles-iw
d wagi i yesxerben assaɣen-inu d baba yessexser daɣen amennuɣ-inu deg unmalu n yinelmaden
ur ssineɣ ara ad skidbeɣ neɣ ad ffreɣ tidet daxel-iw
maca deg taggara xelseɣ-tt ɣlayet
deg useggas-nni ḥefḍeɣ tissit
lliɣ ttemliliɣ yal tameddit n sem d kra n yimeddukkal deg yiwet n tberna seg tbaren yeččuren talemmast n tmanaɣt
d ifran twellsen nkeccem ɣur-sent seg tnafsa n wass nettaṭṭaf ṭṭabla deg teɣmert nessutur asenduq n lbirra dɣa ad nekcem deg umaḍal n ssekran d umeslay ɣef tsertit d tekta tigrawliyin d tmarksiyin
acḥal lhan imeslayen d yiskasiyen-nni  nbedder-d yakk ismawen n yigrawliyen yettwassnen deg umaḍal 
 lurka neruda
muḍaffer ennewwab marsil xalifa bacir ḥaǧ ɛli kateb
yasin atg
nettaṭṭaf ddunit gar yifassen-nneɣ netthudu-tt nettales-as asali amek i ɣ-yehwa
ma yuli uzɣal n lbirra ɣer yiqerra yettuɣal umeslay-nneɣ d aɛeggeḍ d tirga yeffɣen tilawt
nhedder irkelli yal yiwen deg-neɣ yettaɛraḍ amek ad iqenneɛ wiyaḍ s sswab n rray-is
deg yiḍ-nni yessaweḍ-iyi yiwen seg yimeddukkal-nneɣ s ṭumubil-ines armi d tawwurt n teɣremt n yinelmaden
subbeɣ sgerfleɣ ur ẓriɣ anda ad srusuyeɣ iḍarren-iw armi d-usan ɣur-i sin n yirgazen ssutren deg-i ad ten-ḍefreɣ
deg tazwara ɣileɣ d iɛessasen n teɣremt ugin ad i yi-ǧǧen ad kecmeɣ imi yettbin-d fell-i ssekran
ɛerḍeɣ ad ččeɛnenneɣ ciṭuḥ nniɣ-asen kra n teqbucin n lbirra kan i swiɣ ẓriɣ acu xeddmeɣ ur ḥemmleɣ ara ccwal yernu tura ad ruḥeɣ srid ɣer texxamt-iw mebla ma hewwjeɣ yiwen
maca sin n yirgazen-nni ur suggten ara yid-i ameslay
d iɣezzfanen jehdit mačči d kra
srekben-iyi gar-asen daxel n ṭumubil iḥebsen sdat n ẓẓerb n teɣremt yeqleɛ unehhar ɣer yiwen n umkan ur ẓriɣ anda d-yezga
kra n yikilumitren umbaɛd cudden-iyi ifassen ɣummen-iyi allen
yeṭṭef yinig-nni ugar n ssaɛa
tewwi-yi tnafa daxel n ṭumubil
sakin ḥulfaɣ skerkiren deg-i deg ddruj deg lqaɛa yessan s ssima tasemmaḍt
kksen-iyi acuddu-nni d uɣummu ɣef wallen ǧǧan-iyi weḥd-i
ufiɣ iman-iw deg yiwen n bu-yikurdan yeḍyeq mliḥ tkeccem-d ɣur-s tafat seg berra seg yiwen n ṭṭaq d ameẓyan
ɣileɣ daxel n uxxam n temsulta i lliɣ taggara ḍegren-iyi ɣef ḥebsen-iyi ɣef ssekran
ɣef waya ur yi-yeffiɣ ara laɛqel
ḥulfaɣ i leqriḥ deg uqerruy-iw d fad yekkaw yimi-w
ẓẓleɣ ɣef yiwen n umeṭreḥ yettfuḥu mliḥ limmer ad afeɣ abrid ɣer yiḍes
maca ɣelqeɣ kan allen-iw i kra n lweqt armi telli tewwurt-nni kecmen-d kraḍ n yirgazen ɣezzifit tifekkiwin-nsen annect ilatent
mebla ma heḍren yid-i neɣ ma rran-d ɣef yiseqsiyen-inu wwin-iyi s ddreɛ ɣer yiwet n texxamt sɣimen-iyi ɣef ukersi sderɣlen allen-iw s tafat n yiwen n umesbaḥ
bdant tuttriwin deg tazwara ur sxedmen ara yid-i iɣil
imir-n kan i faqeɣ gar yifassen n tɣellist taserdasant i lliɣ
tekkes-iyi ssekkran-nni faqeɣ d yiman-iw deg yir tagnit i lliɣ
sliɣ kra ɣef umaḍal-agi uffir s ubrid n teqsiḍin n yisertiyen ibedden mgal adabu ttwaḥebsen sɛeddan-ten deg ssikis
ɣriɣ adlis  asteqsi  n henri alleg ideg yemmeslay ɣef ssikkis n yiserdasen ifransiyen d udlis  aramek  n umeɣnas azduklan d umedyaz bacir ḥaǧ ɛli ideg ihedder s yifutas ɣef ssikkis sɛeddan fell-as mi t-teṭṭfen umbaɛd ubeddi-ines mgal
bumedyen i yesseɣlin aselway ben bella
ur tteffreɣ ara fell-ak ay ameddakkel-iw ɛebdelqader fecleɣ irkelli teɣli tezmert-iw qrib i ɣliɣ ɣef lqaɛa seg tuggdi seg yixerdusen-a yessewḥacen
ṭṭfeɣ iman-iw sliɣ mliḥ i yiseqsiyen-nsen akken ad ẓreɣ ayɣer i yi-ḥebsen
iseqsiyen irkelli zzin-d ɣef usunded n yinelmaden d yisem n ukabar yellan deffir-s
rdan-iyi srid s uttekki ɣer ukabar n 
mi nekkreɣ wwin-d aqrab-iw ldin-t ssuffɣen-d seg-s sin n wuṭṭunen n uɣmis  tiɣri n uɣref 
ttuɣ-ten maḍi
nniɣ d yiwen seg yimeddukkal-iw i ten-yeǧǧan ɣur-i
sutren deg-i ad sen-fkeɣ isem n umeddakkel-a tawuri-ines d tansa-ines
bdiɣ asqewqew yaɛreq-iyi wawal
ad senzeɣ arfiq-iw 
anda-tt trugza  amer ad mmeslayeɣ ad uɣaleɣ d axabbit
lexdeɛ ɣur-neɣ d lɛib ameqqran yesmektay-aɣ s tallit tamharsant
ttif ad mmteɣ wala ad senzeɣ albaɛḍ ulamma i udabu n tmunnent mačči i udabu amharsan
bɣan ad sen-fkeɣ ismawen n wid yellan deffir n usunded d imekwan n temliliyin-nneɣ
ẓriɣ ɣliɣ deg yiwen n uwaɣiw ayen xedmeɣ tewɛer tuffɣa seg-s
ad meslayeɣ wa ad mɛawaneɣ yid-sen ɣas akken ur ẓriɣ ara aṭas n temsal neɣ ad nekkreɣ wa ad susmeɣ am wakken i yi-tessneḍ yeqqur uqerruy-iw
deg tazwara mmeslayeɣ yid-sen ɣef tekta timatutin ɣef usunded d tlelli n yinelmaden deg usbeddi n tuddsiwin-nsen am wakken iḍerru deg tmura timeqqranin
lḥan yid-i skerkren-iyi ɣer wannar-nsen  amer tuddsiwin-a n yinelmaden s tidet d tilelliyin d inmula timettiyin d tisegmanin tili ur yessekcam ara udabu iman-is akken ad tent-yegdel s lmeqlub ad tent-iɛiwen s yidrimen lemḥellat d wallalen ad tent-yallen deg n uxeddim-nsent
maca adabu yeẓra yinelmaden d ifurkan n yikabaren uffiren iswi-nsen d aseɣli n unagraw qeddcen berra n tmurt ttɛawanen-ten kra n tamiwin timhersanin d temberyaliyin kerhen
lezzayer
nekkreɣ
ur sɛiɣ ara assaɣen d tuddsiwin n berra assaɣen-inu irkelli deg tesdawit i llan
ur iyi-umnen ara
wwin-d yiwen n ukaram uran deg-s yakk tigawin-inu d tuget n yimeslayen i d-nniɣ deg temliliyin timatutin i nessuddes
wehmeɣ deg yifutas-nni aṭas i ttuɣ deg-sen inmula-agi
lliɣ sexdameɣ tamawalt n tedmi taẓelmaḍt d tegrawla tanemlayt
kkateɣ deg terkeft n yiserdasen ttawiɣ-d imeslayen n d amedya
skecmen imucaren gar yinelmaden ttawin-asen-d akk ayen iḍerrun
wehmeɣ mi d-nnan tteffreɣ deg texxamt-iw uṭṭunen n uɣmis  taɣuct n uɣref  aɣmis n ukabar i fferqeɣ ɣef yinelmaden s tuffra
ttqelliben tixxamin yal mi ara ffɣen imawlan-nsent
anamek n waya ula tadbelt n teɣremt tettekka yid-sen
qrib i sen-nniɣ nekk ferrqeɣ-ten kan d arfiq-iw i ten-id-yettawin
maca tban-iyi-d mačči d tiruggza
yernu arfiq-iw ur iḥettem ara fell-i waya yezga d aweṣṣi deg-i ad ḥadreɣ iman-iw
ferqeɣ aɣmis  taɣuct n uɣref  s lebɣi-w
amek ad ǧǧeɣ seg i urfiq-iw  mačči d truggza-inu ad sbibbeɣ kulci leɛwayed-iw
tezzi-d texnaqt ɣef temgarḍt-iw ḥala tasusmi i yi-d-yegran akken ad ḥuddeɣ ɣef yiman-iw
yuɣal unkar d taḍsa fell-i
tasusmi meqqar tettḥarab ɣef nnif-iw
maca aseḥbiber ɣef nnif azal-is ɣlay xellseɣ-t s uksum-iw d yidammen-iw
deg wass wis kraḍ tbeddel lhedra-nsen   ḥala yiwen n ubrid i izemren ad k-yessuffeɣ sya  ad aɣ-d-tiniḍ tidet 
tidet ɣur-sen ad sen-mmleɣ isem n win i yi-d-yefkan uṭṭunen-nni n uɣmis yettwagedlen
amek ad sdukkleɣ gar tidet d lexdeɛ  ɣef waya i friɣ-tt d yiman-iw ur qqareɣ ara yimjelkaḍen-a
azal n tidet meqqer tleḥḥu d tebɣest d tɣersawt
ma d lexdeɛ d tudayt d yir tigawin ɣef waya friɣ-tt d yiman-iw ur tent-sexdameɣ ara deg tudert ɣas ẓriɣ ad tt-xelseɣ ɣlayet
bdan ssaggaden deg-i s tmenɣiwt
tidet
yenna-yi-d yiwen seg wid yesseqsayen deg-i   yeshel maḍi fell-aneɣ ad k-nenɣ ad nḍegger tafekka-inek deg yiwen n lbir ulac win ad yafen later-ik
maca ur nebɣi ara ad k-nenɣ acku neẓra d kečč yellan d arruz ulamma d ahcican d wid ibedden deg wudem n unagraw
neẓra ur telliḍ ara seg wid yebɣan ad yesseɣlin anagraw
tufiḍ iman-ik gar-asen s ugacur
ayen i k-yewwin ɣur-sen d temẓi-inek d leḥmala n tmurt-ik d tmetti-inek
nebɣa ad ɣ-d-tefkeḍ yiwen n yisem kan isem n win i k-d-yefkan aɣmis-agi akken ad t-tferqeḍ sakin ad k-nserreḥ
seg tama-nneɣ nezmer ad k-nerr ɣef uqerru n unmalu n yinelmaden ad k-naf axxam akken ad taɣeḍ tacelhabt-nni tahuskayt i yezgan yid-k
tḥemmel-ik ma ur telliḍ ara yid-s ur tettaf ara iman-is ɣas ulamma keččini tlethaḍ kan s yiskasiyen isertiyen 
ur skidibeɣ ara fell-ak deg tazwara umneɣ lehḍur-nsen qrib i uɣeɣ awal-nsen wa ad neṭqeɣ s yisem n urfiq-iw
maca walaɣ sdat n wallen-iw tugna n lǧar-nneɣ musa i ixeddmen ɣer  la sas  afransis d ccina i ilaḥqen ula d arraw-is iwumi nessawal tarwa n uḥerki wid imeccḥen iḍebsiyen n yifransiyen
dɣa walaɣ iman-iw leḥḥuɣ deg tesdawit d imdelli ttwehhin-d yakk ɣur-i  hatan uxabit-nni afuḥan hatan ubeyyaɛ-nni amelɛun
ṭṭfeɣ imi-w ṭṭfeɣ rray ur sen-ttakeɣ ula d yiwen n usali dɣa yebda ssikkis
wwin-iyi ɣer wannag adday
ẓriɣ taswiɛt iwaɛren tewweḍ-d
rran ifassen-iw ɣer deffir cudden-ten sersen-iyi ɣef yiri n yiwen n usarij yeččuren s waman yeblulɣen s yisufar n usizdeg dɣa yesɛedda-yi umjelkaḍ-nsen deg ssikkis
ayen yessewhamen deg umjelkaḍ-nni d uḍɛif d awezzlan azgen n tuɣmas-ines timezwura ɣlint mi ad yemmeslay imeslayen-is ttuɣalen d aseffer ulac acu ad tfehmeḍ seg wayen d-yeqqar
ad yeṭṭef aqerruy-iw ad t-yessekcem daxel n waman-nni imalusen alamma qrib ad tiqfeɣ
ad t-id-yessuffeɣ i kra n lweqt ad yesrugmet kra n wawalen s yiwet n taɣect yesseḍsayen amer mačči deg yir tagnit ideg tuɣ   ad d-temmeslayeḍ neɣ ur tettmeslayeḍ ara
 ma ur as-fkiɣ ara tiririyin yettarra aqerruy-iw daxel n usarij
iɛawed i tigawt-agi acḥal d abrid mebla ma yeḥbes seg uɛeggeḍ   ad temmeslayeḍ mebla yemma-k

tenɣa-t tsusmi-inu
d acu-iyi nekkini iwakken ur yessawaḍ ara ad i yi-yessenṭeq  win yewwḍen ɣer da yessefk fell-as ad yemmeslay
d alugen amatu ulac win ara yeffɣen fell-as
deg tegnit-a tuqriḥt mmektaɣ-d tanfalit-nni i d-yeqqaren   allal i watan i uḥuddu d anṭag  dɣa nniɣ-as anṭag iwatan i tegnatin yecban tigi d aɛeggeḍ d rregmat d tiyitwin ma zemreɣ
sfeqɛeɣ umjelkaḍ-nni mi t-wwteɣ s uḍar-inu ayeffus bdiɣ aɛeggeḍ  ay arraw n teqjunt ay ilfan ay arraw n lqeḥba yekcem deg-i yibki-nni s lbunyat d tyitwin n rrekel qrib i yi-yenɣa amer ur skecmen ara imidawen-ines iman-nsen
umbaɛd cudden daɣen iḍarren-iw beddlen daɣen tarrayt n ssikis
yeṭṭef ukɛir-nni afus n ugelzim yeɣli-d s tiyitwin ɣef uɛrur-iw ad as-tiniḍ nɣiɣ-as yemma-s
yettbin-d ixuss deg laɛqel wwin-t-id s ddemma i ccɣel-agi amaɛfun
ɣas kerheɣ albaɛḍ urǧin ad as-xedmeɣ am wakken i yi-yexdem
yal tikkelt mi ad ččeɣ tiyita ttḥulfuɣ i tfekka-inu tɣelli d ticeqfin maca ɣas akken ur ḥbiseɣ ara seg uɛeggeḍ wala rregmat  ibki-nni seg tama-s ur yeḥbis ara tiyitwin deg-i armi ɣliɣ ɣef lqaɛa ṣṣerɛeɣ
ǧǧan-iyi ɣef ssiman ffɣen
mi d-ukiɣ ufiɣ iman-iw ttergigiɣ seg usemmiḍ
tuɣmas-iw ṭṭerḍiqent
imi-w yekkaw ur yesɛi ara imetman
taxxamt tella deg ṭṭlam ciṭuḥ n tafat i tt-ikeččmen seg yiwen n ṭṭaq n zzǧaǧ i d-yezgan srid ddaw n ssqef yernu ur ẓriɣ ara ma deg ssbeḥ neɣ deg yiḍ i nella
kemmceɣ ɣef yiman-iw ldiɣ mliḥ imeẓẓuɣen-inu limmer yella acu ad sleɣ
tasusmi tuɣ akk amkan ad as-tiniḍ daxel n uẓekka i lliɣ
bdiɣ imir-n ttḥulfuɣ i leqriḥ n tfekka-inu
lluẓeɣ ɛyiɣ mliḥ
kra n lweqt umbaɛd yekcem-d yiwen n uɛessas yefsi acuddu n yifassen-iw yessers sdat-i imi n uɣrum aquran tzemreḍ ad tfeddxeḍ yis-s albaɛḍ d uskaf d asemmaḍ tuget-ines d aman ulɣen
rraw n leḥram cuḥḥen fell-i ula deg wučči
iɣaḍ-iyi lḥal ṭṭfeɣ rray ur ttnaleɣ ara iẓan-nsen
ur cliɛeɣ ara
ttif tamettant ɣef tudert n ddel
bdiɣ ttxemmimeɣ deg tmettant awaɣzen-agi ara ɣ-yesbelɛen irkelli yiwen n wass
dɣa ɛeddan ɣef uqerruy-iw ismawen n yimeqqran i lḥan ɣef wakal-a tura ṭṭsen ddaw-as
walaɣ iman-iw d abeɛɛuc ur nesɛi azal sdat-sen
ayɣer ad aggadeɣ tamettant ihi  ma tafekka tekḥes maḍi ma ffɣeɣ seg uxerdus-agi d taqqurant ad rnun isem-iw i umuɣ aɣezzfan n wid ibedden mgal lbaṭel d uqhar n yimdanen wid yemmuten ɣef temsalt-a taheggart
tamettant am ta tif tamettant deg ṭumubil deg ubrid neɣ deg ssbiṭar
tuɣal taɛǧeb-iyi lmut armi uɣaleɣ ttganiɣ deg-s
bdiɣ sakin suguneɣ d acu ad d-inin fell-i yimeddukkal-iw umbaɛd n tmettant-inu
iban ad iyi-d-bedren deg lxir kan ad sen-d-uɣaleɣ d amedya deg umennuɣ
yuɣal-d uɛessas-nni yessuffeɣ-iyi seg usugen-inu
mi iwala ur ččiɣ ara lmakla-nni ihucc-iyi s uḍar-is yumeṛ-iyi ad ččeɣ
muqleɣ-t ssusfeɣ deg uḍebsi-nni suɣeɣ  iẓan-agi ečč-iten keččini neɣ awi-ten i yemma-k 
yeffeɣ ur iyi-d-yenni kra
kra n lweqt umbaɛd yekcem-d win i yi-yesɛeddan deg lluleb ḍefren-t-id sin n yirgazen akked yibki-nni
ibedd nnig n uqerruy-iw azmummeg ɣef yimi-s  iban ur k-taɛǧib ara lmakla-nneɣ
d ayen isehlen
ɛiwen-aɣ kan wa ad k-d-nawi ayen i k-yehwan seg wučči yernu tura kan  tayaẓiḍt yewwan ccerba frik tteffaḥ lbanan lḥelwa suter kan aql-aɣ da 
ɛeggḍeɣ fell-as   ruḥet ad tefkem kunwi s yiẓan-nwen 
yeṭṭerḍeq s taḍsa yenna   ah  dayen fehmeɣ tebɣiḍ ad temmteḍ yeshel maḍi ad k-nefk ayen tessarameḍ 
yezzi ɣer yimjelkaḍen-ines yumeṛ-iten 
 rret-t ɣer usarij sɛeddit-t deg ssikkis alamma yessuffeɣ tarwiḥt
 neṭgen fell-i lewḥuc-nni cudden-iyi ɣas akken ɛerḍeɣ ad beddeɣ deg wudem-nsen
d ayen taɛya tfekka-inu
maca ɣas akken ur ḥbiseɣ ara seg uɛeggeḍ d rregmat
yal mi ara yessuffeɣ yibki-nni aqerruy-iw seg waman ad ddun ssuɣat d rregmat d tririt n nnefs-inu
dɣa yuɣal yettɛeṭṭil ur d-yessuffuɣ ara aqerruy-iw s temɣawla armi xenqeɣ iruḥ-iyi nnefs kecmen waman imalusen ɣer tgerjumt-iw
qrib i teffeɣ rruḥ-iw s tidet
sakin yumeṛ-iten ad ḥebsen ssikkis dɣa ḍeggren-iyi ɣef lqaɛa yessan s ssiman
sliɣ-as yettaggez deg-i i tikkelt niḍen   tikkelt-a tɣaḍeḍ-iyi maca tikkelt niḍen ad ffɣeɣ seg texxamt-a ad ten-ǧǧeɣ ad k-nɣen 
ulac acu i as-nniɣ lethaɣ kan s tririt n nnefs i yi-ruḥen
sliɣ-as i tewwurt n wuzzal mi temdel
qemceɣ allen-iw uɣaleɣ i tikkelt niḍen ɣer uhetref-inu ɣef tmettant
sakin tewwi-yi tnafa walaɣ iman-iw nnig n yiwen n useklu yettemcabi ɣer uzumbi n temẓi-inu win iɣef ttaliɣ akken ad nadiɣ ɣef laɛcuc n yigḍaḍ ddaw-as yella yibki-nni akked kra n yimdanen ttsuɣun ttemdeggaren refden ifassen-nsen ɣur-i iqerra-nsen ttwalin irkelli s igenni nekk qqimeɣ ɣef yiwen n ufurk imal qrib ad yeɣli
ur fhimeɣ ara imeslayen-nsen ur ẓriɣ ara acu bɣan ɣur-i
ɛeqleɣ udmawen n yimjelkaḍen n urfiq-iw deg texxamt d wudmawen n kra seg yimeddukkal-iw
tettiɣ iles-iw akken ad ten-seqsiɣ d acu bɣan ɣur-i maca yugi ad yeffeɣ ssut seg tgerjumt-iw
deffir-nsen deg yiwen n umdun walaɣ tamaɛcuqt-iw teckunṭeḍ deg yiri-s teqqim tettmuqul deg-i s wudem uḥzin
ayen yessewhamen d udem-is kan i d-yettbinen akken ilaq
d udem ahuskay maca d uḥzin yebzeg s yimeṭṭawen
imir-n kan yerreẓ ufurk-nni ɣliɣ-d
ukiɣ-d teccef-iyi tidi ttarraɣ nnehta s tmara
yerwi laɛqel-iw ckunṭḍeɣ ɣer tugniwin-nni bɣiɣ ad mmektiɣ ssifat-nsent
maca rewwlent fell-i s laɛqel
yerra-yi-d fad ɣer tfekka-inu ḥulfaɣ i laẓ igezzem iẓerman-iw
nudaɣ s wallen-iw ɣef uḍebsi-nni ufiɣ-t mazal-it deg umkan-is
mrurdeɣ ɣur-s smareɣ ayen yellan deg-s deg uɛebbuḍ-iw
aɣrum-nni sbelɛeɣ-t d asebleɛ
ɣas akken yeqqim uɛebbuḍ-iw yesṭewṭiw seg laẓ
sekmumceɣ iman-iw ɣerqeɣ deg tekta
deg teswiɛt-nni sliɣ seg mbeɛɛid i ladan n lefjer yerra-yi ɣer temẓi-inu d umennuɣ-iw d baba
xemmemeɣ deg
yakuc d tezmert-ines tameqqrant
ayɣer ihi i yeǧǧa imẓiwen-a ad iyi-sɛeddin deg ssikkis wa ad kksen fell-i sser  acu xedmeɣ nekkini anagar tigawin yebɣan lxir i talsa  anda-t ihi yakuc-agi i yettarran iman-is d netta d lxir iḥemmel amdan ayɣer i yeǧǧa imdanen ḥeqqren imdanen niḍen  ur tteffreɣ ara fell-ak deg tfejrit-nni mi qqimeɣ weḥd-i kan ḥulfaɣ iman-iw d awḥid ulac win yellan yid-i ttwaḥeqreɣ ttwaḍelmeɣ ulac win ad iyi-sellken neɣ ad iyi-iwasin deg lmeḥna-inu
mmektaɣ tamuggit n ugellid d zzkara i as-xedmen yakucen iɣriqiyen mi t-ssamsen s sin n yinɣayen ucmiten ɣer yimdanen  tamenɣiwt n ubabat d zzna d yemma-s
dɣa yerwel ɣer wallun n yimenɛulen ideg urǧin yekcem lxir
lsiɣ aselsu n  ttsuɣuɣ tamuggit-inu weḥd-i kan mebla amallal
ur tteffreɣ ara fell-ak deg tfejrijt-nni tamenɛult nekkreɣ yakk yakucen d yisɣanen yellan ckunṭḍeɣ ɣer brumitus amakar n tmes sɣur yakucen i yefka sakin i talsa
sugneɣ iman-iw d brumitus imsellek n talsa seg uqhar n yakucen
maca ufiɣ amdan yettuɣal ula d netta d yakuc uqsiḥ yesseɣlay lbaṭel ɣef tmital-is mi ara yaweḍ ɣer usgeld n udabu
mmektaɣ-d tanfalit n 
 imdanen irkelli ffɣen-d seg ljedra n uneḍlib  yeqsed dagi qabil i yenɣan gma-s habil mi yessegzay takriḍt d wanɣa yellan deg talsa
tura anɣa-agi yelseq deg umdan yeṭṭafar-it i lebda  anamek n waya ur nezmir ara ad t-nekkes seg tudert n yimdanen ɣas ulamma nebna-as lǧennet deg lqaɛa  lmuhim aṭas n tikta i yezzin deg wallaɣ-iw tafejrit-nni myeckaḍent myuwatent daxel n tfekka-inu yaɛyan
sakin tewwi-yi yiwet n tnafa acekki-tt ssarmeɣ urǧin ad akiɣ
tikta-a uɣalent-iyi d asafar mgal ssikkis dɣa sebreɣ i ssikkis-nsen s yiwet n tezmert n wuzzal
sxedmen yid-i lesnaf niḍen n ssikkis ladɣa tasafut d tkaskiḍt talmanit
ad rren ɣef uqerruy-iw yiwen n ssḍel n wuzzal armi d tuyat ad ddmen tafḍist neɣ aɛekkaz ad bdun sakin tiyita deg ssḍel-nni
ssut i ixeddem ssḍel-nni yettɣimi itezzi deg yimeẓẓuɣen-iw s ṭul n wass yernu iqerreḥ mliḥ
ɣas akken ulac acu i sen-nniɣ
s lmeqlub ttsuɣuɣ reggmeɣ tiyemmatin-nsen d twaculin-nsen sexdamen yir lehdur dɣa ad rnnun deg tyitwin-nsen alamma ɣliɣ ṣerɛeɣ
ad akiɣ kan ad d-uɣalen ɣur-i ad kemmlen axeddim-nsen afuḥan
uɣalen ttɛassan-iyi mliḥ
uɣaleɣ tturareɣ yid-sen urar n umcic d uɣerda
ttarraɣ iman-iw ṣerɛeɣ ur ttakiɣ ara alamma bɣiɣ ad ḍeggreɣ aman n tasa yernu ad k-id-iniɣ tidet acḥal d abrid i becceɣ deg userwal-iw akken ur ttenkareɣ ara
ur cliɛeɣ ara deg tezdeg-inu uɣaleɣ umseɣ am uɣerda tafekka-inu tettak-d kra n rriḥa tafuḥant mačči d kra win ad tt-yesriḥen ad yetiqef
faqen i tḥilet-inu uɣalen keccmen fell-i ɛlaɣila melmi i sen-yehwa ad i yi-skerkren mebla rreḥma ɣer tmacint n ssikkis
ɣas akken sebreɣ wehmeɣ deg yiman-iw
ar tura umbaɛd kraḍet n tmerwin n yiseggasen ɣef tedyant-nni tafuḥant mi ara d-mmektiɣ wehmeɣ amek i ssawḍeɣ ad sebreɣ i wannect-nni n ssikkis ɣef tfekka-inu ur sriseɣ ara ifassen-iw ur d-bdireɣ ula d yiwen n yisem
deg taggara maḍi deg yiwen n yiḍ srekben-iyi deg yiwet n tkamyunt ɣummen-iyi allen-iw ǧǧan-iyi s yiselsa-inu icergen fuḥen ḍeggren-iyi ɣef yiri n ubrid umbaɛd snat n tsaɛtin n tuzzya
iḍ-nni yewwet-d ugeffur yernu semmeḍ mliḥ
lḥiɣ deg ṭṭlam armi wwḍeɣ ɣer yiwen n uddaynin n yizgaren ṭṭseɣ ɣef uɛemmur n tuga
bab n uxxam yessaki-yi-d ɣer tafrara yeddem-d ɣur-i yiwen n uɛekkaz yeḥseb-iyi d amakar
maca mi as-mmeslayeɣ s laɛqel nniɣ-as ffɣeɣ seg sbiṭar n yimehbal ɣaḍeɣ-t yefka-yi-d ad ččeɣ iseddeq fell-i kra n yiselsa d imaynuten
sutreɣ deg-s kra n yidinaren akken ad ṭṭfeɣ lkar snemreɣ-t ǧǧiɣ-t
uɣaleɣ ɣer teɣremt n yinelmaden axxam-inu ayiwan
ur ufiɣ ara arfiq-iw
rǧiɣ-t maca ur d-yusi ara
qelbeɣ fell-as deg tesdawit ulac win i d-yefkan tansa-ines
iruḥ-d yiwet n tsebḥit deg wussan n yimuras ur iɛeṭṭel ara yeqqim azgen n ssaɛa kan yenna-yi-d yekcem ɣer tudert tuffirt d akabar-ines i as-yefkan lamer umbaɛd mi tewwi tɣellist taserdasant inelmaden i ttekkan deg usunded ɣer lḥebs lliɣ nekkini yiwen seg yimezwura
mi ɣabeɣ iḍ amezwaru yerkeb-it ccekk ur uɣeɣ ara tannumi gganeɣ berra n teɣremt n yinelmaden
inuda fell-i deg wass wis sin ur iyi-yufi ara later
yuggad ɣef yiman-is yeffer ɣer yiwen seg yimeddukkal-is sakin yunag ɣer temdint niḍen ur yebdir ara isem-is tura yettili deg uxxam n yiwen n umeɣnas niḍen
yessenmer-iyi imi ur bdireɣ ara isem-is
amer senzeɣ-t tili qelben axxam n yimawlan-is maca ulac acu xedmen
yessumer-iyi-d ad iyi-yawi ɣer yiwen n umkan d uffir ma yehwa-yi
yiwen n umkan ulac win ara ixemmemen ɣur-s d yiwet n zzawiya deg tmurt n
leqbayel
ẓriɣ umbaɛd belli zzawiya-nni tella deg yiwet n tallit d amkan ideg ssuffuɣen aɣmis  taɣuct n uɣref  acku yiwen seg yimḍebbren n zzawiya-nni aqeddac-ines d jeddi-s
nniɣ-as i urfiq-iw dayen wwiɣ amur-iw seg lḥebs d ssikkis ur cukkeɣ ara ad iyi-teddem tɣellist taserdasant i tikkelt tis snat acku twala yakan taɣart n uqerruy-inu teẓra daɣen ur tettawi ara sɣur-i ula d yiwen n usekkil
yessers urfiq-nni idrimen ɣef tnarit yenna-yi-d d lemɛawna kan akken ad ffɣeɣ seg lmeḥna-inu dɣa yekker yeffeɣ s temɣawla
sɛeddaɣ s tidet kra n wussan waɛrit lemdeɣ deg-sen amek ad tɛassaɣ iman-iw amek ad meyyzeɣ uqbel ad neggzeɣ
iban tiyita n temsulta d yiserdasen terreẓ asenfar-nni n usbeddi n unmalu amunan n yinelmaden
kecmen kra n yimsfesden d wid yeddan d ukabar aqbur daxel n umussu ssawḍen ɣer taggara ad sbedden yiwen n unmalu n yinelmaden imal ɣer udabu
xemmemeɣ ad ssuffɣeɣ lkarṭa ɣef wid iyi-yukren
walaɣ yiwen n umastan yeḍsa fell-i yenna-yi-d   ayɣer tessneḍ-ten  tzemreḍ ad tɛeqleḍ axerdus anda i k-ǧǧan 
d acu ad d-tiniḍ i unezzarfu  ad k-d-yini tselbeḍ wa ad k-iceggeɛ ɣer ssbiṭar n yimeslab
yernu d acu tɣileḍ yezmer unezzarfu ad yeḥkem ɣef tɣellist taserdasant  ad k-awin tikkelt niḍen yernu tikkelt-a ad k-meḍlen i lebda
sebɛed iman-ik ɣef tsertit lethu kan s leqraya-inek axir-ak
ad k-weṣṣiɣ sebɛed irkelli ɣef tesdawit ruḥ ad tqellbeḍ ɣef uxeddim
afirus n tsertit ma ifut yelseq deg walbaɛḍ ur as-yeṭṭixir ara alamma yečča-t irkelli
tasdawit deg wussan-a d annar ideg yettlal yal ssenf n yifirusen i d-igellun s lmut 
qqimeɣ kra n wussan ttxemmimeɣ ɣef yimal-inu
ǧǧiɣ leqraya-inu
rewleɣ ɣef yirmad n yinelmaden
mi ara tɛeddi fell-i tekti-nni belli yezmer ad d-uɣaleɣ yiwen n wass ɣer uxerdus-nni amelɛun tettaṭṭaf-iyi tergagayt
ṭṭfeɣ daɣen rray ur xeddmeɣ ara akked tɣellist taserdasant
yiwet n tmeddit iruḥ-d ɣur-i yiwen n umdan ur t-ssineɣ ara yessenked iman-is d anawar unnig deg tselwit n tegduda yemmeslay-d yid-i ɣef tudert tanmalant deg tesdawit
iban-d d yiwen i yi-yessnen mliḥ yessumer-iyi-d ad iyi-iɛiwen ad ṭṭfeɣ taselwit n unmalu n yinelmaden ma bɣiɣ
iṛeggem-iyi-d ad iyi-d-yaf ula d tanezduɣt
ur ḥawleɣ ara awal yid-s
faqeɣ d aceggeɛ i t-ceggɛen ɣur-i akken ad xedmeɣ akked tɣellist taserdasant
ur tturebbaɣ ara akken ad senzeɣ imdanen
d yir ssira ur iyi-tlaq ara mačči akka i ttwaliɣ ddunit
ttif ad kecmeɣ ɣer lɛesker neɣ ɣer tɣellist taserdasant s timmad-is wala ad ffreɣ gar yimeddukkal-iw inelmaden akken ad aruɣ ineqqisen uffiren ɣer yirmad-nsen
d yir-tawuri d tawuri n ddel
nekk d amsedrar uɣeɣ tannumi qqareɣ tidet iles-iw ur iqebbel ara ad yenṭeq s tkerkas
amer akka i lliɣ tili ur nuɣeɣ d baba ɣef tẓallit ur iyi-yessuffeɣ seg uxxam
amer d aḥezzaz neɣ d amedlul i lliɣ tili kellxeɣ-as i baba rriɣ iman-iw ttẓallaɣ ad beddeɣ deffir-s am wakken xeddmen tuget n yimdanen deffir n ccix n lǧameɛ akken ur kkaten ara deg-sen ur ten-ɛezzlen ara
maca ur xdimeɣ ara akka acku lxedma-agi ɣur-i ur tlaq ara i urgaz argaz am wakken i t-ttwaliɣ am wakken i t-ḥemmleɣ argaz-nni i sarameɣ ad uɣaleɣ azekka
msefraqeɣ d umdan-nni sfehmeɣ-as ur qbileɣ ara asumer-ines
tiɣimit-inu deg tesdawit d wayen i as-yezzin iban ad iyi-yeskerker i tikkelt niḍen ɣer wannar n umussu n yinelmaden d uttekki deg temliliyin d yigrawen i yettfakkan dima s umennuɣ d temsulta
walaɣ kra n wudmawen i ssneɣ yakan uɣalen ttɛassan deg-i
ladɣa yiwen yezga yettɛassa deg-i seg lebɛid
itteddu yid-i deg lkar ikeccem yid-i ɣer tzeqqa n ssinima mi ara yiliɣ d nasira
ihewwej-iyi mačči d kra rfiɣ ruḥeɣ ad t-nnaɣeɣ
d nasira iyi-yettarran ɣer laɛqel-iw tettheddin deg-i teqqar-iyi-d ur ilaq ara ad geɣ ccan i temsalt-a yernu d lɛib ma nnuɣeɣ deg tlemmast n ubrid
ulseɣ-as ayen yeḍran yid-i asmi iyi-yewwin maca ur as-nniɣ ara kulci
tiruggza tegdel ɣef urgaz ad yini ayen i izemren ad t-ihinen
llant kra n tlisa ur nezmir ara ad tent-nezger akken ad nḥareb ɣef lhiba n tugna-nneɣ
nsebber kan i taẓẓayt d lfuḥa-ines weḥd-neɣ kan  nxeddem iwumi nezmer i wakken ad tent-nesfeḍ seg ccfawat-nneɣ ur nettaf ara iman-nneɣ yiwen n wass deg wussan n rebbi deg yiwet n tegnit ideg yessefk fell-aɣ ad sent-nales i walbaɛḍ
ad k-id-iniɣ tidet d nasira i ibedden ɣer tama-w deg wussan-nni iberkanen d nettat i yi-qennɛen ad nadiɣ ɣef uxeddim
yernu ur faqeɣ ara amek i ufiɣ iman-iw deg usuddu n usileɣ n yiselmaden
zrin yis-i wussan armi ufiɣ iman-iw ɣur-i yiwen n uxeddim yerked ttaɣeɣ yiwet n tjernaḍt tester-iyi
ula d nasira tekfa leqraya-ines tekcem ad texdem deg yiwet n tesnawit nezweǧ s temɣawla mebla ma nekseb axxam
akka i rewleɣ i tsertit tamenɛult i yi-yesseččen ilili
d tagi d taqsiḍt-inu d unagraw aserdasan i yewwten deg yimezdukklanen yesseqwa tiɣermin n watmaten inselmen i yesbedden yiwen n wafud ara t-yesseɣlin netta s timmad-is ma mačči ass-a azekka
teḍra-as i unagraw-nneɣ ungif am urgaz-nni i irebban uccen deg uxxam-is iɣil yezmer s tidet ad t-irebbi ad t-yerr d aqjun ad iɛass fell-as deg taggara yenneqlab fell-as yečča-t
d ineslemẓra ara ihudden anagraw-a ameɛfun wa ad ččen aqerruy-is deg yiseggasen i d-iteddun 
d ssikkis afuḥan s tidet
ayen yessewhamen deg teqsiḍt-agi i igezzmen tasa amek i yezmir uzzayri ad yesɛeddi azzayri am netta deg ssikkis ad as-tiniḍ mazal-aɣ deg tallit tamharsant  anwa ur neẓri belli lɛerbi ben
mhidi asaḍ n tegrawla d umaɣras-ines yemmut ddaw n ssikkis n yiserdasen ifransiyen  anwa ur neẓri belli
ǧamila buḥired d lmujahidat niḍen sɛeddan-tent deg ssikkis seɣlin-d fell-asent ddel sdullen-tent armi d ayen kksen fell-asent sser yernu neẓra ulac lɛar i yugaren wa i izemren ad yaɣen tameṭṭut  dɣa yeqqim ssikkis d lɛar ameqqran yessamsen amezruy n fransa tamhersant ula d aggagen ifransiyen imeqqranen deg tallit-nni wwten deg-s ḥesben-t d anɣa mgal talsa
amek ad d-yas ihi udabu azzayri i d-yeffɣen seg uɛebbuḍ n ṭṭrad n teslullit i d-yekkren mgal lbaṭel d uqhar ad yesɛeddi iɣermanen-is ɣas bedden deg wudem-is deg ssikkis am wa  d acu ad nexdem ad nerr amjelkaḍ-nni d aɣersiw ad as-nekkes ssifa n umdan wa ad t-nessuffeɣ seg talsa  maca aɣersiw ur yekkat ur yettkerric alamma yuggad yebɣa ad iḥudd ɣef yiman-is neɣ ma yelluẓ
ur nezmir ara ad neḥseb ssikkis d aḥuddu ɣef yiman
