d acu yettaǧǧan wid yeṭṭfen adabu ad smersen yakk allalen mgal wid ibedden deg wudem-nsen ulamma d allalen ucmiten ur tqebbel talsa 
tumant n tmenɣiwt d tuṭṭfa n udabu s yiɣil tettwassen mliḥ deg umezruy aɛrab-ineslem d umezruy n talsa s umata
lsas n udadu d takriḍt d uqhar ɣef waya ilaq ad ilin yiɣallen n laman d yiserdasen  tidet tamazrayt tedda d uwernaḍ bakunin i yessutren tukksa n temsulta n yiserdasen akked tlisa gar tmura  ma nekkes tamsulta yezmer ad ḥebsen yimakaren takerḍa yezmer daɣen ad tessekcem timettiwin deg twernaḍt tamatut ara tent-yerren ɣer uswir n uɣersiw ideg tella deg tazwara 
tamenɣiwt tezdeɣ deg ṭṭbiɛa n umdan am wakken i d-yenna deg tenfalit-ines yettwassnen
 imdanen irkelli ffɣen-d seg ljedra n uneḍlib   seg wasmi tebda ddunit ttalsent tiqsiḍin ɣef tismin i yeǧǧan
qabil ad ineɣ gma-s habil acku yakuc yeqbel asefk n
habil deg umkan n win-is
yemmut habil mebla ma yezweǧ
ma d qabil yerna iɛac aṭas yernu yesɛa-d aṭas n dderya
akka ihi i d-tlul talsa seg ljedra n qabil mmi-s n
adem win yenɣan gma-s
anamek n waya timenɣiwt n umdan s ufus n gma-s amdan d ayen i newret seg yimdanen lqaɛa-a
ṭṭuqtent tmenɣiyin gar yiɛeggalen n yiwet n twacult neɣ n yiwen n udrum deg tmettiwin timensayin i yettidiren ar iḍ-a ddaw imezwura yeddren ɣef tsebbiwin i d-yekkren ɣef n unagraw n lɛerc d wassaɣen n tmarrewt
ɣef waya mazal timenɣiwt telseq deg umdan tetteffeɣ ɣer berra deg kra n tegnatin tugi ad truḥ ccil tamussni d sswab n yisɣanen d tfelsufin i yekkaten ɣef tayri d tegmat i ibedden mgal takriḍt d ddɣel akked tegrawliyin n talsa i usbeddi n teɣdemt tamettit d uqader n rray n wiyaḍ d swayes umnen
maca takriḍt tettuqet deg kra n tmettiyin tenɣes deg kra niḍen
amek ad nessegzi tilin n tekriḍt deg tmetti tazzayrit deg yal tallit n umezruy-ines  ulac tallit ideg ulac amennuɣ ama gar yiterrasen neɣ gar trebbuyaɛ tikkwal yettili i lfayda n kra n yimdanen kan tikkwal d amennuɣ tisertiyin neɣ timettanin
ad neqbel ihi s tikti-nni i d-yeqqaren takriḍt tella deg uzzayri seg zik n zik am wakken i d-yenna uɣerbaz amharsan n tesleḍt n tnefsit yettwassnen s yisem n uɣerbaz azzayri
nettaf tikti-a deg tezrawin i yexdem deg uzgen amezwaru n uwinas wis mraw d tẓa
wigi i yettḥuddun ɣef waddud-a bnan ifukal-nsen ɣef tumant n tmenɣiwin yellan gar yizzayriyen ama d iɛraben neɣ d imaziɣen i iɛeddan ɣef uxxam n teɣdemt
walan azzayri yessexdam takriḍt tikkwal ineqq ɣef yiwet n ssebba i yezmer ad yefru s uskasi akked laɛqel
imesdurar ḥemmlen asexdem n lfuciwat acku mi ara amsen yifassen-nsen s yidammen yettnerni nnif-nsen
ma wid izedɣen deg yignan leslaḥ i ḥemmlen ad sxedmen s waṭas d ajenwi i ssufuɣen yal mi ara yili umennuɣ
walan imejjayen-nni tuget n tfekwin yenɣan s ujenwi yellan deg texxamin ideg ttaǧǧan lmeyytin sedxecmen-ten irkelli ttwawtent s waṭas n tiyitwin n ujenwi iswi ihi mačči d timenɣiwt yiwet n tyita neɣ snat ɛumment
tiyitwin niḍen i yefka uneḍlib sɛant iswi niḍen mačči d aḥuddu ɣef yiman neɣ d asekref n uxsim i yeqseḍ d asdexcem n tfekka-nni daya
am wakken teḍra asmi ẓeḍmen ɣef tkamyunt n yimeḥbas kra n wussan aya
yeḥka-yi-d si
aḥmed akumisar n temsulta belli tifekkiwin n yimsulta yettwanɣan sedxecment irkelli s rrsas d tiyitwin n ujenwi ulac acu ara twaliḍ deg-sent
acu-t ddɣel-agi yellan deg wulawen n yineḍliben-agi  aserwel n yimeḥbas weḥd-s ur yezmir ara ad yili d afukel i usdexcem n tfekwin s tiyitwin n ujenwi
yerra-d ɣef yimejjayen i t-yesseɣren
ɣur-s netta takriḍt-a d tiririt ɣef tekriḍt tamharsant ugar n lqern aya
takriḍt tettarew-d takriḍt
i talwit tettarew-d talwit  ayɣer ijur yiwen n wass racid akken ad t-magren s tekriḍt  tamsalt tekres ɣef waya ur nezmir ara ad tt-neqqen kan ɣer umennuɣ i yettilin gar yimdanen
ayen yessewhamen deg waya asmi tewwi
lezzayer timunnent-ines ur ufin ara izzayriyen anwa ara ɛanden anagar fransa
d tumant n win yettwaɣelben i yeṭṭafaren idles d tɣerma n win i t-yernan am wakken i d-yeqqar
ibn-xeldun  anwa i yettwaɣelben anwa i irebḥen gar ruma taserdasant d atina mm-tikta d yidles 
lezzayer tamjahedt tamaɣrast akked fransa mm-tatrarit d tikta  umbaɛd n tmunnent n tmurt uzzlen yimassayen-nneɣ imaynuten tuget deg-sen ɣran s tefransist ad bnun anagraw ur yemgarad ara mliḥ ɣef unagraw n tselwit tafransist tayaɛqubit ǧǧan yakk leqwanen d yisuḍaf n tedbelt n fransa ugar n waya ssawḍen ad ten-ɛanden ula deg usɛeddi n yiɣermanen deg ssikis am wakken xedmen irumiyen deg tallit tamharsant
yuɣal ufransis d amedya i ilaq ad neḍfer i wakken ad nekcem ɣer tɣerma
ur iferreḥ ara uzzayri alamma iɛaned afransis deg tutlayt-is deg uselmed n warraw-is deg yiɣerbazen-ines tutlayt tafransist ur tekcim ara s telqi deg tmetti-nneɣ armi umbaɛd n tmunnent yernu s lemɛawna n uɣerbaz azzayri-d tiɣin n sselɛa-ines faqen-as ula yimsenza ma bɣan ad senzen yal sselɛa yernu s ssuma ɣlayen ad as-inin tekka-d seg fransa  d lmarka n fransa 
daɣen ur nḥesseb ara inig d inig ma ur iruḥ ara ɣer neɣ
marsilya
akka i yuɣal ufransis amhersan aqehar d amedya n tɣerma umbaɛd n tmunnent n tmurt
amek ad d-nessefhem waya  tura ma nuɣal ɣer tilawt ad naf lqern d uzgen n temharsa n uqhar d lbaṭel ad d-yessegri deffir-s lbeɣḍ d ddɣel mgal ufransis
maca mačči d wagi i yeḍran
afransis yuɣal d netta i d ababat s unamek i as-yefka

d ababat i nebɣa ad nenɣ mačči d akrah i nekreh maca d netta i ibedden deg ubrid n unegmu-nneɣ
ad naweḍ ɣer tmeṭṭut i nebɣa
dɣa ad t-nekkes seg ubrid-nneɣ akken ad naf iman-nneɣ weḥd-neɣ deg wannar wa ad nawi amkan-is afeḥli ad nexdem ayen i ixeddem netta uqbel ad t-nɛaned wa ad nuɣal am netta
uma tiqsiḍin-nni n taḍsa i d-yeskanayen bumedyen d afeḥli i yettekksen sser ɣef lezzayer-tameṭṭut d anza ɣef tgensest-a
amedya ɣef teqsiḍin-a yella yiwen n ukerraz d bu-nniya yessuter deg bumedyen i iruḥen ɣer yiwet n taddart i d-yezgan ɣef tqacuct n udrar ad t-yeǧǧ ad yekcem yid-s ɣer ubduz
daxel n ubduz yesseqsa-t
bumedyen acu yebɣa ɣur-s yerr-as bu-nniya-nni  bɣiɣ ad waliɣ abbuc-agi-inek swayes tetteqquḍ aɣref-a ameɣbun
acḥal i ẓewren yizzayriyen deg usnulfu n teqsiḍin am tigi  ur neẓri ara ma d udemkal d unezwu rennun i tekriḍt  anezwu i yettneggizen seg tegrest tasemmaḍt ɣer unebdu aḥmayan mliḥ
ademkal tuget-ines d idurar d tewririn tewɛer tudert deg-sen ɣas akken d imekwan lhan ad yeffer deg-sen umdan mgal ṭṭradat yernu acḥal ṭṭuqtent mgal aɛdaw agensay neɣ azɣaray
ad neddu d rray n ibn-xeldun i d-yennan taweṭṭuft yettidiren deg temnaḍin tisemmaḍin tesdeḥwel ɣef tin yettilin deg temnaḍin tiḥmayanin  ula d imussnawen-nneɣ ttawin-d seg tmura tiberraniyin turdiwin n usegzi n tmettiyin akken ad tent-sesmlen dɣa ad tent-ddmen akken llant wa ad ɛerḍen ad segzin yis-sent timettiyin-nneɣ deg umkan ad kkren ad nadin ɣef wallalen ilelliyin ara yadfen deg wadif n tmettiyin-nneɣ akken ad tent-segzin wa ad ẓren amek leḥḥunt d wamek ttnernint deg umezruy
tuget n yidlisen i yettmeslayen ɣef umezruy n tmurt-agi uran-ten
yirubiyen i d-yeddan d temharsa
dɣa nuɣal nettwali timetti-nneɣ s wallen n yinekmaren-a
ahat d wagi i aɣ-yeǧǧan nḥeqqer iman-nneɣ nḥeqqer daɣen yakk ayen bnan yizzayriyen anagar acu xedmen deg tegrawla d tmettant ɣef tmurt-agi
ad as-tiniḍ ḥala ṭṭrad i nezmer ad nexdem ḥala ṭṭrad
ufiɣ iman-iw ɣerqeɣ deg yiseqsiyen ur nesɛi tazwara wala taggara
yeqreḥ-iyi uqerruy-iw mliḥ dayen iyi-yerran ɣer tilawt
faqeɣ i tezmamt n nabil mazal-itt gar yifassen-iw
mazal kra n yisebtar ur ten-ɣriɣ ara
mi tettiɣ tiwreqtin walaɣ kra n yisebtar ttucergen deg taggara n tezmamt yernu iban d ussan-agi kan i ten-icerreg
kra n yisebtar kan ssawḍeɣ ad ten-ḥesbeɣ acku tazmamt-a d tagruma n tezmamin tiɣurbizin timeẓyanin myinṭaḍent
dɣa yeshel ad ẓreɣ acḥal n yisebtar yellan deg yiwet n tezmamt
ukkuẓ n yisebtar
anwa i ten-icergen  d
nabil  d racid i yufan deg-sen yiwen n uffir ur yebɣi ara ad t-ẓren wiyaḍ  ṭṭfeɣ rray ad kemmleɣ taɣuri-ines wa ad ǧǧeɣ i umbaɛd taqsiḍt-a n yisebtar yettucergen
maca uqbel tlaq-iyi yiwet n lqehwa ara yessafgen fell-i leqriḥ n uqerru i yi-yeṭṭfen
ruḥeɣ ɣer tnawalt ddmeɣ aberrad n lqehwa ur nurad ara seg wacḥal n wussan
walaɣ llan lkisan d uḍebsi d tɣenjawin umsen
ad yexzu rebbi tiffenyent i d-yeɣlin fell-i ussan-a ineggura  ad ten-sirdeɣ azekka ssbeḥ
ḍeggreɣ afus-iw mebla axemmem ɣer umkan ideg ttaǧǧaɣ tabwaḍt n lqehwa yeẓḍen dɣa imir-n kan i d-mmektaɣ ǧǧiɣ-tt d tilemt tasebḥit-a ttuɣ ur d-uɣeɣ ara tayeḍ d tajdiḍt
ad yenɛel rebbi allaɣ-agi i sɛiɣ
d acu ara xedmeɣ tura mi yeɣli yiḍ yerna lehmum-is ɣef tuyat-iw  anda ad d-afeɣ taḥanut yeldin ad i yi-yesenzen tabwaḍt n lqehwa deg wuḍan-a yessewḥacen ideg tteffren medden deg yixxamen-nsen mi ara yeɣli yiṭij terwiḥin d wayla-nsen  qqimeɣ uggaden ttxemmimeɣ ɛerqent-iyi irkelli ɣerqeɣ deg lkas n lqehwa ɣef ur nelli
uɣaleɣ sakin ɣer usalun ttxemmimeɣ amek ad xedmeɣ akken ad d-qḍuɣ azekka-nni ayen ixussen i uxxam
ddmeɣ tazmamt yellan ɣef ṭṭabla s wurfan kecmeɣ ɣer texxamt-iw
ufiɣ ameṭreḥ-inu yexreb irkelli yeqqim am wakken i t-ǧǧiɣ tasebḥit
d ayen uɣaleɣ d amɣar ur zmireɣ ara ad beddeɣ ɣef uxxam-iw
yessefk fell-i ad nadiɣ ɣef yiwet n temɣart ara yelthun s lecɣal-a acku ma teqqim liḥala akka ad yuɣal uxxam-iw d addaynin ideg ad ɛececcen yiɣerdayen
ẓẓleɣ ɣef umeṭreḥ kemmleɣ taɣuri 
ɣuct 
uɣaleɣ-d iḍelli seg yiwen n yinig ukmir i yi-yewwin ɣer unẓul n tmurt
ruḥeɣ d yasin ɣer sseḥra ad nẓur
ɛebdelǧabar
d lǧar n xalti-s i yettẓuru seg wasmi meẓẓi deg udcir n  kalitus 
yenna-yi-d yasin yessen
ɛebdelǧabar d yal yiwen seg yiɛeggalen n twacult-is seg zik
yenna-yi-d daɣen yenwa ad yexḍeb uletma-s tameẓyant
twala xalti-s yemma-s n teqcict teqbel maca yettraǧu tuffɣa n gma-s seg lḥebs akken ad iruḥ ad tt-yexḍeb s wudem unsib
ula d nekk ssneɣ ɛebdelǧabar
yella yettas-d seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ ad ɣ-d-yefk kra n temsirin ɣef usɣan deg lǧameɛ n nnur
d yasin i t-yettmagaren yettɣimi yid-s segmi ara d-yaweḍ alamma yuɣal
yernu ur iḥebbes ara iseqsiyen ɣef usɣan ɣef tsertit d temsal niḍen wehmeɣ seg wansi i ten-id-yettawi
ɛebdelǧabar yesɛa lhiba ladɣa s lqedd-ines aɣezzfan aččamar-ines ameqqran i yesbeɣ s lḥenni d uqendur-ines amellal
teṭṭef-it temsulta deg meɣres yezrin wwin-t sakin ɣer yiwen n lḥebs deg sseḥra
yemma-s tebɣa ad t-tẓur maca argaz-is yugi ad yeddu yid-s
yeḥḍer yasin mi s-yesla teccetkay i xalti-s dɣa yessumer-as ad yeddu yid-s acku ula d netta yejemm ameddakkel-is d uselmad-ines
ɛebdelǧabar
maca nniya n yasin d tayeḍ yebɣa ad yesmil ɣur-s ul n yemma-s n teqcict-nni i yebɣa ad yexḍeb
yessefhem-iyi-d daɣen ɛebdelǧabar d aqcic ayiwan gar waṭas n tullas kra deg-sent zewǧent sɛant dderya
baba-s iɛewweq ur yeẓri ara acu ad yexdem sdat n tigawin n mmi-s
ur as-yaɛǧib ara lḥal mi yekcem ɣer ukabar n yineslemẓra acku ittekka deg tuddsa n yimjuhad iqdimen n tegrawla n teslullit n tmurt
taseglut-a teǧǧa-t ad yeṭṭef amkan ameqqran deg tsirt n lkalitus ideg ixeddem ɣas akken ur yessin ara ad iheǧǧi ula d yiwen n usekkil n ugemmay
aṭas n yimeddukkal i yesɛa gar yimjuhad iqdimen ttɛawanen-t yal tikkelt mi ara yeḥwaǧ kra
ɣef waya yessaweḍ ad yebnu axxam d ameqqran bu-sin n yinnagen
yenna-d daɣen yasin ula d argaz n xalti-s d yiwen seg yimjuhad iqdimen mačči yiwet n tseglut i d-yewwi  akal isufar n lebni s ssuma irexsen urag n taksi i yefka i yiwen seg warraw-is d tɣawsiwin niḍen ḥala rebbi i yeẓran d acu-tent
mi iyi-d-yessumer yasin tikti n yinig ɣer sseḥra qebleɣ imir-n kan mebla axemmem
d tagnit i ufiɣ akken ad ffɣeɣ seg usatel n uxxam i yi-ixenqen
nnuɣeɣ d uletma ɣef yiselsa i tettlus d rrwaḥ-ines ɣer yillel anda i tessucuf d yirgazen
tewɛer tettḥuddu ɣef yizerfan-is am temcict i yettḥaraben ɣef warraw-is imecṭaḥ mgal yal amihi
ɣef waya uɣaleɣ ur as-heddreɣ ara maḍi
ma temmeslay yid-i neɣ asuter deg-i ad as-d-aɣeɣ kra n tɣawsiwin ttarraɣ iman-is ulac acu i sliɣ
deg tazwara tella tetḥettit tettales i usuter-ines acḥal d abrid
qrib i as-uɣeɣ awal maca ttaṭṭafeɣ iman-iw ssawḍeɣ ad beddeɣ deg wudem-is tikwal s tsusmi tikwal niḍen s tuffɣa seg uxxam
yiwet n tikkelt tessekcem-d yemma iman-is  ruḥ aɣ-d i uletma-k ayen teḥwaǧ
nniɣ-as  ayɣer ur tettruḥu ara nettat s timmad-is akken ad d-taɣ ayen i as-yehwa 
tenna  kečč d argaz teshel fell-ak tuffɣa ma d nettat 
nniɣ  nettat d acu-tt 
tenna  nettat d tameṭṭut tebɣiḍ ad twaliḍ uletma-k tettawi tettarra sdat n lǧiran 
nniɣ  ayɣer ur thedreḍ ara akka mi tettruḥu weḥd-s ɣer yillel am urgaz neɣ illel yebɛed ɣef wallen n lǧiran 
tessusem yemma ulac acu i yi-d-tenna
tikkelt taneggarut ideg temmeslay yid-i uletma ur as-rriɣ ara awal tergem-iyi ulac acu i yi-teǧǧa
maca ɣas akken susmeɣ ṭṭfeɣ iles-iw
dɣa tuɣal ula d nettat ur iyi-d-thedder ara
akka xir
ulac acu i as-nniɣ i baba ɣef yinig-inu
ẓriɣ ur iḥebbes ara s yiseqsiyen-nni n temsulta yernu deg taggara maḍi ad yeddem lfiṭu deg wudem-iw
tidet tigedlin-ines neɣsent seg wasmi kecmeɣ ɣer tesdawit maca ussan-a aql-aɣ deg yimuras
d acu ad as-iniɣ ma yesseqsa-yi-d ɣef tnila n yinig-inu yernu ẓriɣ ad iyi-yesseqsi  nniɣ-as kan i yemma-s mebla ifutas
mi iyi-yesseqsa sani leḥḥuɣ nniɣ-as 
 ad dduɣ d yasin ɣer twacult n yemma-s deg temnaḍt n tubiret
ad neqqin sin neɣ kraḍ n wussan d aya

tmuqqel-iyi-d s wallen ččurent s lḥanna tedɛa
rebbi ad iyi-yeḥrez wa ad yili yid-i deg yinig-inu
inig yeḍra-d deg yiḍ
teqleɛ yis-neɣ lkar ɣer lmeɣreb abrid srid ɣer unẓul
tegla-d yemma-s n ɛebdelǧabar s snat n tqeftin annect ilatent ẓẓayit mačči d kra
faqeɣ seg tazwara ččurent s yal ssenf n wučči d yiselsa
yiwet tewwi-tt i mmi-s ameḥbus ma d tayeḍ thegga-aɣ-tt-id i nekkni deg-s akk ayen i yettcedhi wul n umessikel
d tikkelt tamezwarut i walaɣ xalti yamina
d tameṭṭut d tazurant d talemmast deg lqedd telsa yiwen n lḥiǧab d aqehwi terra ɣef wudem-is yiwen n laɛǧar d amellal
tessenmer-aɣ aṭas tedɛa-aɣ s teɣzi n laɛmer mi neqbel ad tt-nsaɛef deg yinig-agi ukmir
lkar teččur s yimessukal tuget deg-sen seg unẓul ttwaɛeqlen s uglim-sen aras iqendyar-nsen imellalen d yizegzawen d ccac ɣef yiqerra-nsen
tuget deg-sen d irgazen ma d tilawin drus deg-sent
amur ameqqran tewwi-ten tnafa mi tebda lkar tikli
tessaɛya-ten tmanaɣt s zzhir d wuguren-ines
ma d nekk ur heggaɣ ara iman-iw i yiḍes
ul-iw ččuren-t tuggdi d cckukat ur ihenni ara
bexlaf yasin i yettbin d aḥewwes i yettḥewwis deg teftist
udem-is yennecraḥ ur yeḥbis ara ameslay
nuɣ imekwan n deffir n lkar
qqimeɣ tama n ṭṭaq akken ad sedhuɣ iman-iw
maca kulci iruḥ deg rrayeɛ ssaɛa umbaɛd yeɣli yiṭij beddat deg temnaḍt n ceffa ideg tebda lkar caterwal deg yiberdan yettin am tella yizerman newweḍ imir-n ɣer ubrid yettawin ɣer temdint n blida
abrid yettawin ɣer lemdiya ssneɣ-t mliḥ acḥal d abrid i t-uɣeɣ mi ttzuruɣ laɛmum-iw asmi meẓẓeyeɣ uqbel ad yegzem d baba assaɣen d yimawlan-is seg wasmi temmut jidda
d idurar iɛlayanen yeččuren s yisekla d tẓegwa yessekcamen tuggdi ɣer wul
deg kra n yimeḍqan ɣileɣ tura ad tegrireb yis-neɣ lkar deg yicerfan-nni tettaṭṭaf-iyi tergagayt
dɣa ttmuquleɣ ɣer yimessukal niḍen ttafeɣ-ten rekden ulac acu i yuggaden
imir-n kan tettuɣal-iyi tebɣest yetthenni lxaṭer-iw ttkemmileɣ sakin askud deg yiɣeẓrawen yessefqaɛen
teḥbes lkar acḥal d abrid ɣer tserglin n yiserdasen
ad d-yali yiwen n uɛeskriw ad yessiked mliḥ deg-neɣ ad yelḥu armi d talemmast n lkar ad yessuter lekwaɣeḍ seg kra n yimessukal ad ten-imuqel kra n lweqt ad ten-yerr i yimawlan-nsen sakin ad yameṛ anehhar n lkar ad ikemmel abrid-is
mi d-newweḍ ɣer yimi n tewwurt n tgennarit taɣezzfant neḥbes ɣer yiwet n tsergelt n temsetla taɣelnawt
sadren-d irgazen qelben-aɣ irkelli walan sakin lekwaɣeḍ-nneɣ yiwen yiwen
iweṣṣa-aɣ yasin ur nettmeslay ara ɣer yiswi n yinig-nneɣ
nemtafaq ɣef yiwet n tririt
yezwar umestul deg yasin
yerra-as yebɣa ad iẓur mmi-s n tǧaret-nneɣ yeqqimen daxel n lkar i iruḥen ɣer lɛesker
sakin yesseqsa-yi-d ula d nekk
nniɣ-as kan yid-s i lliɣ
yessaked-iyi mliḥ
uggadeɣ ciṭuḥ
yella acu i icukk neɣ d tiririt-inu ur as-naɛǧib ara  ssdeɣ ɣef tuɣmas-iw zziɣ tamuɣli-inu ɣer teẓgi-nni i yi-iqublen iruḥ ad
maca amestul-nni yerra-yi-d lekwaɣeḍ-inu yesseqsi argaz niḍen i ibedden tama-w
neqqim s ibeddi nessusem ugar n uzgen n ssaɛa armi kfan anadi d uqelleb deg leḥwal-nneɣ sakin serḥen-as i lkar ad tekemmel abrid-is
deg tazwara lliɣ selleɣ i kra seg lehdur n yasin akked tin ara yuɣalen d taḍeggalt-is
tamuɣli-inu tezga ɣer berra tettwali deg tẓegwa yettɛeddayen sdat-i ad as-tiniḍ d asaru ɣef ugama i ttwaliɣ
maca yeɣli-d ṭṭlam s temɣawla uɣaleɣ ur ttwaliɣ acemma
dɣa terra-yi tmara ad d-mmeslayeɣ d urfiq-iw
tameṭṭut-nni tebda tettezzem deg mmi-s ɛebdelǧabar 
 ur fhimeɣ ara d acu-tt tineslemt-agi i bɣan at-yiččumar-agi
seg wasmi d-nlul nekkni d inselmen
ulac win i ɣ-igedlen taẓallit uẓumm neɣ rrwaḥ ɣer lḥiǧg
yernu ur tettuɣ ara lxir n ddula i ɣ-d-yefkan i nekk d urgaz-iw tagnit ad nḥiǧǧ baṭel
amer mačči d nettat urǧin ad nizmir ad nẓur imekwan uɣrisen d uẓekka n umazzan-nneɣ ucbiḥ muḥemmed taẓallit d sslam n sidi rebbi fell-as
acḥal d abrid i ulseɣ imeslayen-a i mmi ɛebdelǧabar
yeqqar-iyi-d  imeslayen-a meqqrit ɣef tmeṭṭut i yexleq
rebbi akken ad tḍuɛ argaz-is wa ad tbedd ɣef lumur n uxxam d urebbi n warraw-is
ma timsal n usɣan ɛnan-t kan irgazen
yenna-d  tineslemt mačči kan taẓallit d uẓumm d lḥiǧǧ
yettmeslay-iyi-d ɣef tcerɛit tineslemt ineṭṭeq sakin s kra n yimeslayen meqqrit ɣef wallaɣ-iw
ayen i fehmeɣ nekkini win yebɣan ad yili d ineslem yeṭṭef deg tẓallit-ines yeṭṭaxer i leḥram
yernu ur cukkeɣ ara yella lmumen ur nxeddem ara amgared gar leḥlal d leḥram
argaz-iw ɛebdelqader i ijerben ddunit i ixulḍen medden yenna-d d tasertit i xeddmen d tuffra i tteffren deffir n usɣan
wigi daɣen d imeslayen meqqrit ɣef wallaɣ-iw ameẓyan
zgiɣ deɛɛuɣ rebbi akken ad yessebɛed ccer ɣef mmi
ul-is zeddig ur iḥemmel ara ccer i wiyaḍ
ayɣer ad t-awin ɣer lḥebs deg unẓul n tmurt 
ulac leḥbus deg ugafa  deg yiḍ-nni amcum yeḍra-d ayen ur iqebbel laɛqel n lmumen
sfeqɛen-aɣ ad ten-yessefqeɛ
rebbi
ad as-tiniḍ d ineḍliben i nella
zzin-d i uxxam deg tnafsa n yiḍ qrib i ɣ-rẓan tawwurt amer ur iɣawel ara urgaz-iw ad tt-yeldi
rẓan lḥerma n uxxam ad ten-yenɛel
rebbi
yeɛreḍ urgaz-iw ad sen-yegdel anekcum dɣa iḍegger-it yiwen n umestul akin qrib i t-yesseɣli ɣef lqaɛa
yenna-asen urgaz-iw belli d yiwen seg yimjuhad iqdimen ur sɛin ara azref ad kecmen s yiɣil s axxam-is
yerra-as yiwen seg-sen amer s tidet yiwen seg yimjuhad iqdimen i telliḍ tili trebbaḍ mmi-k ɣef uqader n yimjuhad d yimeɣrasen tili ur ireggem ara amjahed ameqqran i yessekren tagrawla akken ad tidirem ass-a deg telwit n tmunnent
imir-n kan iḍal-d mmi seg texxamt-is yenna-as i umestul-nni  amesbaṭli-agi amer s tidet d amjahed ameqqran tili ur yeqbil ara ad yeqqim ɣef ukersi mačči d ayla-s wa ad yekkes i uɣref izerfan-is
yerra-as umestul-nni  d kečč i d aɣella n ccwaṭen yebɣan ad samsen tamurt n yimeɣrasen d tegrawla
ɣiwlet ṭṭfet-t cuddet-as ifassen-is
ẓeḍmen fell-as kraḍ n yirgazen ṭṭfen-t seg yiɣallen-is
mmi ur ten-yuggad ara iqubel-iten s tebɣest d trugza
yenna-asen  ad dduɣ yid-wen sani i wen-yehwa aneft-iyi kan ad lseɣ iselsa-inu
maca imelɛunen-nni deggren-t ɣer berra n uxxam s uqendur n yiḍes
iḍ-nni isemmeḍ lḥal ula d ageffur yekkat
uzzleɣ ɣer texxamt-is ddmeɣ abalṭu-ines n tegrest ḍefreɣ-t ɣer tkamyunt i yettraǧun deg uzniq
acḥal i yethenna wul-iw mi t-walaɣ yettllusu abalṭu-ines uqbel ma ad yeqqim gar yirgazen niḍen ttwaḥebsen am netta
yethenna wul-iw mi walaɣ imeḥbas niḍen
mačči weḥd-s i yella
ur neṭṭis ara iḍ-nni
neqqim deg usalun armi i d-yaden lefjer amur ameqqran n wakud nessusem deg-s
acu i nezmer ad nexdem anagar tasusmi d yimeṭṭawen  ihedden-iyi urgaz-iw mi iyi-d-yenna ad isiwel seg uzekka i kra seg tmussniwin-ines ad sserḥen i
ɛebdelǧabar deg wussan i d-iteddun
maca yuzzel ɣef wulac
ahdum ameqqran ur yessaweḍ ara ad iẓer ula d amkan ideg yella
aṭas n wawal yuzzlen ussan-nni ɣef tfekkiwin yentutren i ttafen yimdanen ɣef yiri n yiberdan
uggadeɣ ad nɣen mmi wa ad t-ḍeggren deg teẓgi
yiwen n wass yenna-as yiwen n umdan i urgaz-iw imeḥbas-nni wwin-ten deg tazwara ɣer lkazirnat sakin ceggɛen-ten ɣer leḥbus yellan deg sseḥra
yuɣal-iyi-d usirem d yiḍes zgiɣ ttakiɣ-d deg tlemmast n yiḍ keccmeɣ deg kra n leḥsabat ur sɛin ara taggara
yal mi ara kkreɣ ad ẓalleɣ deɛɛuɣ
rebbi ad t-iyi-d-yerr d amuddir
hatan yesla-d rebbi i ddeɛwat-inu

tessusem temɣart-nni tamuɣli-ines truḥ ɣer  lebɛid
ahat temmekta-d kra n ccfawat ɛzizet fell-as neɣ tessugun taswiɛt-nni n temlilit d mmi-s i nfan ɣer lqern n ddunit
kra n lweqt kan temmeɣ tsusmi ɣef umkan
sakin yenṭeq yasin ɣur-s ula d netta yessexdem kra n yimeslayen meqqrit ɣef wallaɣ n tmeṭṭut-nni n lxir
yuɣal ɣer usentel i iḥemmel lxilafa tineslemt yerna-d fell-as tacerɛit d leqran i ilaq ad ilin d aɣbalu ayiwan i usaḍuf d ubeddi-ines mgal tugdut d yisuḍaf yessuffɣen imdanen i yettwali d lkefr d tuffɣa seg ubrid n usɣan d tikta niḍen uɣeɣ tannumi selleɣ-asent deg wagguren ineggura
ḥusseɣ-as i xalti yamina taɛya seg yimeslayen-ines maca ur teẓri ara amek ad as-tini ḥbes
tetthuzzu kan aqerruy-is sakin tenna-as   suref-iyi a yasin mmi ɛyiɣ ur ṭṭiseɣ ara mliḥ iḍ yezrin 
terra lximar-ines ɣef wallen-is teḍleq iman-is thegga iman-is i yiḍes
yessusem yasin kra n lweqt
imuqel-iyi-d akken ad ikemmel lehḍur-is
maca dewreɣ aqerruy-iw ɣer ṭṭaq uɣaleɣ i tikkelt niḍen ɣer tikta d ccfawat-inu
neffeɣ seg yiberdan n udrar ḥebsen yihuccan i ɣ-yesduqqusen i ɣ-yessafagen fell-aneɣ iḍes
s laɛqel kan ters-d tsusmi gar yimessukal uɣaleɣ selleɣ kan i ssut n umsuddu
seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ gezzment tiftilin n temdinin d tuddrin i nzegger tikta-inu ttarrant-iyi ɣer tilawt
d tafat i ittekksen ṭṭlam ɣef yiṭrutwaren ilmawen tikwal ɣef kra n i yimessukal
sakin tewwi-yi tnafa
tessaki-yi-d xalti yamina s tyitwin s tiɣmert-ines tessawal-iyi s yisem-iw
ldiɣ allen-iw ɣef tafat n tefrara d lḥess i xeddmen imessukal yettheggin iman-nsen ad rsen
tamersit d agni d ameqqran n yijdi i iqublen yiwen n lebni yunzen yettwasebɣen s yini azegzaw
neɛzel iman-leqhawi yeldin tiwwura-nsen nneɣ deg yiwet n teɣmert nettemseqsi s wallen-nneɣ d acu i ilaq ad nexdem
d yasin i yellan d amnir d netta i yessnen kulci
uqbel ad yenqer yiṭij s yiẓenẓaren-ines n unebdu yufa-aɣ lḥal nerkeb yakan lkar niḍen akked ukkuẓet n twaculin niḍen i d-yusan seg temnaḍin niḍen ad walin arraw-nsen yettwaḥebsen
lkar d taqdimt terreẓ irkelli tettembawal ayeffus aẓelmaḍ ad as-tiniḍ tura ad tenneqlab
allaɣ-iw mazal itezzi ur ṛwiɣ ara iḍes
lḥal yeḥma mliḥ d ayen i yettkemmilen i ɛeggu
sani terriḍ tamuɣli-inek ad k-id-imager wakal yeččuren s yidɣaɣen yesɛan ini n yijdi ticci i d-ttakken qerrḥent mliḥ allen n umdan
tessers-aɣ lkar deg yiwet n taddart tameẓyant tuget n yixxamen-is bnan s yiẓra d wakal ur yemxalaf ara ini-ines ɣer yini n yijdi i as-yezzin
nessers kan iḍarren-nneɣ ɣef yijdi iruḥ-d ɣur-neɣ yiwen n urgaz yettlen deg yiwen n uqendur d azegzaw udem-is iɣumm irkelli anagar tiṭṭucin-is tiberkanin i yettbinen yeɛreḍ ad ɣ-iɛiwen
yeẓra acu i ɣ-d-yewwin ɣer tɣiwant-ines
ur ɣ-yeǧǧi ara lweqt i tuttra
nerkeb deg yiwet n d taqdimt terreẓ irkelli
tenṭeq yemma-s n ɛebdelǧabar imeṭṭawen xenqen taɣuct-is 
d acu-t umkan-a anda i k-ceggɛen a mmi  amek i zemren ad idiren yimdanen deg lqifar am wa 
terra-as yiwet n tmeṭṭut 
am wakken tettwaliḍ a uletma  ad as-tiniḍ tamurt s lekmal-is ur tesɛi ara leḥbus akken ad ten-nfun ɣer lqern n ddunit-a 
yessekcem yiwen n umɣar yeqqimen deg taggara n lkar iman-is
lbaṭel-a yeɣleb win n temharsa
gma d ccix n lǧameɛ yettẓalla s medden yessefham-sen adlis n rebbi deg temsirin n wass n lǧumuɛa ɣas akken ḥebsen-t nfan-t ɣer lqifar-a
yal yiwen yebɣa ad yemmeslay yeḥma wawal gar twaculin ɣef wayen yeḍran i mmi-tsen
yal yiwen iḥar ad yales i teqsiḍt-ines ad tɣileḍ qrib ad tesserɣ iles-is dɣa ifaṛes tagnit ad tt-id-yessusef ɣer berra
yessedha-yi uskasi yeḍran gar-asen dɣa ttuɣ azɣal d teɣzi n ubrid
lḥebs yezga daxel n lkazirna n yiserdasen deg tlemmast n yiwen n ugni n yijdi i d-yezgan ddaw n yiwet n tsili n yiẓra iwumi yezzi yileẓwi
kra n yixxamen bnan-ten s yiẓra d uqermud lbaqi d iqiḍunen n yiserdasen uɣen yakk amkan wwḍen ddaw n tsili
wwin yiserdasen yettɛassen ɣef tewwurt lekwaɣeḍ-nneɣ irkelli qellben tiquftin d tbalizin
sakin yessekcem-aɣ yiwen n userdas ɣer yiwet n tesqift yedlen s lḥila yessuter deg-neɣ ad nerǧu
bdan imeḥbas ttawḍen-d wa deffir wa s tazzla allen-nsen ttnadint ma d-ɛeqlen yiwen seg yimawlan-nsen
rrant tumert ɣef temliliyin-a azmumeg d wudmawen uḥzinen i d-yeddan yid-i tasebḥit-a
yiwet n tmeṭṭut mi twala mmi-s ileḥḥu-d ɣur-s tserreḥ-as i teɣratin
leswat n yimẓuren ččuren amkan simmal ttnernin ur cliɛen ara deg yiserdasen i zzin i tesqift
ɛebdelǧabar yusa-d gar yineggura
ibedd yasin deg umkan-is yebda yettwehhi-d s ufus-is
teṭṭef-it yemma-s gar yifassen-is tɛenneq-it sakin tenna-as   tamayt i
yakuc lḥamdu lillah i yesɣezfen deg tudert-iw akken ad k-waliɣ sdat n wallen-iw
nefren sakin yiwen n umkan neqqim ɣef yijdi allen-nneɣ irkelli zzint ɣer ɛebdelǧabar
yeḍɛef mliḥ iban-iyi-d am wakken yennerna deg lqedd
ur teḥbis ara yemma-s seg yiseqsiyen ɣef tudert-is deg umkan-a ɣef wučči i itett twehha-as-d sakin ɣef tqufet i as-d-tewwi tebda la s-tḥesseb deg lesnaf n wučči i as-d-tewwi
ma d ɛebdelǧabar yeqqim kan yettɛawad bxir i yella ulac acu i t-ixussen anagar imawlan d yimeddukkal
yeḥka-as s tewzel ɣef uneqqel-ines seg lkazirna ɣer tayeḍ seg tkamyunt ɣer tayeḍ uqbel ma t-rren daxel n yiwen n usafag aserdasan i t-yewwin srid ɣer sseḥra
ulac deg yimeslayen-is later n tuzzma n usḥissef neɣ n kra n ddɣel yenna-d kan ayen i as-iḍerrun d lebla i d-yekkan sɣur sidi
rebbi akken ad ijerreb lɛibad-is yumnen yis-s d wid yettḥuddun ɣef usɣan-ines
tirza-nneɣ ur tɛeṭṭel ara aṭas
umbaɛd mi nsellem fell-as yenna-as yasin 
ad d-nuɣal deg waggur i d-iteddun ma yebɣa rebbi
yerra-as ɛebdelǧabar 
ur seɛyu ara iman-ik a gma yasin  ur nettɣimi ara dagi i lebda
aql-aɣ bxir lḥemdu lillah lmeḥna-nneɣ qrib ad tfak
yezmer lḥal ad ɣ-serḥen deg kra n lweqt
tenna-as yemma-s s lferḥ 
ncallah a mmi  ncallah
nemfaraq sakin
yuɣal ɛebdelǧabar ɣer uqiḍun-ines s laɛqel ileḥḥu s yisuraf iẓẓayanen imal ɣer tama n ufus i yeddmen taqufet neṭṭafar-it s wallen-nneɣ almi i iɣab irkelli
nufa lkar mazal tettraǧu deg-neɣ deg uzɣal anehhar-ines yekkumec ɣef yijdi iɣum iman-is s kra n ubeḥnuq ur yekfi ara i tfekka-ines tuḍɛift
udmawen n yimẓuren nnecraḥen ilsawen-nsen ur ḥbisen ara seg umeslay
yettwakkes fell-asen lhemm i yesberken ussan-nsen
wwin yid-sen isallen yelhan s wayes ad sferḥen iɛeggalen n twaculin-nsen i yettraǧun tuɣalin-nsen s lxuf uggaden ad d-uɣalen ɣur-sen s yir lexbar
tuɣalin wezzilet ɣef rrwaḥ ur neɛyi ara mliḥ
nuɣal ɣer tmersit n temdint sakin neṭṭef lkar n yiḍ i yettawin ɣer
lezzayer tamanaɣt
ɛyiɣ mliḥ bɣiɣ ad ṭṭseɣ
ǧǧiɣ yasin yettawi yettara deg umeslay d tin ara yuɣalen d taḍeggalt-is ma d nekk tewwi-yi tnafa
serseɣ tazmamt n nabil
d wigi d isebtar ineggura yuran
yefka-yi-d uɣmis aṭas n yisallen ɣef nabil ɣef tikta-ines d yimeddukkal-is maca ulac acu i ɣ-d-yenna ɣef tegnatin d usatel n tmenɣiwt-ines
ddmeɣ tazmamt-nni i tikkelt niḍen ḥekkreɣ mliḥ deg yisebtar yettucergen
anwa i ten-icerrgen  cergen-ten acku ččuren s yisallen ur ilaq ara ad ten-nẓer  neɣ akken ad ten-sxedmen deg temsal niḍen ur sɛin ara assaɣ d usentel-a  amek ara ẓreɣ  ad mmeslayeɣ d racid ahat yufa-ten gar leḥwal n mmi-s
ɣlint-d twuɣa ɣef ɛin-el-kerma d tirni
ad s-tiniḍ msefhament d yiwen n cciṭan ad kksen ɣef wudmawen n wid ssneɣ tumert d lferḥ
ula d nekk kecmeɣ deg yiwet n tbuciḍant n uxemmem tugi ad iyi-teǧǧ ula yiwet n tegnit tameẓyant n usirem
tizlellit tamezwarut i d-yeɣlin fell-aneɣ ɛlaɣila d tin i yuɣen tameṭṭut n umeddakkel-iw racid
mi d-wwḍeɣ ɣef tesɛa d nnefs n ssbeḥ ufiɣ-t yettraǧu deg-i deg tnarit-inu
taneflust-inu tessen-it yernu weṣṣaɣ-tt yakan ad teǧǧ imidawen-inu gar-asen racid ad ganin deg usalun ameẓyan yellan daxel n tnarit-inu
d attagen s uglim d iqehwiyen zzin-d ɣef yiwet n ṭṭabla taddayt rsen fell-as kra n yiɣmisen d tesɣunin  ɣef uɣrab tella yiwet n temkerḍit tamecṭuḥt deg-s kra n yidlisen n usaḍuf n tsekla d umezruy
tirza n racid ttilint s umata timeddiyin acku d tirza n umeddakkel ur sɛint ara assaɣ maḍi d uxeddim
keffuɣ ccɣel-iw s temɣawla tserriḥeɣ i yimectariyen-inu ttarraɣ ikaramen deg ṭṭerf ad nekcem deg kra n yiskasiyen ur nesɛi taggara sakin ad neffeɣ ɣer lqehwa neɣ ad nruḥ ad nḥewwes s ṭumubil armi newweḍ ɣer ubrid n yillel
faqeɣ liḥala-ines ur tessefraḥ ara
d ameddakkel-iw ẓriɣ melmi yennecraḥ yefreḥ melmi yeḥzen yekkufer qrib ad yeṭṭerḍeq
ur t-seqsaɣ ara
sreḥbeɣ kan yis-s meslayeɣ-as ɣef yisallen ineggura i ɣriɣ deg yisebtar imezwura n yiɣmisen i d-yewwin irkelli ɣef uṭerḍeq n ṭumubil yendin ɣer tewwurt n umraḥ n lkazirna deg temnaḍt n laxdariya
maca ur yebdi ara am wakken ixeddem zik rregmat deg yirebraben ineslemẓra i yellan deffir n uhuddu n tmurt d usenger n yiɣermanen imeɣban ulamma d imsulta neɣ d iserdasen
ma ijiniralen yellan deffir n twaɣit-a ttidiren deg tɣermin ulac win ad ten-yawḍen
ayen i yi-yeswehmen deg-s yebda ameslay s usuter n usuref ɣef tirza-a i d-yusan ɛlaɣila
tigi mačči d leɛwayed-is
imir-n kan faqeɣ teɣli-d fell-as tawaɣit
nniɣ 
urɛad swiɣ lqehwa-inu
kker ad nruḥ ɣer si rabeḥ ablidi ad aɣ-yeẓẓem snat n leqhawi ad aɣ-yeldin allen-nneɣ wa ad safgent fell-aneɣ nadam
yewwi-k-id rebbi deg lweqt
ɣur-i yiwen n wugur yessafeg fell-i iḍes bɣiɣ ad ak-t-id-mmleɣ limmer ad iyi-twelheḍ ɣer yiwet n tifrat 
deg lqehwa urɛad neqqim isuɣ bab n lqehwa bu yiwen n uɛebbuḍ akkenni i ibedden deffir n ukuntwar-ines n usɣar yeferfec irkelli ɣef uxeddam-ines  ay aqcic wali d acu ad swen  el-asatida -nni ɣiwel
yewwi-aɣ-d uxeddem-nni sin n yifenǧalen n lqehwa

ldiɣ aɣmis allen n umeddakkel-iw ttbinent ɛyant nniɣ 
d acu bɣan tura wigi  bennun ddula tineslemt ɣef tfekwin n lmeggtin d yimeṭṭawen n tuǧǧal d yigujilen 
imuqel-iyi-d racid yenna-yi-d s yiwet n taɣect
nettaki-d yal ass ɣef yisallen n tmenɣiwin asṭerḍeq iqudaḥ ahuddu yuysen 
d acu ad nerǧu seg yiderwicen-a  nefɛen kan i uɣizi n yiẓekwan d leqraya n leqran-nsen ɣef lmeggtin
bennun anazir-nsen dagi akken ad qenɛen imdanen s lfayda n lǧennet-nsen dihin
d acu lfayda n umeslay tura  tterka nnig n yiqerra-nneɣ taburdit ddaw n yiḍarren-nneɣ
am wakken iyi-tenniḍ deg kra n wussan  uḥricen ḍebbren lfiza smenɛen iqerra-nsen rewlen ɣer yuruba d marikan
ma d nekkni
yessusem yessider i uqerruy-is
ur inul ara afenǧal-ines n lqehwa
muqleɣ-t kra n lweqt
ziɣ ameddakkel-iw yuɣal d amɣar
iban-iyi-d am wakken yennerna uferḍes-ines yečča amur ameqqran n uqerruy-is
udem-is yenjer-it ukmac tezzi-as tzegzewt i wallen-is
tettbiniḍ-iyi mačči bxir i telliḍ tasebḥit-a
ad as-tiniḍ d aseqsi-inu i yettraǧu akken ad yessuffeɣ lqerḥ yellan deg wul-is
tameṭṭut-iw attan gar tudert d tmettant deg ssbiṭar
skecmeɣ-tt iḍelli
qqimeɣ din almi d tnasfa n yiḍ maca ur d-tuki ara
amek i yeḍra waya  tikkelt taneggarut i tt-walaɣ deg-s tban-iyi-d ulac acu tt-yuɣen
sufella kan
lliɣ ttraǧuɣ ad teɣli tazmert-is wa ad taweḍ ɣer liḥala-a
seg wasmi yemmut nabil tuɣal ur tett ara
ad as-tiniḍ tuqem asunded ɣef wučči
acḥal d abrid i tt-nebbheɣ belli tafekka-ines tuɣal d aglim ɣef yiɣessan
maca tetthuzzu kan tuyat-is ur iyi-d-teqqar acemma
teggugem tuɣal ur tettmeslay ara
ulac taɣawsa i tt-icudden ɣer tudert
ad as-tiniḍ tebɣa ad tenɣ iman-is
ur ttɛawad ara imeslayen-a a racid
tameṭṭut-ik d lmumen teẓra tinɣiman deg usɣan d leḥram
ur cukkeɣ ara tettara deg uqerruy-is timsal yecban ta
tamettant n mmi-s ayiwan d ddeq qessiḥen yewɛer ɣef umdan ad as-yesber
ula d yemma temmut kra n yiseggasen umbaɛd n tmenɣiwt n gma lmilud
urǧin teḥbes imeṭṭawen fell-as ulac tagnit ideg ur t-id-tbedder ara
ula d nekk xedmeɣ ayen iwumi zemreɣ yernu tuɣ-iyi meẓẓeyeɣ deg tallit-nni akken ad tettu leḥzen-ines ad tettu ciṭuḥ seg ubdar n gma wa ad tidir am nettat am yimdanen niḍen
yemma terfa mliḥ ɣef wid yenɣan mmi-s
tdeɛɛu-asen s unazir tessutur deg sidi rebbi d lewliya ad as-rren ttar ulamma deg laxert
zgiɣ qqareɣ-as mačči ḥala nettat iwumi yemmut mmi-s d ilemẓi
akka i tga ddunit tamettant tezga tella gar yimdanen
maca tettara-yi-d s wurfan  
lmilud ur yemmut ara s lmut n rebbi
lmilud nɣan-t
ur sen-ttsamaḥeɣ ara la deg ddunit wala deg laxert
amer d aṭṭan i t-yenɣan tili qebleɣ s tikci n rebbi maca d timenɣiwt i t-nɣan ad ten-iḥaseb rebbi fell-as wa ad ten-yesserɣ deg lqaɛ n unazir am wakken serɣen ul-iw 
ul-is uḍɛif ur yessaweḍ ara ad yesteḥmel dɣa yeǧǧa-tt uqbel ad tessiweḍ ad temḍel leḥzen-ines
yernu ur tettu ara tameṭṭut-ik tuḍen s ukunsir ahat d aṭṭan-a i tt-yessawḍen ɣer liḥala-a
ahatḥkiɣ-as i umejjay kulci
yenna-yi-d ayen yezwaren tura d asuffeɣ-ines seg ssriɛ
sakin ad nwali aṭṭan-ines n lkunsir
deg sin n wussan ineggura walaɣ-tt tcudd aqerruy-is s umendil mi t-seqsaɣ tenna-yi-d d aqraḥ kan n uqerru mačči d lḥaǧa
nniɣ-as ad kem-awiɣ ɣer umejjay terra-yi-d dayen tekreh isufar d sbiṭarat
uɣaleɣ ur as-heddreɣ ara aṭas
yeqqur uqerruy-is tettarra kulci ɣer wul-is ur iyi-tettarra ara ula d awal
iḍelli tasebḥit ffɣeɣ ɣer ssuq ad d-qḍuɣ ayen i ixussen i uxxam mi d-uɣaleɣ ufiɣ-tt teɣli ɣef lqaɛa n tnawalt tesreɛ
rucceɣ-tt s ciṭuḥ n waman limmer ad d-taki
mebla lfayda
ssawleɣ i yisexsayen nnan-iyi-d takerrust-nsen teffeɣ ad d-tawi imejraḥ n yiwen n ubaxix yeḍran deg ubrid yettawin ɣer yillel
regmeɣ-ten nitni d tkerrust-nsen
siwleɣ i lǧar-iw ad iyi-iɛiwen
s tmara tameqqrant i nessaweḍ ad tt-nawi ɣer ssbiṭar
yenna-yi-d umejjay  d ssker i as-yeɣlin ɣef waya i tesreɛ
fehmeɣ seg kra n lehdur iyi-d-yenna belli liḥala-ines ur tessefraḥ ara
kker tura ad nruḥ ɣer sbiṭar ahat tuki-d tura
nufa tameṭṭut n racid teṭṭes ɣef yiwen n umeṭreḥ deg texxamt n usaki taqerɛunt n usirum tettwaɛelleq ɣer tama tayeffust rran ɣef wudem-is yiwen n wallal yettarran nnefs
beddeɣ akked racid sdat n ṭṭaq n zzǧaǧ i aɣ-iferqen nettwali deg-s s wallen n leḥzen ulac acu nezmer ad as-nexdem
tekcem yiwet n tfermlit tbedd sdat-s kra n lweqt tessefqed allalen-nni teqɛed tduli-ines teffeɣ sakin seg yiwet n tewwurt tameẓyant
neqqim deg umkan-nneɣ d isusamen ɛerqent-aɣ irkelli ur neẓri ara ma neqqim din neɣ ad neffeɣ ad neǧǧ amkan acku nella din neɣ ur nelli ara ulac acu ara ibeddlen deg liḥala-ines
tisin n snat seg temdukkal-is ssuffɣent-aɣ seg lmerta-a
tehder yiwet deg-sent d racid
jebdeɣ iman-iw nniɣ-as 
ad k-rǧuɣ deg ṭumubil
deg tilawt bɣiɣ ad ffɣeɣ s temɣawla seg ssbiṭar-a
lerwayeḥ n yisufar qessiḥen i yemmɣen ɣef umkan iɣraben-is yettusebɣen s yini azegzaw ḍuren-iyi xenqen-iyi
ɣawleɣ tikli ffɣeɣ ɣer tebḥirt n sbiṭar ad cummeɣ azwu azedgan ad d-rreɣ nnehta ad tɣileḍ ddaw n waman neɣ daxel n texxamt yeččuren s wabbu i lliɣ
ẓriɣ d yiwet n liḥala tanefsit i yi-yeṭṭafaren seg wasmi meẓẓeyeɣ ulac acu xedmeɣ akken ad thenniɣ seg-s
nnernan urnan-inu mi suggneɣ iman-iw d amuḍin ẓẓleɣ ɣef yiwen n umeṭreḥ deg yiwet n texxamt seg texxamin tuḥzinin
iban ad mmteɣ deg yiḍ amezwaru
tezga yemma teqqar-aɣ-d mi ara d-tebder tamettant   win i iḥemmel sidi rebbi yettawi-t deg yiḍes 
ula nettat tewweḍ laɛfu n rebbi deg tnafa-ines
deg yiḍ-nni sliɣ i yiwen n ccxir yessewhem-iyi kra maca ur faqeɣ ara d acu-t
qqimeɣ ttḥessiseɣ s laɛqel armi sliɣ i yemma tettcehhid s yiwet n taɣect d tafessast
kkreɣ s lxelɛa maca ufiɣ tezwar-iyi tmettant tewwi-tt
hucceɣ-tt s zzur suɣeɣ
tuɣal d tafekka taqqurant
qqimeɣ ɣef lqaɛa serḥeɣ-as i yimeṭṭi
ttruɣ ɣef baba d yemma ttruɣ ɣef tgujelt-inu yernu mazal-iyi d ameẓyan
kkreɣ qemmceɣ-as allen-is
rǧiɣ ladan n lefjer xebbreɣ lǧiran i tt-imeḍlen
mi ḥkiɣ taqsiḍt-inu i yirgazen n udcir nnan-iyi-d yezmer d ul-is i iḥebsen
temmut yemma tameɣbunt s uneḥbus n wul
kra n ddqayeq kan tessuffeɣ tarwiḥt
ssarameɣ ad mmteɣ am wakken temmut yemma taɛzizt akken ur ttneɛtabeɣ ara am tmeɣbunt-a yeṭṭsen tura deg texxamt n usaki
qrib ukkuẓ n yiseggasen aya nettat d tazzla seg ssbiṭar ɣer wayeḍ
tenneɛtab tesseɛya yid-s argaz-is
maca anwa i izemren ad yefren amek d melmi ad yemmet  ulac win yeẓran anta tamurt ideg ara yaweḍ laɛfu n rebbi
ussan-a tamettant tettezzi-d nnig n yiqerra-nneɣ
anta tamettant i yifen tayeḍ  s tersast deg wul ad ak-yawin ɣer umaḍal niḍen deg kra n tsinin neɣ s tɣimit deg yiwet n texxamt deg yiwen n sbiṭar uḥzin ideg tettganiḍ tisin n tmettant dɣa ad tebdu tettnefcic fell-ak wa ad tettmesxer fell-ak  ad tessutreḍ deg-s ssbeḥ tameddit ad d-tas ad ak-tawi yernu ɣas akken ur ak-d-tettara ara awal
dɣa ad d-tafeḍ iman-ik terra-k tmara ad tesxedmeḍ allalen niḍen ad ak-ɛiwnen am uneḥbus ɣef wučči ara yesseɛyun tafekka i yeckunṭḍen ɣer tudert n i yeǧǧan tuggdi seg waṭṭan yessekrafen lebda
d ad yerr talast i tudert-is s tinɣiman s yiwet n tersast  d tabɣest neɣ d tudayt  d tasḍa neɣ d lexdeɛ i tudert i t-imagren s inzikmiren  anwa ad iyi-yemmlen tiririt  d acu ara xedmeɣ ma ur tessaweḍ ara tfekka-inu ad texdem akken ilaq  ad ḍefreɣ abrid i yuɣ
 neɣ ad serseɣ ifassen-iw ad uɣaleɣ d alelluc gar yifassen n yimejjayen ara iyi-sxedmen deg temsirin-nsen  tafekka-inu iṭij anezwi yeḥma maca
yessaki-yi-d racid seg tikta-inu tuḥzinin s ubeddi-ines sdat n tewwurt n ṭumubil yenna 
tanemmirt-ik d tameqqrant a si ɛebdelqader nekk ad qqimeɣ dagi uɣal ɣer tnarit-inek ẓriɣ aṭas n lecɣal i k-yettganin ad ak-in-siwleɣ tameddit-a
ar tufat
ur yerǧi ara tiririt-inu
yeṭṭef abrid n tebḥirt n sbiṭar i iqublen asbad n ṭumubilat
deg tilawt ur ufiɣ ara acu ad as-iniɣ
ula d nekk yenṭeḍ-iyi leḥzen
tban-iyi-d tudert d tamessast ur tesɛi ara lbenna ulamma ass-nni yelha lḥal d teqqim d tasemmaḍt
ssiɣeɣ amseddu ṭumubil tebda ambiwel ɣer tewwurt n umraḥ akken ad teffeɣ racid seg tama-s ihegga iman-is ad yeqqim ɣef yiwen n ukersi ddaw n yiṭij deg tebḥirt n sbiṭar
ffɣeɣ seg ssbiṭar deg ubrid bdiɣ suguneɣ iman-iw ẓẓleɣ ɣef tsili n temẓi-inu ddaw n yiṭij aḥmayan ṭṭafareɣ s wallen-iw affug n uẓerẓur selleɣ i učewčew i yuɣen yal amkan
ctaqeɣ i taddart-iw anda i yi-gezmen timiḍt nniɣ ilaq ad tt-ẓureɣ yiwen n wass deg wussan i d-iteddun
uɣaleɣ ɣer tnarit ɣriɣ kra n yikamaren mmugreɣ-d kra seg wid i yi-wekklen ad ten-ḥuddeɣ
maca ugur n
yusef ɛeyyaci d wayen sliɣ sɣur ɛebdelḥamid ɣef teqsiḍt n umsaltu fateḥ ben slama d umidaw-ines d gma-s aḥeddad ur nban ara yuɣal-d ɣer tidmi-w ur iyi-ǧǧin ara ad kemmleɣ axeddim-iw
tifrat ad waliɣ si aḥmed akumisar n temsulta
ẓriɣ ad d-afeɣ ɣur-s kra n yisumar yelhan
ufiɣ-t ibedd d yiwen seg yimidawen-ines tama n i d-usiɣ ddruj n tewwurt n uxxam n temsulta
yenna-d s uqesser s taɣect-ines tazurant 
lliɣ ttnadiɣ ɣef yiwen ara i yi-xelsen imekli yewwi-k-id rebbi deg lweqt
ihi ad nruḥ ɣer si
ɣef waya
ɛebdelḥamid ajijli d acu tenniḍ deg yiwet n ddubbara taqerḥant 
ddqiqa kan ad n-uɣaleɣ
yekcem s temɣawla ɣer uxxam n temsulta
uɣaleɣ ɣer ṭumubil-inu qqimeɣ ttraǧuɣ
kra n ddqayeq kan hata yuɣal-d iḍegger iman-is ɣef ukursi tama-w 
ɣiwel ḥerrek iman-ik laẓ igezzem iẓerman-iw
yesla mliḥ i teqsiḍt-iw yeskef tajɣimt n lqehwa yenna-yi-d 
tefreḍ fell-i yakk isallen-a imihawen a si ɛebdelqader
ɛerqent-iyi irkelli nniɣ-as ad xemmemeɣ ciṭuḥ uqbel ma xedmeɣ kra
tamsalt n tkerḍa n yixxamen tessewhem-aɣ mliḥ
deg tazwara aṭas n ccikayat i aɣ-d-yewwḍen sɣur n yiɣermanen nnan-aɣ ttwakren yixxamen-nsen mi llan d inabayen
nexdem tisestanin ilaqen
nerna lɛessa deg yiḍ
maca ɣas akken ur newwiḍ ara ɣer yiswan-nneɣ
tikerḍiwin-a ḥebsent umbaɛd weḥd-sent qrib i neɣleq akaram
kečč teẓriḍ takerḍa tuɣal ɣer temsulta d tamsalt ur nesɛi ara azal ameqqran sdat n rebrab
d acu d azal n tkerḍa sdat n tmenɣiwin aserɣu d uhuddu  qrib i nettu tamsalt amer ur aɣ-d-yessawel ara yiwen n umdan s tilifun yenna-aɣ ɛebdelkrim buɛebdellah aḥeddad tḥanut mi nekcem nufa din yesnuzu isɣunen yettwakren
nruḥ ɣer tḥanut nufa-tt teɣleq
nḥewwes nqelleb fell-as deg uxxam n yimawlan-is ur t-nufi ara
nufa iman-nneɣ nettuḥettem ad nerreẓ tawwurt n isɣunen yettwakren neɣ ayen i d-yegran
newwi-d imawlan-nsen iban-d anwa i ten-yukren
nqelleb mliḥ fell-as ulac amkan i neǧǧa acku d netta i d amnir ayiwan i izemren ad aɣ-yessiwḍen ɣer yimeddukkal-is
yenna-yi-d yiwen seg yimsulta mi iwala imawlan-is nnan-as-d usan-d irgazen s yiselsa n yimsulta ẓeḍmen ɣef uxxam-nsen deg yiḍ wwin mmi-tsen ur ẓrin sani
iban ur numin ara ayen i aɣ-d-nnan
nenna-as d tiyita kan i bɣan ad wwten deg-neɣ
neɣ ma ulac nenna-as yezmer d imeddukkal-is i iheddren akka akken ur netcukku ara deg-s neɣ ahat d imeddukkal-is imakaren i t-yenɣan imi ur msefhamen ara ɣef uglaf
nekkni seg tama-nneɣ nɣil yuli s adrar yedda d trebbuyaɛ timeselḥin
asmi d-nufa tafekka-ines neɣleq akaram
ula d anɣa yeqqim mebla tifrat ur neẓri amek i teḍra neɣ anwa yellan deffir-s
a si aḥmed temmeslay-d tɣamsa deg wagguren-a ineggura ɣef tkerḍa n yimdanen sɣur yirgazen s yiselsa unsiben n temsulta neɣ n temsetla
ẓriɣ ur tettuḍ ara aql-aɣ ddaw n usaḍuf n ṭṭrad d ugdal n usikel yernu imeẓla n tɣellist deg tuffra i xeddmen tikkwal ttafen-d ifukal i tigawin-nsen yeffɣen abrid n lqanun s ṭṭrad i tettidir tmurt
ur cukkeɣ ara truḥ-ak temsalt-a  icenfiren-is yeskef sakin tajɣimt niḍen n lqehwa-ines
temsulta aqerruy-is
ihuzz ukumisar n ikerrec
kečč d amastan teẓriḍ axir-iw amek leḥḥun yimeẓla n tɣellist
nekk dagi ssefrakeɣ kan yiwen n uxxam n temsulta i yettḥebbiren ɣef laman n yiɣermanen nxeddem iwumi nezmer akken ad ten-nḥudd seg lbaṭel d uqhar
asaḍuf amedya yegdel fell-aɣ anadi n uxxam mebla ttesriḥ sɣur n uwkil n tegduda
ur nezmir ara daɣen ad neḥbes albaɛḍ mebla tasunḍa sɣur uxxam n teɣdemt ḥala ma nwala-t yexdem tigawt yeffɣen abrid n lqanun
imeẓla n tɣellist mačči d tirebbuyaɛ yeffɣen i lqanun
seg tuɣḍaḍin timendawin-nsen aseḥbiber d uqader n yisuḍaf ur ttarran ara ɣef wanɣa s wanɣa niḍen
d acu lferq yellan ihi gar-asen d trebbuyaɛ n yineḍliben  akka i fehmeɣ tawuri n umsaltu akka i xeddmeɣ axeddim-iw iwakken ur yettili ara umgared gar-as d swayes umneɣ
ma d tamsalt-a n usaḍuf n ṭṭrad d lɛesker yellan d aɣella n tidet
lɛesker ibedd ɣef wumi nessawal zik s tɣellist taserdasant beddlen-as tura isem akken ad yuɣal d tanmehla n umlan d tɣellist
ameẓlu-a d ilelli ɣef temsulta ixeddem ddaw n tmurt ula d taɣdemt ur tesɛi ara azref fell-as
ɣef waya aql-iyi am keččini ur ẓriɣ ara acu yellan daxel n tsenduqt-a taberkant neɣ d acu i txeddem neɣ d acu i tenwa ad texdem i tmurt ma d lxir neɣ d ccer
d nitni i yeṭṭfen rray ad xedmen tifranin sakin walan ilaq ad tent-ḥebsent
d nitni i yesṭaxren aselway wwin-d aselway amaynut suffɣen-d asaḍuf n ṭṭrad d ugdal n usikel
aql-iyi am keččini amen-iyi qqareɣ iɣmisen seqsayeɣ iman-iw ma yella ayen qqareɣ d tidet neɣ d tikerkas
seqsayeɣ daɣen iman-iw ɣef yiɣbula i sen-yettakken isallen-a yessewḥacen
yuzzel wawal d akken aṭas n yineɣmasen xeddmen d yimeẓla n umlan
ur neẓri ara anwa i yessexdamen wayeḍ  ineɣmasen xeddmen akka akken ad senzen iɣmisen-nsen wa ad jemɛen idrimen deg lbankat  ma d imeẓla n umlan iswi-nsen  d asuffeɣ ɣer tmetti i tikta i sen-yehwan 
d ṭṭrad n yisallen d umlan ulac deg-s maḍi imenzayen alsawen kulci yebna ɣef tkerkas d yisallen mebla lsas
ayɣer ayen i iḍerrun ɣur-neɣ d ṭṭrad n yisallen kan neɣ d ṭṭrad iwumi nugi ad nsemmi wa ad nini d acu-t 
ḍerrunt tedyanin yessewḥacen deg yal temnaḍt n tmurt u kečč ɣas akken d akumisar n temsulta ulac acu teẓriḍ am kečč am yiɣermanen niḍen 
d tagi d tilawt a si ɛebdelqader nuɣal am  seksu ddaw n texsayt 
ɛerqent-aɣ irkelli armi nuɣal ur nxeddem ara lferq gar wakraren d wuccanen
d akraren irkelli d uccanen tidet uyseɣ dayen
ttxemmimeɣ ad awiɣ tastaɣt-inu ad ɛezleɣ iman-iw seg lmusayeb d twuɣa i aɣ-yessefqaɛen yal tasebḥit u trennu-aɣ lhemm
d wagi i nessaram irkelli
maca anda ad naf amdan-agi n telwit anda nezmer ad nesɛeddi ussan-nneɣ ineggura deg lehna 
ayen i d-teqqareḍ d tidet
tawacult-iw tesɛa akal deg yidurar n blida mačči d aṭas maca iwulem i tastaɣt n wid yellan am nekk
maca tirebbuyaɛ tinselmin timselḥin irkelli
ad ak-d-iniɣ bdant ttaɣent amkan din ḥekkment nehhrent deg yimezdaɣen-is ttekksent-asen ula d ayla-nsen
kra n twaculin bdant rewwlent uggadent ad ɣlint tullas-nsent gar yifassen n trebbuyaɛ-agi i tent-yettawin d teklatin
ma d wid i yugin ad ǧǧen akal-nsen refden leslaḥ akken ad ḥudden ɣef wayla-nsen
u gma d yiwen seg-sen
tettwaliḍ deg-i ad uɣaleɣ yiwen n wass ɣer din  am win irewlen seg lḥebs yeɣli ɣer tewwurt-is
maca ad farṣeɣ tagnit tamezwarut akken ad ẓureɣ amadaɣ n temẓi-w
acḥal i cedhaɣ lerwayeḥ n tẓegwa d umeslay d yimawlan-is
yessusem si aḥmed yerra-d nnehta
neḥma deg wawal nbeddel asentel dɣa yerwel seg lhem iɣef d-usiɣ
seqsaɣ iman-iw ma yella si aḥmed yeqqar-d tidet mi iyi-d-yenna ur yeẓri ara acu i iḍerrun neɣ d tarrayt i yessexdem akken ad yerwel ɣef yiseqsiyen iɣef yewɛer ad yefk tiririt ma ulac ad yaf iman-is yessuffuɣ uffiren n twuri-ines ara yessamsen isem n tuddsa ideg ixeddem
uɣaleɣ ɣer usentel seg teɣmert niḍen
i umsaltu fateḥ benslama d mmi-s n ɛayn-el-kerma d yiwen seg yimezdaɣ n udcir n  brarik  yernu d ameddakkel n uḥeddad ur nezmir ara ad t-nwali akken ad nissin tidet 
yezmer lḥal maca anwa-t wagi i izemren ad t-yerdun 
nekk ur sɛiɣ acu ara k-xedmeɣ
ur ttraǧu ara deg-i ad refdeɣ ula d yiwen n uḍaḍ neɣ ad neṭqeɣ ula s yiwen n wawal ɣef usentel-a
tamezwarut amsaltu-agi i d-tbedreḍ ur yelli ara deg umeẓlu-inu
wwḍen-iyi-d kra seg yisallen-is s ugacur
ittekka deg trebbuyaɛ yettuxessen deg unekcum arurdan i usefreq n temsbaniyin ameẓlu-a d amunan fell-aɣ
ayen ẓriɣ fell-as wwin-t akked yiwen seg yimidawen-ines seg ɛayn-el-kerma ɣef yir tikli-nsen
nnuɣen sin n yirgazen-a daxel n lkazirna yernu amer ur skecmen ara imidawen niḍen iman-nsen tili yeḍra ubaxix
d yiwen seg yimeddukkal-is i yi-d-yewwin taqsiḍt-a fell-as ula d netta d mmi-s n temdint-a d amaswaḍ yid-i i ixeddem yessuter deg-i ad iliɣ d amnay n lxir gar-as d unemhal n lkazirna akken ur t-ttawin ara s amkan niḍen
ɣef umennuɣ yufa-d ifukal s liḥala iwaɛren ideg yettidir  yir tanezduɣt baba-s d amuḍin berru n tmeṭṭut-is umbaɛd kra n wagguren n zzwaǧ-ines  maca uzzlen wussan ulac acu i as-xedmeɣ
amennuɣ-nni d urfiq-is ahat ɣef uglaf n tkerḍa 
ahat maca amek ad nẓer  yaxi nniɣ-ak-d deg tazwara amsaltu-nni wis sin i nɣan deg ssuq n  miksik  d acrik-is deg tkerḍa
ula d anɣa-a yeqqim mebla tifrat
sefḍen-t irkelli deg rrebrab
ahat d yiwen seg trebbuyaɛ tinselmin i t-iɛussen sakin yenɣa-t akken ad as-yaker tameẓyant-ines
tagi d taqdimt sxedmen-tt yimjuhad imezwura asmi bdan neqqen deg yimsulta d yimestal ifransiyen akken ad asen-kksen leslaḥ-nsen
lemden warraw-nneɣ tamsirt seg deg unmenɣi n temdint n lezzayer
i umsaltu wis kraḍ  ahat d netta i yennuɣen d fateḥ
benslama  tarrayt
ḥala rebbi i yeẓran
ahat d amsaltu-nni i nɣan 
tamsalt teḥwaǧ tasestant
tidyanin-a irkelli ḍrant deg kra n wussan mqaraben mliḥ
tamsalt-a teshel maḍi
yezmer ad tt-nwali deg wannar
ih maca tɣileḍ sin n yimdanen-a ɣas nnuɣen armi qrib i wwḍen ɣer tmenɣiwt ad qqiren s uffir-nsen  isɣunen yettwakren nufa-ten ɣer uḥeddad tafekka-ines nufa-tt tentuter ɣef yiri n ubrid
ḥala netta i yellan d inigi ulac wayeḍ
yella yinigi niḍen ɛebdelḥamid gma-s n uḥeddad
tebɣiḍ ad d-tawiḍ arebrab ad yeched mgal yiwen n umsaltu 
afukel-a i yi-d-yefka yesgugem-iyi
ur ufiɣ ara acu ad as-iniɣ akken ad ḥuddeɣ ɣef tikti-inu
deg tilawt mačči d tamsalt n umsaltu amakar i iceɣben lbal-iw
yewwi-aɣ umeslay ɣer kra n temsal ɛeddant tidmiwin-nneɣ
deg i yi-teqsiḍt-inu yeɛnan nekkini s timmad-iw  ambiwel-inu deg yiḍ ɣer yiwen n umkan ideg teffer tarbaɛt n ɛebdelǧabar
d tuggdi d lemḥadra  ur ẓriɣ ara d tamsalt tewɛer mliḥ ur bɣiɣ ara ad sweqɛeɣ iman-iw seg tazwara
nniɣ-as d yusef ɛeyyaci d ɛebdelḥammid buɛebdellah i d-yusan ɣur-i yiwet n tikkelt kan s axxam deg yiḍ
teɣli-d yiwet n tsusmi d taẓayant gar-aneɣ
qqimeɣ kan sekkfeɣ deg lqehwa-inu
d acu i tettwaliḍ a si aḥmed d acu ara s-iniɣ i uneɣmas amerwal ma iruḥ-d ɣur-i tikkelt niḍen  ttuɣ s ddemma kra n yifutas
ad d-irandi kan i teɣdemt axir-as
qenneɛ-it s waya
win irewlen seg lḥebs ulac azref i yesɛa kulci ibedd deg udem-is
ula d nekk sliɣ am kečč yella yiwen n usaḍuf i ttheggin uwsawen ara yessurfen i yirebraben ara d-isubben seg udrar ad randin i yiɣallen n laman
ad seqsiɣ ɣef temsalt-a akken ad sɛuɣ ugar n yisallen
nwiɣ ad as-mmeslayeɣ ɣef wayen d-yegran seg lexyuḍ n teqsiḍt-inu
imeslayen imezwura ulɣen ɣef yiles-iw maca ɣas akken ulac acu xedmeɣ susmeɣ
tella yiwet n taɣect i d-yeffɣen seg daxel-iw tbedd deg wudem-iw
ayɣer ad ḍeggreɣ iman-iw ɣer umdun yeččuren s yizerman  i wakken ur ttqirriɣ ara s wuffir-inu beddeɣ nniɣ-as ad ruḥeɣ s abduz
mi d-uɣaleɣ ufiɣ si aḥmed ibedd yettmeslay d bab n usečču xelseɣ ayen nečča neffeɣ
uqbel n lmeɣreb uɣaleɣ ɣer ssbiṭar
ruḥeɣ srid ɣer tesga n usaki ad waliɣ sani tewweḍ liḥala n tmeṭṭut n
racid
mi wwḍeɣ ɣer tawwurt n tesga terra-yi-d yiwet n temɣart ɣer deffir d timsizdegt tella tetsiyiq agens
iɛedda wakud n tirza a si muḥemmed eǧǧ-iyi ad seyqeɣ amkan deg lɣerḍ-iw agens yezga yumes tettawim tettaram dagi issebbaḍen-nwen ččuren d aluḍ neɣ d akal u anemhal yezga yekkat deg-nteɣ belli d nekkenti ur nxeddem ara ccɣel-nteɣ
uɣaleɣ srid ɣer ṭumubil-inu
racid ulac-it
ad ruḥeɣ s axxam-is ad nadiɣ fell-as
mazal ur kcimeɣ ara ɣer tnarit-inu armi i yi-d-tmuger tneflust-inu s usali uqsiḥ 
tesliḍ s usali a 
brarḥent wallen-iw qqimeɣ ttmuquleɣ kan deg yicenfiren-is ttraǧuɣ melmi ad td-enṭeq wa ad iyi-d-tini d acu-tt twaɣit-agi tamaynut yeḍran
akumisar n temsulta nɣan-t tasebḥit-a sdat n uxxam-is
si aḥmed  d awezɣi  anwa i am-d-yennan akka 
akka i heddren akk medden tameddakkelt-iw tezdeɣ deg yiwen n uzaduɣ ur nebɛid ara ɣef win ideg yezdeɣ ukumisar
txeddem d tanawart deg umeẓlu n tebzert
tura kan i tt-id-mugreɣ deg ubrid tleḥḥu s axeddim-is
mazal ur as-yekkis ara lfeqɛa
tenna-yi-d tesla i tiyitwin n rrsas seg uxxam-is
d tikkelt tamezwarut ideg tesla i ssut n rrsas sdat-s
mi tella thedder yid-i teqqim tettwali kan ɣer tama tayeffust d tama taẓelmaḍt
tenna-yi-d d at yiččumar i t-yenɣan
nettat ulac acu twala
maca aṭas seg lǧiran-is walan irebraben seg ṭṭwiqan d yibalkuten-nsen
sɛan aččamar lsan iqendyar
win i ijebden fell-as d awezzlan deg lqedd d aberkan
tenna-yi-d temddukkelt-iw iwumi ibeddel wudem yuɣal d awraɣ tettmuqqul ɣer uyeffus d uẓelmaḍ seg tuggdi d yiwet seg tǧartin-ines i as-yennan deg wussan-agi ineggura twala aberkan-nni awezzlan yeddawar gar yizadaɣen d yiwen seg warraw n udcir
ineḍliben ddawaren sdat n tewwura-nneɣ nekkni neṭṭes ur neẓri acemma
nnɣan-t d kraḍ seg yiɣallen n laman daxel n ṭumubil ukren-asen leslaḥ rewlen
anwa ad aɣ-iḥudden imi tamsulta s timmad-is ur tezmir ara ad tḥudd ɣef yiman-is 
tamayt i yakuc lḥamdulillah imi baba d watmanten-iw ur llin ara d imsulta
deg waggur yezrin nɣan yiwen deg ssuq n  miksik  deg ddurt iɛeddan nɣan seddis deg ṭṭerf n temdint  ad yester rebbi tameddit  wigini teḍra-asen am lmektub ulac win i izemren ad ibedd deg wudem-sen neɣ ad asen-yerwel
feqɛeɣ mačči d kra yekref yiles-iw ur ssawḍeɣ ara ad d-suffɣeɣ ula d yiwen n wawal
ǧǧiɣ taneflust-inu tessuffuɣ tuggdi izedɣen ul-is kecmeɣ ɣer tnarit-inu
rriɣ deg uqerruy-iw i kra n lweqt kan tiwlifin n temlilit-nneɣ n yiḍelli
mazal ttwaliɣ si aḥmed lmendad-iw itett u yettmeslay s yiwet n taɣect tazurant
subḥanllah i yettbeddilen kulci deg yiwen n wass
iḍelli kan tuɣ-it yedder yettheggi isenfaren i yimal-ines  ass-a yuɣal d tafekka taqqurant ad yeẓẓel snat n lmitrat ddaw n wakal ad yuɣal d učči i yiwekkiwen ula d imdanen ad ččen aksum-is
serseɣ iman-iw ɣer wattag tiwlifin n yiḍelli mazal-itent ttemyeckaḍent deg wallaɣ-iw
isallen yessefqaɛen ɣellin-d fell-i d tirni
tuggdi n tneflust-inu tesɛa llsas  anwa ad aɣ-iḥudden imi temsulta s timmad-is ur tezmir ara ad tḥudd ɣef yiman-is  d wigi ihi mraw n yiseggasen n tmettant d uhuddu i aɣ-yettraǧun umbaɛd mi nesɛedda mraw n yiseggasen n  i tudert yelhan  i jeggren s lbanan d uguglu n  deg wussan yezrin kan yeɣli
nabil s tersast ur neẓri ara amek i tewweḍ ɣer tfekka-ines tuḍɛift
d tinɣiman s tidet am wakken i d-nnan yimejjayen i walan tafekka-ines  neɣ yella wuffir ur neẓri ara d acu-t 
deffir-s kan yeḍra ubaxix-nni n tkamyunt n yimeḥbas ideg ttwanɣan seddis n yimdanen
nekk s timmad-iw ufiɣ iman-iw leḥḥuɣ deg tlemmast n yiḍ zzuɣuren-iyi ɣer yifri n yimnafqen selleɣ i wayen ur yeettamen laɛqel
uɣaleɣ d taḥjurt n yiwen n uzrar n tedyanin yessewḥacen ur nettwali ḥala deg ssinima teɛna kan timura niḍen baɛdit fell-aneɣ
tura ur lliɣ ara d imferreǧ kan am wakken lliɣ zik-nni qqimeɣ ɣer deffir ttaḍsaɣ ɣef lemḥayen n wiyaḍ skerkren-iyi mebla lebɣi-inu ɣer wannar n umennuɣ amek ad tili taggara-inu
ad yester rebbi tameddit
hatta ula d nasira tesreɛ yezmer lḥal urǧin ad d-taki ad teǧǧ argaz-is weḥd-s d uḥzin ur yeẓri d acu ad yexdem mi yewweḍ ɣer tmeddit n tudert-is
ẓureɣ-t iḍelli deg uxxam-is
ufiɣ-t yeḥzen yuyes
ruḥeɣ ad t-wasiɣ s umeslay ɣef kra n yisental bɣiɣ ad ilin baɛdit ɣef leḥzen maca yewhem deg-i tikkwal yettara-yi-d s tsusmi tikkwal niḍen yettara-yi-d s kra n tenfaliyin ur qqinent ara maḍi ɣer usentel i d-wwiɣ
ziɣ ur iyi-isell ara maḍi yella ihedder kan i yiman-is d tiyita qessiḥen i yečča daxel-is
ɛlaɣila kan mebla ma bniɣ fell-as yeṭṭerḍeq d imeṭṭwen
ssut-is qrib ad yeffeɣ ɣer berra
ugar n yimeṭṭawen i igezzmen tasa-w yekcem deg yiwen n ushetref ur fhimeɣ acemma deg-s anagar ismawen n mmi-s d tmeṭṭut-is d kra n wawalen i d-yemmalen belli ddunit-is txab neɣ ahat qrib ad tekfu
d acu lfayda n wawalen deg tegnatin am tigi  srewleɣ allen-iw fell-as susmeɣ qqimeɣ tzellimeɣ deg-s seg teswiɛt ɣer tayeḍ
seḍḥaɣ deg yiman-iw ad tɣileḍ d yir tugniwin i ttwaliɣ
am win yettwalin albaɛḍ ɛeryan
tuɣ-it ɛeryan d uḍɛif
lewsayef-agi ur ten-tettwaliḍ ara dima deg yirgazen
dayen yeɣli ulac acu i d-yeqqimen deg-s yessers ifassen-is ur yezmir ara ad ibedd mgal uḥemmal n yifrayen i t-yeẓẓmen i t-iqerḥen seg daxel seg wasmi yemmut mmi-s
tilin-inu thewwej-iyi mliḥ ulac lfayda deg-s d amuqel kan i t-ttmuquleɣ
ula d nekk bɣiɣ ad ruɣ ad as-tiniḍ d anṭaḍ n ubeḥri
qemceɣ allen-iw iwakken ur iyi-ɣellin ara yimeṭṭawen kkreɣ deg umkan-iw ruḥeɣ ɣer tzeqqa n usired sardeɣ udem-iw acḥal d abrid s waman isemmaḍen
uɣaleɣ ɣer usalun
ufiɣ racid mazal yessader i uqerruy-is yeṭṭef aqerruy-is d wudem-is deg yifassen-is yettru kan
qqimeɣ s ibeddi ttmuquleɣ deg-s s tmuɣli tuḥzint
xemmemeɣ ad as-iniɣ ad yeḥbes imeṭṭawen wa ad yekker ad yessired udem-is s waman isemmaḍen am wakken xeddmeɣ
ahat ad yerked wa ad d-yuɣal ɣer laɛqel-is
maca d tikti kan
ur ssawḍeɣ ara ad d-ssuffɣeɣ ula d yiwen n wawal
sakin mebla ma sellmeɣ fell-as lḥiɣ ɣer tewwurt ffɣeɣ seg uxxam-is deg wallaɣ-iw imelyunen n twilifin d tenfaliyin
deg yiḍ yezrin ur ṭṭiseɣ ara mliḥ
ɛawaz qqimeɣ ttneqlabeɣ kan deg wusu rnu-as tirga tiberkanin ideg mlalen yakk wudmawen-nni uḥzinen ula d udem n yemma tameɣbunt yella gar-asen
imir-n urɛad ẓriɣ belli ussan i d-teddun heggan-iyi-d tawaɣit iɣelben tiwuɣa yezrin fell-i
refdeɣ aqerruy-iw ɣer tneflust
tbedd luhi n lmitra ɣef wattagen ɣef yiɣallen-is aɛemmur n tewriqin
ɣur-k ass-a yiwet n tbeddi deg uxxam n teɣdemt
muqleɣ ɣur-s snemmreɣ-tt ssutreɣ deg-s sakin ad tessers akaram-nni ɣef tnarit
walaɣ ssaɛa yettuɛelqen deg lḥiḍ
tesɛa u rrbeɛ
ttuɣ irkelli azemz n tbeddi n ddurt n teɣdemt n uswir amezwaru
ddmeɣ akaram walaɣ kra n warraten  amgared yellan gar bab n yiwen n uxxam d aqdim d yiwen n ukerray i yugin ad as-ixelles lekra acku aṭas i yesref fell-as mi yekker ad t-iseggem
dɣa iwekkel-iyi bab n uxxam akken ad as-d-awiɣ izerfan-is
lethaɣ s wuguren i yi-yeḍran ttuɣ ad ɣreɣ akken iwata akaram-a
ad ssutreɣ awexxer
mačči d tamsalt iḥaren
nezmer daɣen ad d-naf amtawi mebla ma nɛedda ɣef unezzarfu
walaɣ imidawen-inu imastanen deg umraḥ n uxxam n teɣdemt llan deg kraḍ yid-sen ttqessiren s laɛqel kan udmawen-nsen ḥeznen
faqeɣ yewweḍ-iten usali n tmenɣiwt n ukumisar d yimɛiwnen-ines
ula d nekk ḥezneɣ maca ur iyi-terri ara tmara ad sbeggneɣ leḥzen-nni ɣef wudem-iw ladɣa ma ur iyi-teɛni ara tamsalt s wudem usrid
ur ḥezzneɣ ara ɣef medden irkelli
ma ulac ur yettisin ara imi-w azmumeg s ṭul n useggas
ixxamen n teɣdemt ččuren s twuɣa d lmusayeb
tuget n wid ikeccmen ɣer uxxam n teɣdemt ttḥulfun iman-nsen ttwaḥeqren dɣa ttaken-d ulac akken ad sbeggnen d acu i ten-iḍuren
ladɣa ɣer tlawin ttaččarent allen-nsent s yimeṭṭawen uqbel ad neṭqent s wawal amezwaru
mazal ur wwiḍeɣ ara ɣur-sen hata iɛeggeḍ buɛlam
saɛdun neɣ takebbanit n buɛlam i yisallen am wakken i as-ssawalen imidaw-nneɣ s usqecmeɛ acku yezga yettawi-d isallen imaynuten
tesliḍ s usali 
ih sliɣ yis-s iḍelli kan i lliɣ d umerḥum deg usečču n uǧiǧli
neqqim ugar n ssaɛa nettawi-d ameslay ɣef yal asentel
d argaz n lɛali ɣedren-t tanezzayt mi yeffeɣ seg uxxam-is
yal ass ɣef sebɛa n ssbeḥ tḥebbes ṭumubil n temsulta sdat n uzaduɣ ideg yezdeɣ deg wannag aneggaru akken ad t-tawi s axeddim-ines
nnan-d kra n yinigan mi teffeɣ kan ṭumubil-nni gar yizaduɣen ffɣen-d sin n yirgazen llan daxel n yiwet n ṭumubil i iḥebsen deffir n uzaduɣ i ten-iqablen
ayen yessewhamen ulac win i sen-ifaqen
yiwen deg-sen yesɛa yiwet n lmitrayet n ssenf n kalacnikuf ixaḍ ṭumubil-nni s tersasin
ibedd sdat n ṭumubil ur ssawḍen ad xedmen kra
mmuten imir-n kan
uẓan sin n yineḍliben-nni ɣur-sen ldin tiwwura n ṭumubil wwin yakk leslaḥ
sakin rewlen s ṭumubil-nsen ulac win yeẓran sani
yesseqsa yiwen seg yimestanen 
amek ad ẓeḍmen ɣef yimsulta s sshala am ta mebla ma zemren ad ḥudden ɣef yiman-nsen 
yerra-as-d buɛlam am leɛwayed-is s yiwet n taɣect n win yessnen yeẓran kulci
d lqella n termit d lqella n usileɣ ay ameddakkel wali kan lḥeṭṭa n yimsulta-nneɣ
d izuranen ččuren d tassemt ccɣel-nsen d aluɛej d uqhar deg yiɣermanen
win yelhan deg-sen ur yezmir ara ad yeḍfer yiwen n yilemẓi yesɛan snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen i yukren tasakuct n tmeṭṭut deg ubrid
ẓewren kan deg usqiqer deg yinehharen n yiṭaksiyen d yimsenza n lxeḍra d lfakya akken ad asen-kksen idrimen
yenna-d umastan wis sin 
d wagi i d ugur n temsulta deg tallit n talwit d uskenwu
aqhar tameḥqranit asemɣer n yiman d tukksa n yidrimen
 ḥala idɣaɣen ara d-yegrin deg wasif 
yewweḍ-d lawan n lemḥasba
win i tt-ixedmen ad tt-ixelles
d lɛib a ssaɛid i s-yenna buɛlam seɛdun
akumisar d argaz lɛali d uɣdim
ur qsiḍeɣ ara argaz-a beddat isem-is zeddig mliḥ nekk ttmeslayeɣ ɣef temsulta s umata
ɣur-wen irkelli iwezla n yiɣermanen yetcetkayen ɣef uqhar n yimsulta neɣ ala 
yal awal deg lawan-is ameslay ass-a ad d-yawi ɣef leḥzen daya kan
bedret lmeggtin-nwen s wawal aẓiḍan
maca ɣas akkenni eǧǧ-iyi ad ak-d-iniɣ belli timsulta ur tɛass ara iman-is ur tbeddel ara tikli-ines
wwten-ten ɛlaɣila ur bnin ara fell-as
ma nquren ɛayn-el-kerma d temdinin niḍen ad nwali takriḍt ur tt-tḥuz ara zik
wwḍen-aɣ-d kra n yisallen d akken tuget seg wid yeffɣen seg leḥbus n sseḥra ulin s adrar suddsen tirebbuyaɛ timselḥin akken ad rren ttar deg udabu i ten-ḍeggren deg bu-yikurdan am wakken texdem fransa d yimesdurar ideg ffɣen yimjuhad s waṭas
wagi d aferdis agejdan deg usnerni n tekriḍt n yirebraben-a
kesben yirebraben tirmit deg tmenɣiwt ma d timsulta teqqim tezzuɣur ibriren-ines seg wass ɣer wayeḍ
nniɣ-as tesɛiḍ lḥeqq
akumisar yella ileḥḥu mebla aɛessas mebla ma iɛass iman-is ad as-tiniḍ mazal-aɣ deg yiseggasen-nni n telwit
iḍelli kan ufiɣ-t ibedd ɣer tewwurt n uxxam n temsulta yettmeslay d yiwen seg yimidawen-ines iruḥ sakin yid-i weḥd-s ɣer usečču yernu ula d tameẓyant-ines swayes yezmer ad iḥudd ɣef yiman-is ur cukkeɣ ara yewwi-tt yid-s
yenna-d umastan amezwaru s yiwet n yennuɣnan 
d ayen yessewhamen ur tfehmeḍ acemma yal ass imegger rrsas timerwin n teɣtas isallen n usedrem n uhuddu d usṭerḍeq ttaččaren isebtar n yiɣmisen maca ɣas akken teqqim temsulta n ɛayn-el-kerma tettḥewwis ad as-tiniḍ deg tmurt n swisra neɣ deg tmurt n ssuwid i tella i nga nekkni s yimestanen nḥemmel ad
akka nemmeslay s laɛyaḍ wa ad nerdu imdanen
ahat mi neẓra taɣect tiwuɣa i iḍerrun deg tmetti-nneɣ nuɣal nettwali ccer d ddɣel deg yal amkan
maca si aḥmed yuklal awal aẓiḍan
ɣef waya skecmeɣ iman-iw nniɣ 
win ur nesɛi ara tuga deg uɛebbuḍ-is ur yettaggad ara times d tagi d liḥala n si aḥmed d amsaltu d uɣdim yeṭṭafar asaḍuf ur iḥeqqer yiwen
ur yeksib ula d yiwet n ṭumubil d anza belli ur yessexdam ara tawuri-ines akken ad yekseb idrimen am wakken xeddmen wiyaḍ
yenna-d buɛlam seɛdun 
amerḥum yella d amedya deg uxeddim-ines ad cehdeɣ ɣef waya
beddren-t-id ḥala deg lxir
bexlaf wiyaḍ i ijemɛen igerrujen deg kra n yiseggasen ad tɣileḍ d ifri n ɛli baba i ufan
yewweḍ-d ssut n umaray neɣ n uneflus n uxxam n teɣdemt i d-yeqqaren yebda yibeddi dɣa nruḥ wa deffir wa ɣer tzeqqa tameqqrant
tawacult n si aḥmed teṭṭef rray ad t-temḍel deg taddart ideg ilul
taddart-nni tameẓyant anda yebɣa ad yesɛeddi tastaɣt-ines gar umadaɣ-ines
aṭas n yimsulta yeddan deg temṭelt-ines
nruḥ d tarbaɛt
deg tazwara ugiɣ ad dduɣ ɣer tẓegwa-nni ideg yekkes laman
acḥal n yisallen yessewḥacen i aɣ-d-yettawḍen seg yidurar-nni akken ad aɣ-ssergigin seg tuggdi wa ad aɣ-gedlen anekcum ɣer-sen
yeffeɣ wawal belli d timnaḍin tilelliyin tḥekkem-itent trebbuyaɛ timselḥin teqher imezdaɣ-is d imesdurar d ikerrazen ur sɛin ara assaɣ d umennuɣ iḍerrun deg tmurt
d tudrin yezgan deg yidurar ulac deg-sent iɣallen n laman
la tamsulta wala tamsetla
ḥala tayunin n lɛesker i yeddawaren tikwal dinna
deg tilawt tayunin-a n lɛesker ur nfiɛent i ucemma
d tarbaɛt taɣezzfant d taẓayant n ṭumubilat d yikumya yeččuren s lɛesker i sluɣmen yiwen n usluɣmu s wudem n tiṭ deg tallit n telwit ur lmiden ara deg-s ulamma amek ad jebden s tmekḥal-nsen ugar n waya lemden kan tataktikt n ṭṭrad tamensayt
tura mi ufan iman-nsen deg yiwen n wannar udemkal-ines d idurar d tẓegwa acengu-ines d tirebbuyaɛ timselḥin yeffren deg yiɣeẓran deg yimudaɣ dɣa ad uɣalen iserdasen-agi iruḥen ad sɛeddin lɛesker-nsen d tiɣtas isehlen wa ad t-nɣen s tersast wa ad t-zlun
mi ara lḥunt tɣelmin-a deg yiberdan n yidurar ad tent-tesleḍ wa ad tent-twaliḍ seg mbaɛid
ɣef waya ttafen yimnafqen yakk lweqt akken ad ffren iman-nsen deg yifran-nsen ad rǧun kan melmi ad ɛeddin mebla ma uggaden kra
acḥal i ɣriɣ deg yiɣmisen ɣef tfextin i ndin yirebraben i tɣelmin-a n yiserdasen deg yiberdan n udrar yecban wigi kfant s yibaxixen ad tessedḥi seg-sen talsa
mi d-wwḍeɣ ɣer umraḥ n uzaduɣ akked buɛlam
seɛdun ayen ijebden lwelha-w d amḍan n yirgazen irefden leslaḥ
meqqrit ciṭuḥ deg laɛmer yernu iban ur llin seg temsulta neɣ seg temsetla wala seg yiserdasen
d iɣarimen kan tuget deg-sen ṭṭfen deg yifassen-nsen timekḥal n ssyada
usan-d deg snat n tkumya timeẓyanin seg ssenf n  mazda  am tidak i ssexdamen i tiɣin n sselɛa
ẓriɣ usan-d seg taddart n si aḥmed yiwet n taddart tameẓyant iwumi ssawalen sidi merzug
nɛezza sin n watmaten-is nsellem sakin ɣef yal argaz i d-yusan yid-sen
yiwen deg-sen yettak anzi i si aḥmed maca iqewwa ciṭuḥ fell-as
yelsa yiwet n lfista taqdimt n lɛesker yessers ɣef uqerruy-is yiwet n teɛmamt d tawinaɣit
cclaɣem-is ččan udem-is ɣur-s daɣen yiwet n tamart d tarqiqant terna-as tebrek ɣef ssifa-s
ɣef tayet-is yerfed yiwet n tmekḥelt seg ssenf n siminuf
d tayiwant gar tmukḥal n ssyada iɛelqen yirgazen ɣef tuyat-nsen
ibedd aqerruy-is ɣer yigenni
ur d-iban ara leḥzen ɣef wudem-is am wakken i nettaf ɣef wudmawen n wid iwumi yemmut yiwen seg twacult-nsen
susmen irkelli ṭṭafaren kan s wallen-nsen ṭumubilat i yettawin yettarran d yimɛezziyen i d-yettassen
deg ṭṭerf n umraḥ qqimen yirgazen d yimeẓyanen ttwalin ayen iḍerrun sdat-sen deg tsusmi
iban d imezdaɣ n yizaduɣen niḍen usan-d ad ḥeḍren i usuffeɣ n tfekka n umerḥum seg uxxam-is
ur cukkeɣ ara ad ddun yid-neɣ
ruḥen-d kan ad sbeggnen ibeddi-nsen d twacult n umerḥum
neɣ ahat usan-d kan akka ur sɛin ara ccɣel niḍen ad t-xedmen
akka i iga uɣref-agi i iḥemmlen ad iferreǧ baṭel wa ad iwali d acu xeddmen wiyaḍ
d aferreǧ ara yefken talalit i tmucuha ara ḥkun deg wussan d wuḍan i d-iteddun
furseɣ tagnit mi yeffreɣ umkan seg yimɛezziyen imaynuten uẓaɣ ɣer yiwet n terbaɛt n yiɣarimen d imselḥen 
ansuf yis-wen  sarameɣ ur ken-yessaɛyi ara yinig lḥemdulillah uẓaɣ mliḥ ɣer gma-s n umerḥum 
sliɣ i kra n usrugmet fehmeɣ kan  labas walu
sliɣ imir-n i leswat  ad t-yerḥem rebbi
si aḥmed d ameddakkel-iw ɛziz fell-i mliḥ aṭas i nettru fell-as iɣaḍ-aɣ mačči d kra
yerra-yi-d s laɛqel kan mebla ma imuqel ɣer wallen-iw 
ad t-yerḥem rebbi  d lmektub n sidi rebbi d tagi d ddunit ɣer din i nleḥḥu irkelli
ur ɛeddan ara sin n wussan mi iyi-d-yenna yejjem ad iwali imawlan-is deg sidi merzug
yenna-d aṭas aya ur iwala ara taddart-is
yessarem seg wul-is ad yaf tagnit akken ad tt-iẓur deg wussan-a i d-iteddun
yerra-d gma-s nnehta yenna 
d tamettant i as-yessawlen akka i tḍerru d yiɣriben ma yectaq albaɛḍ taddart-is anamek-is d yiwen seg twacult-is i yeqqimen deg tmurt ara yawḍen laɛfu n
rebbi s umata d yiwen seg yimawlan-is  d baba-s neɣ d yemma-s
wehmeɣ deg usegzi-a maca susmeɣ ulac acu i as-nniɣ
si aḥmed yaɛya seg uxeddim yebɣa ad yestaɛfu deg taddart n temẓi-s
neccedha irkelli ad nwali akal ideg nlul u netturebba
ahat kunwi ur teffiɣem ara seg tudrin-nwen ur tettḥulfum ara i ucedhi-agi
d tidet urǧin ffɣeɣ seg taddart-iw akal n lejdud-iw anagar deg tallit ideg sɛeddaɣ lɛesker-inu
lliɣ ttganiɣ tikci n ttesriḥ am waggur n lɛid akken ad uɣaleɣ srid ɣer
sidi merzug
tella telwit deg tallit-nni mačči am wass-a
d tidetass-a tewɛer liḥala nekk s timmad-iw weṣṣaɣ gma ur d-yettas ara ɣer sidi merzug urǧin xemmemeɣ ad t-taweḍ lmut ɣer da
ɣef yiqerra-nneɣ nekkni iɣef tettezzi tmettant yal ass
ma d kunwi yellan deg temdint nɣil tettidirem deg telwit n rebbi iɣallen n laman ttḥuddun fell-awen
akka i tɣileḍ maca takriḍt d tmenɣiwin wwḍent yal yiwen yettidiren deg tmurt-a
ɣef waya i nerfed leslaḥ mgal lbaṭel
neṭṭef rray ad nḥudd ɣef yiman-nneɣ s yiman-nneɣ
ad ak-d-iniɣ tidet nella nettidir deg yiwen n unazir urǧin nɣil ad d-yas wass ad neɣli deg-s
taddart-nneɣ tella d lǧennet tettidir deg telwit d lehna
d tidet nekkni d igellilen maca tigellelt urǧin tenɣa albaɛḍ
nkerrez akal-nneɣ yettara-aɣ-d lxir
lliɣ ma serseɣ aqerruy-iw ɣef tsutma ur ttfiqiɣ ara d iman-iw armi yuli wass
ulac tuggdi
nettaǧǧa lmal-nneɣ deg lexla ulac win ad t-innalen
ɣlin-d fell-aneɣ iɛefriten-a ɛlaɣila ur neẓri ara seg wansi i d-usan
usan-d yiwen n yiḍ tuɣ-aɣ neɛmer urar i yiwen seg warraw-nneɣ
llan deg mraw deg-sen s leslaḥ ssutren deg-neɣ ad neḥbes dderbuka d tuɣac d teɣratin n tlawin
newhem deg-sen
naɛreḍ-iten i yimensi ččan sakin hedren-aɣ
nniɣ-asen ayen yellan deg wul-iw  tamsalt-nwen ur aɣ-taɛni ara
ma tesɛam ugur d wat n lezzayer ruḥet ɣer lezzayer ad t-tefrum
d acu i aɣ-idexlen nekkni  deg yiḍ-nni ruḥen nɣil dayen tamsalt teddez tebrez
maca uɣalen-d ɣur-neɣ wwin-d yid-sen wiyaḍ aṭas deg-sen tikkelt-a
kra n yilmeẓyen-nneɣ ddan yid-sen dɣa bḍan wat n sidi
merzug
maca lbaṭel n wigi iɛedda yakk tilisa
tɛeddan ɣef wayla-nneɣ ḥetmen-aɣ ad asen-nefk idrimen
nruḥ acḥal d abrid ad neccetki ɣer yimestal maca ur xdimen acemma
ad d-asen ssbeḥ ad seqsin imezdaɣ ad ruḥen sya u sya ad zzin ciṭuḥ sakin ad d-uɣalen uqbel n uɣelluy n yiṭij
nurǧa ad skecmen yiserdasen iman-nsen akken ad aɣ-hennin seg yimesbaṭliyen-a maca ula d nitni ur xdimen acemma
yiwet n tmeddit ukren yiwet n teqcict i iruḥen ɣer teẓgi ad d-tezdem isɣaren sakin rewlen
nennejmaɛ s temɣawla neṭṭef rray ad nruḥ ad nadi fell-as wa ad tt-id-nerr s ddreɛ
maca rran-aɣ s leslaḥ-nsen nɣan-aɣ yiwen n yilemẓi mazal-it d aleqqaq
imir-n ur nufi ara sdat-neɣ anagar tifrat n usuffeɣ n leslaḥ-nneɣ akken ad nḥareb ɣef yixxamen-nneɣ
nuɣ-d daɣen kra n tmekḥal nbedd ibeddi n yiwen n urgaz ad nḥudd ɣef nnif d wayla-nneɣ
ass-a ula d yiwen seg yifuḥanen-a ur yezmir ara ad yaẓ ɣer yixxamen-nneɣ
ttif lmut wala tudert n ddel
seg zik n zik i nuɣ aẓar deg wakal-a
fransa
fransa s timmad-is ur tessaweḍ ara ad aɣ-tesseknu ad d-asen tura kra n yiqelwacen akken ad aɣ-sseknun
d awezɣi
yernu neṭṭef rray ad nemḍel si aḥmed deg taddart-is akken ad nerreẓ tuggdi izedɣen medden irkelli
ad t-nemḍel deg wakal n lejdud-is win turew yemma-s s ibeddi ad d-yas ad as-nmel amek xeddmen yirgazen n sidi merzug
yessekcem urgaz-a talwit s ul-iw
ad inigeɣ mebla akukru
daɣen aṭas n yimsulta n ɛin-el-kerma ad yeddun yid-neɣ s leslaḥ-nsen
ssutreɣ deg gma-s n si aḥmed ẓriɣ ula d netta qqaren-as ɛebdelqader am nekkini ad yeddu yid-i deg ṭumubil-inu
yeqbel s uzmmumeg
d tagnit ad iyi-d-yales amek i ttidiren deg yidurar ladɣa deg wussan-a ineggura
ula d nekk mmi-s n udrar d taddart maca taddart n temharsa d yiseggasen imezwura n tmunnent
liḥala-nsen mazal-itt tenṭer am tin i ɛaceɣ nekkini deg tallit-inu  neɣ yewweḍ-itt waḍu n tetrarit am wakken yella icennu unagraw n bumedyen 
amastan buɛlam seɛdun yedda-d yid-i ula d netta
iḍelli tameddit mi aɣ-d-yewweḍ usali n tuwin n tfekka n ukumisar ɣer taddart ideg ilul nemtafaq ad neḥḍer tamḍelt-is anda yebɣu tili
buɛlam d argaz bu-tissas ur d-yewwi ara awal ɣef temsalt n laman deg yidurar-nni ibaɛden mliḥ ɣef wallen d leslaḥ n yiɣallen n laman
tiddin d si aḥmed ɣer uẓekka-ines ɣur-neɣ nekkni d tamsalt tuzzmant d tamsalt n trugza
tebda tarbaɛt yeddan d umerḥum tikli uqbel n lɛecra n ssbeḥ
d irgazen n sidi merzug i ineggzen d imezwura ɣer ṭumubilat-nsen akken ad zwiren takerrust n usellek i yewwin tafekka n umerḥum
udmawen n yirgazen-a d arasen d ixemriyen allen-nsen tteḥdiqirent tikli-nsen xfifet uɣen tannumi leḥḥun deg udemkal iwaɛren
ula d iselsa-nsen ttbinin-d d wid n wat tudrin teččur d aɣebbar d taqdimt kra deg-sen qersen ur sɛin ara tiqeffalin
maca ɣas akken bedden leḥḥun s zzux d nnefxa
d irgazen ur nuɣ ara tannumi kennun daɣen ur ttkalayen ara ɣef wayeḍ sɛant tawant deg wul tetten kan ayen d-gemmren s yiɣallen-nsen zgan wejden akken ad bedden ɣer yidis n win i ten-yeḥwaǧen mebla ma rǧan sɣur-s lexlas
d tagi d tudert i ssneɣ yakan tura la tt-twaliɣ deg talɣa d tikli n yimdanen-a
telḥa terbaɛt s temɣawla
ṭumubil-inu teqqim deg tlemmast tettkerkir iman-is deffir n ṭumubilat timezwura
rriɣ lbal-iw kan ad tent-ḍefreɣ ur cliɛeɣ ara deg yismawen n tudrin d temdinin i nzegger
deg tazwara teɣli-d tsusmi gar-aneɣ anagar iwenniten n buɛlam
seɛdun i yeqqimen tama-w yal mi ara nɛeddi ɣef yiwet n taddart neɣ ɣef yiwet n tsergelt n yiɣallen n laman i tt-yettruẓun
tisergalin n temsulta n temsetla d yiserdasen fruzɛent deg ubrid ad tent-tafeḍ yal mi ara tkecmeḍ neɣ mi ara teffɣeḍ seg tudrin neɣ temdinin
kra deg-sent tzegger-itent terbaɛt s tazzla ɣer tiyaḍ tḥebbes deg ṭṭerf akken ad walin yiɣallen n laman ma seḥḥan warraten i sen-imudd urfiq n unehhar n tkerrust n usellek
mi d-newweḍ ɣer yiwet n tsergelt n yiserdasen yeqqim yiwen n ukabural acḥal n lweqt akked yiɣarimen yeddmen leslaḥ imuqel mliḥ kra n wuragen n urfad n leslaḥ
isubb-d sakin umaswaḍ n temsulta n ɛayn-el-kerma yemmeslay yid-s kra n lweqt sakin serrḥen-as i terbaɛt-nni akken ad tkemmel tikli-ines
ugar n ssaɛa n tikli umbaɛd neffeɣ seg uzaɣar n mitiǧa nebda alluy ɣer yidurar
abrid yeḍyeq yernu yennernenni iran-nsen ẓẓan s yisekla iɣummen kulci ulac acu ara twaliḍ
yenneqbaḍ wul-iw uɣalent-d ɣer wallaɣ-iw i xeddment trebbuyaɛ timselḥin
seqsaɣ ɛebdelqader yeqqimen ɣef ukersi n deffir akked yiwen seg yirfiqen-is sersen tiqsiḍin-nni n tsergalin timekḥal-nsen ɣef tgecrar rran udmawen-nsent ɣer tama n ǧǧaj
yenna 
xeddmen tisergalin-nsen deg yiberdan yettawin ɣer tuddar timeẓyanin akken ad kksen idrimen i yimezdaɣ wa ad nadin ɣef wid yellan deg lɛesker
deg waggur yezrin zlan yiwen n yilemẓi ur iɛeddi ara snat n tmerwin n yiseggasen yuɣal-d s axxam umbaɛd mi yekfa lɛesker-ines
serrḥen-as seg lɛesker sani ara iruḥ umeɣbun 
nnan-d kra n yinigan win i t-yessuffɣen seg lkar d amdan i yessen mliḥ d mmi-s n taddart-is
mi t-iwala kan yessers lmeḥcuca-ines ɣef yidmaren-is yenna-as   hata tura teɣliḍ gar yifassen-nneɣ ay aqeddac n yiqehharen
iḥudd yilemẓi-nni ɣef yiman-is yenna-as d tamsetla i t-yewwin s yiɣil tura dayen yekfa lɛesker-ines maca ɣas akken ur nfiɛent ara ttḥalil-ines
ulin-d yirebraben niḍen ɣer lkar ssuffɣen-d ilemẓi s yiɣil umṛen umbaɛd anehher n lkar ad ikemmel tikli
sin n wussan umbaɛd nufa-d ilemẓi-nni yemzel deg tama-nni kan
ur yebɛid ara fell-aneɣ mliḥ tura ad naweḍ ɣur-s deg rrbeɛ n ssaɛa
sya rrbeɛ n ssaɛa  tiyita n ujenwi ur iyi-tqerreḥ ara am tenfalit-a
aql-aɣ newweḍ ɣer yifri n yizerman
ad yester rebbi tameddit wa ad aɣ-yessemneɛ
yenna-d umeddakkel-is yiwen n uferḍas akkenni ad yesɛu ahat ukkuẓet n tmerwin n yiseggasen 
nekk ɣliɣ deg ukkuẓet n tserglin n yirebraben
lliɣ daxel n lkar
ttraǧun dima aɣelluy n lmeɣreb akken ad d-ffɣen seg tuffriwin-nsen
d arraw n temnaḍt-nneɣ ssnen medden
ɣef waya ttawin idrimen kan ttnadin daɣen ɣef lɛesker yesɛeddayen wid am wakken d-yenna
ɛebdelqader
yiwet n tikkelt nnuɣeɣ d yiwen d mmi-s n tmurt-iw ssneɣ-t mliḥ ibedd ɣef uqerruy-iw yenna-yi-d 
 suffeɣ-d ayen yellan deg lǧib-ik
nniɣ-as  yaxi tessneḍ-iyi mliḥ tessneḍ daɣen ayen yellan deg lǧib-iw
yenna-yi-d  nekk ur k-ssineɣ ur cliɛeɣ deg liḥala-inek
ad txellsem irkelli dagi ulac tisuraf
nniɣ-as  ayɣer ur tettruḥum ara ɣer tmanaɣt ad tawim idrimen n yiqehharen i aɣ-d-teqqarem tettḥarabem-ten  imir-n kkren-d kra n leswat bedden yid-i
ɛerqent-as i urebrab-nni yuɣal ɣer deffir
ur yebni ara ɣef waddud-agi-nneɣ
neẓra-ten d imaggaden lleɛben-tt kan d at-tissas d tebɣest
ass-nni ṭṭfeɣ rray ur ttsusumeɣ ara ɣef tmeḥqranit d lbaṭel
mi sliɣ sbedden tarbaɛt n uzbu kecmeɣ ɣur-s d imsebbel ssutreɣ ad iyi-d-ffken leslaḥ
sɛeddaɣ lɛesker-inu deg useggas n  ttekkaɣ deg unmenɣi n amgala mgal lɛesker n lmerruk ar tura zemreɣ ad refdeɣ leslaḥ wa ad ttekkiɣ deg ṭṭradat
aql-aɣ dagi deg tmurt-nneɣ deg wayla-nneɣ ur nettaǧǧa yiwen ad aɣ-yessuffeɣ seg-s
wehmeɣ deg lirad n wigi i yettḥuddun ɣef laman-nsen d wayla-nsen
yenna-d buɛlam 
ad awen-ibarek rebbi kunwi d izzayriyen d lefḥul
azzayri ur iqebbel ara tameḥqranit d ddel s wagi i yettwassen seg zik n zik
yenna-d ɛebdelqader 
ula d nekk deg tazwara bɣan ad iyi-yekksen idrimen
d yiwen n umdan yessen-iyi mliḥ
yiwen n wass nennuɣ seččaɣ-as akal
yuli s adrar yedda d trebbuyaɛ timselḥin yiwen n yiḍ yeqseḍ-iyi yessuter deg-i idrimen
ɣur-i semmuset n tfunasin d uɛecciw n tyuzaḍ
ur tteffreɣ ara fell-ak deg tazwara-nni fkiɣ-as semmus n yigiman n yidinaren akken ad iyi-yefk lehna
nniɣ-as ad iyi-yeṭṭixer
maca ur zrin ara kraḍ n wagguren armi d-yuɣal ɣur-i yessutur zzyada n yidrimen
tikkelt-a yessemɣer aɛebbuḍ-is yessuter deg-i semmus n yimelyan n yisuntimen ɣef yiwen n ubrid
ɛerḍeɣ ad t-qennɛeɣ sfehmeɣ-as ur sɛiɣ ara azal n yidrimen i d-yessuter yernu fkiɣ-as ayen ilaqen
teẓram d acu i yi-d-yenna yenna-yi-d  senz tisita-inek d tyuẓaḍt-inek efk-aɣ-d idrimen-nsent
nniɣ-as  amek ad xedmeɣ umbaɛd akken ad ɛeggceɣ tawacult-iw  yenna-yi-d wagi mačči d ugur-ines
yeggez-iyi nekk akked twacult-iw s lmut d userɣi n uxxam-iw d lmal-iw ma ur as-d-fkiɣ ara idrimen deg snat n ledwar
yessers ajenwi ɣef temgerḍt-iw ur ẓriɣ ara amek ad xedmeɣ
qqimeɣ kraḍ n wussan mebla iḍes ttxemmimeɣ kan deg tifrat
xemmemeɣ ad senzeɣ ayen sɛiɣ ad rewleɣ sakin ɣer temdint n blida
ad d-uɣaleɣ deg taggara n ddunit-iw d axeddam ɣer medden umbaɛd mi lliɣ ḥekkmeɣ deg yiman-iw d yidrimen-iw
yernu deg taddart-iw ttafeɣ iman-iw am uslem deg yillel ma ffɣeɣ-tt ad tiqfeɣ
d acu ara xedmeɣ deg temdint  ad ṭṭfeɣ amkan ɣef uṭruṭwar ad senzeɣ dduxan d lkawkaw am wakken xeddmen yimeɛgazen
yeḍra akk waya mebla ma teẓra tmeṭṭut-iw wala arraw-iw
nniɣ-asen kan d kra n yinebgawen n yiḍ ssutren-d idrimen d wučči
mmeslayeɣ d gma ameqqran ɣef usentel-a netta d aselmad deg uɣerbaz amezwaru i yezgan deg ulmus n sidi merzug
ilaq ad teẓrem sidi merzug d tagrumma n yixxamen mbaɛaden yal tawacult tesɛa akal tkerrez-it
deg ulmus yella yiwen n uɣerbaz amezwaru lǧameɛ kra n tḥuna aḥeffaf amikaniki d sbiṭar ameẓyan yeɣleq seg wasmi yeldi ukkuẓ n yiseggasen aya
axxam-iw yebɛed fell-as s kraḍ n yikulimitren deg ubrid yettawin ɣer teẓgi
ɣef waya teshel tisin n yirebraben ɣur-i
iruḥ-d ɣur-i s axxam aṭas i nemmeslay ɣef usentel-a
dɣa neṭṭef rray ad nezbu ad nessiwel i kra n lǧiran i nessen nesɛa deg-sen taflest akken ad nbedd mgal takerḍa-a
deg sin n wussan nuɣal deg ṭam yid-neɣ newjed ad nesbedd lɛessa deg yiḍ wa ad nqabel yal tanṭagt
yal yiwen deg-neɣ yettɛassa ɣef wayla-s ma iwala kra ad yejbed s leslaḥ-is akken ad d-asen wiyaḍ ad t-allen
yiwen n yiḍ yusa-d mmi-s n teqjunt-nni ssaɛa imir-n tɛedda lɛecra n yiḍ
yebda la yessawal  ya si
ɛebdelqader  ya si ɛebdelqader tewwiḍ-d lamana-nni
mmi-s n tcermuḍt d lamana n yemma-k i teǧǧiḍ ɣur-i
mi sliɣ i lehḍur d lheffa i d-yekkan seg tama n wunẓul anda d-tezga teẓgi ẓẓleɣ ɣef ssqef n uxxam
yusa-d akked sin n yirgazen akken ad yawi idrimen ulac acu yuggad
lliɣ wejdeɣ ad nɣeɣ iwakken ad ḥuddeɣ ɣef tidi n uxeddim-iw d wayen i yi-d-yeǧǧa baba
sutreɣ deg-s ad d-yekcem ɣer umraḥ n uxxam
yekcem yettkel ɣef yiman-is mi yewweḍ ɣer tlemmast yeḥbes
ad as-tiniḍ yella acu yesraḥ
ur as-ǧǧiɣ ara lweqt ad d-yerr nnehta
yiwet n tersast wwiɣ-t-id deg lqaɛa
yuzzel urfiq-is ɣur-s ad t-isellek wwteɣ s tersast tis snat
zegleɣ-t
maca lǧar-iw
ɛmer ur t-yezgil ara yewwi-t-id
yuzzel yilef-nni deffir n uxxam-iw yebɣa ad yeffer deffir n ssur
iqjan bdan seglafen deg yal axxam
rran-d fell-i kra n yirgazen n taddart s tiyita n rrsas bɣan ad iyi-ɛeggnen belli ɣur-i i leḥḥun akken ad iyi-ɛiwnen
ḥkiɣ-asen yakan ayen yeḍran yid-i
beddeɣ deg umkan-iw ɛeggḍeɣ ɣer tama n uxxam n si ɛmer   ilef-nni ɣur-k i ileḥḥu 
ɛeddant kra n ddqayeq sliɣ i ssut n tersasin niḍen kkant-d seg tama n lǧar-iw
sakin sliɣ-as yessawal  nenɣa ilef-nni  dayen nenɣa ilef-nni
iɛedda kra n lweqt zzin-iyi-d yirgazen ittekkan deg terbaɛt-inu deg tlemmast n uxxam-iw
nessemderri lmeggtin nekkes-asen leslaḥ d yikerṭucen i d-wwin yid-sen
tarennawt tuli-aɣ s aqerru
nules i wayen aɣ-yeḍran s zzux d nnefxa
deg yiḍ-nni nfaq i yiman-nneɣ nesɛa tabɣest ulac win i aɣ-izemren
maca ɣas akkenni nkemmel lɛessa
yal yiwen deg-neɣ yuɣal s amkan-is nuggad ad d-ẓeḍmen fell-aneɣ
ahat mazal imeddukkal-nsen ttganin
sɛeddaɣ ayen yegran deg yiḍ deg tuzzya ɣef yixxamen n
sidi merzug ttembadaleɣ tabɣest d wat n taddart
deg yal axxam ttafeɣ-d heggan-d latay d uɣrum n temtunt yeḥman deg kra n yixxamen niḍen ttafeɣ tiḥbulin d teɣrifin s tamemt
uɣalen-d ḥekkun-aɣ-d tiqsiḍin ɣef yimjuhad i ibeden mgal tamhersa tafransisst tid i nesla yakan sɣur yimawlan-nneɣ asmi nella d imeẓyanen
baba ad fell-as yaɛfu yerḥem yella d yiwen seg yimjuhad imeqqranen n lwilaya tis ukkuẓet d yiwen seg yirfiqen n umeɣras si mḥemmed bugerra
deg wass wis sin mi leǧwayeh-nni kan deg tewweḍ tarbaɛt n temsetla nniɣ-as i ufesyan bɣiɣ ad ǧǧeɣ ɣur-i tamekḥelt i kkseɣ i urebrab tagi i tettwaliḍ gar yifassen-iw tura  d azgen n tmitrayit siminuf seg tmurt n
rruss iteddem mrawet n tersasin
zemreɣ ad rreɣ yis-s tanṭagt n terbaɛt n yirebraben
timekḥal-nneɣ d tiqdimin sɛant snat n tersasin kan
deg tazwara yugi umestul
yenna-yi-d timekḥelt-a tettwaker ḥwaǧen ad walin uṭṭun-ines akken ad walin anwa-t bab-is
aṭas i nqesser ɣef temsalt-a armi i t-qennɛeɣ
yenna-yi-d s uzmumeg  kečč d lefḥel d bab n ddreɛ tuklaleḍ kter n waya
awi-tt ad ḍebbreɣ aqerruy-iw
seg wass-nni ur iyi-teṭṭixir ara tettruḥu yid-i ɣer yal amkan tetett yid-i teggan yid-i
ttḥadreɣ-tt kter n yiman-iw
yessusem unazbay walaɣ-t seg lemri n ṭumubil amek i yesluffuy i tmekḥalt-is ad as-tiniḍ d argaz d tmaɛcuqet-is
tuɣ terkeft abrid yessalayen ɣer udrar ɣef yiri-s d iɣẓer yeččur d isekla
iberdan zzin mačči d kra ad ak-yeqreḥ wul-ik wa ad yezzi laɛqel-ik
nekk rriɣ tidmi-w kan ɣer tenhert deg ubriḍ uḍyiq ma d buɛlam yeqqim tugniwin n udemkal n udrar kan yettmuqul deg yessawhamen i yettɛeddayen sdat n wallen-is
neffeɣ seg ubrid n ugezdu nekcem ɣer win n tɣiwant yeṭṭuṭcen
iberdan zzin am yizerman tarbaɛt tettaf-d iman-is tikkwal yettuḥettem fell-as ad tessenɣes deg urured-ines tikwal niḍen tḥebbes maḍi
nniɣ-as deg wul-iw imekwan-a wulmen i tundin n tcerket
yewwet wul-iw
mmektaɣ-d imeslayen n urgaz yeqqimen deffir-iw
ldiɣ mliḥ allen-iw limmer ad waliɣ kra i yessefqaɛen deg tlemmast n yisekla neɣ albaɛḍ yeffer deffir n yiẓra
maca rriɣ ddehn-iw kan ɣer tenhert ttuɣ ayen yellan deg ubrid
mi d-newweḍ ɣer yiwen n umkan yeḍyeq mliḥ yenṭeq-d unazbay yenna 
deg umadaɣ-a i nɣan ilemẓi-nni d-yeffɣen seg lɛesker
yules-d i yifutas n teqsiḍt-ines i aɣ-d-yeḥka yakan iwehha-d s ufus-is ɣer yiwet n tkessart yettawin ɣer yiɣzer
nniɣ-as kan deg wul-iw  d wagi d lawan n teqsiḍin am tigi ay argaz  ahat keččini tennumeḍ ul-ik dayen yuɣal ur yessin ara tuggdi ma d nekkni ala
yenṭeq buɛlam yenna-d ahat akken ad yekkes tuggdi-nni i yemmɣen fell-aneɣ 
tettawim tettaram deg ubrid-a ssbeḥ tameddit  i as-yenna
ur nesɛi ara
ɛebdelqader
anda tebɣiḍ ad nidir  d tagi d tamurt-nneɣ d akal i aɣ-yettɛeggicen
lbaqi mraḥba s tikci n rebbi
yenna-d unazbay wis sin 
deg tallit-a taneggarut uɣalen yiserdasen ttezzin s waṭas dagi
nesla ad bnun yiwet n lkarẓirna deg yiwet seg tewririn n sidi merzug akken ad ɛassen ambiwel n yirebraben
ass-nni ma bɣan ad smenɛen tudert-nsen seg lmut yessefk fell-asen ad ǧǧen tamnaḍt-a
tura imezdaɣ leslaḥ
irebraben uɣalen n taddart ttaggaden ad ẓeḍmen ɣef yixxamen-nneɣ mačči am wakken llan xeddmen deg tazwara
teɣli-d tsusmi i tikkelt niḍen
nuɣal nleḥḥu s laɛqel kan
