iban-d mliḥ ubrid ḥala akal n tfellaḥt d kra n tiferni ulac refden lxetyar irkelli yixxamen iwumi yezzi ukermus i nettwali sdat-neɣ
qrib ad naweḍ ihi ɣer sidi merzug
dayen newweḍ
tban-d ssumɛa n lǧameɛ seg lebɛid
nekcem daxel n taddart yeččan ciṭuḥ seg wakal n tfellaḥt
deg tlemmast n taddart sdat n lǧameɛ nnejmaɛen aṭas n yimezdaɣ n taddart ttraǧun awwaḍ n terbaɛt ara d-yawin tafekka n umerḥum
ḥebsent ṭumubilat udren-d yirgazen s laɛqel kan
inig yesseɛya-aɣ mliḥ
uzzlen yimezdaɣ ddmen tafekka n umerḥum ɣer daxel n lǧameɛ
ssaɛa qrib ad taweḍ d lweḥda
kecmen irkelli ɣer tzeqqa n tẓallit
nudaɣ ɣef buɛlam ur t-ufiɣ ara
ahat yekcem ɣer daxel yettqellib ɣef tzeqqa n luḍu  d amẓallu ur yestehzay ara ɣef tẓallit ur cukkeɣ ara ad as-truḥ taẓallit ɣef yiman n umerḥum si aḥmed
qqimeɣ beddeɣ deg tlemmast n yimsulta i d-yusan yid-neɣ ttmuquleɣ kan deg tewririn yellan deg temnaḍt-nni
nesla i ssut n lmudden yessawal i tẓallit n ṭṭhur s laɛqel kan yerreẓ tasusmi-nni yemmɣen ɣef umkan d rrehba i d-ikecmen deg wulawen-nneɣ
yuẓa-d yiwen n umɣar ɣer terbaɛt-nneɣ yenna-aɣ-d tella yiwet n tzeqqa n luḍu daxel n lǧameɛ i win yebɣan ad iẓal
snemmren-t irkelli
maca ulac win yembawlen seg umkan-is
ẓriɣ aṭas n wid ur nettẓalla ara am nekkini ur ḥemmlen ara ad d-afen iman-nsen deg tegnatin am ta ideg ttazallen irkelli ɣer tẓallit
taẓallit ɣer tuget n yimezdaɣ n tudrin d tigwat tamagnut ur ttxemmimen ara deg-s maḍi
maca ɣas tẓallan xeddmen kra n tigawin yeffɣen tacerɛit am tisit n ccrab amedya ma teɣli-d tegnit akken ad t-swen ur tt-zegglen ara
ur ttwalin ara tanmegla gar snat n tigawin-a
ɣur-sen d abekkaḍ yellan deg ddunit-a ur zmiren ara ad as-rewlen
mi tekfa tẓallit wwin-d yimezdaɣ tirbutin n seksu sersen-ten ɣef tmurt ssawlen i wid yellan din ad awɣen
yewwi-d yiwen seg yilmeẓyen yiwet i terbaɛt-nneɣ
ẓriɣ heggan-tent-id i wid d-iruḥen seg lebɛid ad wajhen
lluẓeɣ ṭṭfeɣ yiwet n tɣenjayt kniɣ ɣef terbut
ula d imsulta-nni xedmen am nekk
učči-nni ẓiḍ mliḥ
mi beddeɣ sefḍeɣ imi-w walaɣ ameddakkel-iw buɛlam yeffeɣ-d seg lǧameɛ ileḥḥu srid ɣer yiwen yeddem tarbuyt nnig n uqerruy-is
walaɣ-t la s-ihedder sakin yessers-itt urgaz-nni ɣer yiḍarren n buɛlam ruḥen-d umbaɛd yimeẓulla ur newwiḍen ara zik zzin-as-d
kra n lweqt umbaɛd ssuffɣen-d amerḥum refden-t ɣef tuyat uɣen abrid yettawin ɣer yiwen n uzniq i d-yezgan deffir n lǧameɛ
timeqbert ur tebɛid ara mliḥ yiwen n ukilumitr neɣ ahat ur yewwiḍ ara
tezga ɣef yiwet n tewrirt ɛlayet ɣef tnezduɣin n taddart
lḥiɣ s laɛqel akked buɛlam
uzzlen medden ad refden tafekka n umerḥum akken ad t-rren deg uẓekka i heggan ssbeḥ zik
mi bdan ttarran akal yekcem buɛlam gar lɣaci-nni akken ad d-yaf abrid ɣer uẓekka yeddem talwaḥt yebda ula d netta yeṭṭeggir akal daxel-is
ur t-ɛandeɣ ara ur xdimeɣ ara am netta
qqimeɣ ɣer deffir ttwaliɣ kan deg tsusmi ttwaliɣ deg ddunit-a yessewhamen
ayɣer i ḥemmlen medden ad meḍlen win yewwḍen laɛfu n rebbi deg umkan ideg ilul deg wakal n leǧdud  d acu lferq yellan  kra n yiseggasen umbaɛd ad yedrem uẓekka-nni dɣa ad t-ttun maḍi
dagi neɣ dihin d acu lfayda yellan  d akal n rebbi irkelli am wakken i d-qqaren
wwḍen-iyi-d imeslayen n ccix n lǧameɛ ɣef tudert d tmettant ɣef lǧennet d unazir i nbedder dima ma nemḍel albaɛḍ
mi bdan medden ttruḥun nudaɣ ɣef si aḥmed gma-s n umerḥum si aḥmed ɛezzaɣ-t i tikkelt tis snat nniɣ-as daɣen wehmeɣ sdat n wayen xeddmen wat sidi merzug akken ad ḥarben ɣef tudert d wayla-nsen
rekbeɣ umbaɛd ṭumubil akked umeddakkel-iw
buɛlam neṭṭef takessart yezzin am uzrem srid ɣer uzaɣar nessusem yal yiwen deg-neɣ ɣef wacu yettxemmim
anwa yenɣan akumisar n temsulta n ɛayn-el-kerma 
anwa-t uberkan-a awezzlan  imir-n kan teffeɣ-d yiwet n tefyirt yeffren deg wallaɣ-iw yenṭeq-d yis-s yiwen n wass
racid asmi t-yesseqsa ukumisar ɣef yimeddukkal n
nabil  d akeḥluc-nni awezzlan i d-yettassen s axxam yettnadi fell-as  d yasin d ameddakkel iɣef yemmeslay
nabil deg uɣmis-ines  din-din kan tecɛel yiwet n iyi-d-tmel udem n  ukeḥluc tcemmaɛt akken ad tarbaɛt n awezzlan 
deg yiḍ-nni
ɛebdelǧabar icebbeh-iyi rebbi walaɣ albaɛḍ s uglam-a yeqqim ɣer tama tayeffust n ɛebdelǧabar yezdel deg yiwet n ubalṭu n uglim aberkan ɣef uqerruy-is yiwen n
 ubuni  d aberkan ula d netta
mmektaɣ-d mliḥ tura d netta
ḥala amecberreq n wallen-is iceɛlen deg ṭṭlam-nni i yessenzen tilin-ines gar-aneɣ
s ṭul n temlilit ur yenṭiq ula s yiwen n wawal
yettḥerrik seg lweqt ɣer wayeḍ akken ad iseggem tiɣimit-ines
iban yeɛya seg tɣimit
walaɣ ideg mlaleɣ amek i ineggez mi yekfa ɛebdelǧabar timlilit-nni yid-i
d netta daɣen i yeffɣen d amezwaru ɣer berra
d yasin ameddakkel n nabil  ulac ccekk d netta
ilaq ad waliɣ tanqiḍt-a d racid iwala-t yiwen n ubrid
ad susmeɣ sdat wayen yeḍran  ad neǧǧ win yenɣan si aḥmed d ilelli akken ad yernu ɣer umuɣ-ines tiɣtas niḍen  ur lliɣ ara d argaz ma susmeɣ
irgazen deg sidi merzug ttqabalen tamettant deg yal ddqiqa maca ɣas akken ur susmen ara kkren-d
ɣef wacu ad aggadeɣ nekkini  ur sɛiɣ tameṭṭut ara yeǧǧlen wala dderya ara yeddren deg lemrar d lḥif neɣ ad issinen tiggujelt
mi ara d-awḍeɣ kan ad ssiwleɣ i umaswaḍ n temsulta ad as-mleɣ amkan ideg tetteffer tarbaɛt n ɛebdelǧabar d tulut n ukeḥluc-a awezzlan
ad tt-xedmeɣ ur cliɛeɣ ara deg wayen ara iyi-yaɣen
sem  seg ctamber
lɛecra n yiḍ
ad yenɛel rebbi tudert-a ad tt-yenɛel rebbi ad tt-yenɛel rebbi
d acu ara xedmeɣ tura  yasin yeqqar-iyi-d enɣ-it d akafriw d amṭurni enɣ-it s yis-s ad taẓeḍ ɣer sidi rebbi wa ad tḥerreḍ amkan-ik deg lǧennet
lǧennet a nabil lǧennet lǧennet mačči am ddunit lǧennet deg-s yakk ayen yelhan deg-s ayen urǧin twala tiṭ wala tesla tmeẓẓuɣt wala tidmi iɛeddan ɣef wallaɣ n umdan učči tissit d tlawin a nabil d lḥur-el-ɛin
anekcum ɣer lǧennet yettili kan s tmenɣiwt-ines  dayen ɣunfaɣ ddunit-a
yettmeslay-d ɣef wučči tissit d tlawin
ayɣer lǧennet d učči d tissit d yiḍes akked lḥur-el-ɛin kan
 ihi ḥala ayen teccihwa tfekka n umdan  tafekka-inu tuɣal ur teccihwi acemma
iḍelli kan teseww-iyi-d yemma aḍaǧin n uyaẓiḍ s uzemmur d zzrudiya teččur-iyi taḍebsit tameqqrant acku teẓra acḥal ḥemmleɣ ssenf-a n wučči
tumert d uzmumeg banen-d ɣef wudem-is yettfeǧǧiǧen am lefnar   ečč a nabil a mmi ɣef derra-k i t-xedmeɣ
tḍaɛfeḍ mliḥ ussan-a ineggura ula d učči ur tetteḍ ara am zik
ečč a mmi ma ur terwiḍ ara ad ak-rnuɣ 
ur cliɛeɣ deg tmessaḍt n uyaẓiḍ deg tɛeqqayin n uzemmur wala deg zzruduya-nni wehmeɣ deg yiman-iw nekk i itetten zik azgen n teccuyt weḥd-i nekk i yeṭṭafaren yemma akken ad iyi-d-tefk ad ččeɣ mi ara sriḥeɣ kan rriḥa n ssenf-a n wučči ɣas akken mazal-it ɣef tmes
amek ad iyi-tewwet tmaggart ad agiɣ ad ččeɣ ayen ḥemmleɣ zik

i ḥur-el-ɛin amek gant ḥur-el-ɛin-agi  nekk kerheɣ tuzzuft kerheɣ tilawin

ɛebdelǧabar
ur t-walaɣ ara ugar n useggas seg wasmi t-ẓureɣ deg sseḥra
yasin i yi-d-yennan yeffeɣ seg lḥebs
maca ur ufiɣ ara tagnit ideg zemreɣ ad t-waliɣ
aṭas i nelḥa gar yixxamen urɛad nekfi lebni deg udcir amaynut n yenna-yi-d yasin tuget n yimeltaɣen n terbaɛt-nsen ttidiren daxel n uzadaɣ-nni ameqqran yellan d ayla n yiwen n umerkenti yeǧǧan
ɛayn-el-kerma iruḥ ɣer fransa
yewhem ɛebdelǧabar mi iyi-iwala
yenna-as yasin  d wagi d nabil mmeslayeɣ-ak-d fell-as yakan
tecfiḍ yid-i i yella mi ak-ẓureɣ deg sseḥra
yesseqsa-yi s tewzel ɣef liḥala-inu
kecmeɣ srid ɣer usentel ulseɣ-as beqqu-inu ad kecmeɣ ɣer terbaɛt-nsen
yenna  leqraya
ya amir   kerheɣ leqraya kerheɣ imawlan-iw bɣiɣ ad uɣaleɣ d aserdas gar yiserdasen n rebbi
imuqel-iyi-d mliḥ ihuzz aqerruy-is isellef i učamar-is yenna-d sakin  ansuf yis-k ɣur-neɣ
maca mačči ass-a
asmi ad ak-neḥwiǧ leqraya-inek  nniɣ  acu i ad ak-nsiwel s ubrid n yasin
yekcem umbaɛd d yasin ɣer yiwet n texxamt i d-yezgan deg ṭṭerf
sliɣ i ssut-is seg berra d aɛeggeḍ i yettɛeggiḍ ad as-tiniḍ yerfa
kra n lweqt umbaɛd yuɣal-d yasin yennuɣna
faqeɣ teḍra lḥaǧa gar sin n yirgazen-nni
ilumm-it ɣef dderra-w 
yasin ur iyi-d-yenni acemma
nelḥa kan amecwar awezzlan ɣef umkan ideg ffren yemsalam yid-i yenna-yi-d ad iɣib kra n wussan mi ad d-yuɣal ad iyi-d-yessiwel
yessefk fell-ak ad t-tenɣeḍ akka i yi-d-yenna yasin mi d-yuɣal umbaɛd semmus n wussan
ma txedmeḍ-tt ad tuklaleḍ s tidet ad tiliḍ yiwen seg aɣ-tesbeggneḍ yiserdasen n rebbi
nekk ḍemneɣ-k ɣer terbaɛt ḥuddeɣ-k
ad ak-d-iniɣ tidet llan kra seg watmaten bedden mgal unekcum-ik ɣur-neɣ
nnan-d baba-k d akafriw d azduklan
amek yezmer ad yekcem mmi-s n ukafriw ɣer terbaɛt n lmumnin
nniɣ-asen ur teḍfireḍ ara asɣan n baba-k kečč tḍefreḍ asɣan-nneɣ tewjḍeḍ ad tefkeḍ ayen ɣlayen ɣur-k d asfel i terbaɛt-nneɣ
ula d ɛebdelǧabar iḥudd-ik yesmekta-ten-id truḥeḍ ɣur-s ɣer sseḥra ɣas deg uzɣal n unebdu
deg leɛnaya-k ur iyi-ttxeyyib ara
ɣur-i nekkini d kečč i d ameddakkel aɛzizen fell-i seg wasmi nella deg uɣerbaz amezwaru
amek ad ten-qableɣ ma txeybeḍ-iyi ur texdimeḍ ara tuɣḍaḍt-inek tamenzut i ak-fkan
ma txedmeḍ-tt akken ilaq ad tuɣaleḍ d yiwen seg-neɣ i lebda
ad ak-magren imeltaɣen n terbaɛt s lferḥ ameqqran
ad d-tuɣaleḍ ula d kečč 
ass-a nemlal-d umbaɛd n tẓallit n lǧumuɛa nruḥ jmiɛ ɣer wasif n ṣefṣafa
yessuffeɣ-d seg lǧib n ubalṭu-ines n uglim aberkan yiwet n tmeẓyant yuẓa ɣer yiwet n tkalitust tameqqrant iwehha ɣer ljedra-s yenna-d   ad taẓeḍ ɣur-s akka ɣef lmitra ad trefdeḍ sakin tameẓyant ad tjebdeḍ fell-as
d ayen isehlen maḍi tamsalt-a ur tettaṭṭaf ara ugar n yiwet n ddqiqa
deg yiḍ-a ur tettu ara
ɛebdelǧabar yettkel fell-ak yeẓra tzemreḍ-as i tuɣḍaḍt-a
yaxi tenniḍ-iyi yal sem yettruḥu ɣer tberna ad isew ccrab aɛudu billah
tissit n ccrab d yiwet n lmeɛsegga tameqqrant win tt-ixedmen ilaq ad yemmet
yezmer ad d-yuɣal yeṣker tamenɣiwt-ines ad ak-tesseqreb ɣer sidi rebbi ad tekkseḍ seg ddunit-a yiwen n ukafriw yiwen n umṭurni lajer-inek ɣer sidi rebbi d ameqqran 
yuẓa-d sakin ɣur-i yessers tameẓyant deg ufus-iw yenna-yi-d   ḥṛes kan dagi ad teffeɣ tersast asmenɣer n tiṭ ad tafeḍ iman-ik d yiwen seg yiserdasen n
rebbi d yiwen seg wid ara ikecmen ɣer lǧennet
ad ak-nessekcem ɣer terbaɛt-nneɣ wa ad tuɣaleḍ d yiwen seg-neɣ 
amek ad as-iniɣ akafriw d umṭurni i yebɣa ad nɣeɣ d baba  yezmer ad ineɣ albaɛḍ baba-s s sshala-a  yasin d agujil ur yessin ara d acu i d azal n ubabat ɣer umdan
d yemma-s i t-irebban yekreh baba-s yezga ireggem deg-s s yir wawalen
acḥal d abrid i d-yeḥka d akken baba-s yebra-as i yemma-s netta mazal ur yessaweḍ ara ukkuẓ n yiseggasen deg tudert-is
ula d baba-s yella itess ccrab yettas-d s axxam yeṣker yekkat yemma-s yal iḍ
asmi imeqqer teḥka-as-d yemma-s kulci
ɣef waya yebda taẓallit meẓẓi akken ur itteffeɣ ara d asekran am baba-s
yenna-yi-d ula d netta yenwa ad ineɣ baba-s ad yaf kan anda i yettili
tewwi-t-id yemma-s ɣer udcir n  lebrarik  aseggas kan umbaɛd n berru-ines asmi d-tufa axeddim n temsizdegt deg uɣerbaz alemmas n ɛin-el-kerma
llan zedɣen deg yiwen n uxxam n uḥelyiw deg tama n
muzaya
yemma-s ur teẓri ara sani i iruḥ baba-s
qqaren-d yuɣ yiwet seg ɛennaba iruḥ yid-s
yenna-yi-d yasin ad isiwel i terbaɛt n watmaten-nneɣ n ɛennaba akken ad nadin fell-as
ma yeẓra anda i yettidir ad iruḥ ad t-ineɣ s ufus-is wa ad t-iceggeɛ s temɣawla ɣer unazir
yasin yezmer ad ineɣ baba-s s sshala mebla akukru
yedɣel wul-is ɣef baba-s acku iḍegger-it akked yemma-s netta mazal-it meẓẓi yedder d igellil d agujil
d acu ad iniɣ ɣef baba ur i yi-iḍegger ara am baba-s n yasin  ur ddireɣ d igellil urǧin ssneɣ lḥif am yasin
maca d akafriw ur yettẓalla ara yernu itess ccrab
yenna-d yasin d amṭurni acku ilul-d deg twacult tineslemt sakin yeffeɣ seg tneslemt
amṭurni ilaq ad yemmet
maca ayɣer d nekk ad t-yenɣen  ur mmeslayeɣ ara d yasin ɣef temsalt-a
txuss-iyi tebɣest
ayɣer mačči d netta iwumi fkan tuɣḍaḍt-a  i yemma tameɣbunt d tamuḍint d tawḥidt anwa ara ibedden ɣur-s  baba urǧin yestehza seg tama-agi
yezga yettruḥu yid-s ɣer yimejjayen d sbiṭarat yettaɣ-as-d yakk isufar yettɛasa-tt akken ad ten-tsew deg lawan
acḥal d abrid i as-sliɣ mi ad tt-yesmekti ad tsew asafar-ines nettat tnedder deg leqriḥ teqqar-as-d taɛya seg tɛeqqacin-a i tett yal ass mebla lfayda
d acu ara xedmeɣ  ur yettɛeṭṭil ara ad d-yuɣal
ad aɣeɣ awal n yasin d ɛebdelǧabar
deg tazwara qebleɣ mebla akukru
ɣileɣ d ayen isehlen maḍi
ad ṭṭfeɣ tameẓyant deg ufus-iw ad qqerseɣ fell-as
am wakken ḍerrunt deg yisura
sugneɣ iman-iw acḥal d abrid sdat-s wehhaɣ s tmeẓyant-iw ɣer wudem-is ad as-iniɣ s yiwet n taɣect tazurant   yewweḍ-d lajel-ik ay akafriw cehhed uqbel ad qqerseɣ fell-ak cehhed ahat ad yiḥnin rebbi fell-ak ad ak-yessemneɛ seg unazir
 acḥal d abrid i sugneɣ yenṭeq s cchada yuɣal ɣer tneslemt itub dɣa ur qqriseɣ ara fell-as
yemneɛ baba seg tmes n unazir
maca baba ur ixeddem ara akka ttwaliɣ-t simmal irennu deg uqhar d lkefr-ines
uɣaleɣ simmal ttxemmimeɣ deg tuɣḍaḍt-inu simmal trekkeb-iyi tuggdi tettergigi tfekka-inu
ad sleɣ i ssut daxel-iw itezzem deg-i  kečč d aderwic a nabil
amek ara taɣeḍ awal n ungifen-nni wa ad tenɣeḍ baba-k 
ayɣer tɛebbed imawlan-is ttarran-ten d amedya ttzuxxun yis-sen
maca imir-n kan ad sleɣ i ssut niḍen yettɛeggiḍ  d akafriw d amṭurni tamernut-ines d tamenɣiwt yernu amkan-ik ɣer
sidi rebbi ad yili d ameqqran
lmeɣreb yuẓa-d yasin ɣur-i
mi nemsefraq ɣer imuqqel-iyi-d s yiwet n tmuɣli tessekref-iyi yenna-d  deg yiḍ-a ur nqebbel ara agellel
ɛebdelǧabar yettraǧu deg-neɣ uqbel taẓallit n lefjer
ad ak-rǧuɣ dagi seg tnafsa n yiḍ
ɣur-neɣ tuɣḍaḍt niḍen ara nexdem azekka ssbeḥ ad tiliḍ d yiwen seg yiserdasen-nneɣ
ad tekkiḍ yid-neɣ deg imawlan-is  dderya tneqq dderya temzelt-inek tamezwarut deg lǧihad
nekkni d iserdasen imaynuten n rebbi inmenɣiyen-nneɣ am yinmenɣiyen n
bedr d uḥudd d yinmenɣiyen niḍen n yinselmen imezwura
ad naẓ ɣer sidi rebbi s yiqerra niḍen n yikafriwen iqehharen
tesliḍ i wayen i ak-d-nniɣ  yeṭṭef-iyi seg tuyat-iw imuqqel-iyi-d mliḥ ɣer wallen-iw  deg yiḍ-a ur ttɛeṭṭil ara ad ak-rǧuɣ dagi ur ttḥerrikeɣ ara seg umkan-a alamma tuɣaleḍ
ruḥ tura ad ak-iɛin rebbi wa ad ak-iḥudd am wakken yettḥarab u yettɛawen tarbaɛt-nneɣ
d acu ara xedmeɣ tura  hata baba yuɣal-d s axxam yekcem ɣer texxamt-is
mi yeldi tawwurt n usalun heggaɣ-d iman-iw ad suffɣeɣ tameẓyant seg lǧib n ubalṭu-inu wa ad qqerseɣ fell-as
allaɣ-iw yeqqar-iyi-d xdem-itt ma d ul-iw yugi yessekref tafekka-inu
ur sliɣ ara acu iyi-d-yenna
ur ẓriɣ ara ma d ssalam neɣ d awalen niḍen
ur ẓriɣ ara uɣaleɣ ulac acu i ẓerreɣ
yenneqbaḍ wul-iw ttḥulfuɣ i yiẓerman-iw qqersen daxel n tɛebbuḍt-iw
tura ad kkreɣ ad waliɣ d acu zemreɣ ad xedmeɣ
ad t-nɣeɣ  ur t-neqqeɣ ara ad t-nɣeɣ ur t-neqqeɣ ara
yasin yettraǧu deg-i d acu ara as-iniɣ 
allaɣ-iw irekkem ɛerqent-iyi tura ad ffɣeɣ  ur zmireɣ ara ad qqimeɣ dagi ur zmireɣ ara
ssdeɣ s yiḍuḍan-iw mliḥ ɣef tewreqtin-nni qemceɣ allen-iw seg leḥzen d wurfan
tɣaḍ-iyi liḥala n nabil uḍɛif i yeɣlin gar yifassen n wid i yesderɣel ddɣel wid ur nufi gar tigawin ad as-fken ḥala tin n tmenɣiwt n baba-s
ixemmem ɛebdelǧabar bu tasa n urumi xerttum ddqiqa kan deg tmenɣiwt n baba-s  ur cukkeɣ ara
amer ixemmem ulamma d tasint kan tili ur as-yettak ara tuɣḍaḍt-agi tucmit n tmenɣiwt n baba-s ur t-yettara ara daɣen deg tegnit ideg ad ineɣ iman-is
ih nabil yenɣa iman-is acku yugi ad ineɣ baba-s
tarsast-nni yettuheggan i racid yenɣa yis-s iman-is
yugi ad yuɣal ɣer yasin mebla ma yexdem tuɣḍaḍt i as-fkan
d acu-t udabu i yesɛa yasin fell-as  ur yezmir ara ad yemmeslay yid-s wa ad as-yini ur qbileɣ ara tuɣḍaḍt-a tafuḥant i yi-d-tefkam
tugna n
nabil hcicet yettseḍḥi mliḥ armi yuɣal ddaw n udabu n
yasin
ldiɣ allen-iw ufiɣ racid yeqqim sdat-i
yettwanɣeḍ tamuɣli-s truḥ mbaɛid
mmeslayeɣ-as ɣef usentel-a iḍelli mi d-nuɣal seg sbiṭar ideg neǧǧa nasira tameṭṭut-is am wakken i tella zik ulac acu i ibeddlen
nemmeslay-d ɣef tmenɣiwt n ukumisar n temsula d tulut n wid i t-yenɣan
akeḥluc-nni awezzlan d netta i d yasin  yenna-d iwala-t ugar n sin n yiseggasen tura sin n yiberdan kan yernu s ugacur
ih d axemri imal ɣer tebrek yettwassen s leqdic-ines d yineslemẓra
suffɣen-t seg tesnawit acku yugi ad iseṭṭel sakin ɣer yisebtar yettucergen seg tezmamt n nabil
yenna-yi-d ur yerri ara tidmi-s ɣer waya maca ad inadi fell-asen
yessawel-iyi-d leɛca deg yiḍ maḍi ixebber-iyi-d dayen yufa isebtar-nni yettucergen
seqsaɣ-t d acu yellan deg-sen yerra-yi-d mačči d lḥaǧa yesɛan azal
maca ḥulfaɣ yella umaynut mi iyi-d-yenna mebla ssebba deg usatel n umeslay-nneɣ  mmi ameɣbun kellxen-t lewḥuc-nni
sakin yesusem aččamar-ines
wehhaɣ faqeɣ yenṭer qrib ad yeṭṭerḍeq d imeṭṭawen
racid yezga yettru
anda-tt nnefxa-nni i t-tesbanayeḍ d argaz bu tissas ulac ugur ad t-ihuccen yezmer ad imager weḥd-s tiwuɣa n ddunit irkelli
mi ara yemmeslay yettkel ɣef yiman-is yeskasay s taɣect-ines tazurant d yifukal iseḥḥan
imerkiden-agi irkelli ruḥen yuɣal d acluḥ mebla lqima i yettawi waḍu
yeḍɛef yuɣal d awraɣ allen-is kecment daxel n wudem-is
nabil iruḥ d asfel d nniya-s d wul-is yesfan i yeglan s uqerruy-is i as-nniɣ akken ad sneɣseɣ fell-as leḥzen
yella iḥemmel-ik ɣas akken temgaradem deg waṭas n tenqiḍin
zzin-as-d yineḍliben-nni ifuḥanen ur yufi ara amek ad iqeṭṭi deg-sen ḥala s tririt n talast i tudert-is i uqerruy-is
allen-is
yerfed racid imeṭṭawen ɣas akken yenna-d s yiwet n yettergigin 
ẓriɣ d nitni i t-yenɣan tagi mačči d timenɣiwt anwa-t umẓiw-agi i as-d-yusan tikti-a n yiblis  amek ad nessuter deg walbaɛḍ ad ineɣ baba-s  ayɣer mačči d nitni i d-yusan ad iyi-nɣen  yewɛer fell-asen ad iyi-awḍen neɣ ufan-tt d tagnit akken ad t-sbaɛden ɣef terbaɛt s tarrayt-agi tucmit  maca ad d-rreɣ ttar-iw ad tt-xellsen yiwen yiwen
dagi yennerna ssut-is yuɣal iremmez seg wurfan am yizem
ad qelɛeɣ iẓuran-nsen i yesfuḥen tamurt
ad xedmeɣ deg-sen ayen ur yexdim ara hitler deg wuydayen
ula d nekk zemreɣ ad refdeɣ leslaḥ wa ad qerseɣ
tura ad sbeddeɣ yiwet n tmilicit yettuselḥen ad ten-ḍefreɣ ɣas ulamma kecmen deg uḥeččun n ttazzalen d taɣect tyemmatin-nsen
sliɣ kra n trebbuyaɛ n uḥuddu bdant ttbinent sya u sya
ad kecmeɣ deg yiwet deg-sent wa ad d-rreɣ ttar i mmi nabil ad d-rreɣ ttar-ik a nabil ad t-id-rreɣ
xenqen-t yimeṭṭawen yessusem
yeffer wudem-is gar yifassen-is yeṭṭerḍeq sakin d imeṭṭawen
eǧǧ fell-ak tura tikta-a tiberkanin a racid a gma
nasira teḥwaǧ-ik tura
d tamuḍint tanefsit-ines teɛya mliḥ teḥwaǧ mliḥ win ara ibedden tama-s wa ad as-yerr lbenna i tudert
ma d taggara n yineḍliben-nni kkes aɣbel wagi mačči d ccɣel-ik
ussan-a ad tesleḍ yis-sen
iḍelli kan walaɣ anmazul n ukumisar n temsulta amaswaḍ sliman fkiɣ-as isallen yellan ɣur-i wid iɣef k-d-mmeslayeɣ yakan
yenna-yi-d ṭṭfen tarbaɛt n yilmeẓyen n ɛayn-el-kerma d adda n deffir n yineslemẓra imselḥen wid i tettafeḍ yal ass bedden ɣef yiṭruṭwaren neɣ ɣer tewwura n yizaduɣen ttɛassan deg medden anwa ikecmen anwa yeffɣen
ur xeddmen ara tiwaculin-nsen d tigellilin maca ɣas akken ttlusun ḥala iselsa ifazen
seg wanda i d-ttawin idrimen amer mačči sɣur tirebbuyaɛ-a  d idrimen i sen-ttaken yimeẓla uffiren n tmura tiberraniyin d trebbuyaɛ n watmaten inselmen yellan deg umaḍal
yenna-yi-d wwḍen-ten kra n yisallen ad ten-yawin srid ɣer yifran n yineḍliben-a
ur ilaq ara ad ruḥen idammen n si aḥmed d yiɣallen n laman niḍen kan akka
ɣef waya ad ak-weṣṣiɣ ad teqqimeḍ d urkid ur ak-itteffeɣ ara laɛqel wa ad teǧǧeḍ iɣallen n laman ad xeddmen ccɣel-nsen
icebbeh-iyi rebbi ukin-d seg yiḍes-nsen tura ad asen-d-rren tiyita yernu qessiḥet
tuggdi tura ad d-tbeddel amkan ad tneggez ɣer tama niḍen
d nekk ara yeskecmen tuggdi daxel n trebbuyaɛ-agi n yiderwicen
ibedd yeqqim yettales kan i tefyirt-a yessed ɣef tuɣmas-is yekkat s lbunya
axxam-is yeḍyeq tura akken yeddari yakk urfan d zzɛaf i izedɣen ul-is
beddeɣ ula d nekk nniɣ-as 
kker ad nruḥ s ṭumubil ad nḥewwes deg ubrid n yillel
illel yessisir lxaṭer yettreccid kker fell-ak
serseɣ ṭumubil-inu deg umkan anda uɣeɣ tannumi srusuyeɣ-tt yebɛed s kra n lmitrat ɣef tewwurt n uzaduɣ ideg sɛiɣ tanarit-inu
munir aɛessas n ṭumubilat ulac-it ass-nni mačči d leɛwayed-is
uɣeɣ tannumi ttmagareɣ-t yal tasebḥit s uzmumeg-ines ahrawan i yeskanayen afermec-ines ladɣa tuɣmas-is n tazwara akked tenfalit n userḥeb i iḥemmel ad yessemres 
yezmer ḥala tafyirt-a i yessen s tefransist ineṭṭeq-itt-id s uɛwaj tqerreḥ imeẓẓuɣen-iw acku tesmektay-id amek i susruyeɣ zik-nni tafransist
acḥal d abrid i as-nniɣ s usqecmeɛ ttmenyifeɣ  alxir 
ɣas akken yeqqim yettɛawad i tenfalit-ines i ineṭṭeq s zzux yal mi ara i yi-iwali subbeɣ-d seg ṭumubil
ur yuɣ ara tannumi yettɣib
 ur ttruẓu ara aqerruy-ik ɛemmu aql-iyi dagi segmi yessuli rebbi ass alamma yewwi-t  am wakken iḥemmel ad i yi-yales yal tanezzayt
yettawi yettarra gar sin n yiṭrutrawen allen-is zgant ɣef ṭumubilat n yimastanen n yimejjayen d yimectariyen-nsen
deg uzaduɣ-nni llant tnariyin tisadranin d yimejjayen imawlan-nsen d isaxiyen yid-s
ula d azniq yeffreɣ
bdiɣ kan alluy n ddruǧ izɣarayen n uzaduɣ armi sliɣ i yiwen ssut yessawal-iyi-d 
muqleɣ ɣer deffir walaɣ-t yettazzal deg ubrid yettwehhi-d s ufus-is
a ruḥ-d ad twaliḍ ayen urǧin yeḍra deg
ɛayn-el-kermatamsulta tenɣa seddis n yirebraben tessers tifekkiwin-nsen deg tlemmast n umraḥ
ibedd ddaw n ddruǧ ilehhet yeḥerḥer
muqleɣ-t wehmeɣ deg-s ttraǧuɣ ad ikemmel ameslay ad iyi-d-yefk ifutas niḍen
dihin deg umraḥ n umenzu n wunbir tifekkiwin n yirebraben ttuḍeggrent ɣef lqaɛa ur tebɣiḍ ara ad tent-twaliḍ 
amraḥ irekkem s yimsulta
tetḥeqqeḍ deg wayen d-teqqareḍ 
am wakken i ak-d-qqareɣ lliɣ din iya-d ad twaliḍ s wallen-ik
mebla ma yerǧa tiririt-inu yuɣal s temɣawla
heggaɣ-d iman-iw ad t-ḍefreɣ maca imir-n kan mmektaɣ-d aqrab aẓayan yeččuren s yikaramen yetteɛlulluqen deg ufus-iw aẓelmaḍ
nniɣ-as ad t-sserseɣ uqbel deg tnarit-inu
twala-yi kan tneflust tekker seg umkan-is iban ɣef taɣect-is yella acu i tt-yuɣen 
a si ɛebdelqader tusiḍ deg lawan
uggadeɣ ad qqimeɣ weḥd-i
muqel afus-iw ur yezmir ara ad yeṭṭef ula d amru
walaɣ tifekkiwin n yirebraben mi tent-tsubbun seg tkamyunt teṭṭeggiren-tent ɣef lqaɛa
walaɣ-tent s ugacur
amer ur ɛeddaɣ ara syin axir
bɣiɣ ad d-aɣeɣ imendilen n lkaɣeḍ deg ukiyusk yellan deg umraḥ n umenzu n wunbir armi d-ɣliɣ fell-asent
ah ya rebbi amer ad tent-twaliḍ a si ɛebdelqader  sewḥacen s yičamaren-nsen iɣezzfanen d yiselsa-nsen yeblulɣen s yidammen d wakal
srewleɣ allen-iw fell-asent rewleɣ s temɣawla
ur ufiɣ ara tabɣest ad qerrbeɣ ɣur-sent
ahat d irebraben-nni i yenɣan akumisar n temsulta neṭgen daɣen ɣef tkamyunt n yimeḥbas
ahat d imeslab ur xeddmen ara leḥsab i wayen xeddmen
ɣilen zemren ad nɣen imestal kan akka mebla lexlas  tura ad ruḥeɣ ɣer din ad waliɣ s wallen-iw
ad iyi-teǧǧeḍ weḥd-i a si ɛebdelqader 
ulac acu ad taggaḍeḍ deg umkan-a
err tawwurt deffir-i ur ttɛeṭṭileɣ ara 
ẓriɣ ad teḍru tedyant am ta
iḍelli mi walaɣ sliman amaswaḍ n temsulta ufiɣ-t yettkel d akken zemren ad snegren tarbaɛt timselleḥt i yesqelqen temsulta deg ɛayn-el-kerma
ruḥen-d ɣur-sen kra n yifesyanen unnigen seg temsulta d yimeẓla uffiren sirden-ten ulac acu i sen-ǧǧan huccen-ten armi i sen-sruḥen lbenna n yiḍes i wacḥal n wussan
ur whimeɣ ara mi i yi-yewweḍ usali n usenger n terbaɛt n ɛebdelǧabar
d ayen ibanen umbaɛd n tmenɣiwt n ukumisar
wwten tamsulta deg uxxam-is
tiyita taqesḥant i tt-ihuccen ɣef waya tiririt-ines ur tɛeṭṭel ara tusa-d daɣen tejhed mliḥ tessewhem medden
ayen i yi-yesdehcen d afsar n tfekkiwin-nni deg tlemmast n umraḥ
ffɣeɣ s temɣawla qesḍeɣ amraḥ n umenzu n wunbir azayez
d tigawt n yigurdan ur xemmemen ara i yinalkamen
d axeddim n trebbuyaɛ yettmenɣan gar-asent ur tlaq ara i yiwet n tuddsa tunsibt i yettqadaren asaḍuf
d tiririt n ttar neɣ d asebgen n tezmert  d yir akernafal yessamasen leqder d lhiba n temsulta mačči d azal i as-yettarra
ɣef uḍar
yuzzel wawal am tmes deg tuga
imdanen ttazzalen seg yal tama ɣer umraḥ lewhama tban-d ɣef wudmawen-nsen ur umin ara s wayen slan
bɣan ad walin s wallen-nsen akken ad amnen
deg wagguren-agi ineggura yezrin nnan-d usan-d lmeyyat n yimsebblen seg yal tamnaḍt akken ad keccmen ɣer trebbuyaɛ-a timselḥin
leslaḥ yellan gar yifassen-nsen yif win yellan ɣer lɛesker amek ihi i ten-rnan s sshala-agi  mačči d nitenti i ten-iṛeggmen d akken ass n trennawt tameqqrant d usbeddi n lxilafa tineslemt qrib ad d-yaweḍ  ttmeslayen medden gar-asen tikwal s ustewtew tikwal s utram ttembaddalen isallen ɣef yiserdasen s yiččamaren yeččuren imudaɣ yezzin i
ɛayn-el-kerma
ttawin-d ifellaḥen d yimezdaɣ n tuddrin i asen-yezzin kra n teqsiḍin timakunin ɣef tigawin n yiserdasen-a n yiḍ
tikwal d imjuhad ara yerren i usɣan azal-is aqdim
tikwal niḍen iqeṭṭaɛen ẓeddmen ɣef tudrin qehhren imezdaɣ-nsen ttakren-ten
anda tella tidet gar ddiɛaya d usigged n lɣaci  tuget n yimdanen d babaɣayu s yiselsa n  ttalsen i wayen sellen ttbeddilen kra seg-sent akken ad gen ttuɣalen d amkan i yiman-nsen ɣas ulamma d inigan kan ama s lqella n tmussni s tuggdi s zzux s nniya neɣ ahat ttafen-d lbenna ma ulsen i teqsiḍin s ubeddel n kra yella deg-sent akken ad tent-rren ɣef yiman-nsen
nejmaɛen yirgazen d warrac ula d kra n tlawin ruḥent-d zzin-as i usebdad n yimeɣrasen
imsulta zzin-as i umraḥ seg yal tama
yal ssenf n ṭumubilat n temsulta d yiwen n ukamyun n yimsexsayen ḥebsen deg tlemmast n ubrid
agraw-nni iɣumm tamuɣli
ɛerḍeɣ ad zelmeɣ kra gar n tfekkiwin-nni
mebla lfayda
dɣa rẓiɣ asalu gar yimdanen-nni s usexdem n yiɣallen-iw akken ad awḍeɣ s amkan
tella lḥaǧa deg-i i yi-d-yeqqaren ilaq ad ɣiwleɣ
asayes-nni i walaɣ yessewhem-iyi mliḥ yerra-d ɣer tidmi-w isura n lwastern i nettwali deg temẓi-nneɣ  isura-nni yeččuren s tfekkiwin n lmeggtin yeẓẓlen ɣef wakal neɣ ijdi ddaw n yiẓenẓaren n yiṭij aqesḥan n sseḥra n
kalifurnya neɣ nifada
seddiset n tfekkiwin ttuḍeggrent ɣef tmurt
iselsa-nsent umsent s wakal d yidammen
udmawen-nsent yečča-tent uččamar jerḥent iban tejhed tiyita gar-asen
zzin-asent yimsulta s yiselsa izegzawen deg yifassen-nsen ṭṭfen timekḥal beggsen i tiyita ma yeḍra kra
ɣummen udmawen-nsen s yikagulen n taḍuḍt taberkant
ḥala allen-nsen yettmecberriqen i yettbinen ttmuqulent ɣer tama tayeffust d tẓelmaḍt ulac acu i sent-iruḥen ad as-tiniḍ d lazer
bedden ibeddi n win i yernan axsim-is iqerra-nsen deg yigenni idmaren-nsen cuffen iḍarren-nsen rsen ɣef wakal ibezgen
yewwet-d ciṭuḥ n ugeffur deg yiḍ
tasebḥit-a tesfa tegnawt
iṭij n ḥertadem yessehma amraḥ deg yigenni anagar kra n usigna i yeqqimen yettawi-t waḍu ɣer usammer
uẓaɣ ɣer tfekkiwin bɣiɣ ad ẓreɣ anwa-ten wigi yettwanɣen
deg tidmi-w myuckaḍent tugniwin  ɛebdelǧabar s teɣzi-ines d uččamar-ines aberkan yessden mi iyi-d-ihedder daxel n texxamt-nni d ɛebdelḥamid uḍɛif mi i yi-yettales i teqsiḍt-nni-ines yessewhamen sakin mi ileḥḥu nekk ṭṭafareɣ-t seg deffir akked yusef ɛeyyaci deg tlemmast n tebrunin n waman d waluḍ
xelḍent tugniwin d yisayasen kra usan-d seg ccfawat-inu tiyaḍ ayen ttwalint wallen-iw sdat-i
udmawen-nni ttemcabin irkelli d ixemriyen malen ɣer tebrek jerḥen ččuren s yidammen yeberguggen akken ad ten-tɛeqleḍ yessefk fell-ak ad tqerbeḍ mliḥ ɣur-sen
ɣas akken tban-d tfekka n ɛebdelǧabar yeẓẓlen deg tlemmast tmal
hata ihi uɣella-nni yebɣan ad yebnu anagraw aserti amaynut s wuzzal d tmes
yumen s tidet yezmer ad yernu yiwen n udabu i ibedden azgen n lqern aya staɛerfent yis-s yakk tmura n umaḍal  neɣ yesderɣel-it ddɣel armi yuɣal ur yettwali acemma anagar tiririt n ttar d iswi-agi i t-yesselḥayen  ahat d ɛeggu akked layas seg ddunit-a i t-yewwin ad iruḥ s yiḍarren-is ɣer lmut acku yumen ma yemmut d amḥaddi ɣef tneslemt ad yettwaḥseb d ccahid neɣ d ameɣras dɣa ad yekcem srid ɣer lǧennet  ayɣer ur as-mmeslayeɣ ara deg yiḍ-nni ɣef temsalt-a akken ad ẓreɣ tikta swayes yumen  aṭas n temsal nettwali-tent kan s wudem n tiṭ ur tent-nettwali ara s telqi dɣa ur nettfiq ara belli ur nessin acemma fell-asent alamma iɛedda lweqt
ur ẓriɣ ara ma nezmer ad nemmeslay akka ɣef trebbuyaɛ-nni timeẓyanin ur nesɛi acemma gar yifassen-nsent maca ɣas akkenn refdent leslaḥ deg wudem n fransa tameqqrant 
anwa i as-yennan imdanen-nni yesɛan kan timekḥal n usegged ad uɣalen yiwen n wass d asaḍen ihumirusiyen iwumi ad zzin luluf n ljunud ad ssawḍen ad ḥettmen ɣef
fransa ad temcawar yid-sen yernu ad tsemmeḥ deg yiwet n tmurt tameqqrant am lezzayer i testaɛmer awinas d uzgen  i wigi fkan tudert-nsen d asfel i tmunnent n tmurt-nsen  neɣ tamsalt-a d lemxaṭra tatrajidit yettawin kan ɣer sin n yiberdan d inemgalen ulac wis kraḍ  tarennawt neɣ tamettant  win yuɣen abrid-a yettwali iman-is deg yiwen n lweqt yerbeḥ yemmut
maca d acu i ten-yesselḥayen s tidet  tudert akked trennawt neɣ tamettant ɣas ma yella ula d abrid-a yettawi ula d netta ɣer tudert niḍen
ayɣer tignatin-a ttemcabint  tamettant ɣef uɣlan akked tmettant ɣef usɣan  zik-nni yexleḍ uɣlan d usɣan  medden ttakken tudert-nsen d asfel ɣef sin n yiswan-a
maca ass-a aɣlan d ayla n medden irkelli ma d asɣan tennulfa-d tarbaɛt-a i yebɣan ad t-yerren d ayla-s nettat kan weḥd-s
dɣa terfed leslaḥ mgal aɣlan
yekker-d ihi uɣlan-a ad iḥudd ɣef yiman-is ɣef usɣan-ines amezwaru daɣen
iban d aɣlan ara yernun asɣan am wakken teḍra deg yuruba
aɣlan d ayla n medden irkelli wid i t-izedɣen yakan d wid ad ikecmen ɣur-s azekka
ma d asɣan yettembeddal seg wakud ɣer wayeḍ
uẓaɣ mliḥ
bɣiɣ ad waliɣ udmawen-nni
iqerreb-d ɣur-i yiwen n umsaltu udem-is iɣumm ad as-tiniḍ yella acu i yeggad
maca ulac acu i d-yenna
muqleɣ-t nniɣ-as s yifassen-iw ulac acu ara yaggad seg tama-w beddeɣ sakin sdat n yiwet n tfekka tawezzlant tumes s yidammen d wakal tettuḍegger ɣer tama tayeffust qrib ad tenṭeḍ ɣer tfekka niḍen
aqerruy-is yečča tiyita ad as-tiniḍ s tɣawsa tuqḍiɛt i yettwawet
kniɣ ɣur-s mliḥ
aglim-is imal ɣer tebrek
d yasin akeḥluc  win yenɣan nabil  asali n tmenɣiwt-ines ad yessenɣes seg ddɣel d leḥzen n racid ahat ad as-tekkes seg wallaɣ-is tikti n urfad n leslaḥ i itezzin deg uqerruy-is ussan-a ineggura 
hata tẓeḍem-d yiwet n tmeṭṭut ɣef uqusis-nni uḍyiq tettsuɣu  mmi yusef
yusef mmi
tḍegger-iyi ɣer ṭṭerf tḥuza-yi qrib i yi-tesseɣli ɣef tmurt
ɛeqleɣ-tt s sshala s lḥiǧab-ines awinaɣ
d acu txeddem dagi yemma-s n yusef ɛeyyaci  ayɣer i tessawal s yisem n mmi-s am wakken deg tlemmast n tfekkiwin-a i yella  walaɣ-tt sakin temmeɣ ɣef yiwet n tfekka tettsuɣu  nɣan mmi yusef nɣan mmi yusef
ula yiwen seg yimsulta ur yembawel ara
bedden qquren
kerfen
walaɣ lewhama d tuggdi ɣef wudmawen n wid i yezzin i umkan rran lwelha-nsen irkelli ɣer tmeṭṭut-nni i yekkaten agejdur
qrib i ttuɣ d akken yusef yella yettiddir akked terbaɛt-agi
mazal ur irandi ara i temsulta  ayɣer ur d-yuɣal ara ɣur-i  ugin-as yimeddakkel-is ad irandi 
grarbent fell-i tuttriwin ur sent-ufiɣ ara ula d yiwet n tririt
qqimeɣ qqureɣ deg umkan-iw ttwaliɣ kan deg tmeṭṭut-nni tameɣbunt
hata mmi-s ayiwan yemmut s tersasin am wakken yemmut baba-s mraw n yiseggasen aya
d mmi-s s tidet  ahat teɣleḍ temmeɣ ɣef tfekka niḍen
maca ur tezmir ara tyemmat ad takez mmi-s  uẓaɣ ɣur-s s laɛqel ɛerḍeɣ ad tt-sbaɛdeɣ ɣef tfekka-nni
tmuqel-iyi-d s yiwen n wudem teffeɣ-it tudert yejmeɛ i yeɣlin ɣef talsa
taɛqel-iyi weḥd-s yakk tiwuɣa teckunṭeḍ deg ubalṭu-inu tsuɣ 
nɣan-t a si ɛebdelqader nɣan-t
hedden iman-im a uletma ahat mačči d netta
muqel-it mliḥ kečč tessneḍ-t muqel mačči d
yusef mmi 
refdeɣ iman-iw ciṭuḥ ɣef tfekka
d netta s tidet
ul ac acu yuɣen udem-is ur yejriḥ ara
ciṭuḥ n wakal kan
maca idmaren-is umsen s yidammen d wakal d yibeɛɛayen
ahat ḥuzan-t s tersasin deg yidmaren
tenna-yi-d deg tlemmast n yimeṭṭawen 
yusa-d ɣur-i snat n ledwar aya yenna-yi-d  azekka ad ruḥeɣ ɣer yimsulta ad randiɣ d acu i ixeddem dagi yemmut  mačči gar yifassen n yimsulta i ilaq ad yili tura 
tḍegger iman-is i tikkelt niḍen ɣef tfekka n mmi-s s yimeṭṭawen
heggaɣ iman-iw ad knuɣ akken ad tt-sbaɛdeɣ ɣef umkan-nni
kukraɣ ciṭuḥ d acu ara as-iniɣ 
tawaɣit-ines d anu ur nesɛi lqaɛwalaɣ liḥala-a yakan deg
racid d nasira
imeslayen weḥd-sen ur zmiren ara ad snejlin leḥzen
d acu ad d-tiniḍ i tyemmat iwumi nɣan mmi-s
nɣan-t ḍeggren-t deg tlemmast n umraḥ azayez am uneḍlib i tessusef tmetti asmi yedder d wasmi yemmut daɣen  nettat i yumnen yernu s tidet d akken ulac acu yexdem d ameslan i yella yezmer ad yemneɛ
kra n lweqt umbaɛd ruḥen-d sin n yimestal sbaɛden-tt
tbedd ur ten-teǧǧi ara ad tt-sbaɛden tennuɣ yid-sen armi tefsex
usan-d sakin yisexsiyen refden-tt wwin-tt ɣer tkerrust-nsen
ula d nekk ččiɣ tiyita ḥezneɣ
ur nwiɣ ara ad d-afeɣ
yusef ɛeyyaci gar teɣtas-nni
ḥala netta i yellan d ameslan gar lmeggtin-nni
ayɣer ur iruḥ ara ɣer temsulta am wakken i d-tenna yemma-s  ahat ass-nni i yenwa ad irandi deg-s yeɣli-d d wass-nni ideg nɣan akumisar n temsulta  snat n ledwar yezrin tura ɣef tedyant-nni daɣen
tamenɣiwt n wass-nni tekkes seg uqerruy-is tikti n urandi  neɣ d ameddakkel-is ɛebdelḥamid i t-iqenɛen ad yeqqim deg terbaɛt  neɣ ahat yuggez-it ad t-ineɣ ma yexdem-itt  anwa i yeẓran  neɣ yerrunda i temsulta dɣa ḥettmen fell-as ad yemɛawan yid-sen wa ad asen-imel anda yella umkan ideg ffren yimeddukkal-is din i yettwawet s tersasin i t-yenɣan  umbaɛd mi sliɣ i teqsiḍt-nni n uḥeddad d sin n yimsulta imakaren zemreɣ ad qebleɣ yakk turdiwin
ṭṭrad-a ifuḥ yumes ad d-yefk talalit i kra n rrwayeḥ d tifuḥanin i iqebbren ulawen wa ad qqiment ttafgent deg walun fellunt deg wulawen ur aɣ-ttaǧǧant ara ad nqabel tidet tafuḥant
yemmut yusef ɛeyyaci ula d uffir-ines yettwamḍel yid-s am wakken yettwamḍel uffir n ɛebdelkrim aḥeddad
kra n lweqt umbaɛd mi wwin yemma-s n yusef ɣer tkerrust n yisexsayen ɣlin-d fell-aneɣ yimsulta iɣummen udmawen-nsen bdan seɛsaqen deg lɣaci
reffden tifekkiwin ḍeggren-tent daxel n tkamyunt i ibedden tama n usebdad n yimeɣrasen
nnejmaɛen sakin deg tlemmast n umraḥ bdan kkaten s leslaḥ ɣer yigenni reffden ifassen-nsen
tiyita n rrsas tessexleɛ lɣaci dɣa rewlen
uɣalen yimsulta-nni ɣer ṭumubilat-nsen ffɣen seg umkan-nni s yisuɣan n trennawt
ula d nekk ulac acu ara xedmeɣ deg umraḥ-nni
skerkreɣ iḍarren-iw teffeɣ-iyi tezmert ttaɛraḍeɣ amek ad qeɛdeɣ iluɣen
ṭṭafaren-iyi wudmawen d tewlifin d yiseqsiyen i irennun deg-i reffu d leḥzen
mmektaɣ-d ass n unekcum-inu amezwaru ɣer
ɛayn-el kerma deg uqrab-iw tawerqet n tummlin-inu deg uɣerbaz alemmas  ibn badis  ul-iw yeččur s tumert bɣiɣ ad ddreɣ akken ilaq allaɣ-iw yeččur s tirga yelhan d yisenfaren dɣa tmuger-iyi-d am yisli i irekben agmer i d-yusan ad tt-inaseb
anda-tt ɛayn-el-kerma-nni anda-tt tamdint-nni turkidt ideg tezdeɣ talwit yesterḥiben s yinebgawen  ad d-tuɣal yiwen n wass  melmi 
tikta-inu deg wallaɣ-iw
